atha śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇaṃ viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhyaśrīdharīya vyākhyādvayopetaṃ prārabhyateśrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥnārāyaṇaṃ namaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam devīṃ sarasvatīvyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet  ViP śrīsūta uvācaoṃ parāśaraṃ munivaraṃ kṛtapaurvāhnikakriyam maitreyaḥ paripapraccha praṇipatyābhivādya ca  ViP tvatto hi vedādhyayanam adhītam akhilaṃ guro dharmaśāstrāṇi sarvāṇi tathāṅgāni yathākramam  ViP tvāprasādān muniśreṣṭa māmanye nākṛtaśramam vakṣyanti sarvaśāstreṣu prayaśo yepi vidviṣaḥ  ViP sohamicchāmi dharmajña śrotuṃ tvatto yathā jagat babhūva bhūyaś ca yathā mahābhāga bhaviṣyati  ViP yanmayaṃ ca jagadbrahmanyataścautaccarācaram līnamāsīdyathā yatra layameṣyati yatra ca  ViP yatpramāṇāni bhūtāni devādīnāṃ ca saṃbhavam samudraparvatānāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ ca yathā bhuvaḥ  ViP sūryādīnāṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ pramāṇaṃ munisattama devādīnāṃ tathā vaṃśānmanūnmanvantarāṇica  ViP kalpān kalpavibhāgāṃś ca cāturyugavikalpitān kalpāntasya svarūpaṃ ca yugadharmāṃś ca kṛtsnaśaḥ  ViP devarṣipārthivānāṃ ca caritaṃ yanmahāmune vedaśākhāpraṇayanaṃ yathāvavdyāsakartṛkam  ViP dharmāṃś ca brahmaṇādīnāṃ tathā cāśramavāsinām śretumicchāmyahaṃ sarvaṃ tvatto vāsiṣṭhanandana  ViP brahmanprasādapravaṇaṃ kuruṣva mayi mānasam yenāhametajjānīyāṃ tvatprasādānmahāmune  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasādhu maitreya dharmajña smāritosmi purātanam pituḥ pitā me bhagavān vasiṣṭho yaduvāca ha  ViP viśvāmitrapuyuktena rakṣasā bhakṣitaḥ purā śrutastātastataḥ krodhe maitreyābhūnmamātulaḥ  ViP tato haṃ rakṣasāṃ satraṃ vināśāya samārabham bhasmī bhūtāś ca śataśastasminsatre niśācarāḥ  ViP tataḥ saṃkṣīyamāṇeṣu teṣu rakṣasvaśeṣataḥ māmuvāca mahābhāgo vasiṣṭhī matpitāmahaḥ  ViP alamatyantakopena tāta manyumimaṃ jahi rākṣasā nāparādhyanti pitus te vihitaṃ hi tat  ViP mūḍhānāmeva bhavati krodho jñānavatāṃ kutaḥ hanyate tāta kaḥ kena yataḥ svakṛtabhukpumān  ViP sañcicasyāpi mahatā vatsa kleśena mānavaiḥ yaśasastapasaścaiva krodho nāśakaraḥ paraḥ  ViP svargāpavargavyāsedhakāraṇaṃ paramarṣayaḥ varjayanti sadā krodhaṃ tāta mā tadvaśo bhavaḥ  ViP alaṃ niśācarair dhagdhair dīnair anapakāribhiḥ satraṃ te viramatvetatkṣamāsārā hi sādhavaḥ  ViP evaṃ tātena tenāhamanunīto mahātmanā upasaṃhṛtavānsatraṃ sadyastadvākyagauravāt  ViP tataḥ prītaḥ sa bhagavānvasiṣṭho munisattamaḥ saṃprāptaś ca tadā tatra pulastyo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ  ViP pitāmahena dattarghyaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ māmuvāca mahābhāgo maitreya pulahāgrajaḥ  ViP pulāstya uvācavaire mahati yadvākyādguroradyāśritā kṣamā tvayā tasmātsamastāni bhavāñśāstrāṇi vetsyati  ViP saṃtaterna mamocchedaḥ kruddhenāpi yataḥ kṛtaḥ tvayā tasmānmahābhāga dadāmyanyaṃ mahāvaram  ViP purāṇasaṃhitākarta bhavānvatsa bhaviṣyati devatāpāramārthyaṃ ca yathāvadvetsyate bhavān  ViP pravṛtte ca nivṛtte ca karmaṇyastamalā matiḥ matprasādādasaṃdigdhā tava vatsa bhaviṣyati  ViP tataś ca prāha bhagavānvasiṣṭho me pitāmahaḥ pulastyena yaduktaṃ te sarvametadbhaviṣyati  ViP iti pūrvaṃ vasiṣṭhena pulastyena ca dhīmatā yaduktaṃ tatsmṛtiṃ yāti tvatpraśrādakhilaṃ mama  ViP so haṃ vadāmyaśeṣaṃ te maitreya paripṛcchate purāmasaṃhitāṃ samyak tāṃ nibodha yathātatham  ViP viṣṇoḥ sakāśādudbhutaṃ jatattatraiva ca sthitam sthitisaṃyamakartāsau jagatosya jagacca saḥ  ViP iti śriviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe prathamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaavikārāya śuddhāya nityāya paramātmane sadaikarūparūpāya viṣṇave sarvajiṣṇave  ViP namo hiraṇyagarbhāya haraye śaṅkarāya ca vāsudevāya tārāya sarvasthityantakāriṇe  ViP ekānekasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmātmane namaḥ avyaktavyaktarūpāya viṣṇave muktihetave  ViP sargasthitivināśānāṃ jagato yo jaganmayaḥ mūlabhūto nasamtasmai viṣṇave paramātmane  ViP ādhārabhūtaṃ viśvasyāpyaṇīyāṃsamaṇīyasām praṇamya sarvabhūtasthamacyutaṃ puruṣottamam  ViP jñānasvarūpamatyantanirmalaṃ paramārthataḥ tamevārthasvarūpeṇa bhrantidarśanataḥ sthitam  ViP viṣṇu grasiṣṇuṃ viśvasya sthitau sarge tathā prabhum praṇamya jagatāmīśamajamakṣayamavyayam  ViP kathayāmi yathāpūrvaṃ dakṣādyair munisattamaiḥ pṛṣṭaḥ provāca bhagavānabjayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ  ViP taiś coktaṃ purukutsāya bhūbhuje narmadātaṭe sārasvatāya tenāpi mahyaṃ sārasvatena ca  ViP paraḥ parāṇāṃ paramaḥ paramātmātmasaṃsthitaḥ rūpavarṇādinirdeśaviśeṣaṇavivarjitaḥ  ViP apakṣayavināśābhyāṃ pariṇāmarddhijanmabhiḥ varjitaḥ śakyate vaktuṃ yaḥ sadāstīti kevalam  ViP sarvatrāsau samastaṃ ca vasatyatreti vai yataḥ tataḥ sa vāsudeveti vidvadbhiḥ paripaṭhyate  ViP tadbrahma paramaṃ nityamajamakṣayamavyayam ekasvarūpaṃ tu sadā heyābhāvācca nirmalam  ViP tadeva sarvamevaitadvyaktāvyaktasvarūpavat tathā puruṣarūpeṇa kālarūpeṇa ca sthitam  ViP parasya brahmaṇo rūpaṃ purūṣaḥ prathamaṃ dvija vyaktāvyakte tathaivānye rūpe kālastathāparam  ViP pradhānapūruṣavyaktakālānāṃ paramaṃ hi yat paśyanti sūrayaḥ śuddhaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP pradhānapūruṣavyaktakālāstu pravibhāgaśaḥ rūpāṇi sthitisargāntavyaktisadbhāvahetavaḥ  ViP vyaktaṃ viṣṇustathavyaktaṃ purūṣaḥ kāla eva ca krīḍato bālakasyeva ceṣṭāṃ tasya niśāmaya  ViP avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattatpradhānamṛṣisattamaiḥ procyate prakṛtiḥ sīkṣmā nityaṃ sadasadātmakam  ViP akṣayyaṃ nānyadādhāramameyamajaraṃ dhruvam śabdasparśavihīnaṃ tadrūpādibhir asaṃhitam  ViP triguṇaṃ tajjagadyoniranādiprabhavāpyayam tenāgre sarvamevāsīvdyāptaṃ vai pralayādanu  ViP vedavādavido vidvanniyatā brahmavādinaḥ paṭhanti caitamevārthaṃ pradhānapratipādakam  ViP nāho na rātrirna nabho na bhūmirnāsīttamojyotirabhūcca nānyat śrotrādibuddhyānupalabhyamekaṃ prādhānikaṃ brahma pumāṃstadāsīt  ViP viṣṇoḥ svarūpātparatodite dve rūpe pradhānaṃ purūṣaś ca vipra tasyaiva te nyena dhṛte viyukte rūpātaraṃ taddvija kālasaṃjñam  ViP prakṛtau saṃsthitaṃ vyaktamatītapralaye tu yat tasmātprākṛtasaṃjñoyamucyate pratisaṃcaraḥ  ViP anādirbhagavānkālo nāntosta dvija vidyate avyucchinnastatastvete sargasthityantasaṃyamāḥ  ViP guṇasāmye tatastasminpṛthakpuṃsi vyavasthite kālasvarūpaṃ tadviṣṇormaitreya parivartate  ViP tatastu tatparaṃ brahma paramātmā jaganmayaḥ sarvagaḥ sarvabhūteśaḥ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ  ViP pradhānapurūṣau cāpi praviśyātmecchayā hariḥ kṣobhayāmāsa saṃprāpte sargakāle vyayāvyayau  ViP yathā sannidhimātreṇa gandhaḥ kṣobhāya jāyate manaso nopakartṛtvāttathāsau parameśvaraḥ  ViP sa eva kṣobhako brahman kṣobhyaś ca purūṣottamaḥ sa saṃkocavikāsābhyāṃ pradhānatvepi ca sthitaḥ  ViP vikāsāṇusvarūpaiś ca brahmarūpādibhis tathā vyaktasvarūpaś ca tathā viṣṇuḥ sarveśvareśvaraḥ  ViP guṇasāmyāttatastasmātkṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitānmune guṇavyañjanasaṃbhūtiḥ sargakāle dvijottama  ViP pradhānatattvamudbhūtaṃ mahāntaṃ tatsamāvṛṇot sāttviko rājasaścaiva tāmasaś ca tridhā mahān  ViP pradhānatattvena samaṃ tvacā bīja mivāvṛtam vaikārekastaijasaś ca bhūtādiścaiva tāmasaḥ  ViP trividhoyamahaṅkāro mahattattvādajāyata bhītendriyāṇāṃ hetuḥsa triguṇatvānmahāmune yathā pradhānena mahānmahatā sa tathā vṛtaḥ  ViP bhūtādistu vikurvāṇaḥ śabdatanmātrakaṃ tataḥ sasarja śabdatanmātrādākāśaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam  ViP śabdamātraṃ tathākāśaṃ bhūtādiḥ sa samāvṛṇot akāśastu vikurvāṇaḥ sparśamātraṃ sasarja ha  ViP balavānabhavadvāyustasya sparśo muṇo mataḥ ākāśaṃ śabdamātraṃ tu svarśamātraṃ samāvṛṇot  ViP tato vāyurvikurvāṇo rūpamātraṃ sasarja ha jyotirutpadyate vāyostadrūpaguṇamucyate  ViP sparśamātraṃ tu vai vāyū rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot jyotiścāpi vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātraṃ sasarja ha  ViP sambhavanti tatoṃbhāṃsi rasādhārāṇi tāni ca rasamātrāṇi cāmbhāṃsi rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot  ViP vikurvāṇāni cāmbhāṃsi gandhamātraṃ sasa rjire saṃghāto jāyate tasmāttasya gandho guṇo mataḥ  ViP tasmiṃstasmiṃstu tanmātraṃ tena tanmātratā smṛtā  ViP tanmātraṇyaviśeṣāṇi aviśeṣāstato hi te  ViP na śāntā nāpi dhorāste na mūḍhāścāviśeṣiṇaḥ bhūtatanmātrasargoyamahaṅkārāttu tāmasāt  ViP tejasānīndriyāṇyāhurdevā vaikārikā daśa ekādaśaṃ manaścātra devā vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP tvak cakṣurnāsikā jihvā śrotramatra ca pañca mam śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni vai dvija  ViP pāyūpasthau karau pādau vāk ca maitreya pañcamī visargaśilpagatyukti karma teṣāṃ ca kathyate  ViP ākāśavāyutejāṃsi salilaṃ pṛthivī tathā śabdādibhir guṇair brahmansaṃyuktānyuttarottarai  ViP śāntā ghorāś ca mūḍhāś ca viśeṣastena te smṛtāḥ  ViP nānāviryāḥ pṛthagbhūtāstataste saṃhatiṃ vinā nāśaknuvanprajāḥ sraṣṭumasamāgamya sṛtstraśaḥ  ViP sametyānyonyasaṃyogaṃ parasparasamāśrayāḥ ekasaṃghātalakṣyāś ca saṃprāpyaikyamaśeṣataḥ  ViP puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca pradhānānugraheṇa ca mahadādya viśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti te  ViP tatkrameṇa vivṛddhaṃ sajjalabudbudavatsamam bhūtebhyoṇḍaṃ mahābuddhe mahattadudakeśayam prakṛtaṃ brahmarūpasya viṣṇoḥ sthānamanuttamam  ViP tatrāvyaktasvarūpo sau vyaktarūpo jagatpatiḥ viṣṇurbrahmasvarūpeṇa svayameva vyavasthitaḥ  ViP merurulbamabhūttasya jarāyuś ca mahīdharāḥ garbhodakaṃ samudrāś ca tasyāsansumahātmanaḥ  ViP sādridvīpasamudrāś ca sajyotirlokasaṃgrahaḥ tasminnaṇḍe bhavadvipra sadevāsuramānuṣāḥ  ViP vārivahnyanilākāśais tato bhūtādinā bahiḥ vṛtaṃ daśaguṇair aṇḍaṃ bhūtādirmahatā tathā  ViP avyaktenāvṛto brahmaṃstai sarvaiḥ sahito mahān ebhir āvaraṇair aṇḍaṃ saptabhiḥ prakṛtair vṛtam nālikeraphalasyāntarbājaṃ bāhyadalair iva  ViP juṣan rajo guṇaṃ tatra svayaṃ viśveśvaro hariḥ brahmābhūtvāsya jagato visṛṣṭau saṃpravartate  ViP sṛṣṭaṃ ca pātyanuyugaṃ yāvatkalpavikalpanā sattvabhṛdbhagavānviṣṇuraprameyaparākramaḥ  ViP tamodrekī ca kalpānte rudrarūpī jarnādanaḥ maitreyākhilabhūtāni bhakṣayatyatidārūṇaḥ  ViP bhakṣayitvā ca bhūtāni jagatyekāṇavīkṛte nāgaparyaṅkaśayane śete ca parameśvaraḥ  ViP prabuddhaś ca punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ karoti brahmarūpadhṛk  ViP sṛṣṭisthityantakaraṇīṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmikām sa saṃjñāṃ yāti bhagavāneka eva janārdanaḥ  ViP straṣṭā sṛjati cātmānaṃ viṣṇuḥ pālyaṃ ca pāti ca upasaṃhriyate cānte saṃhartā ca svayaṃ prabhuḥ  ViP pṛthivyāpas tathā tejo vāyurākāśa eva ca sarvendriyāntaḥkaraṇaṃ puruṣākhyaṃ hi yajjagat  ViP sa eva sarvabhūtātmā viśvarūpo yato vyayaḥ sargādikaṃ tu tasyaiva bhūtasthamupakārakam  ViP sa eva sṛjyaḥ sa ca sargakartā sa eva pātyatti ca pālyate ca brahmādyavasthābhir aśeṣamūrtirviṣṇurvariṣṭho varado vareṇyaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśeṃ dvitīyo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācanirguṇasyāprameyasya śuddhasyāpyamalātmanaḥ kathaṃ sargādikartṛtvaṃ brahmaṇobhyupagamyate  ViP śrīparāśāra uvācaśaktayaḥ sarvabhāvānāmacintyajñānagocarāḥ yato to brahmaṇastastu sargādyā bhāvaśaktayaḥ bhavanti tapatāṃ śreṣṭha pāvakasya yathoṣṇatā  ViP tannibodha yathā sarge bhagavānsaṃpravartate nārāyaṇākhyo bhagavānbrahmā lokapitāmāhaḥ  ViP utpannaḥ procyate vidvannityamevopacārataḥ  ViP nijena tasya mānena āyurvarṣaśataṃ smṛtam tatparākhyaṃ tadarddha ca parārdhamabhidhiyate  ViP kālasvarūpaṃ viṣṇoś ca yanmayoktaṃ tavānagha tena tasya nibodhe tvaṃ parimāṇopapādanam  ViP anyeṣāṃ caiva jantūnāṃ carāṇāmacarāś ca ye bhūbhūbhṛtsāgarādīnāmaśeṣāṇāṃ ca sattama  ViP kāṣṭhā pañcadaśākhyātā nimeṣā munisattama kāṣṭhātriṃśatkalā triṃśatkalā mauhūrtiko vidhiḥ  ViP tāvatsaṃkhyair ahorātraṃ muhūrtair mānuṣaṃ smṛtam ahorātrāṇi tāvanti māsaḥ pakṣadvayātmakaḥ  ViP taiḥ ṣaḍbhir ayanaṃ varṣaṃ dve yane dakṣiṇottare ayanaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ rātrirdevānāmuttaraṃ dinam  ViP divyair varṣasahasrais tu kṛtatretādisaṃjñitam caturyugaṃ dvādaśabhis tadvibhāgaṃ niboda me  ViP catvāritrīṇi dve caikaṃ kṛtādiṣu yathākramam dvivyābdānāṃ sahasrāṇi yugoṣvāhuḥ purāvidaḥ  ViP tatpramāṇaiḥ śataiḥ saṃdhyā pūrvā tatrābhidhīyate sandhyāṃśaścaiva tattulyo yugasyānantaro hi saḥ  ViP sandhyāsaṃdhyāṃśayorantaryaḥ kālo munisattama yugākhyaḥ sa tu vijñeyaḥ kṛtatretādisaṃjñitaḥ  ViP kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaś ca kaliścaiva caturyugam procyate tatsahasraṃ va brahmaṇāṃ divasaṃ mune  ViP brahmaṇo divase brahmanmanavastu caturdaśa bhavanti pariṇāmaṃ ca teṣāṃ kālakṛtaṃ śṛṇu  ViP saptarṣayaḥ surāḥ śaktro manustatsūnavo nṛpāḥ ekakāle hi sṛjyante saṃhniyante ca pūrvavat  ViP caturyugāṇāṃ saṃkhyātā sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ manvantaraṃ manoḥ kālaḥ surādīnāṃ ca sattama  ViP aṣṭau śata sahasrāṇi divyayā saṃkhyayā smṛtam dvipañcāśattathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni tu  ViP triṃśatkoṭyastu saṃpūrṇāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ saṃkhyayā dvija saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutāni mahāmune  ViP viṃśatistu sahasrāṇi kāloyamadhikaṃ vinā manvantarasya saṃkhyeyaṃ mānuṣair vatsarair dvija  ViP caturdaśaguṇo hyeṣa kālo brahmamahaḥ smṛtam brahmo naimittiko nāma tasyānte pratisañcaraḥ  ViP tadā hi dahyate sarva trailokyaṃ bhūrbhuvādikam janaṃ prayānti tāpārtā maharlokanivāsinaḥ  ViP ekārṇave tu traitokye brahmā nārāyaṇātmakaḥ bhogiśayyāṃ gataḥ śete trailokyagrāsabṛṃhitaḥ  ViP janasthair yogibhir devaścityamānobjasambhavaḥ tatpramāṇāṃ hi tāṃrātriṃ tadante sṛjate punaḥ  ViP evaṃ tu brahmaṇo varṣamevaṃ varṣaśataṃ ca yat śataṃ hiṃ tasya varṣāṇāṃ paramāyurmahātmanaḥ  ViP ekamasya vyatītaṃ tu parārdhaṃ brahmaṇo nagha tasyāntebhūnmahākalpaḥ pādma ityabhiviśrutaḥ  ViP dvitīyasya parārdhasya vartamānasya vai dvija vārāha iti kalpoyaḥ prathamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe tṛtīyo dhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācabrahmanārāyaṇākhyo sai kalpādau bhagavānyathā sasarja sarvabhūtāni tadācakṣva mahāmune  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaprajāḥ sasarja bhagavānbrahmā nārāyaṇātmakaḥ prajāpatipatirdevo yathā tanme niśāmaya  ViP atītakalpāvasāne niśāsuptotthitaḥ prabhuḥ sattvodriktas tathā brahmā śūnyaṃ lokamavaikṣata  ViP nārāyaṇaḥ paro cintyaḥ pareṣāmapi sa prabhuḥ brahmasvarūpī bhagavānanādiḥ sarvasambhavaḥ  ViP imaṃ codāharantyatra ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati brahmasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam  ViP āpo nārā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ ayanaṃ tasya tāḥ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP toyāntaḥsthāṃ mahīṃ jñātvā jagatyekārṇavīkṛte anumānāttaduddhāraṃ kartukāmaḥ prajāpatiḥ  ViP akarotsvatanūmanyāṃ kalpādiṣu yathā purā satsyakūrmādikāṃ tadvadvārāhaṃ varurāsthitaḥ  ViP vedayajñamayaṃ rūpamaśeṣajagataḥ sthitau sthitaḥ sthirātmā sarvātmā paramātmā prajāpatiḥ  ViP janalokagataiḥ siddhaiḥ sanakādyair abhiṣṭutaḥ praviveśa tadā toyamātmādhāro dharādharaḥ  ViP nirīkṣya taṃ tadā devī pātālātalamāgatam tuṣṭāva praṇatā bhūtvā bhaktinamrā vasundharā  ViP śrīpṛthivyuvācanamaste puṇḍarīkākṣa śaṅkhacakragadādhara māmuddharāsmādadya tvaṃ tvatto haṃ pūrvasutthitā  ViP tvayāhamuddhṛtā pūrvaṃ tvanmayāhaṃ janārdana tathānyāni ca bhūtāni gaganādinyaśeṣataḥ  ViP namaste para mātmātmanpuruṣātmannamostu te pradhānavyaktabhūtāya kālabhūtāya te namaḥ  ViP tvaṃ kartā sarvabhūtānāṃ tvaṃ pātā tvaṃ vināśakṛt sargādiṣu prabho brahmaviṣṇurudrātmarūpadhṛk  ViP sambhakṣayitvā sakalaṃ jagatyekārṇavīkṛte śeṣe tvameva govinda cintyamāno manīṣibhiḥ  ViP bhavato yatparaṃ tattvaṃ tanna jānāti kaścana avatāreṣu yadrūpaṃ tadarcanti divaukasaḥ  ViP tvāmārādhya paraṃ brahma yātā muktiṃ mumukṣavaḥ vāsudevamanārādhya ko mokṣaṃ samavāpsyati  ViP yatkiñcinmanasā grāhyaṃ yadgrahyaṃ cakṣurādibhiḥ buddhyā ca yatparicchedyaṃ tadrūpamakhilaṃ tava  ViP tvanmayāhaṃ tvadādhārā tvatsṛṣṭā tvatsamāśrayā mādhavīmiti lokoyamabhidhatte tato hi mām  ViP jayākhilajñānamaya jaya sthūlamayāvyaya jayānanta jayāvyakta jaya vyaktamaya prabho  ViP parāparātmanviśvātmañjaya yajña pate nagha tvaṃ yajñastvaṃ paṣaṭkārastvamoṅkārastvamagnayaḥ  ViP tvaṃ vedāstvaṃ tadaṅgāni tvaṃ yajñapuruṣo hare sūryādayo grahāstārā nakṣatrāṇya khitaṃ jagat  ViP mūrtāmūrtamadṛśyaṃ ca dṛśyaṃ ca pūruṣottama yaccoktaṃ yacca naivoktaṃ mayātra parameśvara tatsarvaṃ tvaṃ namastubhyaṃ bhūyobhūyo namonamaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ saṃstūyamānastu pṛthivyā dharaṇīdharaḥ sāmasvaradhvaniḥ śrīmāñ jagarja parighargharam  ViP tataḥ samutkṣipya dharāṃ svadaṃṣṭrayā mahāvarāhaḥ sphuṭapadmalocanaḥ rasātalādutpalapatrasannibhaḥ samutthito nīla ivācalo mahān  ViP uttiṣṭhatā tena mukhānilāhataṃ tatsaṃbhavāmbho janalokasaṃśrayān prakṣālayāmāsa hi tānmahādyutīn sanāndanādīnapakalmaṣān munīn  ViP prayāniti toyāni khurāgravikṣatarasātale dhaḥ kṛtaśabdasantati śvasānilāstājha paritaḥ prayānti siddhā jane ye niyatā vasanti  ViP uttiṣṭhatastasya jalārdrakukṣermahāvarāhasya mahīṃ vigṛhya vidhunvato vedamayaṃ śarīraṃ romāntarasthā munayaḥ stuvanti  ViP ta tuṣṭuvustoṣaparītacetaso loke jane ye nivasanti yoginaḥ sanandanādyā hyatinamrakandharā dharādharaṃ dhīrataroddhatekṣaṇam  ViP jayeśvarāṇāṃ parameśa keśava prabho gadāśaṅkhadharāsicakradhṛk prasūtināśasthiheturīśvarastvameva nānyatparamaṃ ca yatpadam  ViP pādeṣu dedāstava yūpadaṃṣṭrā danteṣu jajñāścitayaś ca vaktre hutāśajihvosi tanuruhāṇi darbhāḥ prabho yajñapumāṃstvameva  ViP vilocane rātryahanī mahātmansarvāśrayaṃ brahmaparaṃ śiraste sūktānyaśeṣāṇi saṭākalāpo ghrāṇaṃ samastāni havīṃṣi deva  ViP muktuṇḍasāmasvaradhīranādaprāgvaṃśakāyā ViP daṃṣṭrāgravinyastamaśeṣametadbhumaṇḍalaṃ nātha vibhāvyate te vigāhataḥ padmavanaṃ vilagānaṃ sarojinīpatramivoḍhapaṅkam  ViP dyāvāpṛthivyoratulaprabhāva yadantaraṃ tadvapuṣā tavaiva vyāptaṃ jagavdyāptisamarthadīpte hitāya viśvasya vibho bhava tvam  ViP paramārthastvamevaiko nānyosti jagataḥ pate tavaiṣa mahimā yena vyāptametaccarācaram  ViP yadetaddṛśyate mūrtametajjñānātmanastava bhrāntijñānena paśyanti jagadrūpamayoginaḥ  ViP jñānasvarūpamakhilaṃ jagadetadabuddhayaḥ arthasvarūpaṃ paśyanto bhrāmyante mohasaṃplave  ViP yetu jñānavidaḥ suddhacetasaste khilaṃ jagat jñānātmakaṃ prapaśyanti tvadrūpaṃ parameśvara  ViP prasīda sarva sarvātmanbhavāya jagatāmimām uddharorvīmameyātmañchanno dehyabjalocana  ViP sattvodrikto si bhagavan govinda pṛthivīmimām samuddhara bhavāyeśa śanno dehyabjalocana  ViP sargapravṛttirbhavato jagatāmupakāriṇi bhavatveṣā namaste stu śanno dehyabjalocana  ViP śrīpāraśara uvācaevaṃ saṃstūyamānastu paramātmā mahīdharaḥ ujjahāra kṣitiṃ kṣipraṃ nyastavāṃś ca mahāmbhasi  ViP tasyopari jalaughasya sahatī nauriva sthitā vitatattvāttu dehasya na mahī yāti saṃplāvam  ViP tataḥ kṣitiṃ samāṃ kṛtvā pṛthivyāṃ socinodgirīn yathāvibhāgaṃ bhagavānanādiḥ parameśvaraḥ  ViP prāksargadagdhān akhilān parvatān pṛthivītale amoghena prabhāveṇa sasarjāmoghavāñchitaḥ  ViP bhūvibhāgaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā saptadvīpānyathātatham bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokānpūrvavatsamakalpayat  ViP brahmarūpadharo devastato sau rajasā vṛtaḥ cakāra sṛṣṭiṃ bhagavāṃścaturvakradharo hariḥ  ViP nimittamātramevāsau sṛjyānāṃ sargakarmaṇi pradhānakāraṇībhūtā yato vai sṛjyaśaktayaḥ  ViP nimittamātraṃ muktvaivaṃ nānyatkiñcidapekṣate nīyate tapatāṃ śreṣṭa svaśaktyā vastu vastutām  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe pṛthivyuddhāraścaturtho dhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācayathā sasarja devo sau devarṣipitṛdāna vān manuṣyatiryagvṛkṣādīnbhūvyomasalilaukasaḥ  ViP yadguṇaṃ yatsvabhāvaṃ ca yadrūpaṃ ca jagaddvija sargādau sṛṣṭavānbrahmā tanmamācakṣva kṛtstraśaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācamaitreya kathayāmyetacchṛṣuṣva susamāhitaḥ yathā sasarja devosau devādīnakhilānvibhuḥ  ViP sṛṣṭiṃ cintaya tastasya kalpādiṣu yathā purā abuddhipūrvakaḥ sargaḥ prādurbhūtastamomayaḥ  ViP tamomoho mahāmohastāmistro hyandhasaṃjñitaḥ avidya pañcaparvaiṣā prāgurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ  ViP pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyato pratibodhavān bahiranto prakāśaś ca saṃvṛtātmā nagātmakaḥ  ViP mukhyā nagā yataḥ proktā mukhyasargastatastvayam  ViP taṃ dṛṣvāsādhakaṃ sargamamanyadaparaṃ punaḥ  ViP tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargastiryakstrotobhyavartata yasmāttiryakpravṛttisya tiryakstrotāstataḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP paśvādayaste vikhyātā stamaḥprāyā hyavedinaḥ utpathagrāhiṇaścaiva te jñāne jñānamāninaḥ  ViP ahaṅkṛtā ahaṃmānā aṣṭāviṃśadvadhātmakāḥ ataḥ prakāśāste sarve āvṛtāś ca parasparam  ViP tamapyasādhakaṃ matvā dhyāyatonyastato bhavat ūrdhvastretāstṛtīyastu sāttvikordhvamavartata  ViP te sukhaprītibahulā bahirantaś ca nāvṛtāḥ prakāśā bahirantaś ca ūrdhvastrotodbhavāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP tuṣṭātmānastṛtīyastu devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ tasminsargebhavatprītirniṣpanne brahmaṇasta dā  ViP tatonyaṃ sa tadā dadhyau sādhakaṃ sargamuttamam asādhakāṃstu tāñjñātvāḥ mukhyasargādisambhavān  ViP tathābhidhyāyatastasya satyābhidhyāyinastataḥ prādurbabhūva cāvyaktādarvāstretāstu sādhakaḥ  ViP yasmādarvāgvyavartanta tatorvākstrotasastu te te ca prakāśabahulāstamodriktā rajodhikāḥ  ViP tasmātte duḥkhabahulā bhūyobhūyaś ca kāriṇaḥ prakāśā bahirantaś ca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāstu te  ViP ityete kathitāḥ sargāḥ ṣaḍatra munisattama prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇastu saḥ  ViP tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyaś ca bhūtasargo hi sa smṛtaḥ vaikārikastṛtīyastu sarga endriyakaḥ smataḥ  ViP ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ sambhūto buddhipūrvakaḥ mukhyasargaścaturthastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP tiryakstrotāstu yaḥ proktas tairyagyonyaḥ sa ucyate tadūrdhvastrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu saṃsmṛtaḥ  ViP tatorvākstrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ  ViP aṣṭamo nugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikastāmasaś ca saḥ pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāstu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ityete vai samākhyātā nava sargāḥ prajāpateḥ  ViP prākṛtā vaikṛtāścaiva jagato mūlahetavaḥ sṛjato jagadīśasya kimanyañchrotumicchasi  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācasaṃkṣepātkathitaḥ sarge devādīnāṃ mune tvayā vistarācchrotumicchami tvatto munivarottama  ViP śrīparāśara uvācakarmabhir bhāvitāḥ pūrvaiḥ kuśalāḥ kuśalais tu tāḥ khyātyā tayā hyanirmuktāḥ saṃhāre hyupasaṃhṛtāḥ  ViP sthāvarāntāḥ surādyāstu prajā brahmaścaturvidhāḥ brahmaṇaḥ kurvataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ jajñire mānasāstu tāḥ  ViP tato devāsurapitṝnmanuṣyāṃś ca catuṣṭayam sisṛkṣurambhāṃsyetāni svamātmānamayūyujat  ViP yuktātmanastamomātrā hy udriktābhūtprajāpateḥ sisṛkṣorjaghanātpūrvamasurā jajñire tataḥ  ViP utsasarja tatastāṃ tu tamomātrātmikāṃ tanum sā tu vyaktā tanustena maitreyābhūdvibhāvarī  ViP sisṛkṣuranyadehasthaḥ prītimāpa tataḥ surāḥ sattvodriktāḥ samudbhutā mukhato brahmaṇo dvijaḥ  ViP tyaktā sāpi tanustena sattvaprāyamabhūddinam tato hi balino rātrāvasurā devatā divā  ViP sattvamātrātmikāmeva tatonyāṃ jagṛhe tanum pitṛvanmanyamānasya pitarastasya jajñire  ViP utsasarja tatastāṃ tu pitṝnsṛṣṭvāpi sa prabhuḥ sā cotsṛṣṭābhavatsaṃdhyā dina naktāntarasthitā  ViP rajomātrātmikāmanyāṃ jagṛhe sa tanuṃ tataḥ rajomātrotkaṭā jātā manuṣyā dvijasattama  ViP tāmapyāśu sa tatyāja tanuṃ sadyaḥ prajāpatiḥ jyotstrā samabhavatsāpi prāksandhyā yābhidhīyate  ViP jyotstrāgame tu balino manuṣyāḥ pitaras tathā maitreya saṃdhyāsamaye tasmādete bhavanti vai  ViP jyotsnā rātryahani saṃdhyā catvāryatāni vai prabhoḥ brahmaṇastu śarīrāṇi triguṇopāśrayāṇi tu  ViP rajomātrātmikāmeva tatonyāṃ jagṛhe tanum tataḥ kṣudbrahmaṇo jātā jajñe kāmastayā tataḥ  ViP kṣutkṣāmānandhakāretha sosṛjadbhagavāṃstataḥ vurūpāḥ śmaśrulā jātāstebhyadhāvaṃ stataḥ prabhum  ViP maivaṃ bho rakṣyatāmeṣa yair uktaṃ rākṣasāstu te ūcuḥ khādāma ityanye ye te yakṣāstu jakṣaṇāt  ViP apriyeṇa tu tāndṛṣṭvā keśāḥ śīryantavedhasaḥ hīnāś ca śiraso bhūyaḥ samārohanta tacchiraḥ  ViP sarpaṇātte bhavan sarpā hīnatvādahayaḥ smṛtāḥ tataḥ kruddho jagatstraṣṭā krodhātmāno vinirmame varṇena kapiśenograbhūtāste piśitāśanāḥ  ViP dhyāyatoṅgātsamutpannā gandharvāstasya tatkṣaṇāt pibanto jajñire vācaṃ gandharvāstena te dvija  ViP etāni sṛṣṭvā bhagavānbrahma tacchakticoditaḥ tataḥ svacchandatonyāni vayāṃsi vayaso sṛjat  ViP apayo vakṣasaścakre mukhatojāḥ sa sṛṣṛvān sṛśṛvānudarādgāś ca pārśvabhyāṃ ca prajāpatiḥ  ViP padbhyāṃ cāśvānsamātaṅgānrāsabhāngavayānmṛgān uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva nyaṅkūnanyāś ca jātayaḥ  ViP oṣadhyaḥ phalamūlinyo romabhyastasya jatrire tretāyugamukhe brahmā kalpasyādau dvijottama sṛṣṭvāpaścauṣadhīḥ samyagyuyojasa tadādhvare  ViP gaurajaḥ puruṣo meṣaścāśvāśvataragardabhāḥ etāngrāmyānpaśūnāhurāraṇyāṃś ca nibodha me  ViP śvāpadā dvikhurā hastī vānarāḥ pakṣipañcamāḥ audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhā saptamāstu sarīsṛpāḥ  ViP gāyatraṃ ca ṛcaścaiva trivṛtsomaṃ rathantaram agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamānmukhāt  ViP yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chandaḥ stomaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā bṛhatsāma tathokthaṃ ca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmu khāt  ViP sāmāni jagatīchandaḥ stomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā vairūpamatirātraṃ ca paścimādasṛjanmukhāt  ViP ekaviṃśamatharvāṇamāptoryāmāṇameva ca anuṣṭubhaṃ ca vairājamuttarādasṛjanmukhāt  ViP uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire devāsurapitṝn sṛṣṭvā manuṣyāṃś ca prajāpatiḥ  ViP tataḥ punaḥ sasarjādau saṃkalpasya pitāmahaḥ yakṣān piśācāngandharvān tathaivāpsarasāṃ gaṇān  ViP narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśumṛgoragān avyayaṃ ca vyayaṃ caiva yadidaṃ sthāṇujaṅgamam  ViP tatsasarja tadā brahma bhagavānādikṛtprabhuḥ teṣāṃ ye yāni karmāṇi praksṛṣṭyāṃ pratipedire tānyeva te prapadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥpunaḥ  ViP histrāhiṃstre mṛdukrūre dharmadharmāvṛtānṛte tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate  ViP indriyārtheṣu bhūteṣu śarīreṣu ca sa prabhuḥ nānātvaṃ viniyogaṃ ca dhātaivaṃ vyasṛjatsvayam  ViP nāma rūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtyānāṃ ca prapañcanam vedaśabdebhya evādau devādīnāṃ cakāra saḥ  ViP ṛṣīṇāṃ nāmadheyāni yathā vedaśrutāni vai tathā niyogayogyāni hyanyeṣāmapi so karot  ViP yathartuṣvṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi parya ye dṛsyante tāni tānyeva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu  ViP karotyevaṃvidhāṃ sṛṣṭiṃ kalpādau sa punaḥ punaḥ sisṛkṣāśaktiyuktosau sṛjyaśaktipracoditaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe pañcamo dhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācaarvākstrotāstu kathito bhavatā yastu mānuṣaḥ brahmanvistarato brūhi brahma tamasṛjadyathā  ViP yathā ca varṇānasṛjadyadguṇāṃ ś ca prajāpatiḥ yacca teṣāṃ smṛtaṃ karma viprādīnāṃ taducyatām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasatyābhidhyāyinaḥ pūrvaṃ sarvametadbrahyā cakāra vai cāturvarṇyaṃ mahābhāga yajñasādhanamuttamam  ViP yajñair āpyāyitā devā vṛṣṭyutsargeṇa vai prajāḥ āpyāyayante dharmajña yajñāḥ kalyāṇahetavaḥ  ViP niṣpādyante narais tais tu sṛṣṭāścāturvarṇyavyavasthi tāḥ samyakchraddhāḥ samācārapravaṇā munisattama  ViP yathecchāvāsaniratāḥ sarvabādhāvivarjitāḥ śuddhāntaḥ karaṇāḥ śuddhāḥ karmānuṣṭhā nanirmalāḥ  ViP śuddhe ca tāsāṃ manasi śuddhentaḥsaṃsthite harau suddhajñānaṃ prapaśyanti bilvākhyaṃ yena tatpadam  ViP tataḥ kālātma ko yo sau sa cāṃśaḥ kathito hareḥ sa pātayatyaghaṃ ghoram alpam alpālpasāravat  ViP adharmabījamudbhutaṃ tamolobhasamudbhavam prajāsu tāsu maitreya rāgādikamasādhakam  ViP tataḥ sā sahajā siddhastāsāṃ nātīva jāyate rasollāsādayaścānyāḥ siddhayoṣṭau bhavanti yāḥ  ViP tāsu kṣīṇāsvaśeṣāsu vardhamāne ca pātake dvandvābhibhavaduḥkhārtāstā bhavanti tataḥ prajāḥ  ViP tato durgāṇi tāścakrurdhānvaṃ pārvatamaudakam kṛtrimaṃ ca tathā durgaṃ purakharvaṭakādikam  ViP gṛhīṇi ca yathānyāyaṃ teṣu cakuḥ purādiṣu śītātapādibādhānāṃ praśamāya mahāmate  ViP pratīkāramimaṃ katvā śītādestāḥ prajāḥ punaḥ vārtopāyaṃ tataścakrurhastasiddhiṃ ca karmajām  ViP vrīhayaś ca yavāścaiva godhūmāścaṇavastilāḥ priyaṅgavo hyudā rāś ca koradūṣāḥ satīnakāḥ  ViP māṣā mudgā masūrāś ca niṣpāvāḥ sakulātthakāḥ āḍhakyaścaṇakāścaiva śaṇāḥ saptadaśa smṛtāḥ  ViP ityetā oṣadhīnāṃ tu grāmyānāṃ jātayo mune oṣadhyo yajñiyāścaiva grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa  ViP vrīhayaḥsayavā māṣā godhūmāścāṇava stilāḥ priyaṅgusaptamā hyete aṣṭamāstu kulatthakāḥ  ViP śyāmākāstvatha nīvārā jartilāḥ sagavedhukāḥ tathā veṇuyavāḥ proktas tathā markaṭakā mune  ViP grāmyāraṇyāḥ smṛtā hyetā oṣadhyastu caturdaśa yajñaniṣpattaye yajñastathāsāṃ heturuttamaḥ  ViP etāś ca saha yajñena prajānāṃ kāraṇaṃ param parāvaravidaḥ prājñāstato yajñānvitanveta  ViP ahanyahanyanuṣṭhānaṃ yajñānāṃ munisattama upakārakaraṃ puṃsāṃ kriyamāṇā ghaśāntidam  ViP yeṣāṃ tu kālasṛṣo sau pāpabandurmahāmune cetaḥsu vavṛdhe cakruste na yajñeṣu mānasam  ViP vedavādāṃs tathā vedānyajña karmādikaṃ ca yat tatsarvaṃ nindayāmāsuryajñavyāsedhakāriṇaḥ  ViP pravṛttimārgavyucchittikāriṇo vedanindakāḥ durātmāno durācārā babhūvuḥ kuṭilāśayāḥ  ViP saṃsiddhāyāṃ tu vārtāyāṃ prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā prajāpatiḥ saryādāṃ sthāpayāmāsa yathāsthānaṃ yathāguṇam  ViP varṇā nāmāśramāṇāṃ ca dharmadharmabhṛtāṃ vara lokāṃś ca sarvavarṇānāṃ samyagdharmānupālinām  ViP prajāpatyaṃ brahmaṇānāṃ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ kriyāvatām sthānamaindraṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ saṃgrameṣvanivartatām  ViP vaiśyānāṃ mārutaṃ sthānaṃ svadharmamanuvartinām gāndharvaṃ śūdrajātīnāṃparicaryānuvartinām  ViP aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnāmūrdhvaretasām smṛtaṃ teṣāṃ tu yatsthānaṃ tadeva guruvāsinām  ViP saptarṣiṇāṃ tu yatsthānaṃ smṛtaṃ tadvai vanaukasām prājāpatyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ nyāsināṃ brahmasaṃjñitam  ViP yogināmamṛtaṃ sthānaṃ svātmasaṃtoṣakāriṇām  ViP ekāntinaḥ sadā brahmadhyāyino yoginaś ca ye teṣāṃ tu paramaṃ sthānaṃ yattatpaśyanti sūrayaḥ  ViP gatvāgatvā nivartante candrasūryādayo grahāḥ adyāpi na nivartante dvādaśākṣaracintakāḥ  ViP tāmistramandhatāmistraṃ mahārauravarauravau asipatravanaṃ ghoraṃ kālasūtramavīcikam  ViP vinindakānāṃ vedasya yajñavyāghātakāriṇām sthānametatsamākhyātaṃ svadharmatyāginaś ca ye  ViP iti śrīviṣṇururāṇe prathame ṃśe ṣaṣṭho dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācatatobhidhyāyatastasya jajñire mānasāḥ prajāḥ taccharīrasamutpannaiḥ kāryais taiḥ karaṇaiḥ saha kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebhyasya syaḥ dhīmataḥ  ViP te sarve samāvartanta ye mayā prāgudāhatāḥ devādyāḥ sthāvarāntāś ca traiguṇyaviṣaye sthitāḥ  ViP evaṃbhūtāni sṛṣṭāni carāṇi sthāvarāṇi ca  ViP yadāsya tāḥ prajāḥ sarvā na vyavardhanta dhīmataḥ athānyānmānasānputrānsadṛśānātmano sṛjat  ViP bhṛguṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratumaṅgirasaṃ tathā marīciṃ dabhamatriṃ ca vasiṣṭhaṃ caiva mānasān  ViP nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ  ViP khyātiṃ bhūtiṃ ca saṃbhūtiṃ kṣamāṃ prītiṃ tathaiva ca sannatiṃ ca tathaivorjamanasūyāṃ tathaiva ca  ViP prasūtiṃ ca tataḥ sṛṣṭvā dadau teṣāṃ mahātmanām patnyo bhavadhva mityuktvā samutpanna stadā rudro madhyāhnārkasamaprabhaḥ  ViP ardhanārīnaravapuḥ pracaṇḍo tiśarīravān vibhajātmānamityuktvā taṃ brahmāntardadhe tataḥ  ViP tathoktosau dvidhā strītvaṃ puruṣatvaṃ tathākarot vibhedapuruṣatvaṃ ca daśadhā caikadhā punaḥ  ViP saumyāsaumyostadāśāntāśāntaiḥ strītvaṃ ca sa prabhuḥ vibheda bahudhā devāḥ svarūpair asitaiḥ sitaiḥ  ViP tato brahmātmasaṃbhūtaṃ pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ prabhu ātmānameva kṛta vānprajāpālye manuṃ dvija  ViP śatarūpāṃ ca tāṃ nārīṃ taponirdhūtakalpaṣām svāyaṃbhuvo manurdevaḥ patnītve jagṛhe prabhuḥ  ViP tasmāttu puruṣāddevī śatarūpā vyajāyata priyavratottānapādau prasūtyākūtisaṃjñitam  ViP kanyādvayaṃ ca dharmajña rūpaudāryaguṇānvitam dadau prasūtiṃ dakṣāya ākūtiṃ rucaye purā  ViP prajāpatiḥ sa jagrāha tayorjajñe sadakṣiṇaḥ putro yajñe mahābhāga dampatyormithunaṃ tataḥ  ViP yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu putrā dvādaśa jajñire yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyaṃbhuve manau  ViP prasūtyāṃ ca tathā dakṣaścatastro viṃśatis tathā sasarja kanyāstāsāṃ ca samyaṅnāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭirmedhā puṣṭis tathā kriyā buddhirlajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtistrayodaśī  ViP patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ tābhyaḥ śiṣṭayavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ  ViP khyātiḥ satyatha saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ pītiḥ kṣamā tathā santatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā  ViP bhṛturbhavo marīciś ca tathā caivāṅgirā muniḥ pulastyaḥ pulahaścaiva kratuścarṣivaras tathā  ViP atrirvasiṣṭho vahniś ca pitaraś ca yathākramama khyātyādya jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayo muni sattama  ViP śraddhā kāmaṃ calā darpaṃ niyamaṃ dhṛtirātmajam santoṣaṃ ca tathā tuṣṭirlobhaṃ puṣṭirasūyata  ViP medhā śrutaṃ kriyā daṇḍaṃ nayaṃ vinayameva ca  ViP bodhaṃ buddhis tathā lajjā vinayaṃ vapurātmajam vyavasāyaṃ prajajñe vai kṣemaṃ śāntirasūyatā  ViP sukhaṃ siddhiryaśaḥ kīrtirityete dharmasūnavaḥ kāmādratiḥ sutaṃ harṣaṃ dharmapautramasūyata  ViP hiṃsā bhāryā tvadharmasya tato jajñe tathānṛtam kanyā ca nikṛtistābhyāṃ māyā jajñe ca vedanā  ViP māyā ca vedanā caiva mithunaṃ tvidametayoḥ tayorjajñetha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam  ViP vedanā svasūtaṃ cāpi duḥkhaṃ jajñe tha rauravāt mṛtyorvyādhijarāśokatṛṣṇakrodhāś ca jajñire  ViP duḥkhottarāḥ smṛtā hyete sarve cādharmalakṣaṇāḥ naiṣāṃ putrosti vai bhāryā te sarve hyūrdhvaretasaḥ  ViP raudrāṇyetānirūpāṇi viṣṇormunivarātmaja nityapralayahetutvaṃ jagatosya prayānti vai  ViP dakṣo marīciratriś sthitirbrahmannityasargastatheritaḥ nityābhāvaś ca teṣāṃ vai svarūpaṃ mama kathyatām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasargasthitivināśāṃś ca bhagavānmadhusūdanaḥ tais tai rūpair acintyātmā karotyavyāhato vibhuḥ  ViP naimittikaḥ prākṛtikastathaivātyantiko dvija nityaś ca sarvabhūtānāṃ pralayo yaṃ caturvidhaḥ  ViP brahmo naimittikastatra ccheteyaṃ jagatīpatiḥ prayāti prākṛtaṃ caiva brahmaṇḍaṃ prakṛtau layam  ViP jñānādātyantikaḥ prokto yoginaḥ paramātmani nityaḥ sadaiva bhūtānāṃ yo vināśo divāniśam  ViP prasūtiḥ prakṛteryā tu sā sṛṣṭiḥ prākṛtā smṛtā dainandinī tathā proktā nāntarapralayādanu  ViP sthitivināśānāṃ śaktayaḥ sarvadehiṣu vaiṣṇavyaḥ parivartante maitreyāharniśaṃ samāḥ  ViP guṇatrayamayaṃ hyatadbrahyan śaktitrayaṃ mahat yo tiyāti sā yātyeva paraṃ nāvartate punaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe saptamo dhyāyaḥ śrīpāraśara uvācakathitastāmasaḥ sargo brahmaṇaste mahāmune rudrasargaṃ pravakṣyāmi tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu  ViP kalpādāvātmanastulyaṃ sutaṃ pradhyāyatastataḥ prādurāsītprabhoraṅke kumāro nīlalohitaḥ  ViP ruroda susvaraṃ sotha prādravaddi jasattama kiṃ tvaṃ rodiṣi taṃ brahma rudantaṃ pratyuvāca ha  ViP nāma dehīti taṃ so tha pratyuvāca prajāpatiḥ rudrastvaṃ devanāmnāsi māro dīrdhairyamāvaha evamuktaḥ punaḥ so tha saptakṛtvo ruroda vai  ViP tatonyāni dadau tasmai sapta nāmāni vai prabhuḥ sthānāni caiṣāmaṣṭānāṃ patnīḥ putrāṃś ca sa prabhuḥ  ViP bhavaṃ śarvamatheśānaṃ tathā paśupatiṃ dvija bhīmamugraṃ mahādevamuvāca sa pitāmahaḥ  ViP cakre nāmānyathaitāni sthānānyeṣāṃ cakāra saḥ sūryo jalaṃ mahī vāyurvahnirākāśameva ca dīkṣito brahmaṇaḥ soma ityetāstanavaḥ kramāt  ViP suvarcalā tathaivoṣā vikeśī cāparā śivā svāhā diśas tathā dīkṣā rohiṇī ca yathākramam  ViP sūryādīnāṃ dvijaśreṣṭha rudrādyair nāmabhiḥ saha patnyaḥ smṛtā mahābhāga devau dhātṛvidhātārau bhṛgoḥ khyātirasūyata śriyaṃ ca devadevasya patnī nārāyaṇasya yā  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācakṣīrābdhau śrīḥ samutpannā śrūyate mṛtamanthane bhṛgoḥ khyātyāṃ samutpannetyetadāha kathaṃ ViP śaṅkaro bhagavāñchaurirgaurīlakṣmīrdvijottama maitreya keśavaḥ sūryastatprabhā kamalālayā  ViP viṣṇuḥ pitṛgaṇaḥ padmā svadhā śāśvatapuṣṭidā dyauḥ śrīḥ sarvātmako viṣṇuravakāśotivistaraḥ  ViP śaśāṅkaḥ śrīdharaḥ kāntiḥ śrīstathaivānapāyinī dhṛtirlakṣmīrjagacceṣṭā vāyuḥ sarvatrago hariḥ  ViP jaladhirdvijagovindastadvelā śrīrmahāmune lakṣmīsvarūpamindrāṇī devendro madhusūdanaḥ  ViP yamaścakradharaḥ sākṣāddhūmorṇā kamalālayā ṛddhiḥ śrīḥ śrīdharo devaḥ svayameva dhaneśvaraḥ  ViP gaurī lakṣmīmaṃhābāgā keśavo varuṇaḥ svayam śrīrdevasenā viprendra devasenāpatirhariḥ  ViP avaṣṭaṃbho nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ratī rāgaś ca maitreya lakṣmīrgovinda eva ca  ViP kiṃ cātibahunoktena saṃkṣepeṇedamucyate  ViP devatiryaṅmanuṣyādau punnāmā bhagavānhariḥ strīnāmnī śrīś ca vijñeyā nānayorvidyate param  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe aṣṭamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaidaṃ ca śṛṇu maitreya yatpṛṣṭohamiha tvayā śrīsambandhaṃ māyāpyetacchrutamāsīnmarīcitaḥ  ViP durvāsāḥ śaṅkarasyāṃśaścāra cikṣeponmattavanmuniḥ  ViP gṛhītvāmararājena sragairāvatamūrdhani nyastā rarāja kailāsaśikhare jāhnavī yathā  ViP madāndhakāritākṣosau gandhākṛṣṭena vāraṇaḥ kareṇāghrāya cikṣepa tāṃ srajaṃ dharaṇītale  ViP tataścukrodha bhagavāndurvāsā muni sattamaḥ maitreya devarājānaṃ kruddhaścaitaduvāca ha  ViP durvāsā uvācaaiśvaryamadaduṣṭātmannatistabdhosi vāsava śriyo dhāma srajaṃ yastvaṃ maddattāṃ nābhinandasi  ViP prasāda iti noktaṃ te praṇipātapuraḥ saram harṣotphullakapolena na cāpi śirasā dhṛtā  ViP mayā dattāmi māṃ mālaṃ yasmānna bahu manyase trailokyaśrīrato mūḍha vināśamupayāsyati  ViP sa tadā praṇipātapuraḥsaram ityuvāca sahasrākṣaṃ durvāsā munisattama  ViP durvāsā uvācanāhaṃ kṛpāluhṛdayo na camāṃ bhajate kṣamā anye te munayaḥ śakra durvāsasamavehi māma  ViP gautamādibhir anyais bhṛkuṭīkuṭilaṃ mukham nirīkṣya kastribhuvane mama yo na gato bhayam  ViP nāhaṃ kṣamiṣye bahunā kimuktena śatakrato viḍaṃbanāmimāṃ bhūyaḥ karoṣyanunayātmikām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā prayayai vipro devarājopi taṃ punaḥ āruhyairāvataṃ brahman prayayāvamarāvatīm  ViP tataḥ prabhṛti niḥśrīkaṃ saśakraṃ bhuvanatrayam maitreyāsīdapadhvastaṃ saṃkṣā ṇauṣadhivīrudham  ViP na yajñāḥ samavartante na prathitaḥ pumān evamatyantaniḥśrīke trailokye sattvavarjite  ViP davān prati balodyogaṃ cakrurdaiteyadānavāḥ  ViP lobhābhibhūtā niḥśrīkā daityāḥ sattvavivarjitāḥ śripāvihīnair niḥsattvair devaiś cakrus tato raṇam  ViP vijitāstridaśā daityair indrādyāḥ śaraṇaṃ yayuḥ pitāmahaṃ mahābhāgaṃ hutāśanapurogamāḥ  ViP yathāvatkathito devair brahmā prāha tataḥ surān parāvareśaṃ śaraṇaṃ vrajadhvamasurārdanam  ViP utpattisthitināśānāmahetuṃ hetumīśvaram prajā patipatiṃ viṣṇumanantamaparājitam  ViP pradhānapuṃsorajayoḥ kāraṇaṃ kāryabhūtayoḥ praṇatārtiharaṃ viṣṇuṃ sa vaḥ śreyo vidhāsyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevamuktvā surānsarvān brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ kṣīrodasyottaraṃ tīraṃ tair eva sahito yayau  ViP sa gatvā tridaśaiḥ sarvaiḥ samavetaḥ pitāmahaḥ tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ parāvarapatiṃ harim  ViP brahmovācanamāmi sarvaṃ sarveśamanantamajamavyayam lokadhāma dharādhāramaprakāśamabhedinam  ViP nārāyaṇamaṇīyāṃsamaśeṣaṇāmaṇīyasām samastānāṃ gariṣṭhaṃ ca bhūrādīnāṃ garīyasām  ViP yatra sarvaṃ yataḥ sarvamutpannaṃ matpuraḥsaram sarvabhūtaś ca yo devaḥ parāṇāmapi yaḥ paraḥ  ViP paraḥ parasmātpuruṣātparamātmasvarūpadhṛk yogibhiścintyate yo sau suktihetormumukṣubhiḥ  ViP sattvādayo na santīśe yatra ca prākṛtā guṇāḥ sa śuddhaḥ sarvaśuddhebhyaḥ pumānādyaḥ prasīdatu  ViP kalā kāṣṭhā muhūrtādikālāsūtrasya gocare yasya śaktirna śuddhasya sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  ViP procyate parameśo hi yaḥ śuddho pyupacārataḥ prasīdatu sa no viṣṇurātmā yaḥ sarvadehinām  ViP yaḥ kāraṇaṃ ca kāryaṃ ca kāraṇasyāpi kāraṇam kārya syāpi ca yaḥ kāryaṃ prasīdatu sa no hariḥ  ViP kāryakāryasya yatkāryaṃ tatkāryasyāpi yaḥ svayam tatkāryakāryabhūto yastataś ca praṇatāsma tam  ViP kāraṇaṃ kāraṇasyāpi tasya kāraṇakāraṇam tatkāraṇānāṃ hetuṃ taṃ praṇatā sma pareśvaram  ViP bhoktāraṃ bhogyabhūtaṃ ca sraṣṭāraṃ sṛjyameva ca kāryakartṛsvarūpaṃ taṃ praṇatā sma paraṃ padam  ViP viśuddhabodhavannityamajamakṣayamavyayam avyaktamavikāraṃ yattadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP na sthulaṃ na ca sūkṣmaṃ yanna viśeṣaṇagocaram tatpadaṃ paramaṃ viṣṇoḥ praṇamāma sadāmalam  ViP yasyā yutāyutāṃśāṃśe viśvaśaktiriyaṃ sthitā parabrahmasvarūpaṃ yatpraṇamāmastamavyayam  ViP yadyoginaḥ sadodyuktāḥ puṇyapāpakṣayekṣayam paśyanti praṇave cintyaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP yanna devā na munayo na cāhaṃ na ca śaṅkaraḥ jānanti parameśa sya tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP śaktayo yasya devasya brahmaviṣṇuśivātmikāḥ bhavantyabhūtapūrvasya tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP sarveśa sarvabhūtātmansarva sarvāśrayācyuta prasīda viṣṇo bhaktānāṃ vraja no dṛṣṭigocaram  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityudīritamākarṇya brahmaṇastridaśāstataḥ praṇamyocuḥ prasīdeti vraja no dṛṣṭi gocaram  ViP yannāyaṃ bhagavān brahma jānāti paramaṃ padam tannatāḥ smajagaddhāma tava sarvagatācyuta  ViP ityante vacasasteṣāṃ devānāṃ brahmaṇasta thā ūcurdevarṣayaḥsarva bṛhaspatipurogamāḥ  ViP adyo yajñaḥ pumānīḍyaḥ pūrveṣāṃ yaś ca pūrvajaḥ tannatāḥ sma jagatstraṣṭuḥ sraṣṭārama viśeṣaṇam  ViP bhagavanbhūtabhavyeśa yajñamūrtidharāvyaya prasīda praṇatānāṃ tvaṃ sarveṣāṃ dehi darśanam  ViP eṣa brahma sahāsmābhiḥ saha rudrais trilocanaḥ sarvādityaiḥ samaṃ pūṣā pāvako yaṃ sahāgnibhaḥ  ViP aśvinau vasavaśceme sarve caite marudgaṇāḥ sādhyā viśve tathā devā devendraścāyamīśvaraḥ  ViP praṇāmapravaṇā nātha daityasainyaiḥ parājitāḥ śaraṇaṃ tvāmanuprāptāḥ samastā devatāgaṇāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ saṃstūyamānastu bhagavāñchaṃkhacakradhṛk jagāma darśanaṃ teṣāṃ maitreya parame śvaraḥ  ViP taṃ dṛṣṭvā te tadā devāḥ śaṅkhacakragadādharam apūrvarūpasaṃsthānaṃ tejasāṃ rāśimūrjitam  ViP praṇamya praṇatāḥ sarve saṃkṣobha stimitekṣaṇāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ pitāmahapurogamāḥ  ViP devā ūcuḥ namonamo viśeṣastvaṃ tvaṃ brahma tvaṃ pinākadhṛk indrastvama gniḥ pavano varuṇaḥ savitā yamaḥ  ViP vasavo marutaḥ sādhyā viśvedevagaṇā bhavān yo yaṃ tavāgrato deva samīpaṃ devatāgaṇaḥ sa tvameva jagatstraṣṭā yataḥ sarvagato bhavān  ViP tvaṃ yajñastvaṃ vaṣaṭkārastvamoṅkāraḥ prajāpatiḥ vidyā vedyaṃ ca sarvātmaṃstvanmayaṃ cākhilaṃ jagat  ViP tvamārtāḥ śaraṇaṃ viṣṇo prayātā daityanirjitāḥ vayaṃ prasīda sarvātmaṃstejasāpyāyayasva naḥ  ViP tāvadārtis tathā vāñchā tāva nmohas tathā mukham yāvanna yāti śaraṇaṃ tvāmaśeṣāghanāśanam  ViP tvaṃ prasādaṃ prasannatman prapannānāṃ kuruṣva naḥ tejasāṃ nātha sarveṣāṃ svaśaktyāpyāyanaṃ kuru  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ saṃstūyamānastu praṇatair amarair hariḥ prasannadṛśṭirbhagavānidamāha sa viśvakṛt  ViP tejaso bhavatāṃ devāḥ kariṣyāmyupabṛṃhaṇam vadāmyahaṃ yatkriyatāṃ bhavadbhis tadidaṃ surāḥ  ViP ānīya sahitā daityaiḥ kṣīrābdhau saralau ṣadhīḥ prakṣipyātramṛtārthaṃ tāḥ sakalā daityadānavaiḥ manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā netraṃ kṛtvā ca vāsukim  ViP mathyatāmamṛte devāḥ sahāye mayyavasthite  ViP sāmapūrvaṃ ca daiteyāstatra sāhāyyakarmaṇi sāmānyaphalabhoktāro yūyaṃ vācyā bhaviṣyatha  ViP mathyamāne ca tatrābdhau yatsamutpatsyate mṛtam tatpānādbalino yūyamamarāś ca bhaviṣyatha  ViP tathā cāhaṃ kariṣyāmi te yathā tridaśadviṣaḥ na prāpsyantyamṛtaṃ devāḥ kevalaṃ kleśabhāginaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktā devadevena sarva eva tadā surāḥ sandhānamasūraiḥ kṛtvā yatnavanto mṛte bhavan  ViP nānauṣadhīḥ samānīya devadaiteyadānavāḥ kṣiptvā kṣīrābdhipayasi śara dabhrāmalatviṣi  ViP manthānaṃ mandaraṃ kṛtvā netraṃ kṛtvā ca vāsukim tato mathitumārabdhā maitreya tarasāmṛtam  ViP vibudhāḥ sahitāḥ sarve yataḥ pucchaṃ tataḥ kṛtāḥ kṛṣṇena vāsukerdaityāḥ pūrvakāye niveśitāḥ  ViP te tasya mukhaniśvāsavahnitāpahatatviṣaḥ nistejaso surāḥ sarve babhūvuramitaujasaḥ  ViP tenaiva mukhaniśvāsavāyunāstabalāhakaiḥ pucchapradeśe varṣadbhis tadā cāpyāyitāḥ surāḥ  ViP kṣīro damadhye bhagavānkūrmarūpī svayaṃ hariḥ manthanādreradhiṣṭhānaṃ bhramato bhūnmahāmune  ViP rūpeṇānyena devānāṃ madhye cakragadādharaḥ cakarṣa nāga rājānaṃ daityamadhye pareṇa ca  ViP uparyākrāntavāñśailaṃ bṛhadrūpeṇa keśavaḥ tathāpareṇa maitreya yanna dṛṣṭaṃ surāsuraiḥ  ViP tejasā nāgarā jānaṃ tathāpyāyitavānhariḥ anyena tejasā devānupabṛṃhitavānprabhuḥ  ViP mathyamāne tatastasminkṣirābdho devadānavaiḥ havirdhāmābhavatpūrvaṃ surabhiḥ surapūjītā  ViP jagmurmudaṃ tato devā dānavāś ca mahāmune vyākṣiptacetasaścaiva babhūvustimitekṣaṇāḥ  ViP kimetaditisiddhānāṃ divi cintayatāṃ tataḥ babhūva vāruṇī devī madāghūrṇitalocanā  ViP kṛtāvartāttatastasmātkṣīrodādvāsayañjagat gandhena pārījātobhūddevastrīnandanastaruḥ  ViP rūpaudāryaguṇopetas tathā cāpsarasāṃ gaṇaḥ kṣīrodadheḥ samutpanno maitreya paramādbhutaḥ  ViP tataḥ śītāṃśurabhavajjagṛhe taṃ maheśvaraḥ jagṛhuś ca viṣaṃ nāgāḥ kṣīrodābdhisamutthitam  ViP tato dhanvantarirdevaḥ śvetāmbaradharasvayam bibhratkamaṇḍaluṃ pūrṇamamṛtasya samutthitaḥ  ViP tataḥ svasthamanaskāste sarve daitaiyadānavāḥ babhūvurmuditāḥ sarve maitreya munibhiḥ saha  ViP tataḥ sphuratkāntimatī vikāsikamale sthitā śrīrdevī payasastasmādudbhūtā dhṛtapaṅkajā  ViP tāṃ tuṣṭuvurmudā yuktāḥ śrīsūktena maharṣayaḥ  ViP viśvāvasumukhāstasyā gandharvāḥ purato jaguḥ ghṛtācīpramukhāstatra nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ  ViP gaṅgādyāḥ saritastoyaiḥ snānārthamupatasthire diggajā hemapātrasthamādāya vimalaṃ jalam strāpayāñcakrire devīṃ sarvalokamaheśvarīm  ViP kṣīrodo rūpadhṛktasyai mālāmamlānapaṅkajām dadau vibhūṣaṇānyaṅge viśvakarmā cakāra ha  ViP divyamālyāmbaradharāstrātā bhūṣaṇabhūṣitā paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ yayau vakṣasthalaṃ hareḥ  ViP tayā vilokitā devā harivakṣasthalasthayā lakṣmyā maitreya sahasā parāṃ nirvṛtimāgatāḥ  ViP udvegaṃ paramaṃ jagmurdaityā viṣṇuparāṅmukhāḥ tyaktā lakṣmyā mahābhāga vipracittirurogamāḥ  ViP tataste jagṛhurdaityā dhanvantarikarasthitam kamaṇḍaluṃ mahāvīryā yatrāste mṛtamuttamam  ViP māyayā mohayitvā tānviṣṇuḥ strīrūpasaṃsthitaḥ dānavebhyastadādāya devebhyaḥ pradadau prabhuḥ  ViP tataḥ papuḥ suraguṇāḥ śakrādyāstattadāmṛtam udyatāyudhanistraṃśā daityāstāṃś ca samābhyayuḥ  ViP pīte mṛte ca balibhir devair daityacamūstadā vadhyamānā diśo bheje pātālaṃ ca viveśa vai  ViP tato devā mudā yuktāḥ śaṅkhacakragadābhṛtam praṇipatya yathāpūrvamāśāsattattriviṣṭapam  ViP tataḥ prasannabhāḥ sūryaḥ prayayau svena vartmanā jyotīṃṣi ca yathāmārgaṃ prayayurmunisattama  ViP jajvāla bhagavāṃścoccaiś cārudīptirvibhāvasuḥ dharme ca sarvabhūtānāṃ tadā matirajāyata  ViP trailokyaṃ ca śriyā juṣṭaṃ babhūva dvijasattama śakraś ca tridaśaśreṣṭhaḥ punaḥ śrīmā najāyata  ViP siṃhāsanagataḥ śakraḥsaṃprāpya tridivaṃ punaḥ devarājye stito devīṃ tuṣṭāvābjakarāṃ tataḥ  ViP indra uvācanamasye sarvalokānāṃ jananīmabjasambhavām śriyamunnidrapadmākṣīṃ viṣṇuvakṣasthalasthitām  ViP padmālayāṃ padmakarāṃ padmapatranibhekṣaṇām vande padmasukhīṃ devīṃ padmanābhapriyāmaham  ViP tvaṃ siddhistvaṃ svadhā svāhā sudhā tvaṃ lokapāvanī sandhyā rātriḥ prabhā bhūtirmedhā śraddhā sarasvatī  ViP yajñavidyā mahāvidya guhyavidya ca śobhane ātmavidyā ca devi tvaṃ visuktiphaladāyinī  ViP ānvīkṣikītrayīvārta daṇḍanītistvameva ca saimyāsaumyair jagadrūpais tvayaittaddevi pūritam  ViP kā tvanyā tvāmṛte devi sarvayajñamayaṃ vapuḥ adhyāste devadevasya yogicintyaṃ gadābhṛtaḥ  ViP tvāyā devi parityaktaṃ sakalaṃ bhuvanatrayam vinaṣṭaprāyamabhavattvayedānīṃ samedhitam  ViP dārāḥ suhṛrdvaga mā paśunmā vibhūṣaṇam tyajethā mama devasya viṣṇorvakṣaḥsthalālaye  ViP sattvena satyaśaucābhyāṃ tathā śīladibhir guṇaiḥ tyajyante te narāḥ sadyaḥ saṃtyaktā ye tvāyāmale  ViP tvayā vilokitāḥ sadyaḥ śīlādyair akhilair guṇaiḥ kulaiśvaryaiś ca yujyante puruṣā nirguṇā api  ViP sar ślāghyaḥ sa guṇī dhanyaḥ sa kulīnaḥ sa buddhimān sa śūraḥ sa ca vikrānto yastvayā devi vīkṣitaḥ  ViP sadyo vaiguṇyamāyānti śīlādyaḥ sakalā guṇāḥ parāṅmukhī jagaddhātrī yasya tvaṃ viṣṇuvallabhe  ViP na te varṇayituṃ śaktā guṇāñcihvāpi bedhasaḥ prasīda devi padmākṣi māsmāṃstyākṣīḥ kadāṭana  ViP śrīparaśara uvācaevaṃ śrīḥ saṃstutā samyak prāha devī śatakratum śṛṇvatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ sarvabhūtasthitā dvija  ViP śrīruvācaparituṣṭāsmi deveśe stotreṇānena te hare varaṃ vṛṇīṣva yastviṣṭo vara dāhaṃ tavāgatā  ViP indra uvācavaradā yadi me devi vārarhe yadi vāpyaham trailokyaṃ na tvayā tyājyameṣa mestu varaḥ paraḥ  ViP stotreṇa yastathaitena tvāṃ stoṣyatyabdhisambhave sa tvayā na parītyājyo dvitīyostu varo mama  ViP śrīruvācatrailokyaṃ trida śaśreṣṭha na santyakṣyāmi vāsava datto varo mayāyante stautrārādhanatuṣṭayā  ViP yaś ca sāyaṃ tathā prātaḥ stotreṇānena mānavaḥ māṃ stoṣyati na devadānavayatnena prasūtāmṛtamanthane  ViP evaṃ yadā jagatsvāmī devadevo janārdanaḥ avatāraṃ karotyeṣā tadā śrīstatmahāyini  ViP punaś ca padmādutpannā ādityobhūdyadā hariḥ yadā tu bhārgavo rāmastadābhūddharaṇī tviyam  ViP rāghavatve bhavatsītā rukmiṇī kṛṣṇajanmani anyeṣu cāvatāreṣu viṣṇoreṣānapāyini  ViP devatve devadeheyaṃ manuṣyatve ca mānuṣī viṣṇordehānurūpāṃ vai karotyeṣātmanastanum  ViP yaścaitacchṛṇuyājjanma lakṣmyā yaś ca paṭhennaraḥ śriyo na vicyutistasya gṛhe yāvatkulatrayam  ViP paṭhyate yeṣu caiveyaṃ gṛheṣu śrīstutirmune alakṣmīḥ kalahādhārā na te ṣvāste kadācana  ViP etate kathitaṃ brahmanyanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi kṣīrābdho śrīryathā jātā pūrvaṃ bhṛgusutā satī  ViP iti sakala vibhūtyavāptihetuḥ stutiriyamindramukhodgatā hi lakṣmyāḥ anudinamiha paṭhyate nṛbhir yair vasati na teṣu kadācidapyalakṣmīḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe navamo dhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācakathitaṃ me tvāyā sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭosi mayā mune bhṛgusargātprabhṛtyeṣa sargo me kathyatāṃ punaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācabhṛgoḥ khyātyāṃ samutpannā lakṣmīrviṣṇuparigrahaḥ tathā dhātṛvidhātārau khyātyāṃ jātau sutau bhṛgoḥ  ViP āyatirniyatiścaiva meroḥ kanye mahātmanaḥ bhārye dhātṛvidhātroste tayorjātau sutāvubhau  ViP prāṇaścaiva mṛkaṇḍuś ca mārkaṇḍeyo mṛkaṇḍutaḥ tato vedaśirā jajñe prāṇasyāpi sutaṃ śṛṇu  ViP prāṇasya dyutimānputro rājavāṃś ca tato bhavat tato vaṃśo mahābhāga vistaraṃ bhārgavo gataḥ  ViP patnī marīceḥ saṃbhūtiḥ paurṇamāsamasūyatā virajāḥ parvataścaiva tasya putro mahātmanaḥ  ViP vaṃśasaṃkīrtane putrānvadiṣyehaṃ tato dvija smṛtiścāṅgīrasaḥ patnī prasūtā kanyakās tathā sinīvālī kuhūścaiva rākā cānumatī tathā  ViP anasūyā tathaivātrerjajñe niṣkalmaṣānsutān somaṃ durvāsasaṃ caiva dattātreyaṃ ca yoginam  ViP prītyāṃ pulastyabhāryāyāṃ dattolistatsuto bhavat pūrvajanmani yo gastyaḥ smṛtaḥ svāyaṃbhuventare  ViP kardamaścārvarīvāṃś ca sahiṣṇuś ca sutāstrayaḥ kṣamā tu suṣave bhāryā pulahasya prajāpateḥ  ViP kratoś ca saṃtatirbhāryā vālakhilyānasūyata ṣaṣṭiputrasahasrāṇi munīnāmūrdhvaretasām aṅguṣṭhaparvamātrāṇāṃ jvaladbhāskaratejasām  ViP ūrjāyāṃ tu vasiṣṭhasya saptājāyanta vai sutāḥ  ViP rajo gotrordhvabāhuś ca savanaścānaghas tathā sutapāḥ śukra ityete sarve saptarṣayo malāḥ  ViP yo sāvagnyabhimānī syāt brahmaṇastanayo grajaḥ tasmātsvāhā sutāṃllebhe trīnudāraujaso dvija  ViP pāvakaṃ pavamānaṃ tu śuciṃ cāpi jalāśinam  ViP teṣāṃ tu santatāvanye catvāriṃśacca pañca ca kathyante vahnayaścaite pitāputratrayaṃ ca yat  ViP evamekonapañcaśadvahnayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ  ViP pitaro brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā vyākhyātā ye mayā dvija āgniṣvātta barhiṣado nagnayaḥ sāgnayaś ca ye  ViP tebhyaḥ svadhā sute jajñe menāṃ vai dhārīṇīṃ tathā te ubhe brahmavādinyau yoginyāvapyubhe dvija  ViP uttamajñānasaṃpanne sarvaiḥ samudirtair guṇaiḥ  ViP ityeṣā dakṣakanyānāṃ kathitā satyasaṃtatiḥ śraddhāvānsaṃsmarannetāmanapatyo na jāyate  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe daśamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācapriyavratottānapādau manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu dvau putrau tu mahāvīryau dharmajñau kathitau tava  ViP tayoruttānapādasya surucyāmuttamaḥ sutaḥ abhīṣṭāyāmabhūdbrahyanpituratyantavallabhaḥ  ViP sunītirnāma yā rājñastasyāsīn mahiṣī dvija sa nāti prītimāṃstasyāmabhūdyasyā dhruvaḥ sutaḥ  ViP rājāsanasthitasyāṅkaṃ piturbhrataramāśritam dṛṣṭvottamaṃ dhruva ścakre tamāroḍhuṃ manoratham  ViP pratyakṣaṃ bhūpatistasyāḥ surucyā nābhyanandata praṇayenāgataṃ putramutsaṃgārohaṇotsukam  ViP sapatnī tanayaṃ dṛṣṭvā tamaṅkārohaṇotsukam svaputraṃ ca tathārūḍhaṃ surucirvākyamabravīt  ViP kriyate kiṃ vṛthā vatsa mahāneṣa manorathaḥ anyastrīgarbhajātena hy asaṃbhūya mamodare  ViP uttamottamamaprāpyamaviveko hi vāñchasi satyaṃ sutastvamapy asya kiṃ tu na tvaṃ mayā dhṛtaḥ  ViP etadrājāsanaṃ sarva bhūbhṛtsaṃśrayaketanam yogyaṃ mamaiva putrasya kimātmā kliśyatetvayā  ViP uccairmanorathasteyaṃ matputrasyeva kiṃ vṛthā sunītyāmātmano janma kiṃ tvayā nāvagamyate  ViP śrīparāśara vācautsṛjya pitaraṃ bālastac chrutvā mātṛbhāṣitam jagāma kupito māturnijāyā dvijamandiram  ViP taṃ dṛṣṭvā kupitaṃ putramīṣatprasphuritādharam sunītiraṅkamāropya maitreyedamabhāṣata  ViP vatsa kaḥ kopahetuste kaś ca tvāṃ nābhi nandati kovajānāti pitaraṃ vatsa yasteparādhyati  ViP śrīparāśara vācaityuktaḥ sakalaṃ mātre kathayāmāsa tadyathā suruciḥ prāha bhūpālapratyakṣamatagarvitā  ViP viniśvasyeti kathite tasminputreṇa durmanāḥ śvasakṣāmekṣaṇā dīnā sunītirvākyamabravīt  ViP sunītiruvācasuruciḥ satyamāhedaṃ mandabhāgyosiḥputraka na hi puṇyavatāṃ vatsa sapatnair eva mucyate  ViP nodvegastāta kartavyaḥ kṛtaṃ yadbhavatā purā tatkopahartu śaknoti dātuṃ kaścākṛtaṃ tvayā  ViP tattvayā nātra kartavyaṃ duḥkhaṃ tadvākyasambhavam  ViP rājāsanaṃ rājacchatraṃ varāścāvaravāraṇāḥ yasya puṇyāni tasyaite matvaitacchāṃmya putraka  ViP anyajanmakṛtaiḥ puṇyaiḥ surucyā surucirnṛpaḥ bhāryeti procyate cānyāṃ madvidhā puṇyavarjitā  ViP puṇyopacayasaṃpannastasyāḥ putrastathottamaḥ mama putras tathā jātaḥ svalpapuṇyo dhruvo bhavān  ViP tathāpi duḥkhaṃ na bhavān kartumarhasi putraka yasya yāvatsa tenaiva svena tuṣyati mānavaḥ  ViP yadi te duḥkhamatyarthaṃ surucyā vacasābhavat tatpuṇyopacaye yatnaṃ kuru sarvaphalaprade  ViP suśīlo bhava dharmātmā maitraḥ prāṇihite rataḥ nimnaṃ yathāpaḥ pravaṇāḥ pātramāyānti sampadaḥ  ViP dhruva uvācaamba yattvamidaṃ prāttha praśamāya vaco mama naitaddurvācasā bhinne hṛdaye mama tiṣṭhati  ViP so haṃ tathā yatiṣyāmi yathā sarvottamottamam sthānaṃ prāpsyāmyaśoṣāṇāṃ jagatāmabhi pūjitam  ViP surucirdayitā rājñastasyā jātosmi nodarāt prabhāvaṃ paśya meṃba tvaṃ vṛddhasyāpi tavodare  ViP uttamaḥ sa mama bhrātā yo garbheṇa dhṛtastayā sa rājāsanamāpnotu pitrā dattaṃ tathāstu tat  ViP nānyadattamabhīpsyāmi stānamamba svakarmaṇā icchāmi tadahaṃ sthānaṃ yatra prāpa pitā mama  ViP śrīparāśara uvācanirjagāma gṛhānmāturityuktvā mātaraṃ dhruvaḥ purācca nirgamya tatastadbāhyopavanaṃ yayo  ViP sa dadarśa munīṃs tatra saptapūrvāgatāndhruvaḥ kuṣmājinottarīyeṣu viṣṭareṣu samāsthitān  ViP sa rājaputrastānsarvānpraṇipatyābhya bhāṣata praśrayāvanataḥ samyagabhivādanapūrvakam  ViP dhruva uvācauttānapādatanayaṃ māṃ nibodhata sattamāḥ jātaṃ sunītyāṃ nirvedādyuṣmākaṃ prāptamantikam  ViP ṛṣaya ūcuḥcatuḥpañcā bdasaṃbhūto bālastvaṃ tṛpanandana nirvedakāraṇaṃ kiñcittava nādyāpi vartate  ViP na cintyaṃ bhavataḥ kiñciddhrayate bhūpatiḥ pitā na caivaiṣṭa viyogādi tava paśyāma bālaka  ViP śarīre na ca te vyādhirasmābhir upalakṣyate nirvedaḥ kinnimittaste kathyatāṃ yadi vidyate  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ sa kathayāmāsa surucyā yadudāhṛtam tanniśamya tataḥ procurmunayaste parasparam  ViP aho kṣātraṃ paraṃ tejo bālasyāpi yadakṣamā sapatnyā māturuktaṃ yaddhṛdayānnāpasarpati  ViP bhobhoḥ kṣatriyadāyādaḥ nirvedādyattvāyādhunā kartuṃ vyavasitaṃ tannaḥ kathyatāṃ yadi rocate  ViP yacca kāryaṃ tavāsmābhiḥ sāhāyyamamitadyute taducyatāṃ vivakṣustvamasmābhir upalakṣyase  ViP dhruva uvācanāha marthamabhīpsāmi na rājyaṃ dvijasattamāḥ tatsthānamekamicchāmi bhuktaṃ nānyena yatpurā  ViP etanme kriyatāṃ samyakkathyatāṃ prāpyate yathā sthānamagryaṃ samastebhyaḥ sthānebhyo munisattamāḥ  ViP marīciruvācaanārādhitagovindair naraiḥ sthānaṃ nṛpātmaja na hi saṃprāpyate śreṣṭhaṃ tasmādārādhayācyutam  ViP atriruvācaparaḥ parāṇāṃ puruṣo yasya tuṣṭo janārdanaḥ saṃprāpnotyakṣayaṃ sthānametatsatyaṃ mayoditam  ViP aṅgirā uvācayasyāntaḥ sarvamevedamacyutasyāvyayātmanaḥ tamārādhaya govindaṃ sthānamagryaṃ yadīcchasi  ViP pulastya uvācaparaṃ brahma paraṃ dhāma yo sau brahma tathā param tamārādhya hariṃ yāti muktimapyati durlabhām  ViP pulaha uvācaaindramindraḥ paraṃ sthānaṃ yamārādhya jagatpatim prāpa yajñapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ tamārādhaya suvrata  ViP kraturuvācayo yajñapuruṣo yajño yogeśaḥ paramaḥ pumān tasmiṃstuṣṭe yadaprāpyaṃ kintadasti janārdane  ViP vasiṣṭha uvācaprāpnoṣyārādhite viṣṇau manasā yadyadicchati trelokyāntargataṃ sthānaṃ kimu vatsottamottamam  ViP dhruva uvācaārādhyaḥ kathito devo bhavadbhiḥ praṇatasya me mayā tatparītoṣāya yajjaptavyaṃ taducyatām  ViP yathā cārādhanaṃ tasya mayā kāryaṃ mahātmanaḥ prasādasumukhāstanme kathayantu maharṣayaḥ  ViP ṛṣaya ūcuḥrājaputra yathā viṣṇorārādhanaparair naraiḥ kāryamārādhanaṃ tanno yathāvacchrotumarhasi  ViP bāhyārthādakhilāccittaṃ tyājayetprathamaṃ naraḥ tasminneva jagaddhāmni tataḥ kurvita niścalam  ViP evamekāgracittena tanmayena dhṛtātmanā japtavyaṃ yanni bodhaitattanraḥ pārthivanandana  ViP hiraṇyagarbhapuruṣapradhānavyaktarūpiṇe oṃ namo vāsudevāya śuddhajñānasvarūpime  ViP etajjajāpa bhagavān japyaṃ svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pitāmahastava purā tasya tuṣṭo janārdanaḥ  ViP dado yathābhilaṣitāṃ siddhiṃ trailokyadurlabhām tathā tvamapi govindaṃ toṣayaitatsadā japan  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathameṃśa ekādaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaniśamyaitadaśeṣeṇa maitreya nṛpate sutaḥ nirjagāma vanāttasmātpraṇipatya sa tānṛṣīn  ViP kṛtakṛtyamivātmānaṃ manyamānastato dvija madhusaṃjñaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ jagāma yamunātaṭam  ViP punaś ca madhusaṃjñena daityenādhiṣṭhitaṃ yataḥ tato madhuvanaṃ nāmnā khyātamatra mahītale  ViP hatvā ca lavaṇaṃ rakṣo madhuputraṃ mahābalam śatrughno madhurāṃ nāma purīṃ yatra cakāra vai  ViP yatra vai devadevasya sānnidhyaṃ harimedhasaḥ sarvapāpahare tasmiṃstapastīrthe cakāra saḥ  ViP marīcimukhyair munibhir yathoddiṣṭamabhūttathā ātmanyaśepadeveśaṃ sthitaṃ viṣṇumamanyata  ViP ananyacetasastasya dhyāyato bhagavānhariḥ sarvabhūtagato vipra sarvabhāvagato bhavat  ViP manasyavasthite tasminviṣṇau maitreya yoginaḥ na śaśāka dharā bhāramudvoḍhuṃ bhūtadhāriṇī  ViP vāmapādasthite tasminnanāmārdhena medinī dvitīyaṃ ca nanāmārdhaṃ kṣiterdakṣiṇataḥ sthite  ViP pādāṃsuṣṭhena saṃpīḍya yathā sa vasudhāṃ sthitaḥ tadā samastā vasudhā cacāla saha parvataiḥ  ViP nadyo nadāḥ samudrāś ca saṃkṣobhaṃ paramaṃ yayuḥ tatkṣobhādamarāḥ kṣobhaṃ paraṃ jagmurmahāmune  ViP yāmā nāma tadā devā maitreya paramākulāḥ indreṇa saha saṃmantrya dhyānabhaṅgaṃ pracakramuḥ  ViP kūṣmāṇḍā vividhai rūpair mahendreṇa mahāmune samādhibhaṅgamatyantamārabdhāḥ kartumāturāḥ  ViP sunītirnāma tanmātā sāstrā tatpurataḥ sthitā putreti karuṇāṃ vācamāha māyāmayī tadā  ViP putrakāsmānnivartasva śarīrātyayadāruṇāt nirbandhato mayā labdho bahubhis tvaṃ manorathai  ViP dīnāmekāṃ parityaktumanāthāṃ na tvamarhasi sapatnīvacanādvatsa agatestvaṃ gatirmama  ViP kva ca tvaṃ pañcavarṣīyaḥ kvacaitaddārūṇaṃ tapaḥ nivartatāṃ manaḥ kaṣṭānnirbandhātphalavarjitāt  ViP kālaḥ krīḍanakānānte tadante dhyayanasya te tataḥ samastabhogānāṃ tadante ceṣyate tapaḥ  ViP kālaḥ krīḍanakānāṃ yastava bālasya putraka tasmiṃstvamicchasi tapaḥ kiṃ nāśāyātmano rataḥ  ViP matprītiḥ paramo dharmo vayovasthākriyākramam anuvartasva mā mohānnivartāsmādadharmataḥ  ViP parityajati vatsādhya yadhyetanna bhavāṃstapaḥ tyakṣyāmyahamiha prāṇāṃstato vai paśyatastava  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatāṃ pralāpavatīmevaṃ bāṣpākulavilocanām samāhitamanā viṣṇau paśyannapi na dṛṣṭavān  ViP vatsa vatsa sughorāṇi rakṣāṃsyetāni bhīṣaṇe vane bhyudyataśastrāṇīḥ samāyāntyapagamyatām  ViP ityuktvā prayayau sātha rakṣāṃsyāvirbabhustataḥ abhyudyatograśastrāṇi jvālāmālākulair mukhaiḥ  ViP tato nādānatīvogranrājaputrasya te puraḥ mumucurdīptaśastrāṇi bhrāmayanto niśācarāḥ  ViP śivāś ca śataśo neduḥ sajvālāḥ kavalair mukhaiḥ trāsāya tasya bālasya yogayuktasya sarvadā  ViP hanyatāṃ danyatāmeṣa chidyatāṃ chidyatāmayam bhakṣyatāṃ bhakṣyatāṃ cāya mityucuste niśācarāḥ  ViP tato nānāvidhānnādān siṃhoṣṭramakarānanāḥ trāsāya rājaputrasya neduste rajanīcarāḥ  ViP rakṣāṃsi tāni te nādāḥ śivāstānyāyudhāni ca govindāsaktacittasya yayurnandriyagocaram  ViP ekāgracetāḥ satataṃ viṣṇumevātmasaṃśrayam dṛṣṭavān pṛthivīnāthaputro nānyaṃ kathañcana  ViP tataḥ sarvāsu māyāsu vilīnāsu punaḥ surāḥ saṃkṣobhaṃ paramaṃ jagmustatparābhavaśaṅkitāḥ  ViP te sametya jagadyonimanādinidhanaṃ harim śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ yātāstapasā tasya tāpitāḥ  ViP devā ūcuḥdevadeva jagannātha pareśa puruṣottama dhruvasya tapasā taptāstvāṃ vayaṃ śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ  ViP dine dine kalāleśaiḥ śaśāṅka pūryate yathā tathāyaṃ tapasā deva prayātyṛddhim aharniṃśam  ViP autānapāditapasā vayamitthaṃ janārdana bhītāstvāṃ śaraṇaṃ yātāstapasastaṃ nivartaya  ViP navidmaḥ kiṃ sa śakratvaṃ sūryatvaṃ kimabhīpsati vittapāmbupasomānāṃ sābhilāṣaḥ padeṣu kim  ViP tadasmākaṃ prasīdeśa hṛdayācchalyamuddhara uttānapādatanayaṃ tapasaḥ sannivartaya  ViP śrībhagavānuvācanendratvaṃ na ca sūryatvaṃ naivāmbupadhaneśatām prārthayatyeṣa yaṃ kāmaṃ taṃ karomyakhilaṃ surā  ViP yāta devā yathākāma svasthānaṃ vigatajvarāḥ nivartayāmyahaṃ bālaṃ tapasyāsaktamānasam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktā devadevena praṇamya tridaśāstataḥ prayayuḥ svāni dhiṣṇyāni śatakratupurogamāḥ  ViP bhagavānapi sarvātmā tanmayatvena toṣitaḥ gatvā dhruvamuvācedaṃ caturbhujavapur hariḥ  ViP śrībhagavānuvācaauttānapāde bhadraṃ te tapasā paritoṣitaḥ varadohamanuprāpto varaṃ varaya suvrata  ViP brāhyārthanirapekṣaṃ te mayi cittaṃ yadā hitam tuṣṭohaṃ bhavatastena tadvṛṇīṣva varaṃ param  ViP parāśara uvācaśrutvetthaṃ gaditaṃ tasya devadevasya bālakaḥ unmīlitākṣo dadṛśe dhyānadṛṣṭaṃ hariṃ puraḥ  ViP śaṅkhacakragadāśārṅgavarāsidharamacyutam kirīṭinaṃ samālokya jagāma śirasā mahīm  ViP romāñcitāṅgaḥ sahasā sādhvasaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ stavāya devadevasya sa cakre mānasaṃ dhruvaḥ  ViP kiṃ vadāmi stutāvasya kenoktenāsya saṃstutiḥ ityākula matirdevaṃ tameva śaraṇaṃ yayau  ViP dhruva uvācabhagavanyadi me toṣaṃ tapasā paramaṃ gataḥ stotuṃ tadahamicchāmi varamenaṃ prayaccha me  ViP brahmādyauryasya vedajñair jñāyate yasya no gatiḥ taṃ tvāṃ kathamahaṃ deva stotuṃ śakromi bālakaḥ tvadbhaktipravaṇaṃ hyetatparameśvara me manaḥ stotuṃ pravṛttaṃ tvatpādau tatra prajñāṃ prayacca meśrīparāśara uvācaśaṅkhaprāntena govindastaṃ pasparśa kṛtāñjalim uttānapādatanayaṃ dvijavarya jagatpatiḥ  ViP atha prasannavadanaḥ sa kṣaṇānnṛpanandanaḥ tuṣṭāva praṇato bhūtvā bhūtadhātāramacyutam  ViP dhruva uvācabhūmirāponalo vāyuḥ khaṃ mano buddhireva ca bhūtādirādi prakṛtiryasya rūpaṃ natosmi tam  ViP śuddhaḥ sūkṣmokhilavyāpī pradhānātparataḥ pumān yasya rūpaṃ namastasmai puruṣāya guṇātmane  ViP bhūtādīnāṃ samastānāṃ gandhādīnāṃ ca śāśvataḥ budhyādīnāṃ pradhānasya puruṣasya ca yaḥ paraḥ  ViP taṃ brahmabhūtamātmānamaśeṣajagataḥ patim prapadye śaraṇaṃ śuddhaṃ tvadrūpaṃ parameśvara  ViP bṛhattvādbṛṃhaṇatvācca yadrūpaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam tasmai namaste sarvātmanyogicintyāvikāriṇe  ViP sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt sarvavyāpī bhuvaḥ sparśādatyatiṣṭhaddaśāṅgulam  ViP yadbhūtaṃ yacca vai bhavyaṃ purūṣottama tadbhavān tvattau virāṭ svarāṭ samrāṭ tvattaścapyadhipūruṣaḥ  ViP atyaricyata sodhaś ca tiryagūrdhvaṃ ca vai bhuvaḥ tvatto viśvamidaṃ jātaṃ tvattau bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP tvadrūpadhāriṇaścāntaḥ sarvabhūtamidaṃ jagat tvatto yajñaḥ sarvahutaḥ pṛṣadājyaṃ paśurdvidhā  ViP tvatto ṛcotha sāmāni tvattaśchandāṃsi jajñire tvatto yajūṃṣyajāyanta tvattośvāścaikato dataḥ  ViP gāvastvattaḥ samudbhūtāstva ttojā avayo mṛgāḥ tvamanmukhādbrāhmaṇā bāhvos tvatto kṣatramajāyata  ViP vaiśvāstavorujāḥ śūdrāstava padbhyāṃ samudgatāḥ ākṣṇoḥ sūryo nilaḥ prāṇāccandramā manasastava  ViP prāṇontaḥ muṣirājjāto mukhādagnirajāyata nābhito gaganaṃ dyauś ca śirasaḥ samavartata  ViP diśaḥ śrotrātkṣitiḥ padbhyāṃ tvattaḥ sarvamabhūdidim  ViP nyagrodhaḥ sumahānalpe yathā bīje vyavasthitaḥ saṃyame visvamakhilaṃ bījabhūte tathātvāyi  ViP bījādaṅkurasambhūte nyagrodhastu samutthitaḥ vistāraṃ ca yathā yāti tvattaḥ sṛṣṭau tathā jagat  ViP yathā hi kadalī nānyā tvakpatrādapi dṛsyate evaṃ viśvasya nānyastvaṃ tvasthayīśvara dṛśyeta  ViP hlādinī saṃdhinī saṃvittvayyekā sarvasaṃsthitau hlādatāpakarī miśrā tvayi no guṇavarjite  ViP pṛthagbhūtaikabhūtāya bhūtabhūtāya te namaḥ prabhūtabhūtabhūtāya tubhyaṃ bhūtātmane namaḥ  ViP vyaktaṃ pradhānapuruṣau virāṭ samrāṭ svarāṭ tathā vibhāvyatentaḥkaraṇe puruṣeṣvakṣayo bhavān  ViP sarvasminsarvabhūtastvaṃ sarvaḥ sarvasvarūpadhṛk sarvaṃ tvattastataś ca tvaṃ namaḥ sarvātmane stu te  ViP sarvātmakosi sarveśa sarvabhūtasthito yataḥ kathayāmi tataḥ kiṃ te sarvaṃ vetsi hṛti sthitam  ViP sarvātmansarvabhūteśa sarvasattvasamudbhava sarvabhūto bhavānvetti sarvasattvamanoratham  ViP yo me manoratho nātha saphalaḥ sa tvayā kṛtaḥ tapaś ca taptaṃ saphalaṃ yaddṛṣṭo si jagatpate  ViP śrībhagavānuvācatapasastatphalaṃ yaddṛṣṭo haṃ tvayā dhruva madṛrśanaṃ hi viphalaṃ rājaputra na jāyate  ViP varaṃ varaya tasmāttvaṃ yathābhimatamātmanaḥ sarvaṃ saṃpadyate puṃsāṃ mayi dṛṣṭipathaṃ gate  ViP dhruva uvācabhagavanbhūtabhavyeśa sarvasyāste bhavān hṛdi kimajñātaṃ tava brahmanmanasā yanmayekṣitam  ViP tathāpi tubhyaṃ deveśa kathayiṣyāmi yanmayā prārthyate durvinītena hṛdayenātidurlabham  ViP kiṃ vā sarvajagatstraṣṭaḥ prasanne tvayi durlabham tvatprasādaphalaṃ bhuṅkte trailokyaṃ magha vānapi  ViP naitadrājāsanaṃ yogyamajātasya mamodarāt iti garvadavocanmāṃ sapatnīmāturuccakaiḥ  ViP ādhārabhūtaṃ jagataḥ sarveṣāmuttamottamam prārthayāmi prabho sthānaṃ tvatprasādādatovyayam  ViP śrībhagavānuvācayattvayā prārthyate sthānametatprāpsyati vai bhavān tvayāhaṃ toṣitaḥ pūrvamanyajanmani vālaka  ViP tvamāsīrbrahmaṇaḥ pūrvaṃ mayyekāgramatiḥ sadā mātāpitroś ca śuśraṣurnijadharmānupālakaḥ  ViP kālena gacchatā mitraṃ rājaputrastavābhavat yovanekhilabhogāḍhyo darśanīyojjvalākṛtiḥ  ViP tatsaṅgāttasya tāmṛddhimavalokyādidurlabhām bhaveyaṃ rājaputrohamiti vāñchā tvayā kṛtā  ViP tato yathābhilaṣitā prāptā te rājaputratā uttānapādasya gṛhe jātosi dhruva durlabhe  ViP anyeṣāṃ durlabhaṃ sthānaṃ kule svāyambhuvasya yat  ViP tasyaitadaparaṃ bāla yenāhaṃ paritoṣitaḥ māmārādhya naro muktimavāpnotyavilambitām  ViP mayyarpitamanā bāla kimu svargādikaṃ padam  ViP trailokyādadhike sthāne sarvatārāgrahāśrayaḥ bhaviṣyati na saṃdeho matprasādādbhāvandhruva  ViP sūryātsomāttathā bhaumātsomaputrādbṛhaspateḥ sitārkatanayādīnāṃ sarvarkṣāṇāṃ tathā dhruvaḥ  ViP saptarṣiṇāmaśeṣāṇāṃ ye ca vaimānikāḥ surāḥ sarveṣāmupari sthānaṃ tava dattaṃ mayā dhruva  ViP keciccaturyugaṃ yāvatkecinmanvantaraṃ surāḥ tiṣṭhanti bhavato dattā mayā vai kalpasaṃsthitiḥ  ViP sunītirapi te mātā tvadāsannātinirmalā vimāne tārakā bhūtvā tāvatkālaṃ nivatsyati  ViP ye ca tvāṃ mānavāḥ prātaḥ sāyaṃ ca susamāhi tāḥ kīrtayiṣyanti teṣāṃ ca mahatpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ pūrvaṃ jagannāthāddevadevājjanārdanāt varaṃ prāpya dhruvaḥ sthāna madhyāste sa mahāmate  ViP svayaṃ śuśrūṣaṇāddharmyānmātāpitroś ca vai tathā ddhādaśākṣaramāhatmyāttapasaś ca prabhāvataḥ  ViP tasyābhimānamṛddhiṃ ca mahimānaṃ nirikṣya hi devāsurāṇāmācāryaḥ ślokamatrośanā jagau  ViP ahosya tapaso vīryamahosya tapasaḥ phalam yadenaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ  ViP dhruvasya jananī ceyaṃ sunītirnāma sūnṛtā asyāś ca mahimānaṃ kaḥ śakto varṇayituṃ bhuvi  ViP trailokyaśrayatāṃ prāptaṃ paraṃ sthānaṃ stirāyati sthānaṃ prāptā paraṃ dhṛtvā yā kukṣivivare dhruvam  ViP yaścaitatkīrtayennityaṃ dhruvasyārohaṇaṃ divi sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate  ViP sthānabhraṃśaṃ na cāpnoti divi vā yadi vā bhuvi sarvakalyāṇasaṃyukto dīrghakālaṃ sa jīvati  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe dvādaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācadhruvācchiṣṭiṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca bhavyācchambhurvyajāyata śiṣṭorādhatta succhāyā pañcaputrānakalmaṣān  ViP ripuṃ ripuñjayaṃ vipraṃ vṛkalaṃ vṛkatejasam riporādhatta bṛhatī cākṣuṣaṃ sarvatejasam  ViP ajījanatpuṣkariṇyāṃ vāruṇyāṃ cākṣuṣo manum prajāpaterātmajāyāṃ vīraṇasya mahātmanaḥ  ViP manorajāyanta daśa naḍvalāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ kanyāyāṃ tapatāṃ śreṣṭha vairājasya prajāpateḥ  ViP kuruḥ puruḥ śata dyumnastapasvī satyavāñchuciḥ agniṣṭomotirātraś ca sudyumnaśceti te nava abhimanyuś ca daśamo naḍvalāyāṃ mahaujasaḥ  ViP kurorajanayatputrān ṣaḍāgnoyī mahāprabhān aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ khyātiṃ kratumaṅgirasaṃ śibim  ViP aṅgātsunīthāpatyaṃ vai venamekamajāyata prajārthamṛṣayastasya mamanthurdakṣiṇaṃ karam  ViP venasya pāṇau mathite sambabhūva mahāmune vainyo nāma mahīpālo yaḥ pṛthuḥ parikīrtitaḥ  ViP yena dugdhā mahī pūrvaṃ prajānāṃ hitakāraṇāt  ViP maitreya uvācakimarthaṃ mathitaḥ pāṇirvenasya paramarṣibhiḥ yatra jajñe mahāvīryaḥ sa pṛthṛrmunisattama  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasunīthā nāma yā kanyā kṛtyo prathamato bhavat aṅgasya bhāryā sā dattā tasyāṃ veno vyajāyata  ViP sa mātāmahadoṣeṇa tena mṛtyoḥ sutātmajaḥ nisargādeṣa maitreya duṣṭa eva vyajāyata  ViP abhiṣikto yadā rājye sa venaḥ paramarṣibhiḥ ghoṣa yāmāsa sa tadā pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ  ViP na yaṣṭavyaṃ na dātavyaṃ na hotavyaṃ kathañcana bhoktā yajñasya kastvanyo hyahaṃ yajñapatiḥ prabhuḥ  ViP tatastamṛṣayaḥ pūrva saṃpūjyaṃ pṛthivīpatim ūcuḥ sāmākalaṃ vākyaṃ maitreya samapasthitāḥ  ViP ṛṣaya ūcuḥbhobho rājan śṛṇuṣva tvaṃ yadvadāma mahīpate rājyaṃ dehopakārāya prajānāṃ ca hitaṃ param  ViP dīrghasatreṇa deveśaṃ sarvayajñeśvaraṃ harim pūjayiṣyāma bhadraṃ te tasyāṃśaste bhaviṣyati  ViP yajñena yajñapuruṣo viṣṇuḥ saṃprīṇite nṛpa asmābhir bhavataḥ kāmānsarvāneva pradāsyati  ViP yajñair yajñeśvaro yeṣāṃ rāṣṭre saṃpūjyate hariḥ teṣāṃ sarvepsitāvāptiṃ dadāti nṛpa bhūbhṛtām  ViP vena uvācamattaḥ ko bhyadhikonyosti kaścārādhyo mamāparaḥ koyaṃ haririti khyāto yo vo yajñaśvaro mataḥ  ViP brahmā janārdanaḥ śambhurindro vāyuryamo raviḥ hutabhugvaruṇo dhātā pūṣā bhūmirniṃśākaraḥ  ViP ete cānye ca ye devāḥ śāpānugrahakāriṇaḥ nṛpasyaite śarīrasthāḥ sarvadevamayo nṛpaḥ  ViP evaṃ jñāsvā mayājñaptaṃ yadyathā kriyatāṃ tathā na dātavyaṃ na yaṣṭavyaṃ na hotavyaṃ ca bho dvijāḥ  ViP bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇaṃ dharmo yathā strīṇāṃ paro mataḥ mamājñāpālanaṃ dharmo bhavatāṃ ca tathā dvijāḥ  ViP ṛṣaya ūcuḥdehyanujñāṃ mahārāja mā dharmo yātu saṃkṣayam haviṣāṃ pariṇāmo yaṃ yadetadakhilaṃ jagat  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti vijñāpyamāno pi sa venaḥ paramarṣibhiḥ yadā dadāti nānujñaṃ proktaḥ proktaḥ punaḥ punaḥ  ViP tataste munayaḥ sarve kopāmarṣasamanvitāḥ hanyatāṃ hanyatāṃ pāpa ityūcuste parasparam  ViP yo yajñapuruṣaṃ viṣṇumanādinidhanaṃ prabhum vinindatyadhamācāro na sa yogyo bhuvaḥ patiḥ  ViP ityuktvā mantrapūtais taiḥ kuśair munigaṇānṛpam nijaghnurnihataṃ purvaṃ bhagavannindanādinā  ViP tataś ca munayo reṇuṃ dadṛśuḥ sarvato dvija kimetaditi cāsannātpapracchuste janāstadā  ViP ākhyātaṃ ca janais teṣāṃ corībhūtair arājake rāṣṭre tu lokair ārabdhaṃ parasvādānamāturaiḥ  ViP teṣāmudīrṇavegānāṃ corāṇāṃ munisattamāḥ sumahaddṛśyate reṇuḥ paravittāpahāriṇām  ViP tataḥ saṃmantrya te sarve sunayastasya bhūbhṛtaḥ mamanthurūruṃ putrārthamanapatyasya yatnataḥ  ViP mathyamānātsamuttasthau tasyoroḥ puruṣaḥ kila dagdhasthūṇāpratīkāśaḥ khalvāṭāsyotihrasvakaḥ  ViP kiṃ karomīti tānsarvānsa viprānāha cāturaḥ niṣīdeti tamūcuste niṣādastena so bhavat  ViP tatastatsaṃbhavā jātā vindhyaśailanivāsinaḥ niṣādā muniśārdūla pāpakarmopalakṣaṇāḥ  ViP tena dvāreṇa tatpāpaṃ niṣkrāntaṃ tasya bhūpateḥ niṣādāste tato jātā venakalmaṣanāśanāḥ  ViP tasyaiva dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ mamanthuste tato dvijāḥ  ViP mathyamāne ca tatrābhūtpṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān dīpyamānaḥ svavapuṣā sākṣādagniriva jvalan  ViP ādyamājagavaṃ nāma khātpapāta tato dhanuḥ śarāś ca divyā nabhasaḥ kavacaṃ ca papāta ha  ViP tasmin jāte tu bhūtāni saṃprahṛṣṭāni sarvaśaḥ  ViP satputreṇaiva jātena venopi tridivaṃ yayo punnāmno narakāt trātaḥ sutena sumahātmanā  ViP taṃ samudrāś ca nadyaś ca ratnānyādāya sarvaśaḥ toyāni cābhiṣekārthaṃ sarvāṇyevopatasthire  ViP pitāmahaś ca bhagavāndevair āṅgirasaiḥ saha sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni jaṅgamāni ca sarvaśaḥ samāgamya tadā vainyamabhyasiñcannarādhipam  ViP haste tu dakṣiṇe cakraṃ dṛṣṭvā tasya pitāmahaḥ viṣṇoraṃśaṃ ṣṛthuṃ matvā paritoṣaṃ paraṃ yayai  ViP viṣṇucakra kare cihnaṃ sarveṣāṃ cakravartinām bhavatyavyāhato yasya prabhāvastridaśerapi  ViP mahatā rājarājyena pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān sobhiṣikto mahātejā vidhivaddharmakovidai  ViP pitrā parājitāstasya prajāstenānurañcitāḥ anurāgāttatastasya nāma rājetyajāyata  ViP āpastastaṃbhire cāsya samudramabhiyāsyataḥ parvatāś ca dadurmārgaṃ dhvajabhaṅgaś ca nābhavat  ViP akṛṣṭapacyā pṛthivī siddhantyannāni cintayā sarvakāmadughā gāvaḥ puṭake puṭake madhu  ViP tasya vai jātamātrasya yajñe paitāmahe śubhe sūtaḥ sūtyāṃ samutpannaḥ sautye hani mahāmatiḥ  ViP tasminneva mahāyajñejajñe prājñe tha māgadhaḥ proktau tadā munivarais tāvubhau sūtamāgadhau  ViP stūyatāmeṣa nṛpatiḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān karmaitadanurūpaṃ vāṃ pātraṃ stotrasya cāparam  ViP tatastāvūcaturviprānsarvāneva kṛtāñjalī adya jātasya no karma jñāyatesya mahīpateḥ  ViP guṇā na cāsya jñāyante na cāsya prathitaṃ yaśaḥ stotraṃ kimāśrayaṃ tvasya kāryamasmābhir ucyatām  ViP kṛṣaya ūcuḥkariṣyatyeṣa yatkarma cakravarti mahābalaḥ guṇā bhaviṣyā ye cāsya tair ayaṃ stūyatāṃ nṛpaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ sa nṛpatistoṣaṃ tacchratvā paramaṃ yayau sadguṇaiḥ ślāghyatāmeti tasmācchlāghyā guṇā mama  ViP tasmādyadadya stotreṇa guṇanirvarṇanaṃ tvimau kariṣyete kariṣyāmi tadevāhaṃ samāhitaḥ  ViP yadimau varjanīyaṃ ca kiñcidatra vadiṣyataḥ tadahaṃ varjayiṣyāmītyevaṃ cakre matiṃ nṛpaḥ  ViP atha tau cakratuḥ stotraṃ pṛthorvainyasya dhīmataḥ bhaviṣyaiḥ karmabhiḥ samyaksusvarau sūtamāgadhau  ViP satyavāgdānaśīloyaṃ satyasandho nareśvaraḥ hrīmānmaitraḥ kṣamāśīlo vikrānto duṣṭaśānaḥ  ViP dharmajñaś ca kṛtajñaś ca dayāvān priyabhāṣakaḥ mānyānmānayitā yajvā brahmaṇyaḥ sādhusaṃmataḥ  ViP samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca vyavahārasthitau nṛpaḥ  ViP sūtenoktān guṇānitthaṃ sa tadā māgadhena ca cakāra hṛdi tādṛk ca karmaṇā kṛtavānasau  ViP tatastu pṛthivīpālaḥ pālayanpṛthivīmimām iyāja vividhair yajñair mahadbhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ  ViP taṃ prajāḥ pṛthivīnāthamupatasthuḥ kṣudhārditāḥ oṣadhīṣu praṇaṣṭāsu tasminkāle hyarājake tamūcuste natāḥ pṛṣṭāstatrāgamanakāraṇam  ViP prajā ūcuḥarājake nṛpaśraṣṭha dharitryā sakalauṣadhīḥ grastāstataḥ kṣayaṃ yānti prajāḥ sarvāḥ prajeśvara  ViP tvanno vṛttiprado dhātrā prajāpālo nirūpitaḥ dehi naḥ kṣutparītā nāṃ prajānāṃ jīvanauṣadhīḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatatastu napatirdivyamādāyajagavaṃ dhanuḥ śarāṃś ca divyānkupitaḥ sonvadhāvadvasundharām  ViP tato nanāśa tvarītā gaurbhūtvā ca vasundharā sā lokānbrahmalokādīnsaṃtrāsādagamanmahī  ViP yatra yatra yayau devī sā tadā bhūtadhāriṇī tatra tatra tu sā vainyaṃ dadṛśe bhyudyatāyudham  ViP tatastaṃ prāha vasudhā pṛthuṃ rājaparākramam pravepamānā tadbāṇaparitrāṇaparāyaṇā  ViP pṛthivyuvācastrīvadhe tvaṃ mahāpāpaṃ kiṃ narendra na paśyasi yena māṃ hantumatyarthaṃ prakaroṣi nṛpodyamam  ViP pṛthuruvācaekasmin yatra nidhanaṃ prāpite duṣṭakāriṇi bahūnāṃ bhavati kṣemaṃ tasya puṇyaprado vadhaḥ  ViP pṛthuvyuvācaprajānāmupakārāya yadi māṃ tvaṃ haniṣyasi ādhāraḥ kaḥ prajānāṃ te nṛpaśreṣṭha bhaviṣyati  ViP pṛthuruvācatvāṃ hatvā vasudhe bāṇair macchāsanaparāṅmukhīm ātma yogabalenemā dhārayiṣyāmyahaṃ prajāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ vasudhā taṃ bhūyaḥ taṃ bhūyaḥ prāha pārthivam pravepitāṅgī paramaṃ sādhvasaṃ samupāgatā  ViP pṛthivyuvācaupāyataḥ samārabdhāḥ sarve siddhyantyupakramāḥ tasmādvadāmyupāyaṃ te taṃ kuruṣva yadīcchasi  ViP samastā yā mayā jīrṇā naranātha mahauṣadhīḥ yadīcchasi pradāsyāmi tāḥ kṣīrapariṇāminīḥ  ViP tasmātprajāhitārthāya mama dharmabhṛtāṃ vara taṃ tu vatsaṃ kuruṣva tvaṃ kṣareyaṃ yena vatsalā  ViP samāṃ ca kuru sarvatra yena kṣīraṃ samantataḥ varauṣadhībījabhūtaṃ bījaṃ sarvatra bhāvaye  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatata utsārayāmāsa śailān śatasahasraśaḥ dhanuṣkoṭyā padā vainyastena śaulā vivardhitāḥ  ViP na hi pūrvavisarge vai viṣame pṛthivītale pravībhāgaḥ purāṇāṃ vā grāmāṇāṃ vā purābhavāt  ViP na sasyāni na gorakṣyaṃ na kṛṣirna vaṇikpathaḥ vainyātprabhṛti maitreya sarvasyaitasya sambhavaḥ  ViP yatrayatra samaṃ tvasya bhūmerāsīdddvajottama tatratatra prajāḥ sarvā nivāsaṃ samarocayant  ViP āhāraḥ phalamūlāni prajānāmabhavattadā kṛcchreṇa mahatā so pi praṇaṣṭāsvaiṣadīṣu vai  ViP sa kalpayitvā vatsaṃ tu manuṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ prabhum svapāṇau pṛtivīnātho dudoha pṛthivīṃ pṛthuḥ sasyājātāni sarvāṇi prajānāṃ hitakāmyayā  ViP tenānnena prajāstāta vartantedyāpi nityaśaḥ  ViP prāṇapradātā sa pṛthuryasmādbhumerabhītpitā tatastu pṛthivīsaṃjñāmavāpākhilādhāriṇī  ViP tataś ca devair munibhir daityai rakṣobhir adribhiḥ gandharvair uragair yakṣaiḥ pitṛbhis tarubhis tathā  ViP tattatpātramupādāya tattaddugdhaṃ mune payaḥ vatsado gdhṛviśeṣāś ca teṣāṃ tadyonayo bhavan  ViP saiṣā dhatrī vidhātrī ca dhāriṇī poṣaṇī tathā sarvasya tu tataḥ pṛthvī viṣṇupādatalodbhāvā  ViP evaṃ prabhāvaḥsa pṛthuḥ putro vainyasya vīryavān jajñe mahīpatiḥ pūrvo rājābhūjjanarañjanāt  ViP ya idaṃ janma vainyasya pṛthoḥ saṃkīrtarennaraḥ na tasya duṣkṛtaṃ kiñcitphaladāyi prajāyate  ViP duḥsvapnopaśamaṃ nṝṇāṃ śṛṇvatāmetaduttamam pṛthorjanma prabhāvaś ca karoti satataṃ nṛṇām  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe trayodaśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācapṛtoḥ putro tu dharmajño jajñātentardhivādinau śikhaṇḍinī havirdhānamantardhānāvdyajāyata  ViP havirdhānāt ṣaḍāgnoyī dhiṣaṇājayatsutānā prācīnabarhiṣaṃ śukraṃ gayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ vṛjājinau  ViP pracīnabarhirbhagavānmahānāsītprajāpatiḥ havirdhānānmahābhāga yena saṃvardhitāḥ prajāḥ  ViP prācīnāgrāḥ kuśāstasya pṛthivyāṃ viśrutā mune prācīnavarhirabhavatkhyāto bhuvi mahābalaḥ  ViP samudratanayāyāṃ tu kṛtadāro mahīpatiḥ mahatastamasaḥ pāre savarṇāyāṃ mahāmate  ViP savarṇādhatta sāmudrī daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ sarve prācetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ  ViP apṛthagdharmacaraṇāste tapyanta mahattapaḥ daśavarṣasahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayaḥ  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācayadarthaṃ te mahātmānastapastepurmahāmune prācetasaḥ samudrāmbhasyetadākhyātumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācapitrā pracetasaḥ proktāḥ prajārthamamitātmanā prajāpatiniyuktena bahumānapuraḥsaram  ViP prācīnabarhiruvācabrahmaṇā devadevena samādiṣṭosmyahaṃ sutāḥ prajāḥ saṃvardhanīyāste mayā coktaṃ tatheti tat  ViP tanmama prītaye putrāḥ prajāvṛddhimatandritāḥ kurudhvaṃ mānanīyā vaḥ samyagājñā prajāpateḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataste tatpituḥ śrutvā vacanaṃ nṛpanandanāḥ tathetyuktvā ca taṃ bhūyaḥ papracchuḥ pitaraṃ mune  ViP pracetasa ūcuḥyena tāta prajāvṛddhau samarthā karmaṇā vayam bhavema tat samastaṃ naḥ karma vyākhyātumarhasi  ViP pitovācaārādhya varadaṃ viṣṇum iṣṭaprāptim asaṃśayam sameti nānyathā martyaḥ kima nyatkathayāmi vaḥ  ViP tasmātprajā vivṛddhyarthaṃ sarvabhūtaprabhuṃ harim ārādhayata govindaṃ yadi siddhimabhīpsathaḥ  ViP dharmamarthaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca mokṣaṃ cānvicchatāṃ sadā ārādhanīyo bhagavānanādipuruṣottamaḥ  ViP yasminnārādhite sargaṃ cakārādau prajāpatiḥ tamārādhyācyutaṃ vṛddhiḥ prajānāṃ vo bhaviṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityevamuktāste pitrā putrāḥ prācetaso daśa magnāḥ payodhisalile tapasteṣuḥ samāhitāḥ  ViP daśavarṣasahasrāṇi nyastacittā jagatpatau nārāyaṇe muniśreṣṭha sarvalokaparāyaṇe  ViP tatraivāvasthitā devamekāgramanaso harim tuṣṭuvuryaḥstutaḥ kāmān stoturiṣṭānprayacchati  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācastavaṃ pracetaso viṣṇoḥ samudrāmbhasi saṃsthitāḥ cakrustanme muniśreṣṭha supuṇyaṃ vaktumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaśṛṇu maitreya govindaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ pracetasaḥ tuṣṭuvus tanmayībhūtāḥ samudrasalileśayāḥ  ViP pracetasa ūcuḥnatāḥ sma sarvavacasāṃ pratiṣṭhā yatra śāśvatī tamādyantamaśeṣasya jagataḥ paramaṃ prabhum  ViP jyotirādyamanaupamyamaṇvanantamapāravat yonibhūtamaśeṣasya sthāvarasya carasya ca  ViP yasyāhaḥ prathamaṃ rūpamarūpasya tathā niśā saṃdhyā ca parameśasya tasmai kālātmane namaḥ  ViP bujyate nudinaṃ devaiḥ pitṛbhiś ca sudhātmakaḥ bījabhūtaṃ samastasya tasmai somātmanena maḥ  ViP yastamāsyatti tīvrātmā prabhābhir bhāsayannabhaḥ gharmaśītāmbhasā yonistasmai sūryatmane namaḥ  ViP kāṭhinyavān yo bibharti jagadetadaśeṣataḥ śabdādisaṃśrayo vyāpī tasmai bhūmyātmane namaḥ  ViP yadyonibhūtaṃ jagato vījaṃ yatsarvadehinām tattoyarūpamīśasya namāmo harimedhasaḥ  ViP yo mukhaṃ sarvadevānāṃ havyabhukkavyabhuk tathā pitṝṇāṃ ca namastasmai viṣṇave pāvakātmane  ViP pañcadhāvasthito dehe yaśceṣṭāṃ kurute niśam ākāśayonirbhagavāṃstasmai vāyvātmane namaḥ  ViP avakāśamaśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ yaḥ prayacchati anantamūrtimāñdhuddhastasmai vyomātmane namaḥ  ViP samastondriyasargasya yaḥ sadā sthānamuttamam tasmai śabdādirūpāya namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase  ViP gṛhṇāti viṣayānnityamindriyātmākṣarākṣaraḥ yastasmai jñānamūlāya natāsma harimedhase  ViP hṛhītānindriyair arthānātmane yaḥ prayacchati antaḥkaraṇarūpāya tasmai viśvatmane namaḥ  ViP yasminnanante sakalaṃ viśvaṃ yasmāttathodgatam layasthānaṃ ca yastasmai namaḥ prakṛtidharmiṇe  ViP śuddhaḥ saṃllakṣyate bhrāntyā guṇavāniva yo guṇaḥ tamātmarūpiṇaṃ deva natāsma puruṣottamam  ViP avikāramajaṃ śuddhaṃ nirguṇaṃ yannirajanam natāḥsmatatparaṃ brahma viṣṇoryatparamaṃ padam  ViP adīrghahrasvamasthūlaṇvanamaśyāmalohitam asnehacchāyamatanumasaktamaśarīrīṇam  ViP anākāśamasaṃsparśamagandhamarasaṃ ca yat acakṣuśrotramacalamavākpāṇimamānisam  ViP anāmagomatrasukhamatejaskamahetukam abhayaṃ bhrāntirahitama nidramajarāmaram  ViP arajośabdamamṛtamaplutaṃ yadasaṃvṛtam pūrvāpareṇa vai yasmistadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP sthīyatāmityabhāṣata  ViP punargate varṣaśate sādhika sā śubhānanā yāmītyāha divaṃ brahmanpraṇayasmitaśobhanam  ViP uktastayaivaṃ sa munirupaguhyāyate kṣaṇām ihāsyatāṃ kṣaṇaṃ subhu cirakālaṃ gamiṣyasi  ViP sā krīḍamānā suśroṇī saha tenarṣiṇā punaḥ śatadvayaṃ kiñcidūnaṃ varṣaṇāmanvatiṣṭhata  ViP gamanāya mahābhāga devarājaniveśanam proktaḥ proktastayā tanvyā sthīyatāmityabhāṣata  ViP tasya śāpabhayādbhītā dākṣiṇyena ca dakṣiṇā proktā praṇayabhaṅgartivedinī na jahau munim  ViP tayā ca ramatastasya paramarṣeraharniśam navaṃnavamabhūtprama manmathāviṣṭacetasaḥ  ViP ekadā tu tvarāyukto niścakrāmoṭajānmuniḥ niṣkrāmantaṃ ca kutreti gamyate prāha sā śubhā  ViP ityuktaḥ sa tayā prāha parivṛttamahaḥ śubhe sandhyopāstiṃ kariṣyāmi kriyāloponyathā bhavet  ViP tataḥ prahasya sudadī taṃ sā ViP pramlocovācavadiṣyāmyanṛtaṃ brahmankathamatra tavāntike viśeṣeṇādya bhavatā pṛṣṭā mārgānuvartinā  ViP soma uvācaniśamya tadvacaḥ satyaṃ sa munirnṛpanandanāḥ dhikdhik māmityatīvetthaṃ śrutvā prayātāḥ sarvato diśam adyāpi no nivartante samudrebhya ivāpagāḥ  ViP harya śveṣvatha naṣṭoṣu dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ punaḥ vairuṇyāmatha putrāṇāṃ sahasramasṛjatprabhuḥ  ViP vivardhayiṣavaste tu śabalāśvāḥ prajāḥ punaḥ pūrvoktaṃ vacanaṃ brahmannāradenaiva noditāḥ  ViP anyonyamūcuste sarve samyag āha mahāmuniḥ bhratṝṇāṃ padavī caiva gantavyā nātra saṃśayaḥ  ViP jñātvā pramāṇaṃ pṛthvyāś ca
