vijānatā  ViP tāṃ ścāpi naṣṭān vijñāya putrān dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ krodhaṃ cakre mahābhāgo nāradaṃ sa śaśāpa ca  ViP sargakāmastato vidvānsa maitreya prajāpatiḥ ṣaṣṭiṃ takṣo sṛjatkanyā vairuṇyāmiti naḥ śrutam  ViP dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayodaśa saptaviṃśati somāya catastro riṣṭanemine  ViP dve caiva bahuputrāya dve caivāṅgirase tathā dvekṛśāśvāya viduṣe tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP arundhatī vasurjāmirlaṅghā bhānumarutvatī saṃkalpā ca muhūrtā ca sādhyā viśvā ca tādṛśī dharmapatnyo daśatvetāstāsvapatyāni me śṛṇu viśvedevāstu viśvāyāḥ sādhyā sādhyānajāyata marutvatyāṃ sarutvanto vasoś ca vasavaḥ smṛtā  ViP bhānostu bhānavaḥ putrā muhūrtāyāṃ muhūrtajāḥ  ViP laṅghāyāścaiva ghoṣotha nāgavīthī tu jāmitā  ViP pṛthivīviṣayaṃ sarvamarundhatyāma jāyata saṃkalpāyāstu sarvātmā jajñe saṃkalpa eva hi  ViP ye tvanekavasuprāṇadevā jyotiḥ purogamāḥ vasavoṣṭau samākhyātāsteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi vistaram  ViP āpo dhruvaś ca somaś ca dharmaścaivānilo nalaḥ pratyūṣaś ca prabhāsaś ca vasavo nāmabhiḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP āpasya putro vaitaṇḍaḥ śramaḥ śānto dhvanis tathā dhruvasya putro bhagavānkālo lokaprakālanaḥ  ViP somasya bhagavānvarco varcasvī yena jāyate  ViP dharmasya putro draviṇo hutahavyavahas tathā manoharāyāṃ śiśiraḥ prāṇotha ravaṇas tathā  ViP anilasya śivā bhāryā tasyāḥ putro manojavaḥ avijñātagatiścaiva dvau putrāvanilasya tu  ViP agniputraḥ kumārastu śarastambe vyajāyata tasya śākho viśākhaś ca naigameyaś ca pṛṣṭhajāḥ  ViP apatyaṃ kṛttikānāṃ tu kārttikeya iti smṛtaḥ  ViP pratyūṣasya viduḥ putraṃ ṛṣi nāmnātha devalam dvau putrau devalasyāpi kṣamāvantau manīṣiṇau  ViP bṛhaspatestu bhaginī varastrī brahmacāriṇī yogasiddhā jagatkṛtsnamasaktā vicaratyuta prabhāsasya tu sā bhāryā vasūnāmaṣṭamasya tu  ViP viśvakarmā mahābhāgastasyāṃ jajñe prajāpatiḥ kartā śilpasahasrāṇāṃ tridaśānāṃ ca vārdhakiḥ  ViP bhūṣaṇānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ kartāśilpavatāṃ varaḥ yaḥ sarvaiṣāṃ vimānāni devatānāṃ cakāra ha manuṣyāścopajīvanti yasya śilpaṃ mahātmanaḥ  ViP ajaikapād ahirbudhnyas tvaṣṭā rudraś ca vīryavān tvaṣṭuścāpyātmajaḥ putro viśvarūpo mahātapāḥ  ViP haraś ca bahurūpaś ca tryambakaścāparājitaḥ vṛṣākapiś ca śambhuś ca kapardīraivataḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP mṛgavyādhaś ca śarvaś ca kapālī ca mahāmune ekādaśaite kathitā rudrāstribhuvaneśvarāḥ  ViP śataṃ tvekaṃ samākhyātaṃ rudrāṇāmamitaujasām kāśyapasya tu bhāryā yāstāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu aditirditirdanuścaivāriṣṭā ca surasā khasā  ViP surabhir vinatā caiva tāmrā krodhavaśā irā kadrurmuniś ca dharmajña tadapatyāni me śṛṇu  ViP pūrvamanvantare śreṣṭhā dvādaśāsansurottamāḥ tuṣitā nāma te nyonyamūcurvaivasvatentare  ViP upasthite tiyaśasaścākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ samavāyīkṛtāḥ sarve samāgamya parasparam  ViP āgacchata drutaṃ devā aditiṃ saṃpraviśya vai manvantare prasūyāmastannaḥ śreyo bhavediti  ViP evamuktvā tu te sarve cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ mārīcātkaśyapājjātā adityā dakṣakanyayā  ViP tatra viṣṇuś ca śakraś ca jajñāte punar eva hi aryamā caiva dhātā ca tvaṣṭā pūṣā tathaiva ca  ViP vivasvānsavitā caiva mitro varuṇa eva ca aṃśurbhagaścātitejā ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ  ViP cākṣuṣasyāntare pūrvamāsanye tuṣitāḥ surāḥ vaivasvate ntare te vai ādityā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ  ViP saptaviṃśati yāḥ proktāḥ somapatnyotha suvratāḥ sarvā nakṣatrayoginyastannāmnaścaiva tāḥ smṛtāḥ tāsāmapatyānyabhavandīptānyamitatejasām  ViP ariṣṭanemipatnīnāmapatyānīha ṣoḍaśa  ViP bahuputrasya viduṣaścatastrovidyutaḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP pratyaṅgirasajāḥ śreṣṭhā ṛco brahmarṣisatkṛtāḥ  ViP kṛśāśvasya tu devarṣerdevapraharaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP ete yugasahasrānte jāyante punareva hi sarve devagaṇāstāta trayastriṃśattu chandajāḥ teṣāmapīha satataṃ nirodhotpattirucyate  ViP yathā sūryasya maitreya udayāstamanāviha evaṃ devanikāyāste sambhavanti yugeyuge  ViP dityā putradvayaṃ jajñe kaśyapāditi naḥ śrutam hiraṇyakaśipuścaiva hiraṇyākṣaś ca durjayaḥ  ViP siṃhikā cābhavatkanyā vipracitteḥ parigrahaḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāścātvāraḥ prathitaujasaḥ anuhlādaś ca hlādaś ca prahlādaścaiva buddhimān saṃhlādaś ca mahāvīryā daityavaṃśavivardhanāḥ  ViP teṣāṃ madhye mahābhāga sarvatra samadṛgvāśī prahlādaḥ paramāṃ bhaktiṃ ca uvāca janārdane  ViP daityendradīpito vahniḥ sarvāṅgopacito dvija na dadāha ca yaṃ vipra vāsudeva hṛdi sthite  ViP mahārṇavāntaḥ salile sthitasya calato mahī cacāla calatā yasya pāśabaddhasya dhīmataḥ  ViP na bhinnaṃ vividhaiḥ śastrair yasya daityendrapātitaiḥ śarīramadrikaṭhinaṃ sarvatrācyutacetasaḥ  ViP viṣānalojjvalamukhā yasya daityapracoditāḥ nāntāya sarpapatayo babhūvururutejasaḥ  ViP śailair ākrāntadehopi yaḥ smaranpuruṣottamam tatyāja nātmanaḥ prāṇān viṣṇusmaraṇadaṃśitaḥ  ViP patantamuccādavaniryamupetya mahāmatim dadhāra daityapatinā kṣiptaṃ svarganivāsinā  ViP yasya saśoṣako vāyurdehe daityendrayojitaḥ avāpa saṃkṣayaṃ sadyaścittasthe madhusūdane  ViP viṣāṇabhaṅgamunmattā madahāniṃ ca diggajāḥ yasya vakṣaḥsthale prāptā daityendrapariṇāmitāḥ  ViP yasya cotpāditā kṛtyā daityarājapurohitaiḥ babhūva nāntāya purā govindāsaktacetasaḥ  ViP śambarasya ca māyānāṃ sahasramatimāyinaḥ yasminprayuktaṃ cakreṇa kṛṣṇasya vitathikṛtam  ViP daityendrasūdopahṛtaṃ yasya hālāhalaṃ viṣam jarayāmāsa matimānavikāramamatsarī  ViP samacetā jagatyasminyaḥ sarveṣveva jantuṣu yathātmani tathānyeṣāṃ paraṃ maitraguṇānvitaḥ  ViP dharmātmā satyaśauryādiguṇānāmākaraḥ paraḥ upamānamaśeṣāṇāṃ sādhūnāṃ yaḥ sadābhavat  ViP itiśrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācakathito bhavatā vaṃśo mānavānāṃ mahātmanām kāraṇaṃ cāsya jagato viṣṇureva sanātanaḥ  ViP yattvetadbhagavānāha prahlādaṃ daityasattamam dadāha nāgnirnāstraiś ca kṣuṇṇastatyāja jīvitam  ViP jagāma vasudhā kṣobhaṃ yatrābdhisalile sthite pāśaurbaddhe vicalati vikṣiptāṅgaiḥ samāhatā  ViP śailair ākrāntadehopi na mamāra ca yaḥ purā tvāya cātīva māhātmyaṃ kathitaṃ yasya dhīmataḥ  ViP tasya prabhāvamatulaṃ viṣṇorbhaktimato mune śrotumicchāmi yasyaitaccaritaṃ dīptatejasaḥ  ViP kiṃnimittamasau śastrair vikṣipto ditijemuna kimarthaṃ cābdhisalile vikṣipto dharmatatparaḥ  ViP ākrāntaḥ parvataiḥ kasmāddaṣṭaścaiva mahoragaiḥ kṣiptaḥ kimadriśikharāktiṃ vā pāvakasañcaye  ViP digdantināṃ dantabhūmiṃ sa ca kasmānnirūpitaḥ saśoṣakonilaścāsya prayuktaḥ kiṃ mahāsuraiḥ  ViP kṛtyāṃ ca daityaguravo yuyujus tatra kiṃ mune śambaraścāpi māyānāṃ sahasraṃ kiṃ prayuktāvān  ViP hālāhalaṃ viṣamaho daityasūdair mahātmanaḥ kasmāddattaṃ vināśāya yajjīrṇaṃ tena dhīmatā  ViP etatsarvaṃ mahābhāga prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ caritaṃ śrotumicchāmi mahāmāhātmyasūcakam  ViP na hi kautūhalaṃ tatra yaddaityaurnihato hi saḥ ananyamanaso viṣṇo kaḥ samartho nipātane  ViP tasmindharmaparenityaṃ keśavārādhanodyate svavaṃśaprabhavair daityaiḥ kṛto dveṣotidupkaraḥ  ViP dharmātmani mahābhāgo viṣṇubhakte vimatsare daitayaiḥ prahṛtaṃ kasmāttanmamākhyātumarhasi  ViP praharanti mahātmāno vipakṣā api neddaśe guṇaiḥ samanvite sādhau kiṃ punaryaḥ svapakṣajaḥ  ViP tadetatkathyatāṃ sarvaṃ vistarānmunipuṅgava daityeśvarasya cāritaṃ śrotumicchāmyaśeṣataḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe ṣoḍaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācamaitreya kṣūyatāṃ samyak caritaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ prahlādasya sadodāracaritasya mahātmanaḥ  ViP diteḥ putro mahāvīryo hiraṇyakaśipuḥ purā trailokyaṃ vaśamāninye brahmaṇo varadarpitaḥ  ViP indratvamakaroddaityaḥ sa cāsītsavitā svayam vāyuragnirapāṃ nāthaḥ somaścābhūnmahāsuraḥ  ViP dhanānāmadhipaḥ so bhūt sa evāsītsvayaṃ yamaḥ yajñabhāgānaśeṣāṃstu sa svayaṃ bubhuje suraḥ  ViP devāḥ svargaṃ parityajya tartrāsān munisattama viceruravanau sarve bibhrāṇā mānuṣīṃ tanum  ViP jitvā tribhuvanaṃ sarvaṃ trailokyaiśvaryadarpitaḥ upagīyamāno gandharvair bubhuje viṣayānpriyān  ViP pānāsaktaṃ mahātmānaṃ hiraṇyakaśipuṃ tadā upāsāṃcakrire sarve siddhagandharvapannagāḥ  ViP avādayan jaguścānye jayaśabdaṃ tathāpare daityarājasya purataścakruḥ siddhā mudānvitāḥ  ViP tatra pranṛttapsarasi sphāṭikābhramaye suraḥ papau pānaṃ mudā yuktaḥ prāsāde sumanohare  ViP tasya putro mahābhāgaḥ prahlādo nāma nāmataḥ papāṭha bālapāṭhyāni gurugehaṅgatorbhakaḥ  ViP ekadā tu sa dharmātmā jagāma guruṇā saha pānāsaktasya purataḥ puturdaityapatestadā  ViP pādapraṇāmāvanataṃ tamutthāpya pitā sutam hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prāha prahlādamamitaujasam  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācapaṭhyatāṃ bhavatā vatsa sārabhūtaṃ subhāṣitam kālenaitāvatā yatte sadodyoktena śikṣitam  ViP prahlāda uvācaśrūyatāṃ tāta vakṣyāmi sārabhūtaṃ tavājñayā samāhitamanā bhūtvā yanme cetasyavasthitam  ViP anādimadhyāntamajamavṛddhikṣayamacyutam praṇatosmyantamantānaṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaetanniśamya daityendraḥ sakopo raktalocanaḥ vilokya tadguruṃ prāha sphuritādharapallavaḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipuruvācabrahmabandho kimetatte vipakṣastutisaṃhitam asāraṃ grāhito bālo māmavajñāya durmate  ViP gururuvācadaityeśvara na kopasya vaśamāgantumarhasi mamopadeśajanitaṃnāyaṃ vadati te sutaḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipuruvācaanuśiṣṭosi kenedṛgvatsa brahlāda kathyatām mayopadiṣṭaṃ netyeṣa prabravīti gurustava  ViP prahlāda uvācaśāstā viṣṇuraśeṣasya jagato yo hṛdi sthitaḥ tamṛte paramātmānaṃ tāta kaḥ kena śāsyate  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācakoyaṃ viṣṇuḥ sudurbuddhe yaṃ bravīṣi punaḥ punaḥ jagatāmīśvarasyeha purataḥ prasabha mama  ViP prahlāda uvācana śabdagocare yasya yogidhyeyaṃ paraṃ padam yato yaś ca svayaṃ viśvaṃ sa viṣṇuḥ parameśvaraḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācaparameśvarasaṃjñojña kimanyo mayyavasthite tathāpi martukāmastvaṃ prabravīṣi punaḥ punaḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācana kevalaṃ tāta mama prajānāṃ sa brahmabhūto bhavataś ca viṣṇuḥ dhātā vidhātā parameśvaraś ca prakīda kopaṃ kuruṣe kimartham  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācapraviṣṭaḥ ko sya hṛdaye durbuddheratipāpakṛt yenedṛśānyasādhūni vadatyāviṣṭamānasaḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācana kevalaṃ maddhṛdayaṃ sa viṣṇurākramya lalokānakhilānavasthitaḥ sa māṃ tvadāndīś ca pitaḥsamastānsamastaceṣṭāsu yunakti sarvagaḥ  ViP hiraṇyakiśipur uvācaniṣkāsyatāmayaṃ pāpaḥ śāsyatāṃ ca gurorgṛhe yojito durmatiḥ kena vipakṣaviṣayastutau  ViP śrīpāraśara uvācaityukto sau tadā daityair nīto gurugṛhaṃ punaḥ jagrāha vidyamaniśaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇodyataḥ  ViP kālotīteti mahati prahlādamasureśvaraḥ samāhūyābravīdrāthā kācitputraka gīyatām  ViP prahlāda uvācayataḥ pradhānapuruṣau yataścaitaccarācaram kāraṇaṃ sakalasyāsya sa no viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācadurātmā vadhyatāmeṣa nānenārthosti jīvatā svapakṣahānikartṛtvādyaḥ kulāṅgāratāṃ gataḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityājñaptāstatastena pragṛhītamahāyudhāḥ udyatāstasya nāśāya daityāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācaviṣṇuḥ śastreṣu yuṣmāsu mayi cāsau vyavasthitaḥ daiteyāstena satyena mākramantvāyudhāni me  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatatastaiḥ śataśo daityaiḥ śastroghair āhatopi san nāvāca vedanāmalpāmabhūccaiva punarnavaḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācadurbuddhe vinivartasva vairipakṣastavāhataḥ abhayaṃ te prayacchāmi mātimūḍhamatirbhava  ViP prahlāda uvācabhayaṃ bhayānāmapahāriṇa sthite manasyanante mama kutra tiṣṭhati yasminsmṛte janmajarāntakādibhayāni sarvāmyapayānti tāta  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācabhobhoḥ sarpāḥ durācāramenamatyantadurmatim viṣajvālākulair vakraiḥ sadyo nayataḥ saṃkṣayam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktāste tataḥ sarpāḥ kuhakāstakṣakādayaḥ adaśanta samasteṣu gātreṣvativiṣolbaṇāḥ  ViP sa tvāsaktamatiḥ kṛṣṇe daśyamāno mahoragaiḥ na vivedātmano gātraṃ tatsmṛtyāhlādasusthitaḥ  ViP sarpā ūcuḥdaṃṣṭrā viśīrṇā maṇyaḥ sphuṭanti phaṇeṣu tāpo hṛdayeṣu kaṃpaḥ nāsya tvacaḥ svalpamapīha bhinnaṃ prasādhi daityeśvara kāryamanyata  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur upācahe diggājāḥ saṃkaṭadantamiśra ghnatainamasmadripupakṣabhinnam tajjā vināśāya bhavanti tasya yathāraṇeḥ prajvalito hutāśaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ sa diggajair bālo bhūbhṛcchikharasannibhaiḥ pātito dharaṇīpṛṣṭhe viṣāṇair vāvapīḍitaḥ  ViP smaratastasya govindamibhadantāḥ sahasraśaḥ śīrṇā vakṣasthalaṃ prāpya sa prāha pitaraṃ tataḥ  ViP dantā gajānāṃ kuliśāgraniṣṭhurājha śīrṇā yadetena balaṃ mamaitat mahāvipattāpavināśano yaṃ janārdanānusmaraṇānubhāvaḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācajvālyatāmasurā bahnirapasarpata diggajāḥ vāyo samedhayāgniṃ tvaṃ dahyatāmeṣa pāpakṛt  ViP śrīparāśara uvācamahākāṣṭhacayasthaṃ tamasurendrasutaṃ tataḥ prajvālya dānavā vahniṃ dadahuḥ svāminoditāḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācatātaiṣa vahniḥ pavaneritopi na māṃ dahatyatra samantatoham paśyāmi padmāstaraṇāstṛtāni śītāni sarvāṇi diśāṃ mukhāni  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaatha daityeśvaraṃ procurbhārgavasyātmajā dvājāḥ purohitā mahātmānaḥ sāmnā saṃstūya vāgminaḥ  ViP purohitā ūcuḥrājanniyamyatāṃ kopo bālepi tanaye nije kopo devanikāyeṣu teṣu te śapalo yataḥ  ViP tataḥ purohitair ukto hiraṇyakaśipuḥ svakaiḥtathātathainaṃ bālaṃ te śāsitāro vayaṃ nṛpaḥ yathā vipabhanāśāya vinītaste bhaviṣyati  ViP bālatvaṃ sarvadoṣāṇāṃ daityarājāspadaṃ yataḥ tatotra kopamatyarthaṃ yoktumarhasi nārbhake  ViP na tyakṣyati hareḥ pakṣamasmākaṃ vacanādyadi tataḥ kṛtyāṃ vadhāyāsya kariṣyāmo nivartinīm  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevamabhyarthitastais tu daityarājaḥ purohitaiḥ daityair niṣkāsayāmāsa putraṃ pāvakasaṃcayāt  ViP tato gurugṛhe vālaḥ sa vasanbāladānavān adhyāpayāmāsa muhurupadeśāntare guroḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācaśrūyatāṃ paramārtho me daiteyā ditijātmajāḥ na cānyathaitanmantavyaṃ nātra lobhādikāraṇam  ViP janma bālyaṃ tataḥ sarvo jantuḥ prāpnoti yauvanam avyāhataiva bhavati tatonudivasaṃ jarāḥ  ViP tataś ca sṛtyumabhyeti janturdaityeśvarātmajāḥ pratyakṣaṃ dṛsyate caitadasmākaṃ bhavatāṃ tathā  ViP mṛtasya ca punarjanma bhavatyetacca nānyathā āgamo yaṃ tathā yacca nopādānaṃ vinodbhavaḥ  ViP garbhavāsādi yāvattu punarjanmopapādanam saha stāvasthakaṃ tāvadduḥkhamevāvagamyatām  ViP kṣuttṛṣṇopaśamaṃ tadvac chītādyupaśamaṃ mukham manyate bālabuddhitvādduḥkhameva hi tatpunaḥ  ViP atyantastimitāṅgānāṃ vyāyāmena sukhaiṣiṇām bhrāntijñānāvṛtākṣāṇāṃ duḥkhameva sukhāyate  ViP kva śarīramaśeṣāṇāṃ śleṣmādīnāṃ mahācayaḥ kva kāntiśobhāsaundaryaramaṇīyādayo guṇāḥ  ViP māṃsāsṛkpūyaviṇmūtrasnāyumajjāsthisaṃhatau dehe cetprītimān mūḍho bhavitā narakepyasau  ViP agnoḥ śītena toyasya tṛṣā bhaktasya ca kṣudhā kriyate sukhakartṛtvaṃ tadvilomasya cetaraiḥ  ViP karoti he daityasutā yāvanmātraṃ parigraham tāvanmātraṃ sa evāsya duḥkhaṃ cetasi yacchati  ViP yāvataḥ kurute jantuḥ sambandhānmanasaḥ priyān tāvantosya nikhanyante hṛdaye śokaśaṅkavaḥ  ViP yadyadgṛhe tanmanasi yatra tatrāvatiṣṭhataḥ nāśadāhopakaraṇaṃ tasya tatraiva tiṣṭhati  ViP janmanyatra mahadduḥkhaṃ mriyamāṇasya cāpi tat yātanāsu yamasyograṃ garbhasaṃkramaṇeṣu ca  ViP garbheṣu sukhalośopi bhavadbhir anumīyate yadi tatkathyatāmevaṃ sarvaṃ duḥkhamayaṃ jagat  ViP tadevamatidukhānāmāspadetra bhavārmave bhavatāṃ kathyate satyaṃ viṣṇurekaḥ parāyaṇaḥ  ViP mā jānīta vayaṃ bālā dehī deheṣu śāśvataḥ jarāyauvanajanmādya dharmā dehasya nātmanaḥ  ViP bālohaṃ tāvadicchāto yatiṣye śreyase yuvā yuvāhaṃ vārdhake prāpte kariṣyāmyatmano hitam  ViP vṛddho haṃ mama kāryāṇi samastāni na gocare kiṃ kariṣyāmi mandātmā samarthena na yatkṛtam  ViP evaṃ durāśayā kṣiptamānasaḥ puruṣaḥ sadā śreyaso bhimukhaṃ yāti na kādācitpipāsitaḥ  ViP bālye kriḍanakāsaktā yovane viṣayonmukhāḥ ajñā nayantyaśaktyā ca vārdhakaṃ samupasthitam  ViP tasmādbālye vivekātmā yateta śreyase sadā bālyayauvanavṛdvādyair dehabhāvair asaṃyutaḥ  ViP tadetadvo mayākhyātaṃ yadi jānīta nānṛtam tadasmatprītaye viṣṇuḥ smaryatāṃ bandhamuktidaḥ  ViP prayāsaḥ smaraṇe kosya smṛto yacchati śobhanam pāpakṣayaś ca bhavati smaratāṃ tamaharniśam  ViP sarvabhūtasthite tasminmatirmaitrī divāniśam bhavatāṃ jāyatāmevaṃ sarvakleśānprahāsyatha  ViP tāpatrayeṇābhihataṃ yadetadakhilaṃ jagat tadā śocyeṣu bhūteṣu dveṣaṃ prājñaḥ karoti kaḥ  ViP atha bhadrāṇi bhūtāni hīnaśaktirahaṃ param mudaṃ tadāpi kurvita hānirdveṣaphalaṃ yataḥ  ViP baddhavairāṇi bhūtāni dveṣaṃ kurvanti cettataḥ suśocyānyatimohena vyāptānīti manīṣiṇām  ViP ete bhinnadṛsāṃ daityā vikalpāḥ kathitā mayā kṛtvābhyupagamaṃ tatra saṃbhepaḥ śrūyatāṃ mama  ViP vistāraḥ sarvabhūtasya viṣṇoḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat draṣṭavyamātmavattasmādabhedena vicakṣaṇaiḥ  ViP samutsṛjyāsuraṃ bhāvaṃ tasmādyayaṃ yathā vayam tathā yatnaṃ kariṣyāmo yathā prāpsyāma nirvṛtim  ViP yā nāgninā na cārkeṇa nendunā na ca vāyunā pajanyavaruṇābhyāṃ vā na siddherna ca sākṣasaiḥ  ViP na yakṣair na ca daityendrair noragair na ca kinnaraiḥ na manuṣyair na paśubhir doṣair naivātmasambhavaiḥ  ViP jvārākṣirogātīsāraplīhagulmādikais tathā dveṣorṣyāmatsarādyaurvā rāgalobhādibhiḥ kṣayam  ViP na cānyair nīyate kaiścinnityā yātyantanirmalā tāmāpnotyamalenyasya keśave hṛdayaṃ naraḥ  ViP asārasaṃsāravivartaneṣu mā yāta toṣaṃ prasabhaṃ bravīmi sarvatra daityāḥsamatāmupaita samatvamārādhanamacyutasya  ViP tasminprasanne kimihāstyalabhyaṃ dharmārthakāmair alamalpakāste samāśritādbrahyataroranantānniḥ saṃśayaṃ prāpstatha vai mahatphalam  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe prahlādānucaritaṃ nāma saptadaśodhyāyaḥ śrīpāraśara uvācatasyaitāṃ dānavāśceṣṭāṃ dṛṣṭvā daityapaterbhayāt ācacakhyuḥ sa covāca sūdānāhūya satvaraḥ  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācahe sūdāḥmama putrosāvanyoṣāmapi durmatiḥ kumārgadeśiko duṣṭo hanyatāmavilambitam  ViP hālāhalaṃ viṣaṃ tasya sarvabhakṣeṣu dīyatām avijñātamasau pāpo hanyatāṃ mā vicāryatām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācate tathaiva tataścakruḥ prahlādāya mahātmane viṣadānaṃ yathājñāptaṃ pitrā tasya mahātmanaḥ  ViP hālāhalaṃ viṣaṃ ghoramanantoccāraṇena saḥ abhimantrya sahānnena maitreya bubhuje tadā  ViP avikāraṃ sa tadbhuktvā prahlādaḥ svasthamānasaḥ anantakhyātinirviryajarayāmāsa tadviṣam  ViP tataḥ sūdā bhayatrastā jīrṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahadviṣam daityeśvaramupāgamya praṇipatyedamabruvan  ViP sūdā ūcuḥdaityarāja viṣaṃ dattamasmābhir atibhīṣaṇam jīrṇaṃ tena sahānnena prahlāhena sutena te  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācatvaryatāṃ tvaryatāṃ he he sadyo daityapurohitāḥ kṛtyāṃ tasyavināśāya utpādayata mā ciram  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasakāśamāgamya tataḥ prahlādasya purohitāḥ sāmapūrvamathocuste prahlādaṃ vinayānvitam  ViP purohitā ūcuḥjātastrailokyavikhyāta āyuṣmanbrahmaṇaḥ kule daityarājasya tanayo hiraṇyakaśiporbhavāt  ViP kindevaiḥ kimanantena kimanyena tavāśrayaḥ pitā te sarvalokānāṃ tvaṃ tathaiva bhaviṣyasi  ViP tasmātparityajaināṃ tvaṃ vipakṣastavasaṃhitām ślāghyaḥ pitā samastānāṃ gurūṇāṃ paramo guruḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācaevam etan mahābhāgāḥ ślāghyametanmahākulam mariceḥ sakalepyasmin trailokye nā nyāthā vadet  ViP pitā ca mama sarvāsmiñjagatyuktṛṣṭaceṣṭitaḥ etadapyavagacchāmi satyamatrāpi nānṛtam  ViP gurūṇāmapi sarveṣāṃ pitā paramako guruḥ yaduktaṃ bhrāntistatrāpi svalpāpi hi na vidyate  ViP pitā gururna sandehaḥ pūjanīyaḥ pūyatnataḥ tatrāpi nāparādhyāmītyevaṃ manasi se sthitam  ViP yattvetatkimanantenetyuktaṃ yuṣmābhir idṛsam ko bravīti yathānyāyyaṃ kiṃ tu naitadvacorthavat  ViP ityuktvā so bhavanmaunī teṣāṃ goravayantritaḥ prahasya ca punaḥ prāha kimanantena sādhviti  ViP sādhu bhoḥ kimanantena sādhu bho guruvo mama śrūyatāṃ yadanantena yadi khedaṃ na yāsyatha  ViP dharmārthakāmamokṣāś ca puruṣārthā udāhṛtāḥ catuṣṭayamidaṃ yasmāttasmāktiṃ kimidaṃ vaca  ViP marīcimiśrair dakṣādyais tathaivānyair anantataḥ dharma prāptas tathā cānyair arthaḥ kāmastathāparaiḥ  ViP tantattvavedino bhūtvā jñānadhyānasamādhibhiḥ avāpurmuktimapare puruṣā dhvastabandhanāḥ  ViP sampadaiśvaryamāhātmyajñānasaṃtatikarmaṇām vimukteścaikato labhyaṃ mūlamārādhanaṃ hareḥ  ViP yato dharmārthakāmākhyaṃ muktiścapi phalaṃ dvijāḥ tenāpi kiṅkimityevamanantena kimucyate  ViP kiṃ cāpi bahunoktena bhavanto guravo mama vadantu sādhu vāsādhu viveko smākam alpakaḥ  ViP bahunātra kimuktena sa eva jagataḥ patiḥ sa kartā ca vikartā ca saṃhartā ca hṛdi sthitaḥ  ViP sa bhoktā bhojyamapyevaṃ sa eva jagadīśvaraḥ bhavadbhir etatkṣantavyaṃ bālyāduktaṃ tu yanmayā  ViP purohitā ūcuḥdahyamānastvamasmābhir agninā bāla rakṣitaḥ bhūyo na vakṣyasītyevaṃ naiva jñātosyabuddhimān  ViP yadāsmadvacanānmohagrāhaṃ na tyakṣate bhavān tataḥ kṛtyāṃ vināśāya tava sṛkṣyāma durmate  ViP prahlāda uvācakaḥ kena hanyate jantur jantuḥ kaḥ kena rakṣyate hanti rakṣati caivātmā hyasatsādhu samācaran  ViP karmaṇā jāyate sarvaṃ karmaiva gatisādhanam tasmātsarvaprayatnena sādhu karma samācaret  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktāstena te kruddhā daityarājapurohitāḥ kṛtyāmutpādayāmāsurjvālāmālojjvalākṛtim  ViP atibhīmā samāgamya pādanyāsakṣatakṣitiḥ śulena sādhu saṃkruddhā taṃ jaghānāśu vakṣasi  ViP tattasya hṛdayaṃ prāpya śūlaṃ bālasya dīptimat jagāma khaṇḍitaṃ bhūmau tatrāpi śatadhā gatam  ViP yatrānapāyī bhagavān hṛdyāste haririśvaraḥ bhaṅgo bhavati vajrasya tatra śūlasya kā kathā  ViP āpāpe tatra pāpaiś ca pātitā daityāyājakaiḥ tāneva sā jaghānāśu kṛtyā nāśaṃ jagāma ca  ViP kṛtyayā dahyamānāṃstanvilokya sa mahāmatiḥ trāhi kṛṣṇetyananteti vadannabhyavapadyata  ViP prahlāda uvācasarvavyāpin jagadrūpa jagatstraṣṭarjanārdana pāhi viprānimānasmādduḥ sahānmantrapāvakāt  ViP yathā sarveṣu bhūteṣu sarvavyāpī jagadguruḥ viṣṇureva tathā sarve jīvantvete purohitāḥ  ViP yathā sarvagataṃ viṣṇuṃ manyamānonapāyinam cintayāmyaripakṣepi jīvantvete purohitāḥ  ViP ye hantumāgatā dattaṃ yorviṣaṃ yair hutāśanaḥ yair diggajair ahaṃ kṣuṇṇo daṣṭaḥ sarpaiś ca yair api  ViP teṣvahaṃ mitrabhāvena samaḥ pāposmi na kvacit yathā tenādya satyena jīvantvasurayājakāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktāstena te sarve saṃspṛṣṭāś ca nirāmayāḥ samuttasthurdvijā bhūyastamūcuḥ praśrayānvitam  ViP purohitā ūcuḥdīrghāyurapratihato balavīryasamanvitaḥ putrapautradhanaśvair yair yukto vatsa bhavottamaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā taṃ tato gatvā yathāvṛttaṃ purohitāḥ daityarājāya sakalamācacakhyurmahāmune  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathame ṃśe prahlādacārite ṣṭādaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācahiraṇyakaśipuḥ śrutvā tāṃ kṛtyāṃ vitathīkṛtām āhūya putraṃ papraccha prabhāvasyāsya kāraṇam  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācaprahlāda suprabhāvosi kimetatte viceṣṭitam etanmantrādijanitamutāho sahajaṃ tava  ViP śrīparāśara uvacāevaṃ pṛṣṭastadā pitrā prahlādo surabālakaḥ praṇipatya pituḥ pādāvidaṃ vacanamabravīt  ViP na mantrādikṛtaṃ tāta na ca naisargiko mama prabhāva eṣa sāmānyo yasya yasyācyuto hṛdi  ViP anyeṣāṃ yo na pāpāni cintayatyātmano yathā tasya pāpāgamastāta hetva bhāvānna vidyate  ViP karmaṇā manasā vāca paripīḍāṃ karoti yaḥ tadvījaṃ janma phalati prabhūtaṃ tasya cāśubham  ViP so haṃ na pāpa micchāmi na karomi vadāmi vā cintayansarvabhūtasthamātmanyapi ca keśavam  ViP śārīraṃ mānasaṃ duḥkhaṃ daivaṃ bhūtabhavaṃ tathā sarvatra śubhacittasya tasya me jāyeta kutaḥ  ViP evaṃ sarveṣu bhūteṣu bhaktiravyabhicāriṇī kartavyā paṇḍitair jñātvā sarvabhūtamayaṃ harim  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti śrutvā sa daityendraḥ prāsādaśikhare sthitaḥ krodhāndhakāritamukhaḥ prāha daiteyakiṅkarān  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācadurātmā kṣipyatāmasmātprāsādācchatayojanāt giripṛṣṭhe patatvasmin śilābhinnāṅgasaṃhatiḥ  ViP tatastaṃ cikṣupuḥ sarve bālaṃ daiteyadānavāḥ papāta so py adhaḥ kṣipto hṛdayenodvahahnarim  ViP patamānaṃ jagaddhātrī jagaddhātari keśave bhaktiyuktaṃ dadhārainamupasaṃgamyamaijinī  ViP tato vilokya taṃ svasthamaviśirṇasthipañjaram hiraṇyakaśipuḥ prāha śambaraṃ māyināṃ varam  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācanāsmābhiḥ śakyate hantumasau durbuddhibālakaḥ māyāṃ vetti bhavāṃstasmānmāyayainaṃ niṣūdaya  ViP śambara uvācasūdayāmyeva daityaindra paśya māyābalaṃ mama sahasramatra māyānāṃ paśya koṭiśataṃ tathā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ sa sasṛje māyāṃ prahlāde śambaro suraḥ vināśamicchandurbuddhiḥ sarvatra samadarśini  ViP samāhitamatirbhūtvā śambarepi vimatsaraḥ maitreya so pi prahlādaḥ sasmāra madhusūdanam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatato bhagavatā tasya rakṣārthaṃ cakramuttamam ājagāma samājñaptaṃ jvālāmāli sudarśanam  ViP tena māyāmahasraṃ tacchambarasyāśugāminā bālasya rakṣatā dehamekaikaṃ cāriśodhitam  ViP saṃśoṣakaṃ tathā vāyuṃ daityendrastvidamabravīt śīgrameṣa mamādeśāddurātmā nīyatāṃ kṣayam  ViP tathetyuktvā tu so py enaṃ viveśa pavano laghu śītotirukṣaḥ śoṣāya taddehasyātiduḥ sahaḥ  ViP tenāviṣṭamathātmānaṃ sa buddha datyabālakaḥ hṛdayena mahātmānaṃ dadhāra dharaṇīdharam  ViP hṛdayasthastatastasya taṃ vāyumati bhīṣaṇam papau janārdhanaḥ kruddhaḥ sa yayau pavanaḥ kṣayam  ViP kṣīṇāsu sarvamāyāsu pavane ca kṣayaṃ gate jagāma so pi bhavanaṃ kuroreva mahāmatiḥ  ViP ahanyahanyathācāryo nītiṃ rājyaphalapradām grāhayāmāsa taṃ bālaṃ rājñāmusanasā kṛtām  ViP gṛhītanītiśāstraṃ taṃ vinītaṃ ca yadā guruḥ mene tadainaṃ tatpitre kathayāmāsa śikṣitam  ViP ācārya uvācagṛhītanītiśāstraste putro daityapate kṛtaḥ prahlādastattvato vetti bhārgaveṇa yadīritam  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācamitreṣu varteta kathamarivargeṣu bhūpatiḥ prahlāda triṣu lokeṣu madhyastheṣu kathaṃ caret  ViP kathaṃ mantri ṣvamātyeṣu bāhyoṣvābhyantareṣu ca cāreṣu pauravargeṣu śaṅkiteṣvitareṣu ca  ViP kṛtyākṛtyavidhānañca durgāṭavikasādhanam prahlāda kathyatāṃ samyak tathā kaṇṭakaśodhanam  ViP etaccānyacca sakalamadhītaṃ bhavatā yathā tathā me kathyatāṃ jñātuṃ tavecchāmi manogatam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācapraṇipatya pituḥ pādau tadā praśrayabhūṣaṇaḥ prahlādaḥ prāha daityendraṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭas tathā  ViP prahlāda uvācamamo padiṣṭaṃ sakalaṃ gurumā nātra saṃśayaḥ gṛhītantu mayā kintu na sadetanmataṃmama  ViP sāma copapradānaṃ ca bhedadaṇḍau tathāparau upāyāḥ kathitāḥ sarve mitrādināṃ ca sādhane  ViP paramātmani govinde mitrādīṃstāta mā kruddhaḥ sādhyābhāve mahābāho sādhanaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  ViP sarvabhūtātmake tāta jagannāthe jaganmaye paramātmani govindai mitrādīṃstāta mā kruddhaḥ sādhyābhāve mahābāho sādhanaiḥ kiṃ prayojanam  ViP sarvabūtātmake tāta jagannāthe jaganmaye paramātmani govinde mitrāmitrakathā kutaḥ  ViP tvāyyasti bhagavān viṣṇurmayi cānyatra cāsti saḥ yatastatoyaṃ mitraṃ me śatruśceti pṛthaktutaḥ  ViP tad ebhir alam atyarthaṃ duṣṭārambhoktivistaraiḥ avidyāntargatair yatnaḥ kartavyastāta śobhene  ViP vidyābuddhiravidyāyāmajñānāntāta jāyate bālo gniṃ kiṃ na khadyotam asureśvara manyate  ViP tatkarma yan na bandhāya sā vidyā yā vimuktaye āyāsāyāparaṃ karma vidyānyā śilpanaipuṇam  ViP tadetadavagamyāhamasāraṃ sāramuttamam niśāmaya mahābhāga praṇipatya bravīmi te  ViP na cintayati ko rājyaṃ ko dhanaṃ nābhivāñchati tathāpi bhāvyamevaitadubhayaṃ prāpyate naraiḥ  ViP sarva eva mahābhāga mahattvaṃ prati sodyamāḥ tathāpi puṃsāṃ bhagyāni nodyamā bhūtihetavaḥ  ViP jaḍānāmavivekānāmaśūrāṇamapi prabho bhāgyabhojyāni rājyāni santyanītimatāmapi  ViP tasmādyateta puṇyeṣu ya icchenmahatīṃ śriyam yatitavyaṃ samatve ca nirvāṇamapi cecchatā  ViP devā manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ pakṣivṛkṣasarīsṛpāḥ rūpametadanantasya viṣṇor bhinnam iva sthitam  ViP etadvijānatā sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam draṣṭavyamātmavadviṣṇur yato yaṃ viśvarūpadhṛk  ViP evaṃ jñāte sa bhagavānanādiḥ parameśvaraḥ prasīdatyacyutastasminprasanne kleśasaṃkṣayaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaetacchrutvā tu kopena samutthāya varāsanāt hiraṇyakaśipuḥ putraṃ padā vakṣasyatāḍayat  ViP uvāca ca sa kopena sāmarṣaḥ prajyalanniva niṣpiṣya pāṇinā piṇiṃ hantukāmo jagadyathā  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācahe vipracitte he rāho he balaiṣa mahārṇave nāgāpāśair daḍhair baddhā kṣipyatāṃ mā vilaṃbyatām  ViP anyathā sakalā lokās tathā daiteyadānavāḥ anuyāsyanti mūḍhasya matamasya durātmanaḥ  ViP bahuśo vāri tosmābhir ayaṃ pāpastathāpyareḥ stutiṃ karoti duṣṭānāṃ vadha evopakārakaḥ  ViP parāśara uvācatataste satvarā daityā baddhā taṃ nāgabandhanaiḥ bharturājñāṃ puraskṛtya cikṣipuḥ salilārṇave  ViP tataścacāla calatā prahlādena mahārṇavaḥ udvelobhūtparaṃ kṣobhamupetya ca sama ntataḥ  ViP bhurlokamakhilaṃ dṛṣṭvā plāvyamānaṃ mahāmbhasā hiraṇyakaśipurdaityānidamāha māhamate  ViP hiraṇyakaśipur uvācadaiteyāḥ sakalaiḥ śailair atraiva varuṇālaye niśchidraiḥ sarvaśaḥ sarvaiś cīyatāmeṣa durmatiḥ  ViP nāgnirdahati naivāyaṃ śastraiś chinno na coragaiḥ kṣayaṃ nīto na vātena na viṣeṇa na kṛtyayā  ViP na māyābhir na caivoccatpātito na ca diggajaiḥ bālotiduṣṭacittoyaṃ nānenārthosti jīvatā  ViP tadeṣa toyamadhye tu samākrānto mahīdharaiḥ tiṣṭhatvabdasahasrāntaṃ prāṇānhāsyati durmatiḥ  ViP tato daityādānavāś ca parvatais taṃ mahodadhau ākramya cayanaṃ cakruryojanāni sahasraśaḥ  ViP sa citaḥ parvaterantaḥ samudrasya mahāmatiḥ tuṣṭāvāhnika velāyāmekāgramatiracyutam  ViP prahlā uvācanamaste puṇḍarīkākṣa namaste puruṣottama namaste sarvalokātmannamaste tigmacakriṇe  ViP namo brahmaṇyadevāya gobrāhmaṇahitāya ca jagaddhitāya kṛṣṇāya govindāya namonamaḥ  ViP brahmatve sṛjate viśvaṃ sthitau pālayate punaḥ rudrarūpāya kalpānte namastubhyaṃ trimūrtaye  ViP devā yakṣāḥ surāḥ siddhā nāgā gandharvakinnarāḥ piśācā rākṣasāścaiva manuṣyāḥ paśavas tathā  ViP pakṣiṇasthāvarāścaiva pipīlikasarīsṛpāḥ bhūmyāpognirnabhovāyuḥ śabdaḥ sparśas tathā rasaḥ  ViP rūpaṃ gandho mano buddhirātmā kālas tathā guṇāḥ eteṣāṃ paramārthaś ca sarvametattvamacyuta  ViP vidyāvidye bhavānsatyamasatyaṃ tvaṃ viṣāmṛte pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca karma vedoditaṃ bhavān  ViP samastakarmabhoktā ca karmopakaraṇāni ca tvameva viṣṇo sarvāṇi sarvakarmaphalaṃ ca yat  ViP mayyanyatra tathānyeṣu bhūteṣu bhuvaneṣu ca tavaivāvyāptiraiśvaryaguṇasaṃsūcikī prabho  ViP tvāṃ yoginaścintayanti tvāṃ yajanti ca yājakāḥ havyakavyabhugekastvaṃ pitṛdevasvarūpadhṛk  ViP rūpaṃ mahatte sthitamatra viśvaṃ tataś ca sūkṣmaṃ jagadetadīśa rūpāmi sarvāṇi ca bhūtabhedāsteṣvantarātmākhyamatīva sūkṣmam  ViP tasmācca sūkṣmādiviśeṣaṇānāmagocare yatparamātmarūpam kimapyacintyaṃ tava rūpamasti tasmai namaste puruṣottamāya  ViP sarvabhūteṣu sarvātmanyā śaktiraparā tava guṇāśrayā namastasyai śāśvatāyai sureśvara  ViP yātītagocarā vācāṃ manāsāṃ cāviśeṣaṇā jñānijñānaparicchedya tāṃ vande sveśvarīṃ parām  ViP oṃ namo vāsudevāya tasmai bhagavate sadā vyatiriktaṃ na yasyāsti vyatiriktokhilasya yaḥ  ViP namastasmai namastasmai namastasmai mahātmane nāma rūpaṃ na yasyaiko yostitvenopalabhyate  ViP yasyāvatārarūpāmi samarcanti divaukasaḥ apaśyantaḥ paraṃ rūpaṃ namastasmai mahātmane  ViP yontastiṣṭhannaśoṣasya paśyatīśaḥ śubhāśubham taṃ sarvasākṣiṇaṃ viśvaṃ namasye parameśvaram  ViP namostu viṣṇave tasmai yasyā bhinnamidaṃ jagat dhyeyaḥ sa jagatāmādyaḥ sa prasīdatu me vyayaḥ  ViP yatrotametatprotaṃ ca viśvamakṣaramavyayam ādhārabhūtaḥ sarvasya sa prasīdatu me hariḥ  ViP oṃ namo viṣṇave tasmai namastasmai punaḥ punaḥ yatra sarvaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ yaḥ sarvaṃ sarvasaṃśrayaḥ  ViP sarvagatvādanantasya sa evāhamavasthitaḥ mattaḥ sarvamahaṃ sarvaṃ mayi sarvaṃ sanātane  ViP ahamevākṣayo nityaḥ paramātmātmasaṃśrayaḥ brahmasaṃjño hamevāgre tathānte ca paraḥ pumān  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathameṃśa ekonaviṃśatitamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ saṃcintayanviṣṇumabhedenātmano dvija tanmayatvamavāpyagrya mene cātmānamacyutam  ViP visasmāra tathātmānaṃ nānyatkiñcidajānata ahamevāvyayo nantaḥ paramātmetyacintayat  ViP tasya tadbhāvanāyogātkṣīṇapāpasya vai kramāt śuddhentaḥkaraṇe viṣṇustasthau jñānamayocyutaḥ  ViP yogaprabhāvātprahlāde jāte viṣṇumaye sure calatyuragabandhais tair maitreya truṭitaṃ kṣaṇāt  ViP bhrantagrāhagamaḥ sormiryayau kṣobhaṃ mahārṇavaḥ cacāla ca mahī sarvā saśailavanakānanā  ViP sa ca taṃ śailasaṃghātaṃ daityair nyastamathopari utkṣipya tasmātsalilānniścakrāma mahāmatiḥ  ViP dṛṣṭvā ca sa jagadbhūyo gaganādyupalakṣaṇam prahlādosmīti sasmāra punarātmānamātmani  ViP tuṣṭāva ca punardhāmānanādiṃ puruṣottamam ekāgramatiravyagro yatavākvāyamānasaḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācaoṃnamaḥ paramārthāya sthūla sūkṣmakṣarākṣara vyaktāvyaktakalātīta sakaleśa nicañjana  ViP guṇāñjana guṇādhāra nirguṇātman guṇasthita mūrtāmūrtamahāmūrte sūkṣmamūrte sphuṭāsphuṭa  ViP karālasaumyarūpātmanvidyāvidyāmayācyuta sadasadrūpasadbhāva sadasadbhāvabhāvana  ViP nityānityaprapañcātmanniṣprapañcāmalāśrita ekāneka namastubhyaṃ vāsudevādikāraṇa  ViP yaḥ sthūlasūkṣmaḥ prakaṭaḥ prakāśo yaḥ sarvabhūto na ca sarvabhūtaḥ viśvaṃ yataścaitadaviśvaheto namostu tasmai puruṣottamāya  ViP parāśara uvācatasya taccetaso devaḥ stutimitthaṃ prakṛrvataḥ āvirbabhūva bhagavān pītāmbaradharo hariḥ  ViP sasambhramas tam ālokya samutthāyākulākṣaram namostu viṣṇavetyetavdyājahārāsa kṛddvija  ViP prahlāda uvācadeva prapannārtihara prasādaṃ kuru keśava avalokanadānena bhūyo māṃ pāvayācyuta  ViP śrībhagavān uvācakurvataste prasannohaṃ bhaktimavyabhicāriṇīm yathābhilaṣito mattaḥ prahlāda vrīyatāṃ varaḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācanātha yonisahasreṣu yeṣu yeṣu vrajāmy aham teṣu teṣvacyutābhaktiracyutāstu sadā tvayi  ViP yā prītiravivekānāṃ viṣayeṣvanapāyinī tvāmanusmarataḥ sā me hṛdayānmāpasarpatu  ViP śrībhagavānuvācamayi bhaktistavāstyeva bhūyo py evaṃ bhaviṣyati varastu mattaḥ prahlāda vrīyatāṃ yastavepsitaḥ  ViP prahlāda uvācamayi dveṣānubandhobhūtsaṃstutāvudyate tava matpitustatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ deva tasya pramaśyatu  ViP śastrāṇi pātitānyaṅge kṣipto yaccāgnisaṃhatau daṃśitaścoragair dattaṃ yadviṣaṃ mama bhojane  ViP baddhā samudre yatkṣipto yaccito smi śiloccayaiḥ anyāni cāpyasādhūni yāni pitrā kṛtāti me  ViP tvayi bhaktimato dveṣādaghaṃ tatsaṃbhavaṃ ca yat tvatprasādātprabho sadyastena mucyatu me pitā  ViP śrībhagavānuvācaprahlāda sarvametatte matprasādādbhāviṣyati anyacca te varaṃ daghni vrīyatāmasurātmaja  ViP prahalāda uvācakṛtakṛtyosmi bhagavanvare ṇānena yattvayi bhavitrī tvatprasādena bhaktiravyabhicāriṇī  ViP dharmārthakāmaiḥ kiṃ tasya muktistasya kare stitā samastajagatāṃ mūle yasya bhaktiḥ sthirā tvayi  ViP śrībhagavānuvācayathā te niścalaṃ ceto mayi bhaktisamanvitam tathā tvaṃ matprasādena nirvāṇamparamāpsyasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvāntardadhe viṣṇus tasya maitreya paśyataḥ sa cāpi punarāgamya vavande caraṇau pituḥ  ViP taṃ pitā mūrdhnyupāghrāya pariṣvajya ca pīḍitam jīvasītyāha vatseti bāṣpārdranayanodvija  ViP prītimāṃścābhavattasminnanutāpī mahāsuraḥ gurupitroścakāraivaṃ śuśrūṣāṃ so pi dharmatam  ViP pitaryuparatiṃ nīte narasiṃha svarūpiṇā viṣṇunā so pi daityānāṃ maitreyābhūtpatistataḥ  ViP tato rājyadyutiṃ prāpya karmaśuddhikarīṃ dvīja putrapautrāṃś ca subahūn avāpyaiśvaryameva ca  ViP kṣīṇādhikāraḥ sa yadā puṇyapāpavivirjitaḥ tadā sa bhagavaddhyānātparaṃ nīrvāṇamāppavān  ViP evaṃ prabhāvo daityo sau maitreyāsīn mahāmatiḥ prahlādo bhagavadbhakto yaṃ tvaṃ mām anupṛcchasi  ViP yastvetaccārītaṃ tasya prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ śṛṇoti tasya pāpāni sadyo gacchanti saṃkṣayam  ViP ahorātrakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ prahlādacaritaṃ naraḥ śṛṇvan paṭhaṃś ca maitreya vyapohati na saṃśayaḥ  ViP paurmamāsyāmamāvāsyāmaṣṭamyāmatha vā paṭhan dvādaśyāṃ tadāprantoti gopradānaphalaṃ dvija  ViP prahlādaṃ sakalāpatsu yathā rakṣitavānhariḥ tathā rakṣati yastasya śṛṇoti caritaṃ sadā  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe prathameṃśodhyāyaḥ prahlādaputra āyuṣmāñchibirbāṣkala eva ca virocanastu prāhladirbalirjajñe virocanāt  ViP baleḥ putraśataṃ tvasīdbāṇajyeṣṭhaṃ mahāmune hiraṇyākṣasutāścāsansarva eva mahā balā  ViP jharjharaḥ śakuniścaiva bhūtasantāpanas tathā mahānābho mahābāhuḥ kālanābhastathāparaḥ  ViP abhavandanupūtrāś ca dvimūrdha śaṃbaras tathā ayomukhaḥ śaṅkuśirāḥ kapilaḥ śaṅkaras tathā  ViP ekacakro mahābāhustārakaś ca mahābalaḥ svarbhānurvṛṣaparvā ca puloma ca mahābalaḥ  ViP ete danoḥ sutāḥ khyātā vipracittiś ca viryavān  ViP svarbhānostu prabhā kanyā śarmiṣṭhā vārṣaparvaṇī upadānī hayaśiraḥ prakhyātā varakanyakāḥ  ViP vaiśvānarasute cobhe pulomā kālakā tathā ubhe sute mahābhāge mārīcestu parigrahaḥ  ViP tābhyā putrasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭirdānavasattamāḥ paulomāḥ kālake yāś ca mārīcatanayāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP tato pare mahāvīryā dāruṇā stvatinirghṛṇā siṃhikāyāmathotpannā vipracitte sutās tathā  ViP tryaṃśaḥ śalyaś ca balavān nabhaścaiva mahābalaḥ vātāpī namuciścaiva ilvalaḥ khasṛmas tathā  ViP āndhako narakaścaiva kālanābhastathaiva ca svarbhānuś ca mahāvīryo vaktrayodhī mahāsuraḥ  ViP ete vai dānavāḥ śreṣṭhā danuvaṃśavivardhanāḥ eteṣāṃ putrapautraś ca śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ  ViP prahlādasya tu daityasya nivāta kavacāḥ kule samutpannāḥ sumahatā tapasā bhāvitātmanaḥ  ViP ṣaṭ sutāḥ sumahāsattvāstāmrāyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ śukī śyenī ca bhāsī ca sugrīvī śucigṛddhrakā  ViP śukī śukānajanayadulūkapratyulūkikān śyenī śyenāṃs tathā bhāsī bhāsāngṛrdhyāṃś ca gṛddhryapi  ViP śucyau dakānpakṣigaṇānsugrīvī tu vyajāyata aśvānuṣṭrāngardabhāṃ ś ca tāmrāvaṃśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  ViP vinatāyāstu dvau putrau viratau garuḍāruṇau suparṇaḥ patatāṃ śreṣṭho dāruṇaḥ pannagāśanaḥ  ViP surasāyāṃ sahasraṃ tu sarpāṇāmamitaujasām anekaśirasāṃ brahman khecarāmāṃ mahātmanām  ViP kāndraveyāstu balinaḥ sahasramamitaujasaḥ suparṇavaśāgā brahman jajñire naikamastakāḥ  ViP teṣāṃ pradhānabhūtāstu śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ śaṅkhaśveto mahāpadmaḥ kambalāśvatarau tathā  ViP elāputras tathā nāgaḥ karkoṭakadhanañjayau ete cānye ca bahavo dandaśukā viṣolbaṇā  ViP gaṇaṃ krodhavaśaṃ viddhi tasyāḥ sarve ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ sthalajāḥ pakṣiṇobjāś ca dāruṇāḥ piśitāśanāḥ  ViP krodhāttu piśācāṃś ca janayāmāsa mahābalān gāstu vai janayāmāsa surābhīrmahiṣīs tathā irāvṛkṣalatāvallīstṛmajatīś ca sarvaśaḥ  ViP svasā tu yakṣarakṣāṃsi munirapsarasas tathā ārīṣṭā tu mahāsattvān gandharvānsamajījanat  ViP ete kaśyapadāyādāḥ kīrtitāḥ sthāṇujaṅgamāḥ teṣāṃ putrāś ca pautrāś ca śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ  ViP eṣa manvantare sargo brahmansvārociṣesmṛtaḥ  ViP vaivasvate ca mahati vāruṇe vitate kṛtau juhvānasya brahmaṇo vai prajāsarga ihocyate  ViP pūrvaṃ yatra tu saptarṣinutpannānsaptamānasān putratve kalpayāmāsa svayameva pitāmahaḥ gandharvabhogidevānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca sattama  ViP ditirvinaṣṭaputrā vai toṣayāmāsa kāśyapam tayā cārādhitaḥ samyakkāśyapastapatāṃ paraḥ  ViP vareṇa cchandayāmāsa sā ca vavre tato varam putramindravadhārthāya samarthama mitaujasam  ViP sa ca tasmai varaṃ prādādbhāryāyai munisattamaḥ dattvā ca varamatyugraṃ kaśyapastāmuvāca ha  ViP śakraṃ putro nihantā te yadi garbhaṃ śaracchatam samāhitātiprayatā śaucinī dhārayiṣyasi  ViP ityevasuktvā tāṃ devīṃ saṃgataḥ kaśyapo muniḥ dadhāra sā ca taṃ garbhaṃ samyakchocasamanvitā  ViP garbhamātmavadhārthāya jñātvā taṃ maghavānapi śuśrūṣustāmathāgacchadvinayādamarādhipaḥ  ViP tasyā ścaivāntaraprepsuratiṣṭhatpākaśāsanaḥ ūne varṣaśate cāsyā dadarśāntaramātmanā  ViP akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucaṃ ditiḥ śayanamāviśat nidrāṃ cāhārayāmāsa tasyāḥ kukṣiṃ praviśya saḥ  ViP vajrapāṇirmahāgarbhaṃ cicchedātha sa saptadhā sampīḍyamāno pajreṇa sa rurodādidāruṇam  ViP mā rodīriti taṃ śakraḥ punaḥpunarabhāṣata so bhavatsaptadhā garbhastamidraḥ kupitaḥ punaḥ  ViP ekaikaṃ saptadhā cakre vajreṇārividāriṇā maruto nāma devāste babhūvurativeginaḥ  ViP yaduktaṃ vai bhagavatā tenaiva maruto bhavan devā ekonapachcāśatsahāyā vajrapāṇinaḥ  ViP iti śriviṣṇupurāme prathamaiṃśa ekaviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācayadābhiṣiktaḥ sa pṛthuḥ pūrvaṃ rājye maharṣibhiḥ tataḥ krameṇa rājyāni dadau lokapitāmahaḥ  ViP nakṣatragrahaviprāṇāṃ vīrudhāṃ cāpyaśeṣataḥ somaṃ rājye dadhadbrahma yajñānāṃ tapasāmapi  ViP rājñāṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ rājye jalānāṃ varuṇaṃ tathā ādityānāṃ patiṃ viṣṇuṃ vasūnāmatha pāvakam  ViP prajāpatīnāṃ dakṣaṃ tu vāsavaṃ marutāmapi daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca prahlādamadhipaṃ dadau  ViP pitṝṇāṃ dharmarājānaṃ yamaṃ rājye bhyaṣecayat airāvataṃ garjedrāṇāmaśoṣāṇāṃ patiṃ dadau  ViP patatriṇāṃ tu guruḍaṃ devānāmapi vāsavam uccaiḥśravasamaśvānāṃ vṛṣabhaṃ tu gavāmapi  ViP mṛgāṇāṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ rājye siṃhaṃ dadau prabhuḥ śeṣaṃ tu dandaśūkānāmakarotpatimavyayaḥ  ViP himālayaṃ sthāvaraṇāṃ munīnāṃ kapilaṃ munim nakhināṃ deṣṭriṇāṃ caiva mṛgāṇāṃ vyāghramīśvaram  ViP vanaspatīnāṃ rājāneḥ plakṣamaivābyaṣecayat evamevānyajātīnāṃ prādhānyenākarotprabhūn  ViP evaṃ vibhajya rājyāni diśāṃ pālānanantaram prajāpatipatirbrahmā sthāpayāmāsa sarvataḥ  ViP pūrvasyāṃ diśi rājānaṃ vairājasya putramacyutam ketumantaṃ mahātmānaṃ rājānaṃ so bhyaṣaicayat  ViP tathā hiraṇyaromāṇaṃ parjanyasya prajāpateḥ udīcyāṃ diśi durdharṣaṃ rājānamabhyaṣecayat  ViP tair iyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā yathāpradeśamadyāpi dharmataḥ paripālyate  ViP ete sarve pravṛttasya sthitau viṣṇormahātmanaḥ vibhūtibhūtā rājāno ye cānye munisattama  ViP ye bhaviṣyanti ye bhūtāḥ sarve bhūteśvarā dvija te sarve sarvabhūtasya viṣṇoraṃśā dvijottama  ViP ye tu devādhipatayo ye ca daityādhipās tathā dānavānāṃ ca ye nāthā ye nāthāḥ piśitāśinām  ViP paśunāṃ ye ca patayaḥ patayo ye ca pakṣiṇām manuṣyāṇāṃ ca sarpāṇāṃ nāgānāmadhipāś ca ye  ViP vṛkṣāṇāṃ parvatānāṃ ca grahāṇāṃ cāpi ye dhipāḥ atītā vartamānāś ca ye bhaviṣyanti cāpare te sarve sarvabhūtasya viṣṇoraṃśasamudbhāvāḥ  ViP na hi pālanasāmarthyamṛte sarveśvaraṃ harim sthitaṃ sthitau mahāprājña bhavatyanyasya kasyacit  ViP sṛjatyeṣa jagatsṛṣṭau sthitau pāti sanātanaḥ hanti caivāntakatvena rajaḥsattvādisaṃśrayaḥ  ViP caturvibhāgaḥ saṃsṛṣṭau caturdhā saṃsthitaḥ sthitau pralayaṃ ca karotyante caturbhedo janārdanaḥ  ViP ekenāṃśena brahmasau bhavatyavyaktamūrtimān marīcimiśrāḥ patayaḥ prajānāñcānyabhāgaśaḥ  ViP kālastṛtīyastasyāṃśaḥ sarvabhūtāni cāparaḥ itthaṃ caturdhā saṃsṛṣṭau vartatesau rajoguṇaḥ  ViP ekāṃśenāsthito viṣṇuḥ karoti pratipālanam manvādirūpaścānyena kālarūpo paroṇa ca  ViP sarvabhūteṣu cānyena saṃśthitaḥ kurute sthitim sattvaṃ guṇaṃ samāśritya jagataḥ puruṣottamaḥ  ViP āśritya tamaso vṛttimantakāle tathā punaḥ rudrasvarūpo bhagavānekāṃśena bhavatyajaḥ  ViP agnyantakādirūpeṇa bhāgenānyena vartate kālasvarūpo bhāgo yaḥsarvabhūtāni cāparaḥ  ViP vināśaṃ kurvatastasya caturdhaivaṃ mahātmanaḥ vibhāgakalpanā brahman kathyate sārvakālikī  ViP brahma dakṣādayaḥ kālastathai vākhilajantavaḥ vibhūtayo hareretā jagataḥ sṛṣṭihetavaḥ  ViP viṣṇurmanvādayaḥ kālaḥ sarvabhūtāni ca dvija sthiternimittabhūtasya viṣṇoretā vibhūtayaḥ  ViP rudraḥ kālāntakādyāś ca samastāścaiva jantavaḥ caturdhā pralāyāyaitā janārdanavibhūtayaḥ  ViP jagadādau tathā madhye sṛṣṭirāpralayā dvija dhātrā marīcimiśraiś ca kriyate jantubhis tathā  ViP brahma sṛjatyādikāle marīcipramukhāstataḥ utpādayantyapatyāni jantavaś ca pratikṣaṇam  ViP kālena na vinā brahma sṛṣṭiniṣpādako dvija na prajāpatayaḥ sarve na caivākhilajantavaḥ  ViP evameva vibhāgoyaṃ stitāvapyupadiśyati caturdā tasya devasya maitreya pralaye tathā  ViP yatkiñcitsṛjyate yena sattvajātena vai dvija tasya sṛjyasya sambhūto tatsarvaṃ vai harestanuḥ  ViP hanti yāvacca yatkiñcitsattvaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam janārdanasya tadraudraṃ maitreyāntakaraṃ vatuḥ  ViP evameṣa jagatstraṣṭā jagatpātā tathā jagat jagadbhakṣayitā devaḥ samastasya janārdanaḥ  ViP sṛṣṭhisthityantakāleṣu tridhaivaṃ saṃpravartate guṇapravṛtyā paramaṃ padaṃ tasyāguṇaṃ mahat  ViP tacca jñānamayaṃ vyāpi svāsaṃvedyamanaupamam catuṣprakāraṃ tadapi svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācacatuḥprakāratāṃ tasya brahmabhūtasya he mune mamācakṣva yathānyāyaṃ yaduktaṃ paramaṃ padam  ViP śrīparāsara uvācamaitreya kāraṇaṃ proktaṃ sādhanaṃ sarvavastuṣu sādhyaṃ ca vastvabhimataṃ yatsādhayitumātmanaḥ  ViP yogino muktikāmasya prāṇāyāmādisādhanam sādhyaṃ ca paramaṃ brahma punarnavartateyataḥ  ViP sādhanālambanaṃ jñānaṃ muktaye yogināṃ hi yat sa bhedaḥ prathamastasya brahmabhūtasya vai mune  ViP yuñjataḥ kleśamuktyarthaṃ sādhyaṃ yadbrahma yoginaḥ tadālambanavijñānaṃ dvitīyo ṃśo mahāmune  ViP ubhayostvavibhāgena sādhyasādhanayorhi yat vijñānamadvaitamayaṃ tadbhāgonyo mayoditaḥ  ViP jñānatrayasya vai tasya viśeṣo yo mahāmune tannirākaraṇadvārā darśitātmasvarūpavat  ViP nirvyāpāramanākhyeyaṃ vyāptimātramanūpamam ātmasambodhaviṣayaṃ sattāmātramalakṣaṇam  ViP praśāntamabhayaṃ śuddhaṃ durvibhāvyamasaṃśrayam viṣṇorjñānamayasyoktaṃ tajjñānaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam  ViP tatra jñānanirodhena yogino yānti ye layam saṃsārakarṣaṇoptau te yānti nirbījatāṃ dvijā  ViP evaṃprakāramamalaṃ nityaṃ vyāpakamakṣayam samastaheyarahitaṃ viṣṇvākhyaṃ paramaṃ padam  ViP tadbrahma paramaṃ yogī yato nāvartate punaḥ śrayatyapuṇyoparame kṣīṇakleśe tinirmale  ViP dve rūpe brahmaṇastasya mūrta cāmūrtameva ca kṣarākṣarāsvarūpe te sarvabhūteṣvavasthite  ViP akṣaraṃ tatparaṃ brahma kṣaraṃ sarvamidaṃ jagat ekadeśasthitasyāgnerjyotstrā vistāriṇi yathā parasya brahmaṇaḥ śaktistathodamakhilaṃ jagat  ViP tatrāpyāsannadūratvād bahutvasvalpatāmayaḥ jyotsnābhedosti tacchaktestadvanmaitreya vidyate  ViP bahmaviṣṇuśivā brahmanpradhānā brahmaśaktayaḥ tataś ca devā maitreya nyūnā dakṣādayastataḥ  ViP tato manuṣyāḥ paśavau mṛgapakṣisarīsṛpāḥ nyūnānyūnatarāścaiva vṛkṣagulmādayas tathā  ViP tadetadakṣaraṃ nityaṃ jaganmunivarākhitam āvirbhāvatirobhāvajanmanāśavikalpavat  ViP sarvaśakti mayo viṣṇuḥ svarūpaṃ brahmaṇaḥ param mūrtaṃ yadyogibhiḥ purvaṃ yogārambheṣu cintyate  ViP sālambano mahāyogaḥ sabījo yatrasaṃsthitaḥ manasyavyāhate samyagyuñjatāṃ jāyate mune  ViP sa paraḥ paraśaktīnāṃ brahmaṇaḥ samanantaram mūrtaṃ brahma mahābhāga sarvabrahmamayo hariḥ  ViP yatra sarvamidaṃ protamotaṃ caivākhitaṃ jagat tato jagajjagatyasminsa jagaccakhilaṃ mune  ViP kṣarākṣaramayo viṣṇurbibhartyakhilamīśvaraḥ puruṣāvyākṛtamayaṃ bhūṣaṇāstrasvarūpavat  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācabhūṣaṇāstrasvarūpasthaṃ yaccaitadakhilaṃ jagat bibharti bhagavanviṣṇu stanmamākhyātumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācanamaskṛtvāprameyāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave kathayāmi yathākhyātaṃ vasiṣṭhena mamā bhavat  ViP ātmānamasya jagato nirlepamaguṇāmalam bibharti kaustubhamaṇisvarūpaṃ bhagavānhariḥ  ViP śrīvatsasaṃsthānadhara manante na samāśritam pradhānaṃ buddhirapyāste gadarūpeṇa mādhave  ViP bhūtādimindriyādiṃ ca dvidhāhaṅkāramīśvaraḥ bibharti śaṃkharūpeṇa śārṅgarūpeṇa ca sthitam  ViP calatsvarūpamatyantaṃ javenāntāritānilam cakrasvarūpaṃ ca mano dhatte viṣṇukare sthitam  ViP pañcarūpā tu yā mālā vaijayantī gadābhṛtaḥ sā bhūtahetusaṃghātā bhūtamālā ca vai dvija  ViP yānīndriyāṇyaśeṣāṇi buddhikarmātmakāni vai śararūpāṇyaśeṣāṇi tāni dhatte janārdanaḥ  ViP bibharti yaccāsiratnamacyutotyantanirmalam vidyāmaya tu tajjñānamavidyākośasaṃsthitam  ViP itthaṃ pumānpradhānaṃ ca buddhyahaṅkārameva ca bhūtāni ca hṛṣīkeśe manaḥ sarvendriyāṇi ca vidyāvidye ca maitreya sarvametatsamāśritam  ViP astrabhūṣaṇasaṃsthānasvarūpaṃ rūpavarjitaḥ bibhārti māyārūposau śreyase prāṇināṃ hariḥ  ViP savikāraṃ pradhānaṃ ca pumāṃścaivākhilaṃ jagat bibharti puṇḍahīkākṣastadevaṃ parameśvaraḥ  ViP yā vidyā yā tathāvidyā yatsadyaccāsadavyayam tatsarvaṃ sarvabhūteśe maitreya madhusūdane  ViP kalākāṣṭhānimeṣādidinartvayanahāyanaiḥ kālasvarūpo bhagavānapāpo hariravyayaḥ  ViP bhūrlokotha bhuvarlokaḥ svarloko munisattama maharjanastapaḥ satyaṃ sapta lokā ime vibhuḥ  ViP lokātmamūrtiḥ sarveṣāṃ pūrveṣāmapi pūrvajaḥ ādhāraḥ sarvavidyānāṃ svayameva hariḥ sthitaḥ  ViP devamānuṣapaśvādiśvarūpair bahubhiḥ sthitaḥ tataḥ sarveśvaro nanto bhūtamūrtiramūrtimān  ViP ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni tathaivātharvāṇāni vai itihāsopavedāś ca vedānteṣu tathoktayaḥ  ViP vedāṅgāni samastāni manvādigaditāni ca śāstrāṇyaśeṣāṇyākhyānāny anuvākāś ca ye kvacit  ViP kāvyālāpāś ca ye kecidrītakānyakhilāni ca śabdamūrtidharasyaitad vapurviṣṇor mahātmanaḥ  ViP yāni mūrtāny amūrtāni yānyatrānyatra vā kvacit santi vai vastujātāni tāni sarvāṇi tadvapuḥ  ViP ahaṃ hariḥ sarvamidaṃ janārdano nānyattataḥ kāraṇakāryajātam īdṛṅmano yasya na tasyaṭa bhūyo bhavodbhāvā dvandvagadā bhavanti  ViP ityaiṣa teṃśaḥ prathamaḥ purāṇasyāsya vai dvija yathāvatkathito yasmindhṛte pāpaiḥ pramucyate  ViP kārttikyāṃ puṣkarasnāne dvādaśābdena yatphalam tadasya śravaṇātsava maitreyāpnoti mānavaḥ  ViP devarṣipitṛgandharvayakṣādināṃ ca sambhavam bhavanti śṛṇvataḥ puṃso devādya varadā mune  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe prathame ṃśe dvāviṃśo dhyāyaḥiti śrīparāśaramuniviracite śriviṣṇuparatvanirṇāyake śrīmati viṣṇumahāpurāṇe prathamāṃśaḥ samāptaḥ atha śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhyaśrīdharīya vyākhyādvayopete dvitīyoṃśaḥ prārabhyateśrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥmaitreya uvācabhagavansamyagākhyātaṃ mamaitadakhilaṃ tvāyā jagataḥ sargasambandhi yatpṛṣṭosi guro mayā  ViP yoyamaṃśo jagatsṛṣṭisambandho gaditastvayā tatrāhaṃ śrotumicchāmi bhūyopi munisattama  ViP priyavratottānapādau sutau svāyambhuvasya yau tayoruttānapādasya dhruvaḥ putrastvayoditaḥ  ViP priyavratasya naivoktā bhavatā dvija santatiḥ tāmahaṃ śrotumicchāmi prasanno vaktumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācakardamasyātmajāṃ kanyāmupayeme prayivrataḥ samrāṭ kukṣi ca tatkanye daśaputrastathāpare  ViP mahāprajñā mahāvīryā vinītā dayitāḥ pituḥ priyavratasutāḥ khyātāsteṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP āgnīdhraścāgnibāhuś ca vapuṣmāndyutimāṃs tathā medhā medhātithirbhavyaḥ savanaḥ putra eva ca  ViP jyotiṣmāndaśamasteṣāṃ satyanāmā suto bhavat priyavratasya putrāste prakhyātā balavīryataḥ  ViP medhāgnibāhuputrāstu trayo yogaparāyaṇāḥ jātismārā mahābhāgāna rājyāya mano dadhuḥ  ViP nirmalāḥ sarvakālantu samastārtheṣu vai mune cakruḥ kriyāṃ yathānyāyamaphalākākṣiṇo hi te  ViP priyavrato dadau teṣāṃ saptānāṃ munisattama saptadvīpāni maitreya vibhajya sumahātmanām  ViP jambūdvīpe mahābhāga sognīdhrāya dadau pitā medhātithes tathā prādātplakṣadvīpaṃ tathāparam  ViP śālmale ca vapuṣmantaṃ narendramabhiṣiktavān jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśadvīpe rājānaṃ kṛtāvānprabhuḥ  ViP dyutimantaṃ ca rājānaṃ krauñcadvīpe samādiśat śākadvīpeśvaraṃ cāpi bhavyaṃ cakre priyavrataḥ  ViP puṣkarādhipatiṃ cakre savanaṃ cāpi sa prabhuḥ jambūdvīpeśvaro yastu āgnīdhro munisattama  ViP tasya putrā babhūvuste prajāpatisamā nava nābhiḥ kiṃpuruṣaścaiva harivarṣa ilāvṛtaḥ  ViP ramyo hiraṇvānṣaṣṭhaś ca kurubhadrāśva eva ca ketumālastathaivānyaḥ sādhuceṣṭo bhavantṛpaḥ  ViP janbūdvīpavi bhāgāṃś ca teṣāṃ vipra niśāmaya pitrā dattaṃ himāhvaṃ tu varṣaṃ nābhestu dakṣiṇam  ViP hemakūṭaṃ tathā varṣaṃ dadau kiṃpuruṣāya saḥ tṛtīyaṃ naiṣadhaṃ varṣaṃ harivarṣāya dattavān  ViP ilāvṛtāya pradadau meruryatra tu madhyamaḥ nīlācalāśritaṃ varṣa ramyāya pradadau pitā  ViP śvetaṃ yaduttaraṃ tasmātpitrā dattaṃ hiraṇvate  ViP yaduttaraṃ śṛṅgavato varṣa tatkurave dadau meroḥ purveṇa yadvarṣa bhadrāśvāya pradattavān  ViP gandhamādhanavarṣa tu ketumālāya dattavān ityetāni dadau tebhyaḥ putrebhyaḥ sa nareśvaraḥ  ViP varṣeṣveteṣu tānputrānabhiṣicya sa bhūmipaḥ sālāgrāmaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ maitreya tapase yayau  ViP yani kiṃpuruṣādīti varṣāvyaṣṭau mahāmune teṣāṃ svābhāviki siddhiḥ sukhaprāyā hyayatnataḥ  ViP viparyayo na teṣvasti jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ na ca dharmadhamau na teṣvāstāṃ nottamādhamamadhyamāḥ  ViP na teṣvasti yugāvasthā kṣetreṣvaṣṭasu sarvadā himāhvayaṃ tu vai varṣaṃ nāberāsīnmahātmanaḥ tasyarṣabho bhavatputro merudevyāṃ mahādyutiḥ  ViP ṛṣabhādbhārato jajñe jyeṣṭhaḥ putraśatasya saḥ kṛtvā rājyaṃ svadharmeṇa tathaiṣṭvā vividhānmakhān  ViP abhiṣicya sutaṃ vīraṃ bharataṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ tapase sa mahābhāgaḥ pulahasyāśramaṃ yayau  ViP vānaprasthavidhānena tatrāpi kṛtaniścayaḥ tapastepe yathānyāyamiyāja sa mahīpatiḥ  ViP tapasā karṣitotyarthaṃ kṛśo dhamanisantataḥ nagno vīṭāṃ mukhe kṛtvā vīrādhvānaṃ tato gataḥ  ViP tataś ca bhārataṃ varṣametallokeṣu gīyate bharatāya yataḥ pitrā dattaṃ prātiṣṭhatā vanam  ViP sumatīrbharatasyābhūtputraḥ paramadhārmikaḥ kṛtvā samyagdadau tasmai rājyamiṣṭamakhaṃ pitā  ViP putrasaṃkrāmita śrīstu bharataḥ sa mahīpatiḥ yogābhyāsarataḥ prāṇānsālagrāme yajanmune  ViP ajāyata ca viprosau yogīnāṃ pravare kule maitreya tasya caritaṃ kathayiṣyāmi te punaḥ  ViP mumatestejasastasmādindradyumno vyajāyata parameṣṭhī tatastasmātpratihārastadanvayaḥ  ViP pratiharteti vikhyāta utpannastasya cātmajaḥ bhavastasmādathodgīthaḥ prāstavistatsuto vibhuḥ  ViP pṛthustatastato nakto naktasyāpi gayaḥ sutaḥ naro gayasya natayastatputrobhūdvirāṭ tataḥ  ViP tasya putro mahāvīryo dhīmāṃstasmādajāyata mahāntastatsutaścābhūnmanasyustasya cātmajaḥ  ViP tpaṣṭā tvaṣṭuś ca virajo rajastasyāpyabhūtsutaḥ śatajidrajasastasya jajñe putraśanta mune  ViP viṣvagjyotipradhānāste yair imā vardhitāḥ prajāḥ tair idaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ navabhedamalaṅkṛtam  ViP teṣāṃ vaṃśaprasūtaiś ca bhukteyaṃ bhāratī purā kṛtatretādisargeṇa yugākhyāmekasaptatim  ViP eṣa svāyaṃbhuvaḥ sargau yenedaṃ pūritaṃ jagat vārāhe tu mune kalpe pūrvamanvantarādhipaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇupurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe prathamo dhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācakathito bhavatā brahmansargaḥ svāyambhuvaś ca me śrotumicchāmyahaṃ tvattaḥ sakalaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhuvaḥ  ViP yāvantaḥ sāgara dvīpās tathā varṣāṇi parvatāḥ vanāni satitaḥ puryo devādīnāṃ tathā mune  ViP yatpramāṇamidaṃ sarvaṃ yadādhāraṃ yadātmakam saṃsthānamasya ca mune yathābadvaktumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācamaitreya śrūyatāmetatsaṃkṣepādgadato mama nāsya varṣaśatenāpi vaktuṃ śakyo hi vistaraḥ  ViP jambūplakṣāhvayau dvīpau śālmaliścāparo dvija kuśaḥ kraiñcas tathā śākaḥ puṣkaraścaiva saptamaḥ  ViP ete dvīpāḥ samudrais tu saptasaptabhir āvṛtāḥ lavaṇekṣusurāsarpirdadhigugdhajalaiḥ samam  ViP praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastāddvātriṃśanmūrdhri vistṛta mūle ṣoḍaśasāhasro vistārastasya sarvaśaḥ  ViP bhūpadmasyāsya śailosau karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ  ViP himāvānhemakūṭaś ca viṣadhaścasya dakṣiṇe nīlaḥ śvetaś ca śṛṅgī ca uttare varṣaparvatāḥ  ViP lakṣapramāṇo dvau madhyau daśahīnāstathāpare sahasradvitayocchrāyās tāvadvistāriṇaś ca te  ViP bhārataṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ tataḥ kipuruṣaṃ smṛtam harivarṣaṃ tathaivānyanmerordakṣiṇato dvija  ViP ramyakaṃ cottaraṃ varṣaṃ tasyaivānu hiraṇmayam uttarāḥ kuravaścaiva yathā vai bhārataṃ tathā  ViP navasāhasramaikaikam eteṣāṃ dvijasattama ilāvṛtaṃ ca tanmadhye sauvarṇo merurucchritaḥ  ViP meroścaturdiśaṃ tattu navasāhasravistṛtam ilāvṛtaṃ mahābhāga catvāraścātra parvatāḥ  ViP viṣkaṃbhāracitā meroryojanāyutamucchritaḥ navaiḥ sarobhiś ca samaṃ dikṣvete keśavācalāḥ  ViP purveṇa mandaro nāma dakṣiṇe gandhamādanaḥ viplalaḥ paścime pārśve mupārśvaścottara smṛtaḥ  ViP kadambasteṣu jambūś ca pippalo vaṭa eva ca ekādaśaśatāyāmāḥ pādapā giriketavaḥ  ViP jambūdvīpasya sā jambūr nāmahetur mahāmune mahāgajapramāmāni jambvāstasyāḥ phalani vai patanti bhūbhṛtaḥ pṛṣṭhe śīryamāṇāni sarvataḥ  ViP rasena teṣāṃ prakhyātā tatra jāmbūnadīti vai saritpravartate cāpi pīyate tannivāsibhiḥ  ViP na svedo na ca daurgandhyaṃ na jarā nendriyakṣayaḥ tatpānātsvacchamanāsāṃjanānāṃ tatra jāyate  ViP tīramṛttadrasaṃ prāpya sukhavāyuviśoṣitā jāmbūnadākhyaṃ bhavati suvarṇaṃ siddhabhūṣaṇam  ViP bhadrāśvaṃ pūrvato meroḥ ketumālaṃ ca paścime varṣe dve tu muniśreṣṭha tayormadhyamilāvṛtaḥ  ViP vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ pūrve dakṣiṇe gandhamādanam vaibhrājaṃ paścime tadvaduttare nandanaṃ smṛtam  ViP aruṇodaṃ mahābhadramasitodaṃ samānasam sarāṃsyotāni catvāri devabhogyāni sarvadā  ViP śītāmbhaś ca kumundaś ca kurarī mālyavāṃs tathā vaikaṅkaprasukhā meroḥ pūrvataḥ kesarācalāḥ  ViP trikūṭaḥ śiśiraścaiva pataṅgo rucakas tathā niṣadādyā dakṣiṇatastasya kesaraparvataḥ  ViP śikhivāsāḥ savaiḍūryaḥ kapilo gandhamādanaḥ jārudhipramukhāstadvat paścime kesarācalāḥ  ViP meror anantarāṅgeṣu jaṭharādiṣvavasthitāḥ śaṃśakūṭotha ṛṣabho haṃso nāgas tathā paraḥ kālañjanādyāś ca tathā uttare kesarācalāḥ  ViP caturdaśasahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ mahāpurī merorupari maitreya brahmaṇaḥ prathitā divi  ViP tasyāḥsamantataścāṣṭau diśāsu vidiśāsu ca indrādilokapālānāṃ prakhyātāḥ pravarāḥ puraḥ  ViP viṣṇupādaviniṣkrāntā plāvayitvendumaṇḍalam samantādbrahyaṇaḥ puryāṃ gaṅga patati vai divaḥ  ViP sā tatra patitā dikṣu caturdhā pratipadyate sītā cālakanandā ca cakṣurbhadrā ca vai kramāt  ViP pūrveṇa śailācchītā tu śailaṃ yātyantarīkṣagā tataś ca pūrvavarṣaiṇa bhadrāśvainaiti sārṇavam  ViP tathaivālakanandāpi dakṣiṇenaitya bhāratam prayāti sāgaraṃ bhūtvā saptabhedā mahāmune  ViP cakṣuścaṃ paścimagirīnatītya sakalāṃstataḥ paścimaṃ ketumālākhya varṣaṃ gatvaiti sāgaram  ViP bhadrā tathottaragirīnuttarāṃś ca tathā kurūn atītyottaramambhodhiṃ samabhyeti mahāmune  ViP ānīlaniṣadhāyāmau mālyavadgandhamādanau tayormadhyagato merūḥ karṇikākārasaṃsthitaḥ  ViP bhāratāḥ ketumālāś ca bhadrāśvāḥ kuravas tathā patrāṇi lokapadmasya maryādāśailabāhyataḥ  ViP jaṭharo hemakūṭaś ca maryādāparvatāvubhau tau dakṣimottarāyāmāvānīlaniṣadhāyatau  ViP gandhamādanakailāsau pūrvavaccāyatāvubhau āśīti yojanāyāmāvarṇavāntavyavasthitau  ViP niṣadhaḥ pariyātraś ca maryādāparvatāvubhau meroḥ paścimadigbhāge yathā pūrve tathā sthitau  ViP triśṛṅgo jārudhiścaiva uttarau varṣaparvatau pūrvapaścāyatāvetāvarṇavāntarvyavasthitau  ViP ityete munivaryoktā maryādāparvatāstava jaṭharādyāḥ sthitā merosteṣāṃ dvaudvau caturdiśam  ViP mero ścaturdiśaṃ yetu proktāḥ kesaraparvatāḥ śītāntādyā mune teṣāmatīva hi manoramāḥ śailānāmantare droṇyaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitāḥ  ViP suramyāṇi tathā tāsu kānanāni purāṇi ca lakṣmīviṣṇvagnisūryādidevānāṃ muni sattama tāsvāyatanavaryāṇi juṣṭāni varakinnaraiḥ  ViP gandharvayakṣarakṣāṃsi tathā daiteyadānavāḥ krīḍanti tāsu ramyāsu śailadroṇīṣvaharnisam  ViP bhaumā hyete smṛtāḥ svargā dharmiṇāmālayā mune naituṣu pāpakarmāṇo yānti janmaśatair api  ViP bhadrāśve bhagavānviṣṇurāste hayaśirā dvija varājaḥ ketumāle tu bhārate kūrmarūpadhṛk  ViP matsyarūpaś ca govindaḥ kuruṣvāste janārdanaḥ viśvarūpeṇa sarvatra sarvaḥ sarvatrago hariḥ  ViP sarvasyādhārabhūtosau maitreyāstekhilātmakaḥ  ViP yāniṃ kiṃpuruṣādini varṣāṇyaṣṭau mahāmune na teṣu śauko nāyāso nodvegaḥ kṣudbhayādikam  ViP svasthāḥ prajā nirātaṅkāḥsarvaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ daśa dvādaśavarṣāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sthirāyuṣaḥ  ViP na teṣu varṣate devo bhaumānyambhāṃsi teṣu vai kṛtatretādikaṃ naiva teṣu sthāneṣu kalpanā  ViP sarveṣveteṣu varṣeṣu saptasaptakulācalāḥ nadyaś ca śataśastebhyaḥ prasūtā yā dvijottama  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe dvitīyo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācauttaraṃ yatsamudrasya himādreścaiva dakṣiṇam varṣaṃ tadbhārataṃ nāma bhāratī yatra santatiḥ  ViP navayojanasāhasro vistārosya mahāmune karmabhūmiriyaṃ svargamapavargaṃ ca gacchatām  ViP mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimānṛkṣaparvataḥ vindhyaś ca pārīyātraś ca saptātra kulaparvatāḥ  ViP ataḥ saṃprāpyate svargo suktimasmātprayānti vai tiryaktvaṃ narakaṃ cāpi yāntyataḥ puruṣā mune  ViP itaḥ svargaś ca mokṣaś ca madhyaṃ cāntaś ca gamyate na khlavanyatra martyānāṃ karmabhūmau vidhīyate  ViP bhāratasyāsya varṣasya navabhādānnaśāmaya idradvīpaḥ kaseruś ca tāmraparṇāṃ gabhastimān  ViP nāgadvīpas tathā sāmyo gandharvastvatha cāruṇaḥ ayaṃ tu navamastaṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgārasaṃvṛtaḥ  ViP yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu dvīpoyaṃ dakṣiṇottarāt pūrve kirātā yasyānte paścime yavanāḥ sthitāḥ  ViP brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā madhye śabdrāś ca bhāgaśaḥ ijyāyudhavaṇijyādyair vartayanto vyavasthitāḥ  ViP śatadrūcandrabhāgādyā himayatpādanirgatāḥ vedasmṛtimukhādyāś ca pārīyātrodbhavā mune  ViP narmadā murasādyāś ca nadyo vindhyādrinirgatāḥ tāpīpayoṣṇīnirvindhyā prasūkhā ṛkṣasaṃbhavāḥ  ViP godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇyādikās tathā sahyapādodbhavā nadyaḥ smṛtāḥ pāpabhayāpahāḥ  ViP kṛtamālā tāmraparṇiprasukhā malayodbhavāḥ trisāmā carṣikulyādyā mahendraprabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP ṛṣikulyākumārādyāḥ śuktimatpādasambhavāḥ āsāṃ nadya upānadyaḥ santyanyāś ca sahasraśaḥ  ViP tāsvime kurupāñcālā madhyadeśādayo janāḥ pūrvadeśādikāścaiva kāmarūpanivāsinaḥ  ViP puṇḍrāḥ kaliṅgā magadhā dakṣiṇādyāś ca sarvaśaḥ tathāparāntāḥ saurāṣṭrāḥ śūrābhīrāstathārbudāḥ  ViP kārūṣā mālabāścaiva pāriyātra nivāsinaḥ sauvīrāḥ saindhavā hūṇāḥ sālvāḥ kosalavāsināḥ  ViP mādrārāmāstathāmbaṣṭhā pārasīkādayas tathā āsāṃ pibanti salilaṃ vasanti sahitāḥ sadā samīpato mahābhāga hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulāḥ  ViP catvāri bhārate varṣe yugānyatra mahāmune kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparañca kaliścānyatra na kvacit  ViP tapastapyanti munayo juhvate cātra yajvanaḥ dānāni cātra dīyante paralokārthamādarāt  ViP puruṣair yajñapuruṣo jambūdvīpe sadejyate yajñair yajñamayo viṣṇuranyadvīpeṣu cānyathā  ViP atrāpi bhārataṃ śreṣṭhaṃ janbūdvīpe mahāmune yato hi karmabhūreṣā hyatonyā bhogabhūmayaḥ  ViP atra janmasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrair api sattama kadācillabhate janturmānuṣyaṃ puṇyasaṃcayāt  ViP gāyanti devāḥ kila gītakāni dhanyāstu te bhārata bhūmibhāge svargāpavargāspadamārgabhūte bhavanti bhūyaḥ puruṣāḥ suratvāt  ViP karmāṇyasaṃkalpitatatphalāni saṃnyasya viṣṇo paramātmbhūte avāpya tāṃ karmamahīmanante tasmillayaṃ ye tvamalāḥ prayānti  ViP jānīma naitatkva vayaṃ vilīne svargaprade karmaṇi dehabandham prāpsyāma dhanyāḥ khalu te manuṣyā ye bhārate nendriyaviprahīnāḥ  ViP navavarṣaṃ tu maitreya jambudvīpamidaṃ mayā lakṣayojanavistāraṃ saṃkṣepāt kathitaṃ tava  ViP jambūdvīpaṃ samāvṛtya lakṣayojanavistaraḥ maitreya valayākāraḥ sthitaḥ kṣārodadhirbahiḥ  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe tṛtīyodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācakṣārodena yathā dvīpo jambūsaṃjño bhiveṣṭitaḥ saṃveṣṭya kṣāramudadhiṃ plakṣadvīpas tathā sthitaḥ  ViP jambūdvīpasya vistāraḥ śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ sa evaṃ dviguṇo brahman plakṣadvīpa udāhṛtaḥ  ViP sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpeśvarasya vai jyeṣṭha śāntahayo nāma śiśirastadanantaraḥ  ViP sukhodayastathānandaḥ śivaḥ kṣemaka eva ca dhruvaś ca saptamasteṣāṃ plakṣadvīpeśvarā hi te  ViP pūrvaṃ śāntahayaṃ varṣaṃ śiśiraṃ ca sukhaṃ tathā ānandaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva kṣemakaṃ dhruvameva ca  ViP maryādākārakāsteṣāṃ tathānye varṣaparvatāḥ saptaiva teṣāṃ nāmāni śṛṇuṣva munisattama  ViP gomadeścaiva candraś ca nāradau dundubhis tathā somakaḥ mumanāścaiva vaibhrājaścaiva saptamaḥ  ViP varṣācaleṣu ramyeṣu varṣeṣveteṣu cānaghāḥ vasaṃti devagandharvasahitāḥ satataṃ prajāḥ  ViP teṣu puṇyā janapadāścirācca mriyate janaḥ nādhayo vyādhayo vāpi sarvakālasukhaṃ hi tat  ViP teṣāṃ nadyastu saptaiva varṣāṇāṃ ca samudragāḥ nāmatastāḥ pravakṣyāmi śrutāḥ pāpaṃ haranti yāḥ  ViP anutaptā śikhī caiva vipāśā tridivāklamaḥ amṛtā sukṛtā caiva saptaitāstatra nimnagāḥ  ViP ete śailās tathā nadyaḥ pradhānāḥ kathitāstava kṣudraśailās tathā nadyastatra santi sahasraśaḥ tāḥ pibandi sadāhṛṣṭā nadīrjanapadāstute  ViP apasarpiṇī na teṣāṃ vai na caivotsarpiṇī dvija na tvevāsti yugāvasthā teṣu stāneṣu saptasu  ViP tretāyugasamaḥ kālaḥ sarvadaiva mahāmate plakṣadvīpādiṣu brahmañ śākadvīpāntikeṣu vai  ViP pañca varṣasahasrāṇi janā jīvantyanāmayāḥ dharmaḥ pañcasvathaiteṣu varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ  ViP varṇāś ca tatra catvārastānnibodha vadāmi te  ViP āryakāḥ kurāraścaiva vidiśyā bhāvinaśce te viprakṣatrivaiśyāste śūdrāś ca munisattama  ViP jmabūvṛkṣapramāṇastu tanmadhye sumahāṃstaruḥ plakṣastannāmasaṃjñoyaṃ plakṣadvīpo dvijottama  ViP ijyate tatra bhagavāṃstair varṇair āryakādibhiḥ sīmarūpi jagatstraṣṭā sarvaḥ sarveśvaro hariḥ  ViP plakṣadvīpapramāṇena plakṣadvīpaḥ samāvṛtaḥ tathaivekṣuramodena pariveṣānukāriṇā  ViP ityevaṃ tava maitreya plakṣadvīpa udāhṛtaḥ saṃkṣepeṇa mayā bhūyaḥ śālmalaṃ me nisāmaya  ViP śālmamasyeśvaroḥvīro vapuṣmāṃstatsutāñchṛṇu teṣāṃ tu nāmasaṃjñāni saptavarṣāṇi tāni vai  ViP śvetotha haritaścaiva jīmūto rohitas tathā vaidyuto mānasaścaiva suprabhaś ca mahāmune  ViP śālmalena samudrosau dvīpenekṣurasodakaḥ vistāradviguṇenātha sarvataḥ saṃvṛtaḥ sthitaḥ  ViP tatrāpi parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyā ratnayonayaḥ varṣābhivyañjakā ye tu tathā sapta ca nimnagāḥ  ViP kumudaścennataścaiva tṛtīyaś ca balāhakaḥ droṇo yatra mahauṣadhyaḥ sa caturtho mahīdharaḥ  ViP kaṅkastupañcamaḥ ṣaṣṭhī mahiṣaḥ saptamas tathā kakudmānparvatavaraḥ sarinnāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP yonitoyo vitṛṣṇā ca candrā muktā vimocanī ye tu varṇāś ca vasantyete mahāmune kapilāścāruṇāḥ pītāḥ kṛṣṇāścaiva pṛthak pṛthak  ViP brahmaṇāḥ kṣatrayā vaiśyāḥ śudrāścaiva yajantitam bhagavantaṃ samastasya viṣṇumātmānamavyayam vāyubhūtaṃ makhaśreṣṭhair yajvano yajñasaṃsthitim  ViP devānāmatra sānnadhyamatīva sumanohare śālmaliḥ sumahānvṛkṣo nāmnā nirvṛtikārakaḥ  ViP eṣa dvīpaḥ samudreṇa surodena samāvṛtaḥ vistārācchālmalasyaiva samena tu samantataḥ  ViP surodakaḥ parivṛtaḥ kuśadvīpena sarvataḥ śālmalasya tu vistarāddviguṇena samantataḥ  ViP jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe sapta putrāñchṛṇuṣva tān  ViP udbhido veṇumāṃścaiva veratho lambano dhṛtiḥ prabhākarotikapilastannāmā varṣapaddhatiḥ  ViP tasminvasanti manujāḥ saha daite yadānavaiḥ tathaiva devagandharvayakṣakiṃpuruṣādayaḥ  ViP varṇāstatrāpi catvāro nijānuṣṭhānatatparāḥ daminaḥ śuṣmiṇaḥ snehā mandehāś ca mahāmune  ViP brahmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścānukramoditāḥ  ViP yathoskakarmakartṛtvātsvādhikārokṣayāya te tatraiva taṃ kuśadvīpe brahmarūpaṃ janārdanam yajantaḥ kṣapayanty ugram adhikāraphalapradam  ViP vidrumo hemaśailaś ca dyatimān puṣpavāṃs tathā kuśaśayo hariścaiva saptamo mandarācalaḥ  ViP varṣācalāstu saptaite tatra dvīpe mahāmune nadyaś ca sapta tāsāṃ tu śṛṇu nāmānyanukramāt  ViP dhūtapāpā śivā caiva pavitrā saṃmatis tathā vidyudambhā mahī cānyā sarvapāpa harāstvimāḥ  ViP anyāḥ sahasraśastatra kṣudranadyastathācalāḥ kuśadvīpe guśastambaḥ saṃjñayā tasya tatsmṛtam  ViP tatpramāṇena sa dvīpo ghṛtodena samāvṛtaḥ ghṛtodaś ca samudro vai krauñcadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ  ViP krauñcadvīpo mahābhāga śruyatāñcāparo mahān kuśadvīpasya vistārā ddviguṇo yasya vistaraḥ  ViP krauñcadvīpe dyutimataḥ putrāstasya mahātmanaḥ tannāmāni ca varṣāṇi teṣāṃ cakre mahīpatiḥ  ViP kuśalo mallagaścoṣṇaḥ pīvarothāndhakārakaḥ muniś ca dundubhiścaiva saptaite tatsutā mune  ViP tatrāpi devagandharvasevitāḥ sumanoharāḥ varṣācalā mahābuddhe teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP krauñcaś ca vāmanaścaiva tṛtīyaścāndhakārakaḥ caturtho ratnaśailaś ca svāhinī hayasannibhaḥ  ViP divāvṛtpañcamaścātra tathānyaḥ puṇḍarīkavān dundubhiś ca mahāśailo dviguṇāsta parasparam dvīpādvīpeṣu ye śailā yathā dvīpāni te tathā  ViP varṣeṣveteṣu ramyeṣu tathā śailavareṣu ca nivasaṃti nirātaṅkāḥ saha devagaṇaiḥ prajāḥ  ViP puṣkarāḥ puṣkalā dhanyāstitikhyāś ca mahāmune brahmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śudrāścānukramoditāḥ  ViP nadīrmaitreya te tatra yāḥ pibanti śṛṇuṣva tāḥ saptapradhānāḥ śataśas tatrānyāḥ kṣudranimnagāḥ  ViP gaurī kumudvatī caiva sandhyā rātrirmanojavā kṣāntiś ca puṇḍarīkā ca saptaitā varṣanimnagāḥ  ViP tatrāpi viṣṇurbhagavānpuṣkārādyair jānārdanaḥ yāgau rudrasvarūpaś ca ijyate yajñasannidhau  ViP krauñcadvīpaḥ samudreṇa dadhimaṇḍodakena ca āvṛtaḥ sarvataḥ krauñca dvīpatulyena mānataḥ  ViP dadhimaṇḍodakaścāpi śākadvīpena saṃvṛtaḥ krauñcadvīpasya vistārāddviguṇena mahāmune  ViP śākadvīpeśvarasyāpi bhavyasya mumahātmanaḥ saptaiva tanayāstaṣāṃ dadau varṣāṇi sapta saḥ  ViP jaladaś ca kumāraś ca mukumāro marīcakaḥ kusumodaś ca maudākiḥ saptamaś ca mahādrumaḥ  ViP tatsaṃjñānyeva tatrāpi sapta varṣāṇyanukramāt tatrāpi parvatāḥ spata varṣavicchedakāriṇaḥ  ViP pūrvastatrodayagirirjalādhārastathāparaḥ tathā raivatakaḥ śyāmastathaivāstagirirdvija āmbikeyas tathā sarvapāpabhayāpahāḥ  ViP sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī dhenukā ca yā ikṣuś ca veṇukā caiva gabhastī saptamī tathā  ViP anyāś ca śataśastatra kṣudranadyo mahāmune mahīdharās tathā santi śataśotha sahasraśaḥ  ViP tāḥ pibanti mudāyuktā jaladādiṣu ye sthitāḥ varṣaṣu te janapadāḥ svargādabhyetya medinīm  ViP dharmahānirna teṣvasti na saṃgharṣaḥ parasparam maryādāvyutkramo nāpi teṣu deśeṣu saptasu  ViP vaṅgāś ca māgadhāścaiva mānasā mandagās tathā vaṅgā brahmaṇabhūyiṣṭhā māgadhāḥ kṣatriyās tathā vaiśyāstu mānasāsteṣāṃ śūdrasteṣāṃ tu mandagāḥ  ViP śākadvīpe tu tair viṣṇuḥ sūryarūpadharo muneṃ yathoktaurijyate samyakkarmabhir niyatātmabhiḥ  ViP śākadvīpastu maitreya kṣirodena samāvṛtaḥ śākadvīpapramāṇena valayeneva veṣṭitaḥ  ViP kṣirābdhiḥ sarvato brahmanpuṣkarākhyena veṣṭitaḥ dvīpena śākadvīpāttu dvīguṇena samantataḥ  ViP puṣkare savanasyāpi mahāvīro bhavatsutaḥ dhātukiś ca tayostatra dve varṣe nāmacihnite mahāvīraṃ tathaivānyaddhātukīkhaṇḍasaṃjñitam  ViP ekaścatra mahābhāga vibhajanniva sthitosau tena vichinnaṃ jātaṃ tadvarṣakadvayam  ViP valayākāramekaikaṃ tayorvarṣaṃ tathā giriḥ  ViP daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tatra jīvanti mānavāḥ virāmayā viśokāś ca rāgadveṣādivarjitāḥ  ViP adhamottamau na teṣvāstāṃ na vadhyavadhakau dvija nerṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ dveṣo doṣo lobhādiko na ca  ViP mahāpītaṃbahirvarṣaṃ dhātakīkhaṇḍamantataḥ mānasottaraśaulasya devadaityādisevitam  ViP satyānṛtena tatrāstāṃ dvīpe puṣkarasaṃjñite na tatra nadyaḥ śailā vā dvīpe varṣadvayānvite  ViP tulyapeṣāstu manujā devāstatraikarūpiṇaḥ  ViP varṇāśramācārahīnaṃ dharmācaraṇavarjitam trayīvārtādaṇḍanītiśuśrūṣārahitañca yat  ViP varṣadvayaṃ tu maitreya bhaumaḥ svargoyamuttamaḥ sarvartusukhadaḥ kālo jarārogādivarjitaḥ dhātakīkhaṇḍasaṃjñe tha mahāvīre ca vai mune  ViP nyagrodhaḥ puṣkaradvīpe brahmaṇaḥ sthānamuttamam tasminnavasati brahmā pūjyamānaḥ surāsuraiḥ  ViP svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ pariveṣṭitaḥ samena puṣkarasyaiva vistārānmaṇḍalaṃ tathā  ViP evaṃ dvīpāḥ samudraiś ca saptasaptabhir āvṛtāḥ dvīpaścaiva samudraś ca samāno dviguṇau parau  ViP payāṃsi sarvadā sarvasamudreṣu samāni vai nyūnātiriktatā teṣāṃ kadācinnaiva jāyate  ViP sthālīsthamagnīsaṃyogādudrekisalile yatha tathenduvṛddhau salilamaṃbhodhau munisattama  ViP anyūnānatiriktāś ca vardhantyāpo hrasaṃti ca udayāstamaneṣvindoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ  ViP daśottarāṇi pañcaiva hyaṅgulānāṃ śatāni vai apāṃ vṛddhikṣaṇo dṛṣṭau sāmudrīṇāṃ mahāmune  ViP bhojanaṃ puṣkaradvīpe tatra svayamupasthitam ṣaḍrasaṃ bhuñjate vipra prajāḥ sarvāḥ sadaiva hi  ViP svādūdakasya parito dṛsyate lokasaṃsthitiḥ dviguṇā kāñcanī bhūmiḥ sarvajantuvivarjitā  ViP lokālokastataḥ śailo jojanāyutavistṛtaḥ ucchrāyeṇāpi tāvanti sahasrāṇyacalo hi saḥ  ViP tatastamaḥ samāvṛtya taṃ śaulaṃ sarvataḥ sthitam tamaścāṇḍakaṭāhena samantātpariveṣṭitam  ViP pañcaśatkoṭivistārā seyamurva mahāmune sahaivāṇḍakaṭāhena sadvīpābdhimahīdharā  ViP seyaṃ dhātrī vidhātrī ca sarvabhūtaguṇādhikā ādhārabhūtā sarveṣāṃ maitreya jagatāmiti  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe caturtho dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācavistāra eṣa kathitaḥ pṛthivyā bhavato mayā saptatistu sahasrāṇi dvijocchrāyopi kathyate  ViP daśasāhasramekaikaṃ pātālaṃ munisattama atalaṃ vitalaṃ caiva nitalaṃ ca gabhastimat mahākhyaṃ sutalaṃ cāgryaṃ pātālaṃ cāpi saptamam  ViP śuklākṛṣṇāruṇāḥ pītāḥ śarkarāḥ śailakāñcanāḥ bhūmayo yatra maitreya paragrāsādamaṇḍitāḥ  ViP teṣu dānavadaiteyā yakṣāś ca śataśas tathā nivasanti mahānāgajā tayaś ca mahāmune  ViP svarlokādapi ramyāṇi pātālānīti nāradaḥ prāha svargasadaṃ madhye pātālābhyāgato divi  ViP āhlādakāriṇaḥ śubhrā maṇayo yatra suprabhāḥ nāgābharaṇabhūṣāsu pātālaṃ kena tatsamam  ViP daityadānavakanyābhir itaścaitaś ca śobhite pātāle kasya na prītirvimuktasyāpi jāyate  ViP divārkaraśmayo yatra prabhāṃ tanvanti nātapam śaśiraśmir na śītāya niśi dyotāya kevalam  ViP bhakṣyabhojyamahāpānamuditair api bhogibhiḥ yatra na jñāyate kālo gatopi danujādibhiḥ  ViP vanāni nadyo ramyāṇi sarāṃsi kamalākarāḥ puṃskokilābhilāpāś ca manojñānyambarāṇi ca  ViP bhūṣaṇānyatiśubhrāṇi gandhāḍhyaṃ cānulepanam vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgānāṃ svanair apūritāni ca  ViP etānyanyāni codārabhagyabhogyāni tānavaiḥ daityoragaiś ca bhujyante pātālāntaragocaraiḥ  ViP pātālānāmadhaścāste viṣṇoryā tāmasī tanuḥ śeṣakhyā yadruṇānvaktuṃ na śaktā daityadānavāḥ  ViP yonantaḥ pāṭhyate siddhair daivo devarṣipūjitaḥ sa sahasraśirā vyaktasvastikāmalabhūṣaṇaḥ  ViP phaṇāmaṇisahasreṇa yaḥ sa vidyotayandiśaḥ sarvānkaroti nirviryān hitāya jagato surān  ViP madāghūrṇitanetrosau yaḥ sadaivaikakumḍalaḥ kiriṭī sragdharo bhāti sāgniḥ śveta ivācalaḥ  ViP nīlavāsā madotsiktaḥ śvetahāropaśobhitaḥ sābhragaṅgāpravāhosau kailāsādririvāparaḥ  ViP lāṅgalāsaktahastāgro bibhranmusalamutamam upāsyate svayaṃ kāntyā yo vāruṇyā ca mūrtayā  ViP kalpānte yasya vaktrebhyo viṣānalaśikhojjvalaḥ saṃkarṣaṇātmako rūdro niṣkramyātti jagattrayam  ViP sa bibhracchekharībhūtamaśeṣaṃ kṣitimaṇḍalam āste pātālamūlasthaḥ śeṣo śeṣasurārcitaḥ  ViP tasya vīryaṃ prabhāvaś ca svarūpaṃ rūpameva ca na hi varṇayituṃ śakyaṃ jñātuṃ ca tridaśair api  ViP yasyaiṣā sakalā pṛthvī phaṇāmaṇiśikhārūṇā āste kusumamāleva kastadvīryaṃ vadiṣyati  ViP yadā vijṛmbhatenanto madāghūrṇitalocanaḥ tadā calati bhūreṣā sābdhitoyā sakānanā  ViP gandharvāpsarasaḥ siddhāḥ kinnaroragacāraṇāḥ nāntaṃ guṇānāṃ gacchanti tenānantoyamavyayaḥ  ViP yasya nāgavadhūhastair laṃbitaṃ hari candanam muhuḥ śvāsānilāpāstaṃ yāti dikkṣodavāsatām  ViP yamārādhya pūrāṇarṣirgargo jyotīṃṣi tattvataḥ jñātavānsakalaṃ caiva nimittapaṭhitaṃ phalam  ViP teneyaṃ nāgavaryeṇa śirasā vidhṛtā mahī bibharti mālāṃ lokānāṃ sadevāsuramānuṣām  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāhurāṇe dvitīraye ṃśe pañcamo dhyāya parāśara uvācatataś ca narakā vipra bhuvodhaḥ salilasya ca pāpino yeṣu pātyante tāñchṛṇuṣvamahāmune  ViP rauravaḥ sūkaro rodhastālo viśasanas tathā mahājvālastaptakumbho lavaṇetha vilohitaḥ  ViP rūdhirāmbho vaitaraṇiḥ krimiśaḥ krimibhojanaḥ asipatravanaṃ kṛṣṇo lālābhakṣaś ca dāruṇaḥ  ViP tathā pūyavahaḥ pāpo vahnijvālo hyadhaḥ śirāḥ saṃdaṃśaḥ kālasūtraś ca tamaścāvīcireva ca  ViP śvabhojanothāpratiṣṭhaścāpraciś ca tathā paraḥ ityevamādayaścānye narakā bhṛśadārūṇāḥ  ViP yamasya viṣaye ghorāḥ śastrāgnibhayadāyinaḥ patanti yeṣu puruṣāḥ pāpakarmaratāstu ye  ViP kūṭasākṣī tathāsamyakpakṣapātena yo vadet yaścānyadanṛtaṃ vakti sa naro yāti rauravam  ViP bhrūṇahā purahantā ca gaughnaś ca munisattama yānti te narakaṃ rodhaṃ yaścocchvāsanirodhakaḥ  ViP surāpo brahmahā hartā suvarṇasya ca sūkare prayānti narake yaś ca taiḥ saṃsargamupaiti vai  ViP rājanyavaiśyahantā ca tathaiva gurutalpagaḥ taptakuṇḍesvasṛgāmī hanti rājabhaṭāṃś ca yaḥ  ViP sādhvīvikrayakṛdbandhapālaḥ kesarivikrayī taptalohe patanty ete yaś ca ca bhaktaṃ parityajet  ViP snuṣāṃ sutāṃ cāpi gatvā mahājvāle nipātyate avamantā gurūṇāṃ yo yaścākroṣṭā narādhamaḥ  ViP vedadūṣayitāyaś ca vedavikrayakaś ca yaḥ agamyagāmī yaś ca syātte yānti lavaṇaṃ dvija  ViP coro vilohe patati maryādādūṣakas tathā  ViP devadvijapitṛdveṣṭā ratnadvaṣayitā ca yaḥ sa yāti krimibhakṣe vai krimiśe ca duriṣṭakṛt  ViP pitṛdevātithīṃs tyaktvā paryaśnāti narādhamaḥ lālābhakṣe sa yāty ugre śarakartā ca vedhake  ViP karoti karṇano yaś ca yaś ca khaṅgādikṛnnaraḥ prayāntyete viśasane narake bhṛśadaruṇe  ViP asatpratigṛhītā tu narake yātyadhomukhe ayājyayājakaścaiva tathā nakṣatrasūcakaḥ  ViP vegī pūyavahe caiko yāti maṣṭānnabhuṅgaraḥ  ViP lākṣāmāsarasānāṃ ca tilānāṃ lavaṇasya ca vikretā brahmaṇo yāti tameva narakaṃ dvija  ViP mārjārakukkuṭacchāga śvavarāhavihaṅgamān poṣayannarakaṃ yāti tameva dvijasattama  ViP raṅgopajīvī kaivartaḥ kumḍāśī garadas tathā sūcī māhiṣakaścaiva parvakārī ca yo dvijaḥ  ViP agāradāhī mitraghnaḥ śākunirgramayājakaḥ rudhirāndhe patantyete somaṃ vikrīṇate ca ye  ViP makhahā grāmahantā ca yāti vaitaraṇīṃ naraḥ  ViP retaḥ pātādikartāro maryādābhedino hi ye te kṛṣṇe yāntyaśaucāś ca kuhakājīvinaś ca ye  ViP asipatravanaṃ yāti vanacchedī vṛthaiva yaḥ aurabhriko mṛgavyādho vahnijvāle patanti vai  ViP yāntyete dvija tatraiva ye cāpākeṣu vahnidāḥ  ViP vratānāṃ lopako yaścasvāśramādvicyutaś ca yaḥ sandaṃśayātanāmadhye patatastāvubhāvapi  ViP divā svapne ca skandante ye narā brahmacāriṇaḥ putrair adhyāpitā ye ca te patanti śvabhojane  ViP ete cānye ca narakāḥ śataśotha sahasraśaḥ yeṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇaḥ pacyante yātanāgatāḥ  ViP yathaiva pāpānyetāni tathānyāni sahasraśaḥ bhujyante tāni puruṣair narakāntaragocaraiḥ  ViP varṇāśramaviruddhaṃ ca karma kurvanti ye narāḥ karmaṇā manasā vācā nirayeṣu patanti te  ViP adhaḥ śirobhidṛśyante nārakair divi devatāḥ devāścādhomukhānsarvānadhaḥ paśyanti nārakān  ViP sthāvarāḥ krimayobjāś ca pakṣiṇaḥ paśavo narāḥ dhārmikāstridaśāstaddhanmokṣiṇaś ca yathākramam  ViP sahasrabhāgaprathamā dvitīyānukramās tathā sarve hyete mahābhāgā yāvanmuktisamāśrayāḥ  ViP yāvanto jantavaḥ svarge tāvanto narakaukasaḥ pāpakṛdyāti narakaṃ prāyāścittaparāṅmukhaḥ  ViP pāpānāmanurūpāṇi prāyaścittāni yadyathā tathā tathaiva saṃsmṛtya proktāni paramarṣibhiḥ  ViP pāpe gurūṇi guruṇi svalpānyalpe ca tadvidaḥ prāyaścittāni maitreya jaguḥ svāyaṃbhuvādayaḥ  ViP prāyaścittānyaśeṣāṇi tapaḥkarmatmakāni vai yāni teṣāṇaśeṣāṇāṃ kṛṣṇānusmaraṇamparam  ViP kṛte pāpe nutāpo vai yasya puṃsaḥ prajāyate prāyaścittaṃ tu tasyaikaṃ harisaṃsmaraṇaṃ param  ViP prātarniśi tathā sandhyāmadhyāhnādiṣu saṃsmaran nārāyaṇamavāpnoti sadyaḥ pāpakṣayannaraḥ viṣṇusaṃsmaraṇātkṣīṇasamastakleśasañcayaḥ muktiṃ prayāti svargāptistasya vighnonumīyate  ViP vāsudeve mano yasyajapahomārcanādiṣu tasyāntarāyo maitreya devendratvādikaṃ phalam  ViP kva nākapṛṣṭhagamanaṃ punarāvṛttilakṣaṇam kva japo vāsudeveti muktibījamanuttamam  ViP tasmādaharniśaṃ viṣṇu saṃsmaranpuruṣo mune na yāti narakaṃ martyaḥ saṃkṣīṇākhilapātakaḥ  ViP manaḥ prītikaraḥ svargo narakastadviparyayaḥ narakasvargasaṃjñe vai pāpapuṇye dvijottama  ViP vastvekameva duḥkhāya sukhāyeṣryāgamāya ca kopāya ca yatastasmādvastu vastvātmakaṃ kutaḥ  ViP tadeva prītaye bhūtvā punarduḥkhā ya jāyate tadeva kopāya yataḥ prasādāya ca jāyate  ViP tasmādduḥkhātmakaṃ nāsti na ca kiñcitsukhātmakam manasaḥ parimāmoyaṃ sukhaduḥkhādilakṣamaḥ  ViP jñānameva paraṃ brahma jñānaṃ bandhāya ceṣyate jñānatmakamidaṃ viśvaṃ na jñānādvidyate param  ViP vidyāvidyeti maitreya jñānamevopadhāraya  ViP evametanmayākhyātaṃ bhavato maṇḍalaṃ bhuvaḥ pātālāni ca sarvāṇi tathāva narakā dvija  ViP samudrāḥ parvatāścaiva dvīpā varṣāṇi nimnagāḥ saṃkṣepātsarvamākhyātaṃ kiṃ bhūyaḥ śrotumicchasi  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe ṣaṣṭho dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācakathitaṃ bhūtalaṃ brahmanbhamaitadakhilaṃ tvayā bhuvarlokādikāṃl lokāñ chrotumicchāmyahaṃ mune  ViP tathaiva grahasaṃsthānaṃ pramāṇāni yathā tathā samācakṣva mahābhāga tanmahyaṃ paripṛcchate  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaravicandramasoryāvanmayūkhair avabhāsyate sasamudrasaricchailā tāvatī pṛthivī smṛtā  ViP yāvatpramāṇā pṛthivī vistāraparimaṇḍalāt nabhastāvanpramāṇaṃ vai vyāsamaṇḍalato dvija  ViP bhūmeryo janalakṣe tu sauraṃ maitreya maṇḍalam lakṣāddivākarasyāpi maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ sthitam  ViP pūrṇo śatasahasre tu yojanānāṃ niśākarāt nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtstramupariṣṭātprakāśate  ViP dve lakṣe cottare brahman budho nakṣatramaṇḍalāt tāvatpramāṇabhāge tu budhasyāpyuśanāḥ sthitaḥ  ViP aṅgarakopi śukrasya tatpramāṇe vyavasthitaḥ lakṣadvaye tu bhaumasya sthito devapurohitaḥ  ViP saurirbṛhaspateścordhvaṃ dvilakṣe samavasthitaḥ saptarṣimaṇḍalaṃ tasmāllakṣamekaṃ dvijottamā  ViP ṛṣibhyastu sahasrāṇāṃ śatādūrdhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ meḍhībhūtaḥ samastasya jyotiścakrasya vai dhruvaḥ  ViP trailokyametatkathitamutsedhena mahāmune ijyāphalasya bhūreṣā ijyā cātra pratiṣṭhitā  ViP dhruvādūrdhvaṃ maharloko yatra te kalpavāsināḥ ekayojanakoṭistu yatra te kalpavāsinaḥ  ViP dve koṭī tu jano loko yatra te brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ sanandanādyāḥ prathitā maitreyāmalacetasaḥ  ViP caturgaṇottare cordhvaṃ janalokāttapaḥ sthitaḥ vairājā yatra te devāḥ sthitā dāhavivarjitāḥ  ViP ṣaḍguṇenatapolokānsatyaloko virājate apunarmārakā yatra brahmaloko hi saṃsmṛtaḥ  ViP pādagamyantu yatkiñcidvastvasti pṛthivīmayam sa bhūrlokaḥ samākhyāto vistaro sya mayoditaḥ  ViP bhūmimūryāntaraṃ yacca siddhādimunisevitam bhuvarlokastu so py ukto dvitīyo munisattama  ViP dhruvasūryāntaraṃ yacca niyutāni caturdaśa svarlokaḥ so pi gadito lokasaṃsthānacintakaiḥ  ViP trailokyamatatkṛtakaṃ maitreya paripaṭhyate janastapas tathā satyamiti cākṛtakaṃ trayam  ViP kṛtakākṛtayormadhye maharloka iti smṛtaḥ śunyo bhavati kalpānte yotyantaṃ na vinaśyati  ViP ete sapta mayā lokā maitreya kathitāstava pātālāni ca saptaiva brahmāṇḍasyaiṣa vistaraḥ  ViP etadaṇḍakaṭāhena tiryak codhvamadhas tathā kapitthasya yathā bījaṃ sarvato vai samāvṛtam  ViP daśottareṇa payasā maitreyāṇḍaṃ ca tadvṛtam sarvombuparidhānosau vahninā veṣṭito bahiḥ  ViP vahniś ca vāyunā vāyurmaitreya nabhasā vṛtaḥ bhūtādinā nabhaḥ so pi mahatā pariveṣṭitaḥ deśottarāmyaśeṣāṇi maitreyaitāni sapta vai  ViP mahāntaṃ ca samāvṛtya pradhānaṃ samavasthitam anantasya na tasyāntaḥ saṃkhyānaṃ cāpi vidyate  ViP tadanantam asaṃkhyātapramāṇaṃ cāpi vai yataḥ hetubhūtamaśeṣasya prakṛtiḥ sā parā mune  ViP aṇḍānāṃ tu sahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇyayutāni ca īdṛśānāṃ tathā tatra koṭikoṭiśatāni ca  ViP hāruṇyagniryathā tailaṃ tile tadvatpumānapi pradhāne vasthito vyāpī cetanātmātmavedanaḥ  ViP pradhānaṃ ca pumāṃścaiva sarvabhūtātmabhūtayā viṣṇuśaktyā mahābuddhe vṛtau saṃśrayadharmiṇau  ViP tayoḥ saiva pṛthagbhāvakāraṇaṃ saṃśrayasya ca kṣobhakāraṇabhūtā ca sargakāle mahāmate  ViP yathā saktaṃ jale vāto bibharti kaṇikāśatam śaktiḥ sāpi tathā viṣṇoḥ pradhānapuruṣātmakam  ViP yathā ca pādayaur mūlaskandhaśākhādisaṃyutaḥ ādibījātprabhavati bījānyanyāni vai tataḥ  ViP prabhāvantitatastebhyaḥ sambhavantyapare drumāḥ tepi tallakṣaṇadravyakāraṇānugatā mune  ViP evamavyākṛtātpūrvaṃ jāyante mahadādayaḥ viśaṃṣāntā statastebhyaḥ saṃbhavantyasurādayaḥ tebhyaś ca putrāsteṣāṃ ca putrāṇāmapare sutāḥ  ViP bījādvṛkṣapraroheṇa yathā nāpacayastaroḥ bhūtānāṃ bhūtasargeṇa naivāstyapacayas tathā  ViP sannidhānādyathākāśakālādyāḥ kāraṇaṃ taroḥ tathaivāpariṇāmeva viśvasya bhagavānhariḥ  ViP vrīhibīje yathā mūlaṃ nālaṃ patrāṅkurau tathā kāṇḍakoṣastu puṣpaṃ ca kṣīraṃ tadvacca taṇjulāḥ  ViP tuṣāḥ kaṇāś ca santo vai yāntyāvirbhāvamātmanaḥ prarohahetusāmagryamāsādya munisattama  ViP tathā karmasvanekeṣu devādyāḥ samavasthitāḥ viṣṇuśaktiṃ samāsādya prarohamupayānti vai  ViP sa ca viṣṇuḥ paraṃ brahma yataḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat jagacca yo yatra cedaṃ yasmiṃś ca layameṣyati  ViP tadbrahma tatparaṃ dhāma sadasatparamaṃ padam yasya sarvamabhedena yataścaitaccarācaram  ViP sa eva mūla prakṛtirvyaktarūpī jagacca saḥ tasminneva layaṃ sarvaṃ yāti tatra ca tiṣṭhati  ViP kattā kriyāṇāṃ sa ca ijyate kratuḥ sa evatatkarmaphalaṃ ca tasya strugādiyatsādhanamapyaśeṣaṃ harerna kiñcivdyatiriktamasti  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe saptamo dhyāyaḥ prāśara uvācavyākhyātamaitadbrahmaṇḍasaṃsthānaṃ tava suvrata tataḥ pramāṇasaṃsthāne sūryādīnāṃ śṛṇuṣva mai  ViP yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi bhāskarasya ratho nava īṣādaṇḍastathaivāsya dviguṇo munisattama  ViP sārdhakoṭis tathā sapta niyutānyadhikāni vai yojanānāṃ tu tasyākṣastatra cakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam  ViP trinābhimati pañcāre ṣaṇṇeminyatrayātmake saṃvatsaramaye kṛtstraṃ kālacakraṃ pratiṣṭhitam  ViP hayāś ca saptacchadāṃsi teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu gāyatrī ca bṛhatyuṣṇigjagatī triṣṭubheva ca anuṣṭuppaṅktirityuktā chandāṃsi harayo raveḥ  ViP catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi dvitīyo kṣo vivasvataḥ pañcānyāni tu sārdhāni syandanasya mahāmate  ViP ākṣapramāṇamubhayoḥ pramāṇaṃ tadyugārdhayo hrasvokṣastadyugārdhena dhruvādhāro rathasya vai dvitīyekṣe tu taccakraṃ sasthitaṃ mānasācale  ViP mānasottaraśailasya pūrvato vāsavī purī dakṣiṇe tu yama syānyāpratīcyāṃ varuṇasya ca uttareṇa ca somasya tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP vasvaukasārā śakrasya yāmyā saṃyamanī tathā purī sukhājaleśasya somasya ca vibhāvarī  ViP kāṣṭhāṃ gato dakṣiṇataḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati maitreya bhagavānbhānurjyotiṣāṃ cakrasaṃyutaḥ  ViP ahorātravyavasthānakāraṇaṃ bhagavānraviḥ devayānaḥ paraḥ panthā yogināṃ kleśasaṃkṣaye  ViP divasasya varirmadhye sarvākālaṃ vyavasthitaḥ sarvadvīpeṣu maitreya niśārdhasya ca sanmukhaḥ  ViP udayāstamane caiva sarvakālaṃ tu
