saṃmukhe vidiśāsu tvaśeṣāsu tathā brahman diśāsu ca  ViP yair yatra dṛśyate bhāsvānsa teṣāmudayaḥ smṛtaḥ tirobhāvaṃ ca yatraiti tatraivāstamanaṃ raveḥ  ViP naivāstamanamarkasya nodayaḥ sarvadā sataḥ udayāstamanākhyaṃ hi darśanādarśanaṃ raveḥ  ViP śakrādīnāṃ pure tiṣṭhan spṛśatyeṣa puratrayam vikoṇau dvau vikoṇasthastrīn koṇāndve pure tathā  ViP udito vardhamānābhirāmadhyāhnāttapanraviḥ tataḥ paraṃ hrasantībhir gobhir astaṃ niyacchati  ViP udayāstamanābhyāṃ ca smṛte pūrvāpare diśau yāvatpurastāttapati tāvatpṛṣṭhe ca pārśvayoḥ  ViP ṛte maragirermerorupari brahmaṇaḥ sabhām yeye marīcayorkasya prayānti brahmaṇaḥ sabhām tete nirastāstadbhāsā pratīpamupayānti vai  ViP tasmāddiśyuttarasyāṃ vai divārātriḥ sadaiva hi sarveṣāṃ dvīpavarṣāṇāṃ seruruttarato yataḥ  ViP prabhā vivasvato rātrāvastaṃ gacchati bhāskare viśatyagnimato rātrau vahnirdūrātprakāśate  ViP vahnoḥ prabhā tathā bhānurdineṣvāviśati dvija atīva vahnisaṃyogādataḥ sūryaḥ prakāśate  ViP tejasī bhāskarāgneye prakāśoṣṇasvarūpiṇī parasparānupraveśādāpyāyete divāniśam  ViP dakṣiṇottarabhūmyardha samuttiṣṭhati bhāskare āhorātraṃ viśatyambhastamaḥ prākāśyaśīlavat  ViP ātāmrā hi bhavatyāpo divānaktapraveśanāt dinaṃ viśati caivāṃbho bhāskarestamupeyuṣi tasmācchuklā bhavantyāpo naktamahnaḥ praveśanāt  ViP evaṃ puṣkaramadhyena yadā yāti divākaraḥ triṃśadbhāgastu medinyāstadā mauhūrtikī gatiḥ  ViP kulālacakraparyante bhramanneṣa divākaraḥ karotyahas tathā rātriṃ vimuñcanmedinīṃ dvijaḥ  ViP ayanasyottarasyādau makaraṃ yāti bhāskaraḥ tataḥ kumbhaṃ ca mīnaṃ ca rāśe rāśyantaraṃ dvija  ViP triṣveteṣvatha bhukteṣu tato vaiṣuvatīṃ gatim prayāti savitā kurvannahorātraṃ tataḥ samam  ViP tato rātriḥ kṣayaṃ yāti vardhate nudinaṃ dinam  ViP tataś ca mithunasyānte parāṃ kāṣṭhāmupāgataḥ rāśiṃ karkaṭakaṃ prāpya kurute dakṣiṇāyanam  ViP kulālacakraparyanto yathāśīghraṃ pravartate dakṣiṇaprakrame sūryas tathā śīghraṃ pravartate  ViP ativegitayā kālaṃ vāyuvegabalāccaran tasmātprakaṣṭāṃ bhūmiṃ tu kālenālpena gacchati  ViP sūryo dvādaśabhiḥ śaighryān muhūrte dakṣiṇāyane trayodaśārdhamṛkṣāṇāmahnā tu carati dvija muhūrtais tāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiś caran  ViP kulālacakramadhyastho yathā mandaṃ prasarpati tathodagayane sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ  ViP tasmāddīrgheṇa kālena bhūmimalpāṃ tu gaccati aṣṭādaśasuhūrtaṃ yaduttarāyaṇapaścimam  ViP aharbhavati taccāpi carate mandavikramaḥ  ViP trayodaśārdhamahnā tu ṛkṣāṇāṃ carate raviḥ muhūrtais tāvadṛkṣāṇi rātrau dvādaśabhiścaran  ViP ato mandataraṃ nābhyāṃ cakraṃ bhramati vai yathā mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho dhruvo bhramati vai tathā  ViP kulālacakranābhis tu yathā tatraivavartate dhruvas tathā hi maitreya tatraiva parivartate  ViP ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramato maṇḍalāni tu divā naktaṃ ca sūryasya mandā śīghrāca vai gatiḥ  ViP mandāhni yasminnayane śīghrā naktaṃ tadā gatiḥ śīghrā niśi yadā cāsya tadā mandā divā gatiḥ  ViP eka pramāṇamevaiṣa mārgaṃ yāti divākaraḥ ahorātreṇa yo bhuṅkte samastā rāśayo dvija  ViP ṣaḍeva rāśīn yo bhuṅkte rātrāvanyāṃś ca ṣaḍdivā  ViP rāśipramāṇajanitā dīrghahrasvātmatā dine tathā niśāyāṃ rāśīnāṃ pramāṇair laghudīrghatā  ViP dināderdirghahrasvatvaṃ tadbhogenaiva jāyate uttare prakrame śīghrā niśi mandā gatirdivā  ViP dakṣiṇe tvayane caiva viparītāṃ vivasvataḥ  ViP uṣā rātriḥ samākhyātāvyuṣṭiścāpyucyate dinam procyate ca tathā saṃdhyā uṣāvyuṣṭyoryadantaram  ViP saṃdhyākāle ca saṃprāpte raudre paramadāruṇe mandehā rākṣasā ghorāḥ sūryamicchinti khāditum  ViP prajāpatikṛtaḥ śāpasteṣāṃ maitreya rakṣasām akṣayatvaṃ śarīrāṇāṃ maraṇaṃ ca dine dine  ViP tataḥ sūryasya tair yuddhaṃ bhavatyatyantadāruṇam tato dvijottamā stoyaṃ saṃkṣipanti mahāmune  ViP oṅkārabrahmasaṃyuktaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantritam tena dahyanti te pāpā vajrībhūtena vāriṇā  ViP agnihotre hūyate yā samantrā prathamāhutiḥ sūryojyotiḥ sahasrāṃśu samā dīpyati bhāskaraḥ  ViP oṅkāro bhagavānviṣṇustridhāmā vacasāṃ patiḥ taduccāraṇataste tu vināśaṃ yānti rākṣasāḥ  ViP vaiṣṇuvoṃśaḥ paraḥ sūryo yontarjyotirasaṃplavam abhiyāyaka oṅkārastasya tatprerakaṃ param  ViP tena saṃpreritaṃ jyotir oṃkāreṇātha dīptimat dahatyaśeṣarakṣāṃsi mandehākhyānyaghāni vai  ViP tasmānnollaṅghanaṃ kāryaṃ saṃdhyopāsanakarmaṇaḥ sa hanti sūryaṃ sandhyāyā nopāstiṃ kurute tu yaḥ  ViP tataḥ prayāti bhagavānbrāhmaṇair abhirakṣitaḥ vālakhilyādibhiścaiva jagataḥ pālanodyataḥ  ViP kāṣṭhā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triṃśacca kāṣṭhā gaṇayetkalāṃ ca triṃśatkalaścaiva bhavenmuhūrtastais triṃśatā rātryahanī samete  ViP hrāsavṛddhī tvaharbhāgordivasānāṃ yathākramam sandhyāmuhūrtamātrā vai hrāsavṛddhau samā smṛtā  ViP rekhāprabhṛtyathāditye trimuhūrtagate ravau prātaḥ smṛtastataḥ kālo bhāgaścāhnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ  ViP tasmātprātastanātkālāttramuhūrtastu saṅgavaḥ madhyāhnastrimuhūrtastu tasmātkālāttu saṅgavāt  ViP tasmānmādhyāhnikātkālādaparāhna iti smṛtaḥ traya eva muhūrtāstu kālabhāgaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ  ViP āparāhne vyatīte tu kālaḥ sāyāhna eva ca daśapañca muhūrtaṃ vai muhūrtāstraya eva ca  ViP daśapañca muhūrtaṃ vai aharvaiṣuvataṃ smṛtam  ViP vardhate hraseta caivāpyayane dakṣiṇottare ahastu grasate rātriṃ rātrirgrasati vāsaram  ViP śaradvasantayormadhye viṣuvaṃ tu vibhāvyate tulāmeṣagate bhānau samarātridinaṃ tu tat  ViP karkaṭāvasthite bhānau dakṣiṇāyanamucyate uttarāyaṇamapyuktaṃ makarasthe divākare  ViP triṃśanmuhūrtaṃ kathitamahorātraṃ tu yanmayā tānipañcadaśa brahman pakṣa ityabhidhīyate  ViP māsaḥ pakṣadvayenokto dvau māsau cārkajāvṛtuḥ ṛtutrayaṃ cāpyayanaṃ dve yane varṣasaṃjñite  ViP saṃvatsarādayaḥ pañca caturmāsavikalpitāḥ niścayaḥ sarvakālsaya yugamityabhidhīyate  ViP saṃvatsarastu prathamo dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ idvatsarastṛtīyastu caturthaścānuvatsaraḥ vatsaraḥ pañcamaścātra kāloyaṃ yugasaṃjñitaḥ  ViP yaḥ śvetasyottaraḥ śailaḥ śṛṅgavāniti viśrutaḥ trīṇi tasya tu śṛṅgāṇi mairayaṃ śṛṅgavān smṛtaḥ  ViP dakṣiṇaṃ cottaraṃ caiva madhyaṃ vaiṣuvataṃ tathā śaradvasaṃtayormadhye tadbhānuḥ pratipadyate meṣādau ca tulādau ca maitreya viṣuvaṃ smṛtam  ViP tadā tulyamahorātraṃ karoti timirāpahaḥ daśapañca muhūrtaṃ vai tad etad ubhayaṃ smṛtam  ViP prathame kṛttikābhāge yadā bhāsvāṃstadā śaśī viśākhānāṃ caturthe ṃśe mune tiṣṭhatyasaṃśayam  ViP viśākhānāṃ yadā sūryaścaratyaṃśaṃ tṛtīyakam tadā candraṃ vijānīyātkṛttikāśirasi sthitam  ViP tadaiva viṣuvākhyo yaṃ kālaḥ puṇyo bhidhīyate tadā dānādi deyāni devebhyaḥ prayatātmabhiḥ  ViP brahmaṇebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca mukhametattu dānājam dattadānastu viṣuve kṛtakṛtyobhijāyate  ViP ahorātrārdhamāsā tu kalāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kṣaṇās tathā paurṇamāsī tathā jñeyā amāvāsyā tathaiva ca sinīvālī kuhūścaiva ekā cānumatis tathā  ViP tapastapasyai madhumādhavau ca śukraḥ śuciścāyanamuttaraṃ syāt nabhonabhasyau ca iṣastathorjaḥsahaḥ sahasyāviti dakṣiṇaṃ tat  ViP lokā lokaś ca yaḥ śailaḥ prāg ukto bhavato mayā lokapālāstu catvārastatra tiṣṭhanti suvratāḥ  ViP sudhāmā śaṅkhapāccaiva kardamasyātmajau dvija hiraṇyaromā caivānyaścaturthaḥ kekumānapi  ViP nirdhandvā nirabhīmānā nistandrā niṣparigrahāḥ lokapālāḥ sthitā hyete lokā loke caturdiśam  ViP uttaraṃ padagastyasya ajavīthyāś ca dakṣiṇam pitṛyānaḥ sa vai panthā vaiśvānarapathādbāhiḥ  ViP tatrāsate mahātmāna ṛṣayo ye gnihotriṇaḥ bhūtāraṃbhakṛtaṃ brahma śaṃsanto ṛtvigudyatāḥ prārabhante tu ye lokāsteṣāṃ panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇaḥ  ViP calitaṃ te punarbrahma sthāpayanti yugeyuge santatyā tapasā caiva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca  ViP jāyamānāstu pūrve ca paścimānāṃ gṛheṣu vai paścimāścaiva pūrveṣāṃ jāyante vidhaneṣviha  ViP evamāvartamānāste tiṣṭhanti niyatavratāḥ saviturdakṣiṇaṃ mārgaṃ śritā hyacandratārakam  ViP nāgāvīthyuttaraṃ yacca saptarṣibhyaś ca dakṣiṇam uttaraḥ savituḥ panthā devayānaś ca sa smṛtaḥ  ViP tatra te vāsinaḥ siddhāvimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ santatiṃ te jugupsaṃti tasmānmṛtyurjitaś ca taiḥ  ViP aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi munīnāmūrdhvareta sām udakpanthanamaryamṇaḥ sthitā hyābhūtasaṃplavam  ViP te seprayogāllobhasya maithunasya ca varjanāt icchādveṣāpravṛttyā ca bhūtārambhavi varjanāt  ViP punaś ca kāmāsaṃyogācchabdāderdeṣadarśanāt ityebhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ śuddhāstemṛtatvaṃ hi bhejire  ViP ābhūtasaṃplavaṃ sthānamamṛtatvaṃ vibhāvyate trailokyasthitikāloyamapunarmāra ucyate  ViP brahmahatyāśvamedhābhyāṃ pāpapuṇyakṛto vidhiḥ ābhūtasaṃplavāntantu phalamuktaṃ tayordvija  ViP yāvanmātre pradeśe tu maitreyāvasthito dhruvaḥ kṣayamāyāti tāvattu bhūmerābhūtasaṃplavāt  ViP ūrdhvottaramṛṣibhyastu dhruvo yatra vyavasthitaḥ etadviṣṇupadaṃ divyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vyomni bhāsuram  ViP nirdhūtadoṣapaṅkānāṃ yatīnāṃ saṃyatātmanām sthānaṃ tatparamaṃ vipra puṇyapāpaparikṣaye  ViP apuṇyapuṇyoparame kṣīṇāśeṣāptihetavaḥ yatra gatvā na śocanti tadviṣṇoḥ parapaṃ padam  ViP dharmadhruvādyāstiṣṭhanti yatra te lokasākṣiṇaḥ tatsārṣṭyotpannayogardhistadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃpadam  ViP yatrotametatprotaṃ ca yadbhūtaṃ sacarācaram bhavyaṃ ya viśvaṃ maitreya tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP divīva cakṣurātataṃyogināṃ tanmayātmanām vivekajñānadṛṣṭaṃ ca tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP yasminpratiṣṭhito bhāsvānmeḍhībhūtaḥ svayaṃ dhruvaḥ dhruve ca sarvajyotīṃṣi jyotiṣvambhomuco dvija  ViP megheṣu saṃgatā vṛṣṭirvṛṣṭeḥ sṛṣṭeś ca poṣaṇam āpyāyanaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ devādīnāṃ mahāmune  ViP tataścājyāhutidvārā poṣitāste havirbhujaḥ vṛṣṭeḥ kāraṇatāṃ yānti bhūtānāṃ sthitaye punaḥ  ViP evametatpadaṃ viṣṇostṛtīyamamalātmakam ādhārabhūtaṃ lokānāṃ trayāṇāṃ vṛṣṭikāraṇam  ViP tataḥ prabhavati brahman sarvapāpaharā sarit gaṅgā devāṅganāṅgānāmanulepanapiñjarā  ViP vāmapādāmbujāṅguṣṭhanakhastrotovinirgatām viṣṇorbibhārti yāṃ bhaktyā śirasāharniśaṃ dhruvaḥ  ViP tataḥ saptarṣayo yasyāḥ prāṇāyāmaparā yaṇāḥ tiṣṭhanti vīcimālābhiruhyamānajaṭājale  ViP vāryoghaiḥ saṃtatair yasyāḥ plāvitaṃ śaśimaṇḍalam bhūyodhikatarāṃ kāntiṃ vahatyetaduha kṣaye  ViP merupṛṣṭe patatyuccair niṣkrāntā śaśimaṇḍalāt jagataḥ pāvanārthāya prayāti ca caturdiśam  ViP sītī cālakanandā ca cakṣurbhadrā ca saṃsthitā ekaiva yā caturbhedā digbhedagatilakṣaṇā  ViP bhedaṃ cālakanandākhyaṃ yasyāḥ śarvopi dakṣiṇām dadhāra śirasā prītya varṣāṇāmadhikaṃ śatam  ViP śambhorjaṭākalāpācca viniṣkrāntāśthiśarkarāḥ plāvayitvā divaṃ ninye yā pāpānsagarātmajān  ViP strātasya salile yasyāḥ sadyaḥ pāpaṃ praṇaśyati apūrvapuṇyaprāptiś ca sadyo maitreya jāyate  ViP dattāḥ pitṛbhyo yatrāpastanayaiḥ śraddhayānvitaiḥ samāśataṃ prayacchanti tṛptiṃ maitreya durlabhām  ViP yasyāmiṣṭvā mahāyajñair yajñeśaṃ puruṣottamam dvijabhūpāḥ parāṃ siddhimavāpurdivi ceha ca  ViP snānādvidhūtapāpāś ca yajjalair yatayas tathā keśabāsaktamanasaḥ prāptā nirvāṇamuttamam  ViP śrutābhilaṣitā dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā pītāvagāhitā yā pāvayati bhūtāni kīrtitā ca divedine  ViP gagāgaṅgeti yair nāmayojanānā śataṣvapi sthitair uccāritaṃ hanti pāpaṃ janmatrayārjitam  ViP yataḥ sā pāvanāyālaṃ trayāṇāṃ jagatāmapi samudbhūtā paraṃ tattu tṛtīyaṃ bhagavatpadam  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe ṣṭamo dhyāyaḥ śrīpāraśara uvācatārāmayaṃ bhagavataḥ śiśumārākṛti prabhoḥ divi rūpaṃ harer yattu tasya pucche sthito dhruvaḥ  ViP saiṣa bhraman bhrāmayati candrādityādikān grahān bhramantamanu taṃ yānti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat  ViP sūryācandramasau tārā nakṣatrāmi grahaiḥ saha vātānīkamayair bandhair dhruve baddhāni tāni vai  ViP śiśumārākṛti proktaṃ yadrūpaṃ jyotiṣāṃ divi nārāyaṇo yanaṃ dhāmnāṃ tasyādhāraḥ svayaṃ hṛdi  ViP uttānapādaputrastu tamārādhya jagatpatim sa tārā śiśumārasya dhruvaḥ pucche vyavasthitaḥ  ViP ādhāraḥ śiśumārasya sarvādhyakṣo janārdanaḥ dhruvasya śiśumārastu dhruve bhānurvyavasthitaḥ  ViP tadādhāraṃ jagaccedaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam  ViP yena vipravidhānena tanmamaikamanāḥ śṛṇu vivasvānaṣṭabhir māsair ādāyāpo rasātmikāḥ varṣatyambutataścānnamannādapyakhilaṃ jagat  ViP vivasvānaṃśubhis tīkṣṇair ādāya jagato jatam somaṃ puṣmātyathenduś ca vāyunāḍīmayair divi nālair vikṣipate bhreṣu dhūmāgnyanilamūrtiṣu  ViP na bhraśyanti yatastebhyo jalānyabhrāṇi tānyataḥ abhrasthāḥ prapatantyāpo vāyunā samudīritāḥ saṃskāraṃ kāṃlajanitaṃ maitreyāsādya nirmalāḥ  ViP saritsamudrabhomāstu tathāpaḥ prāṇisambhavāḥ catuṣprakārā bhagavānādatte savitā mune  ViP ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ tathādāyagabhastimān anabhragatamevorvyāṃ sadyaḥ kṣipati raśmibhiḥ  ViP tasya saṃsparśanirdhūtapāpapaṅko dvijottama na yāti narakaṃ martyo divyaṃ snānaṃ hi tatsmṛtam  ViP dṛṣṭasūryaṃ hi yadvāri patatyabhrair vinā divaḥ ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ tadgobhiḥ kṣipyate raveḥ  ViP kṛttikādiṣu ṛkṣeṣu viṣameṣu ca yaddivaḥ dṛṣṭārkapatitaṃ jñeyaṃ tadgāṅgaṃ diggajojjhitam  ViP yugmarkṣeṣu ca yattoyaṃ patatyarkojjhitaṃ divaḥ tatsūryaraśmibhiḥ sarvaṃ samādāya nirasyate  ViP ubhayaṃ puṇyamatyarthaṃ nṛṇāṃ pāpabhayāpaham ākāśagaṅgāsalilaṃ divyaṃ snānaṃ mahāmune  ViP yattu maighaiḥ samutsṛṣṭaṃ vāri tatprāṇināṃ dvija puṣṇātyauṣadhayaḥ sarvā jīvanāyāmṛtaṃ hi tat  ViP tena vṛddhiṃ parāṃ nītaḥ sakalaścauṣadhīgaṇaḥ sādhakaḥ phalapākantaḥ prajānāṃ dvija jāyate  ViP tena yajñānyathāproktānmānavāḥ śāstracakṣuṣaḥ kurvantyaharahastaiś ca devānāpyāyayantite  ViP evaṃ yajñāś ca vedāś ca varṇāś ca dvijapūrvakāḥ sarve devanikāyāś ca sarve bhūtagaṇāś ca ye  ViP vṛṣṭyā dhṛtamidaṃ sarvamannaṃ niṣpādyate yayā sāpi niṣpādyate vṛṣṭiḥ savitrā munisattama  ViP ādhārabhūtaḥ saviturdhruvo munivarottama dhruvasya śiśupāro sau so pi nārāyaṇātmakaḥ  ViP hṛdi nārāyaṇastasya śiśumārasyaṃ saṃsthitaḥ bibhartā sarvabhūtānāmādibhūtaḥ sanātanaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe navamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācatryaśītimaṇḍalaśataṃ kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ dvayoḥ ārohaṇāvarohābhyāṃ bhānorabdena yā gatiḥ  ViP sa rathodhiṣṭhito devair ādityai ṛṣibhis tathā gandharvair apsarobhiś ca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ  ViP dhātā kratusthalā caiva pulastyo bāsukis tathā rathabhṛdgrāmaṇīrhetistumburuścaiva saptamaḥ  ViP ete vasanti vai caitre madhumāse sadaiva hi maitreya syandane bhānoḥ saptamāsādhikāriṇaḥ  ViP aryamā pulahaścaiva rathaujāḥ puñcikasthalā prahetiḥ kacchavīraśva nāradaś ca rathe raveḥ  ViP mādhave nivasantyete śucisaṃjñe nibodha me  ViP mitrotristakṣako rakṣaḥ pauruṣeyotha menakā hāhā rathasvanaścaiva maitreyaite vasanti vai  ViP varuṇo vasiṣṭho rambhā ca sahajanyā huhūrathaḥ rathacitras tathā śukre vasantyāṣāḍhasaṃjñake  ViP indro viśvāvasuḥ srotā elāputrastathāṅgirāḥ pramlocā ca na bhasyete saptiścārke vasanti vai  ViP vivasvānugrasenaś ca bhṛgurāpūraṇas tathā anumlocā śaṅkhapālo vyāghro bhādrapade tathā  ViP pūṣā ca surucirvāto gautamotha dhanañjayaḥ suṣeṇo nyo ghṛtācī ca vasantyāśvayuje ravau  ViP viśvāvasurbharadvājaḥ parjanyair āvatau tathā viśvācī senajiccāpi kārttike ca vasanti vai  ViP aṃśaḥ kāśyapatārkṣyāstu mahāpadmastathorvaśī citrasenas tathā vidyunmārgaśīrṣedhikāriṇaḥ  ViP kraturbhagastatorṇāyuḥ sphūrjaḥ kārkoṭakas tathā ariṣṭanemiścaivānyā pūrvācittirvarāpsarāḥ  ViP pauṣamāse vasantyete saptabhāskaramaṇāle lokaprakāśanārthāya vigravaryādhikāriṇaḥ  ViP tvaṣṭātha jamadagniś ca kambalobha tilottamā brahmopetotha ṛtajiddhṛtarāṣṭrotha saptamaḥ  ViP māghamāse vasanttyete sapta maitreya bhāskare śrūyatāṃ cāpare sūrye phālgunenivasanti yo  ViP viṣṇuraśvataro rambhā sūryavarcāś ca satyajit viśvāmitras tathā rakṣo yajñopeto mahāmune  ViP māseṣveteṣu maitreya vasantyete tu saptakāḥ saviturmaṇḍale brahmanviṣṇusaktyupabṛṃhitāḥ  ViP stuvanti munayaḥ sūryaṃ gandharvair gīyate puraḥ nṛtyantyapsaraso yānti sūryasyānuniśācarāḥ  ViP vahanti pannagā yakṣaiḥ kriyate bhīṣusaṃgrahaḥ  ViP vālakhityāstathaivainaṃ parivārya samāsate  ViP soyaṃ saptagaṇaḥ sūryamaṇḍale munisattama himoṣṇavārivṛṣṭīnāṃ hetuḥ svasamayaṃ gataḥ  ViP iti kṣiviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe daśamo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācayadetadbhagavānāha gaṇaḥ saptavidho raveḥ maṇḍale himatāpādeḥ kāraṇaṃ tanmayā śrutam  ViP vyāpāraścāpikathito gandharvoragarakṣasām ṛṣīṇāṃ vālakhilyānāṃ tathaivāpsarasāṃ guro  ViP yakṣāṇāṃ ca rathe bhānorviṣṇuśaktidhṛtātmanām kiṃ cādityasya yatkarma tannātroktaṃ tvayā mune  ViP yadi saptagaṇo vāri himamuṣṇaṃ ca varṣati tatkimatra raveryena vṛṣṭiḥ sūryāditīryate  ViP vivasvānudito madhye yātyastamiti kiṃ janaḥ bravītyetatsamaṃ karma yadi saptagaṇasya tat  ViP parāśara uvācamaitreyaśrūyatāmetadyadbhavānparipṛccati yathā saptagaṇopyekaḥ prādhānyenādhiko raviḥ  ViP sarvaśaktiḥ parā viṣṇo ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñitā saiṣātrayī tapatyaṃho jagataś ca hinasti yā  ViP saiṣa viṣṇuḥ sthitaḥ sthityāṃ jagataḥ pālanodyataḥ ṛgyajuḥ sāmabhūtontaḥ saviturdvijatiṣṭhati  ViP māsimāsi raviryoyastatra tatra hi sā parā trayīmayī viṣṇuśaktiravasthānaṃ karoti vai  ViP ṛcastuvantiḥ pūrvāhne madhyāhnetha yajūṃṣi vai bṛhadrathantarādīni sāmānyahnaḥ kṣaye ravim  ViP aṅgameṣā trayī viṣṇo ṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃjñitā viṣṇuśaktiravasthānaṃ sadāditye karoti sā  ViP na kevalaṃ raveḥ śaktirvaiṣṇavī sā trayīmayī brahmātha puruṣo rudrastrayametattrayīmayam  ViP sargādau ṛṅmayo brahmā sthitau viṣṇuryajurmayaḥ rudraḥ sāmamayontāya tasmāttasyāśucirthvaniḥ  ViP evaṃ sā sāttvikī śaktirvaiṣṇavī yā trayīmayī ātmasaptagaṇasthaṃ taṃ bhāsvantamadhitiṣṭhati  ViP tayā cādhiṣṭhitaḥ so pi jājvalīti svaraśmibhiḥ tamaḥ samastajagatāṃ nāśaṃnayati cākhilam  ViP stuvanti cainaṃ munayo gandharvair gīyate puraḥ nṛtyantyo psaraso yānti tasya cānu niśācarāḥ  ViP vahanti pannagā yakṣaiḥ kriyate bhīṣusaṃgrahaḥ vālakhilyāstathaivainaṃ parivārya samāsate  ViP nodetā nāstametā ca kadācicchaktirūpadhṛk viṣṇurviṣṇoḥ pṛthak tasya gaṇāḥsaptavidho pyayam  ViP stambhasthadarpaṇasyeva yo yamāsannatāṃ gataḥ chāyādarśanasaṃyogaṃ sa taṃ prāpnotyathātmanaḥ  ViP evaṃ sā vaiṣṇavī śaktirnaivāpaiti tato dvija māsānumāsaṃ bhāsvantamadhyāste tatra saṃsthitam  ViP pitṛdevamanuṣyādīnsa sadāpyāyayanprabhuḥ parivartatyahorātrakāraṇaṃ savitā dvaja  ViP sūryaraśmisuṣumṇāyastarpitastena candramāḥ kṛṣṇapakṣemaraiḥ śaśvatpīyate vai sudhāmayaḥ  ViP pītaṃ taṃ dvikalaṃ somaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣakṣaye dvija pibanti patarasteṣāṃ bhāskarāttarpamaṃ tathā  ViP ādatte raśmibhir yaṃtu kṣitisaṃsthaṃ rasaṃ raviḥ tamutsṛjati bhūtānāṃ puṣṭyarthaṃ sasyavṛddhaye  ViP tena prīṇātyaśeṣāṇi bhūtāni bhagavānraviḥ pitṛdevamanuṣyādīnevamāpyāyayatyasau  ViP pakṣatṛptiṃ tu devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ caiva māsikīm śaśvattṛptiṃ ca martyānāṃ maitreyārkaḥ prayacchati  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīyeṃśa ekādaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācarathastricakraḥ somasya kundābhāstasya vājinaḥ vāmadakṣiṇato yuktā daśatena caratyasau  ViP vīthyāśrayāṇi ṛkṣāṇi dhruvādhāreṇa veginā hrāsavṛddhikramastasya raśmīnāṃ savituryathā  ViP arkasyeva hi tasyāśvāḥ sakṛdyuktā vahanti te kalpamekaṃ muniśreṣṭha vārīgarbhasamudbhavāḥ  ViP kṣīṇaṃ pītaṃ suraiḥ somamāpyāyayati dīptimān maitreyaikakalaṃ santaṃ raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ  ViP krameṇa yena pīto sau devais tena niśākaram āpyāyayatyanudinaṃ bhāskaro vāritaskaraḥ  ViP saṃbhṛtaṃ cārdhamāsena tatsomasthaṃ sudhāmṛtam pibandi devā maitreya sudhāhārā yato marāḥ  ViP trayāstriṃśatsahasrāṇi trayastriṃśacchatāni ca trayastriṃśattathā devāḥ pibanti kṣaṇadākaram  ViP kalādvayāviśiṣṭastu praviṣṭaḥ sūryamaṇḍalam amākhyāraśmau vasati amāvāsyā tataḥ smṛtā  ViP apsu tasminnahorātre pūrvam viśati candramāḥ tato vīrutsu vasati prayātyarkaṃ tataḥ kramāt  ViP chinatti virudho yastu vīrutsaṃsthe niśākare patraṃ vā pātayatyekaṃ brahmahatyāṃ sa vindati  ViP somaṃ pañcadaśe bhāge kiñcicchiṣṭe kalātmake apārāhne pitṛgaṇājaghanyaṃ paryupāsate  ViP pibanti dvikalākāraṃ śiṣṭā tasya kalā tu yā sudhāmṛtamayī puṇyā tāmindoḥ pitaro mune  ViP niḥsṛtantadamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyaḥ sudhāmṛtam māsaṃ tṛptimavāpyāgryāṃ pitaraḥ santi nirvṛtāḥ saumyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāś ca te tridhā  ViP evaṃ devān site pakṣe kṛṣṇapakṣe tathā pitṝn vīrudhaścāmṛtamayaiḥ śītair apparamāṇubhiḥ  ViP vīrudhauṣadhiniṣpattyā manuṣyapaśukīṭakān āpyāyayati śītāṃśuḥ prākāśyāhlādanena tu  ViP vāyvagnidravyasaṃbhūto rathaścandrasutasya ca piśaṅgais turagair yuktaḥ so ṣṭābhir vāyuvegibhiḥ  ViP savarūthaḥ sānukarṣo yukto bhūsaṃbhavair hayaiḥ sopāsaṃgapatākastu śukrasyāpi ratho mahān  ViP aṣṭāśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmānbhaumasyāpi ratho mahān padmarāgāruṇair aśvaiḥ saṃyukto vahnisambhavaiḥ  ViP aṣṭābhiḥ pāṇḍurair yukto vājibhiḥ kāñcanorathaḥ tasmiṃstiṣṭhati varṣānte rāśaurāśau vṛhaspatiḥ  ViP ākāśasambhavair aśvaiḥ śabalaiḥ syandanaṃ yutam tamāruhya śanair yāti mandagāmīśanaiścaraḥ  ViP svarbhānosturagā hyaṣṭau bhṛṅgābhā dhūsaraṃ ratham sakṛdyuktāstu maitreya vahantyavirataṃ sadā  ViP ādityānniḥsṛto rāhuḥ somaṃ gacchati parvasu ādityameti somācca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu  ViP tathā keturathasyāśvā apyaṣṭau vātaraṃhasaḥ palāladhūmavarṇābhā lākṣārasanibhāruṇāḥ  ViP ete mayā grahāṇāṃ vai tavākhyātā rathā nava sarve dhruve mahābhāga prabaddhā vāyuraśmibhiḥ  ViP graharkṣatārādhiṣṇyāni dhruve baddhānyaśeṣataḥ bhramantyucitacāreṇa maitreyānilaraśmibhiḥ  ViP yāvāntyaścaiva tārāstā tāvanto vātaraśmayaḥ sarve dhruve nibaddhāste bhramanto bhrāmayanti tam  ViP tailapīḍā yathā cakraṃ bhramanto bhrāmayanti vai tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vātaviddhāni sarvaśaḥ  ViP alātacakravadyānti vātacakreritāni tu yasmajyotīṃṣi vahati pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ  ViP śiśumārastu yaḥ proktaḥ sa dhruvo yatra tiṣṭhati sanniveśaṃ ca tasyāpi śṛṇuṣva munisattama  ViP yadahnā kurute pāpaṃ taṃ dṛṣṭvā niśi mucyate yāvantyaścaiva tārāstāḥ śiśumārāśritā divi tāvantyeva tu varṣāṇi jīvatyabhyadhikānica  ViP uttānapādastasyādho vijñeyo hyuttaro hanuḥ yajño dharaś ca vijñeyo dharmo mūrdhānamāśritaḥ  ViP hṛdi nārāyaṇaścāste aśvinau pūrvapādayoḥ varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sakthinī  ViP śiśraḥ saṃvatsarastasya mitro pānaṃ samāśritaḥ  ViP pucchegniś ca mahendraś ca kasyapotha tato dhruvaḥ tārakā śiśumārasya nāstameti catuṣṭayam  ViP ityeṣa sanniveśo yaṃ pṛthivyā jyotiṣāṃ tathā dvīpānāmudadhīnāṃ ca parvatānāṃ ca kīrtitaḥ  ViP varṣāṇāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca ye ca teṣu vasanti vai teṣāṃ svarūpamākhyātaṃ saṃkṣepaḥ śruyatāṃ punaḥ  ViP yadambu vaiṣṇavaḥ kāyastato vipra vasundharā padmākārā samudbhūtā parvatābdhyādisaṃyutā  ViP jyotīṣi viṣṇurbhuvanāni viṣṇurvanāni viṣṇurgirayo diśaś ca nadyaḥ samudrāś ca sa eva sarvaṃ yadasti yannāsti ca vipravarya  ViP jñānasvarūpo bhagavānyatosā vaśeṣamūrtirna tu vastubhūtaḥ tato hi śailabdhidharādibhedāñjānīhi vijñānavijṛmbhitāni  ViP yadā tu śuddhaṃ nijarūpi sarvaṃ karmakṣaye jñānamapāstadoṣam tadā hi saṃkalpataroḥ phalāni bhavanti no vastuṣu vastubhedāḥ  ViP vastvasti kiṃ kutrācidādimadhyaparyantahīnaṃ satataikarūpam yaccānyathātvaṃ dvija yāti bhūyo na tattathā tatra kuto hi tattvam  ViP mahī ghaṭatvaṃ ghaṭataḥ kapālikā kapālikācūrṇarajastato ṇuḥ janaiḥ svakarmastimitātmaniścayair ālakṣyate brūhi kimatra vastu  ViP tasmān na vijñānam ṛte sti kiṃcit kvacit kadācid dvija vastujātam vijñānam ekaṃ nijakarmabhedavibhinnacitter bahudhābhyupetam  ViP jñānaṃ viśuddhaṃ vimalaṃ viśo kamaśeṣalobhādinirastasaṅgam ekaṃ sadaikaṃ paramaḥ sa vāsudevo na yato nyadasti  ViP sadbhāva evaṃ bhavato mayokto jñānaṃ yathā satyamastayatyamanyat etattu yatsaṃvyavahārabhūtaṃ tatrāpi coktaṃ bhuvanāśritaṃ te  ViP yajñaḥ paśurvahniraśeṣaṛtviksomaḥ surāḥ svargamayaś ca kāmaḥ ityādikarmāśritamārgadṛṣṭaṃ bhūrādibhogāś ca phalāni teṣām  ViP yaccaitadbhuvanagataṃ mayā tavoktaṃ sarvatra vrajati hi tatra karmavaśyaḥ jñātvaivaṃ dhruvamacalaṃ sadaikarūpaṃ tatkuryādviśati hi yena vāsudevam  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe dvādaśo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācabhagavansamyagākhyātaṃ yatpṛṣṭosi mayā kila bhūsamudrādisaritāṃ saṃsthānaṃ grahasaṃ sthitiḥ  ViP viṣṇvādhāraṃ yathā caitattrailokyaṃ samavasthitam paramārthastu te prokto yathājñānaṃ pradhānataḥ  ViP yattvetadbhagavānāha bharatasya mahīpateḥ śrotumicchami caritaṃ tanmamākhyātumarhasi  ViP bharataḥ sa mahīpālaḥ sālagrāme vasatkila yogayuktaḥ samādhāya vāsudeve sadā manaḥ  ViP puṇyedeśaprabhāvena dhyāyataś ca sadā harim kathaṃ tu nābhavanmuktiryadabhūtsa dvijaḥ punaḥ  ViP vipratve ca kṛtaṃ tena yadbhūyaḥ sumahātmanā bharatena muniśreṣṭha tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasālagrāme mahābhāgo bhagavannyastamānasaḥ sa uvāsa ciraṃ kālaṃ maitreya pṛtivīpatiḥ  ViP ahiṃsādiṣvaśeṣeṣu guṇeṣu guṇināṃ varaḥ avāpa paramāṃ kāṣṭhāṃ manasaścāpi saṃyame  ViP yajñeśācyuta govinda mādhavānanta keśava kṛṣṇa viṣṇo hṛṣīkeśa vāsudeva namostu te  ViP iti rājāha bharato harernāmāni kevalam nānyajjagāda maitreya kiñcitsvaprāntarepi ca etatpadantadarthaṃ ca vinā nānyadacintayat  ViP samitpuṣpakuśādānaṃ cakre devakriyākṛte nānyāni cakre karmāṇi niḥsaṅgo yogatāpasaḥ  ViP jagāma sobhiṣekārthamekadā tu mahānadīm sasnau tatra tadā cakre snānasyānantarakriyāḥ  ViP athājagāma tattīraṃ jalaṃ pātuṃ pipāsitā āsannaprasavā brahmannekaiva hariṇī vanāt  ViP tataḥ samabhavattatra pītaprāye jale tathā siṃhasya nādaḥ sumahānsarvaprāṇibhayaṅkaraḥ  ViP tataḥ sā sahasā trāsādāplutā nimnagātaṭam atyuccārohaṇenāsyā nadyāṃ garbhaḥ papāta ha  ViP tamūhyamānaṃ vegena vīcimālāpariplutam jagrāha sa nṛpo garbhātpatitaṃ mṛgapotakam  ViP garbhapracyutidoṣeṇa prottuṅgākramaṇena ca maitreya sāpi hariṇī papāta ca mamāra ca  ViP hariṇīṃ tāṃ vilokyātha vipannāṃ tṛpatāpasaḥ mṛgapotaṃ samādāya nijamāśramamāgataḥ  ViP cakārānudinaṃ cāsau mṛgapotasya vai nṛpaḥ poṣaṇaṃ puṣyamāṇaś ca sa tena vavṛdhe mune  ViP cacārāśramaparyante tṛṇāni gahaneṣu saḥ dvaraṃ gatvā ca śārdulatrāsādabhyāyayau punaḥ  ViP prātargatvātidūraṃ ca sāyamāyātyathāśramam punaś ca bharatasyabhūdāśramasyoṭajājire  ViP tasya tasminmṛge dūrasamīpaparivartini āsīccetaḥ samāsaktaṃ na yayāvanyato dvija  ViP vimuktarājyatanayaḥ projjhitāśeṣabāndhavaḥ mamatvaṃ sa cakāroccais tasminhariṇabālake  ViP kiṃ vṛkair bhakṣito vyaghraiḥ kiṃ siṃhena nipātitaḥ cirāyamāṇe niṣkrānte tasyāsīditi mānasam  ViP eṣā vasumatī tasya khurāgrakṣatakarburā  ViP prītaye mama jātosau kva mamaiṇakabālakaḥ viṣāmāgroṇa madbāhuṃ kaṇḍūyanaparo hi saḥ kṣemeṇābhyāgatoraṇyādapi māṃ sukhayiṣyati  ViP ete lūnaśikhāstasya daśanair acirodgataiḥ kuśāḥ kāśā virājante baṭavaḥ sāmāgā iva  ViP itthaṃ ciragate tasminsa cakre mānasaṃ muniḥ prītiprasannavadanaḥ pārśvasthe cābhavanmṛge  ViP samādhibhaṅgastasyāsīttanmayatvādṛtātmanaḥ santyaktarājyabhogardhisvajanasyāpi bhūpateḥ  ViP capalaṃ capale tasmindūragaṃ dūragāmini mṛgapote bhavaccittaṃ stairyavattasya bhūpateḥ  ViP kālena gacchatā so tha kālaṃ cakre mahīpatiḥ piteva sāstraṃ putreṇa mṛgapotena vīkṣitaḥ  ViP mṛgameva tadādrākṣīttyajanprāṇānasāvapi tanmayatvena maitreya nānyatkiñcidacintayat  ViP tataś ca tatkālakṛtāṃ bhāvanāṃ prāpya tādṛśīm jambūmārge mahāraṇye jāto jātismaromṛgaḥ  ViP jātismaratvadudvignaḥ saṃsārasya dvijottama vihāya mātaraṃ bhūyaḥ sālagrāmamupāyayo  ViP śuṣkais tṛṇais tathā parṇaiḥ sa kurvann ātmapoṣaṇam mṛgatvahetubhūtasya karmaṇo niṣkṛtiṃ yayau  ViP tatra cotsṛṣṭadeho sau jajñe jātismaro dvijaḥ sadācāravatāṃśuddhe yogināṃ pravare kule  ViP sarvavijñānasaṃpannaḥ sarvaśāstrarthatattvavit apaśyatya ca maitreya ātmānaṃ prakṛteḥ param  ViP ātmano dhigatajñāno devādīni mahāmune sarvabhūtānyabhedena sa dadarśa tadātmanaḥ  ViP na papāṭha guruproktaṃ kṛtopanayanaḥ śrutim na dadarśa ca karmāṇi śāstrāṇi jagṛhe na ca  ViP uktopi bahuśaḥ kiñcijjaḍavākyamabhāṣata tadapyasaṃskāraguṇaṃ grāmyavākyoktisaṃśritam  ViP apadhvastavapuḥ so pi malināmbaragdvijaḥ klinnadantāntaraḥ sarvaiḥ paribhūtaḥ sa nāgaraiḥ  ViP saṃmānanāparāṃ hāniṃ yogardhaḥ kurute yataḥ janenāvamato yogī yogasiddhaṃ ca vindati  ViP tasmāccareta vai yogī satāṃ dharmamadūṣayan janā yathā vamanyerangaccheyurnaiva saṅgatim  ViP hiraṇyagarbhavacanaṃ vicintyetthaṃ mahāmatiḥ ātmānaṃ darśayāmāsa jaḍonmattākṛtiṃ jane  ViP bhukte kulmāṣavāṭyādiśākaṃ vanyaṃ phalaṃ kaṇān yadyadāpnoti subahu tadatte kālasaṃyamam  ViP pitaryuparate so tha bhrātṛbhrātṛvyabāndhavaiḥ kāritaḥ kṣetrakarmādikadannāhārapoṣitaḥ  ViP samākṣapīnāvayavo jaḍakārī ca karmaṇi sarvalokopakaraṇaṃ babhūvāhāracetanaḥ  ViP taṃ tādṛśamasaṃskāraṃ viprākṛtiviceṣṭitam kṣattāsauvīrarājasya kālyai paśumakalpayat  ViP rātrau taṃ samalaṅkṛtya vaiśasasya vidhānataḥ adhiṣṭhitaṃ mahākālī jñātvā yogeśvaraṃ tathā  ViP tataḥ khaṅgaṃ samādāya niśitaṃ niśi sā tathā kṣattāraṃ krūrakarmāṇamacchinatkaṇṭhamūlataḥ svapārṣadayutā devī papau rudhiramulbaṇam  ViP tataḥsauvīrarājasya prayātasya mahātmanaḥ viṣṭakartātha manyeta viṣṭiyogyoyamityapi  ViP taṃ tādṛśaṃ mahātmānaṃ bhasmacchannamivānalam kṣattā sauvīrarājasya viṣṭiyogyamamanyata  ViP sa rājā śibikārūḍho gantuṃ kṛtamatirdvija babhūvekṣumatītīre kapilarṣer varāśramam  ViP śreyaḥ kimatra saṃsāre duḥkhaprāye nṛṇāmiti praṣṭuṃ taṃ mokṣadharmajñaṃ kapilākhyaṃ mahāmunim  ViP uvāha śibikāṃ tasya kṣatturvacanacoditaḥ nṛṇāṃ viṣṭigṛhītānāmanyeṣāṃ so pi madhyagaḥ  ViP gṛhīto viṣṭinā vipraḥ sarvajñānaikabhājanam jātismarosau papāsya kṣayakāma uvāha tām  ViP yayau jaḍamatiḥ sotha mṛgamātrāvalokanam kurvanmatimatāṃ śraṣṭhastadanye tvaritaṃ yayuḥ  ViP vilokya nṛpatiḥ sotha viṣamāṃ śibikāgatim kimetadityāha samaṃ gamyatāṃ śibikāvahāḥ  ViP punastathaiva śibikaṃ vilokya viṣamāṃ hi saḥ nṛpaḥ kimetadityāha bhavadbhir gamyatenyathā  ViP bhūpatervadatastasya śrutvetthaṃbahuśo vacaḥ śibikāvāhakāḥ projurayaṃ yātītyasatvaram  ViP rājovācakiṃ śrintosyalpamadhvānaṃ tvayoḍhā śibikā mama kimāyā sasaho na tvaṃ pīvānasi nirīkṣyase  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācanāhaṃ pīvā na caivoḍhā śibikā bhavato mayā na śrāntosmi na cāyāso soḍhavyosti mahīpate  ViP rājovācapratyakṣaṃ dṛśyase pīvānadyāpi śibikā tvayi śramaś ca bhārodvahane bhavatyeva hi dehinām  ViP brahmaṇa uvācapratyakṣaṃ bhavatā bhūpa yaddṛṣṭaṃ mama tadvada balavānabalaśceti vācyaṃ paścādviśeṣaṇam  ViP tvayoḍhā śibikā ceti tvayyadyāpi ca saṃsthitā mithyaitadatra tu bhavāñchṛṇotu vacanaṃ mama  ViP bhūmau pādayugaṃ tvāste jaṅghe pādadvaye sthite ūrvorjaṅghādvayāvasthau tadādhāraṃ tathodaram  ViP vakṣasthalaṃ tathā bāhū skandhau codarasaṃsthitau skandhāśriteyaṃ śibikā mama bhārotra kiṃ kṛtaḥ  ViP śibikāyāṃ sthitaṃ cedaṃ vapustvadupalakṣitam tatra tvamahamapyatra projyate cedamanyathā  ViP ahaṃ tvaṃ ca tathānye ca bhūtair uhyāma parthiva guṇapravāhapatito bhūtavargaupi yātyayam  ViP karmavaśyā guṇaścaite sattvādyāḥ pṛthivīpate avidyāsaṃcitaṃ karma taccāseṣeṣu jantuṣu  ViP ātmā śuddhokṣaraḥ śānto nirguṇaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ pravṛddhyapacayau nāsya ekasyākhilajantuṣu  ViP yadā nopacayastasya na caivāpacayo nṛpa tadā pīvānasītītthaṃ kayā yuktyā tvayeritam  ViP bhūpādajaṅghākaṭyūrujaṭharādiṣu saṃsthite śibikeyaṃ yathā skandhe tathā bhāraḥ samastvayā  ViP tathānyair jantubhir bhūpa śibikoḍhā na kevalam śailadrumagṛhotthopi pṛthivī saṃbhavopi vā  ViP yadā puṃsaḥ sṛthagbhāvaḥ prākṛtaiḥ kāraṇernṛpa soḍhavyastu tadāyāsaḥ kathaṃ vā nṛpate mayā  ViP yaddravyā śibikā ceyaṃ taddravyo bhūtasaṃgrahaḥ bhavato me kilasyāsya mamatvenopabṛṃhitaḥ  ViP śrīpāraśara uvācaevamuktvābhavanmaunī sa vahañchibikāṃ dvija so pi rājāvatīryovyāṃ tatpādau jagṛhe tvaran  ViP rājovācabhobhovisṛjya śibikāṃ prasādaṃ kuru me dvijaḥ kathyatāṃ ko bhavānatra jālmarūpadharaḥ sthitaḥ  ViP yo bhavānyannimittaṃ vā yadāgamanakāraṇam tatsarvaṃ kathyatāṃ vidvanmahyaṃ śuśrūṣave tvayā  ViP brahmaṇa uvācaśrūyatāṃ sohamityetadvaktuṃ bhūpa na śakyate upabhoganimittaṃ ca sarvatrāgamanakriyā  ViP sukhaduḥkhopabhogau tu tau dehādyupapādakau dharmādharmodbhavau bhoktuṃ janturdehādimṛcchati  ViP sarvasyaiva hi bhūpāla jantoḥ sarvatra kāraṇam dharmādharmau yataḥ kasmātkāraṇaṃ pṛcchate tvayā  ViP rājovācadharmādharmau na sandehaḥsarvakāryeṣu kāraṇam upabhoganimittaṃ ca dehāddehāntarāgamaḥ  ViP yastvetadbhavatā proktaṃ sohamityetadātmanaḥ vaktuṃ na sakyate śrotuṃ tanmamecchā pravartate  ViP yosti sohamiti brahmankathaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyate ātmanyeṣa na doṣāya śabdohamiti yo dvija  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācaśabdohamiti doṣāya nātmanyeṣa tathaiva tat anātmanyātmavijñānaṃ śabdo vā bhrāntilakṣaṇaḥ  ViP jihvā bravītyahamiti dantoṣṭhau tāluke nṛpa etenāhaṃ yataḥ sarve vāṅniṣpādanahetavaḥ  ViP kiṃ hetubhir vadatyeṣā vāgevāhamiti svayam ataḥ pīvānasītyetad vaktum itthaṃ na yujyate  ViP piṇḍaḥ pṛthagyataḥ puṃsaḥ śiraḥ pāṇyādilakṣaṇaḥ tatohamiti kutraitāṃ saṃjñāṃ rājankaromyaham  ViP yadyanyosti paraḥ kopi mattaḥ pārthivasattama tadaiṣohamayaṃ cānyo vaktumevamapīṣyate  ViP yadā samastadeheṣu pumāneko vyavasthitaḥ tadā hi ko bhavānsohamityetadviphalaṃ vacaḥ  ViP tvaṃ rājā śibikā ceyamime vāhāḥ puraḥ sarāḥ ayaṃ ca bhavato loko na sadetannṛpocyate  ViP vṛkṣāddāru tataśceyaṃ śibikā tvadadhiṣṭhitā kiṃ vṛkṣasaṃjñā vāsyāḥ syāddārusaṃjñātha vā nṛpa  ViP vṛkṣārūḍho mahārājo nāyaṃ vadati te janaḥ na ca dāruṇi sarvastvāṃ bravītiśibikāgatam  ViP śibikādārusaṃghāto racanāsthitisaṃsthitaḥ anviṣyatāṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha tadbhede śibikā tvayā  ViP evaṃ chatraśalākānāṃ pṛthagbhāve vimṛśyatām kva yātaṃ chatramityetannyāyastvayi tathā mayi  ViP pumāṃstrīgaurajo vājī kuñjaro vihagastaruḥ deheṣulokasaṃjñeyaṃ vijñeyā karmahetuṣu  ViP pumānna devo na naro na paśurna ca pādapaḥ śarīrākṛtibhedāstu bhūpaite karmayonayaḥ  ViP vastu rājeti yalloke yacca rājabhaṭātmakam tathānyacca nṛpetthaṃ tanna satsaṃkalpanāmayam  ViP yattu kālāntereṇāpi nānyāṃ saṃjñāmupaiti vai pariṇāmādisaṃbhūtāṃ tadvastu nṛpa tacca kim  ViP tvaṃ rājā sarvalokasya pituḥ putro ripo ripuḥ patnyāḥ patiḥ pitā sūnoḥ kiṃ tvaṃ bhūpavadāmyaham  ViP tvaṃ kimetacchiraḥ kiṃ nu grīvā tava tathodaram kimu pādādikaṃ tvaṃ vā tavaitatkiṃ mahīpate  ViP samastāvayavebhyastvaṃ pṛthagbhūya vyavasthitaḥ ko hamityatra nipuṇo bhūtvā cintaya parthiva  ViP evaṃ vyavasthite tattve mayāhamiti bhāṣitum pṛthakkaraṇaniṣpādyaṃ śakyate nṛpate katham  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīyeṃse trayodaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaniśamya tasyeti vacaḥ paramārthasamanvitam praśrayāvanato bhūtvā tamāha nṛpatirdvijam  ViP rājovācabhagavanyattvayā proktaṃ paramārthamayaṃ vacaḥ śrute tasminbhramantīva manaso mama vṛttayaḥ  ViP etadvivekavijñānaṃ yadaśeṣeṣu jantuṣu bhavatā darśitaṃ vipratatparaṃ prakṛtermahat  ViP nāhaṃ vahāmi śibikāṃ śivikā na mayi sthitā śarīramanyadasmattau yoneyaṃ śibikā dhṛtā  ViP guṇapravṛttyā bhūtānāṃ pravṛttiḥ karmacoditā pravartante guṇā hyete kiṃ mameti tvayoditam  ViP etasminparamārthajña mama śrotrapathaṃ gate mano vihvalatāmeti paramārthārthitāṃ gatam  ViP pūrvameva mahābhāgaṃ kapilarṣimahaṃ dvija praṣṭumabhyudyato gatvā śreyaḥ kiṃ tvatra śaṃsa me  ViP tadantare ca bhavatā yadeta dvākyamīritam tenaiva paramārthārthaṃ tvayi cetaḥ pradhāvati  ViP kapilarṣirbāgavataḥ sarvabhūtasya vai dvija viṣṇoraṃśo jaganmohanāśāyorvīmupāgataḥ  ViP sa eva bhagavānnūnamasmākaṃ hitakāmyayā pratyakṣatāmatra gato yathaitadbhāvatocyate  ViP tanmahyaṃ praṇatāya tvaṃ yacchreyaḥ paramaṃ dvijaḥ tadvadākhila vijñānajalavīcyudadhirbhavān  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācabhūpa pṛcchasi kiṃ śreyaḥ paramārthaṃ nu pṛcchasi śreyāṃsyaparamārthāni aśeṣāṇi ca bhūpate  ViP devatārādhanaṃ kṛtvā dhanasampadamicchati putrānicchati rājyaṃ ca śreyastasyaiva tannṛpa  ViP karma yajñātmakaṃ śreyaḥ phalaṃ tatprāptilakṣaṇam śreyaḥ pradhānaṃ ca phale tadevānabhisaṃhite  ViP ātmā dhyeyaḥ sadā bhupa yogayuktais tathā param śreyastasyaiva saṃyogaḥ śreyo yaḥ paramātmanaḥ  ViP śreyāṃsyevamanekāni śataśoya sahasrasaḥ santyatra paramārthastu na tvete śrūyatāṃ ca me  ViP dharmāya tyajyate kintu paramārtho dhanaṃ yadi vyayaś ca kriyate kasmāt kāmaprāptyupalakṣaṇaḥ  ViP putraścetparamārthaḥ syātso py anyasya nareśvara paramārthabhūtaḥ sonyasya paramārtho hi tatpitā  ViP evaṃ na paramārthosti jagatyasmiñcarācare paramārtho hi kāryāṇi kāraṇānāmaśeṣataḥ  ViP rājyādiprāptiratroktā paramārthatayā yadi paramārthā bhavantyatra na bhavanti ca vai tataḥ  ViP ṛgyajuḥsāmaniṣpādyaṃ yajñakarma mataṃ tava paramārthabhūtaṃ tatrāpi śruyatāṃ gadato mama  ViP yattu niṣpādyate kāryaṃ mṛdā kāraṇabhūtayā tatkāraṇānugamanāj jñāyate nṛpa mṛṇmayam  ViP evaṃ vināśibhir dravyaiḥ samidājyakuśādibhiḥ niṣpādyate kriyā yā tu sā bhavitrī vināśinī  ViP anāśo paramārthaś ca prājñaurabhyupagamyate tattu nāśi na sandeho nāśidravyopapāditam  ViP tadevāphaladaṃ karma paramārtho matastava muktisādhanabhūtatvātparamārtho na sādhanam  ViP dhyānaṃ caivātmano bhūpu paramārthārthaśabditam bhedakāri parebhyastu paramārtho na bhedavān  ViP paramātmātmanoryogaḥ paramārtha itīṣyate mithyaitadanyadravyaṃ hi naiti taddravyatāṃ yataḥ  ViP tasmācchreyāṃsyaśeṣāṇi nṛvaitāni na saṃśayaḥ paramārthastu bhūpāla saṃkṣepācchrūyatāṃ mama  ViP eko vyāpī samaḥ śuddho nirguṇaḥ prakṛteḥ paraḥ janmavṛddhyādirahita ātmā sarvagatovyayaḥ  ViP parajñānamayo sadbhir nāmajātyādibhir vibhuḥ na yogavānna yuktobhūnnaiva pārthiva yokṣyate  ViP tasyātmaparadeheṣu satopyekamayaṃ hi yat vijñānaṃ paramārtho sau dvaitino tathyarśinaḥ  ViP veṇurandhraprabhedena bhedaḥ ṣaṅjādisaṃjñitaḥ abhedavyāpinovāyostathāsya paramātmanaḥ  ViP ekasvarūpabhedaś ca brāhmakarmāvṛtiprajaḥ devādibhede padhvasteṃ nāstyevāvaraṇe hi saḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe caturdaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaśrīparāśara uvācaityukte mauninaṃ bhūyaścintayānaṃ mahīpatim pratyuvācātha viprosāvadvaitāntargatāṃ kathām  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācaśrūyatāṃ nṛpaśārdūla yadgītamṛbhuṇā purā avabodhaṃ janayatā nidāghasya mahātmanaḥ  ViP ṛbhunāmābhavatputro brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ vijñātatattvasadbhāvo nisargādeva bhūpate  ViP tasya śiṣyo nidāghobhūtpulastyatanayaḥ purā prādādaśeṣavijñānaṃ sa tasmai parayā mudā  ViP apāptajñānatantrasya na tasyādvaitavāsanā sa ṛbhustarkayāmāsa nidāghasya nareśvara  ViP devikāyāstaṭe vīranagaraṃ nāma vai puram samṛddamatiramyaṃ ca pulastyena viveśitma  ViP ramyopavanaparyante sa tasminpārthivottama nidāgho nāma yogajña ṛbhuśiṣyo vasat purā  ViP divye varṣasahasre tu samatītesya tatpuram jagāma sa ṛbhuḥ śiṣyaṃ nidāghamavalokakaḥ  ViP sa tasya vaiśvadevānte dvārālokanagocare sthitastena gṛhītārghyo nijaveśma praveśitaḥ  ViP prakṣālitāṅghripāṇiṃ ca kṛtā sanaparigrahma uvāca sa dvijāśreṣṭho bhujyatāmiti sādaram  ViP ṛbhuruvācabho vipravarya bhoktavyaṃ yadannaṃ bhavato guhe tatkathyatāṃ kadanneṣu na prītiḥ satataṃ mama  ViP nidāgha uvācasaktuyāvakavāṭyānāmapūpānāṃ ca me gṛhe yadrocate dvijaśreṣṭha tattvaṃ bhukṣva yathecchayā  ViP ṛbhuruvācakadannāni dvijautāni mṛṣṭamannaṃ prayaccha me saṃyāvapāyasādīni drapsaphāṇitavanti ca  ViP nidāgha uvācahehe śālini madgehe yatkiñcidatiśobhanam bhakṣyopasādhanaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ tenāsyānnaṃ prasādhaya  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācaityuktā tena sā patnīmṛṣṭamannaṃ dvijasya yat prasāditavatī tadvai bharturvacanagauravāt  ViP taṃ bhuktavantamicchāto mṛṣṭamannaṃ mahāmunim nidādhaḥ prāha bhūpāla praśrayāvanataḥ sthitaḥ  ViP nidāgha uvācaapite paramā tṛptirutpannā tuṣṭireva ca api te mānasaṃsvasthamāhāreṇa kṛtaṃ dvija  ViP kvanivāso bhavānvipra kva ca gantuṃsamudyataḥ āgamyate ca bhavatā yatastacca dvijocyatām  ViP ṛmuruvācakṣudyasya tasya bhuktenne tṛptirbrāhmaṇa jāyate na me kṣunnābhavattṛptiḥ kasmānmāṃ paripṛcchasi  ViP vahninā pārthive dhātau kṣapite kṣutsamudbhavaḥ bhavatyambhasi ca kṣīṇe nṛṇāṃ tṛḍapi jāyate  ViP kṣuttuṣṇe dehadharmākhye na mamaite yato dvija tataḥ kṣutsambhavābhāvāttṛptirastyeva me sadā  ViP manasaḥ svasthatā tuṣṭiścittadharmāvimau dvija cetaso yasya tatpṛccha pumān ebhir na yujyate  ViP kva nivāsastavetyuktaṃ kva gantāsi ca yattvāyā kutāścāgamyate tatra tritayepi nibodha meḥ  ViP pumānsarvagato vyāpī ākāśavadayaṃ yataḥ kutaḥ kutra kva gantāsītye tadapyarthavatkatham  ViP so haṃ gantā na cāgantā naikadeśaniketanaḥ tvaṃ cānye ca na ca tvaṃ ca nānye naivāhamapyaham  ViP mṛṣṭaṃ na mṛṣṭamapyeṣā jijñāsā me kṛtā tava kiṃ vakṣyasīti tatrāpi śrūyatāṃ dvijasattama  ViP kimasvādvatha vā mṛṣṭaṃ bhuñjatosti dvijottama mṛṣṭameva yathā mṛṣṭaṃ tadevodvegakārakam  ViP amṛṣṭaṃ jāyate mṛṣṭaṃ mṛṣṭādudvijate janaḥ ādimadhyāvasāneṣu kimannaṃ rucikārakam  ViP mṛṇmayaṃ hi gṛhaṃ yadvan mṛdā liptaṃ sthiraṃ bhavet parthivoyaṃ tathā dehaḥ pārthivaiḥ paramāṇubhiḥ  ViP yavagodhūmamudgādi ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ payo dadhi guḍaṃphalādīni tathā pārthivāḥ paramāṇavaḥ  ViP tadetadbhavatā jñātvā mṛṣṭāmṛṣṭavicāri yat tanmanaḥsamatālambi kāryaṃ sāmyaṃ hi muktaye  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācaityākarṇya vacastasya paramārthaśritaṃ nṛpa praṇipatya mahābhāgo nidāgho vākyamabravīt  ViP prasīda maddhitārthāya kathyatāṃ yattvamāgataḥ naṣṭo mohastavākarṇya vacāṃsyetāni me dvīja  ViP ṛbhuruvācaṛmurasmi tavācāryaḥ prajñādānāya te dvija ihāga tohaṃ yāsyāmi paramārthastavoditaḥ  ViP evamekamidaṃ viddhi na bhedi sakalaṃ jagat vāsudevābhidheyasya svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācatathatyuktvā nidāghena praṇipātapuraḥsaram pūjataḥ parayā bhaktyā icchātaḥ prayayāv ṛbhuḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīye ṃśe pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥ brāhmaṇa uvācaṛbhurvarṣasahasre tu samatīte nareśvara nidāghajñānadānāya tadeva nagaraṃ yayau  ViP nagarasya bahiḥ sotha nidāghaṃ dadṛśe muniḥ mahībalaparīvāre puraṃ viśati pārthive  ViP dūre sthitaṃ mahābhāgaṃ najasaṃmardavarjakam kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭhamāyāntamaraṇyātsasamitkuśam  ViP dṛṣṭvā nidāghaṃ sa ṛbhurupagamyābhivādya ca uvāca kasmādekānte sthīyate bhavatā dvija  ViP nidāgha uvācabho vipra janasaṃmarde mahāneṣa nareśvaraḥ pravivikṣuḥ puraṃ ramyaṃ tenātra sthīyate mayā  ViP ṛbhuruvācanarādhipotra katamaḥ katamaścetarojanaḥ kathyatāṃ me dvija śreṣṭha tvamabhijño mato mama  ViP nidāgha uvācayoyaṃ gajendramunmattamadriśṛṅgasamucchritam adhirūḍho naredro yaṃ parilo kastathetaraḥ  ViP ṛbhuruvācaetau hi gajarājānau yugapaddarśitau mama bhavatā na viśeṣeṇa pṛthakcihnopalakṣaṇau  ViP tatkathyatāṃ mahābhāga viśeṣo bhavatānayoḥ jñātumicchāmyahaṃ kotra gajaḥ ko vā narādhipaḥ  ViP nidāgha uvācagajo yoyamatho brahmannuparyasyaiṣa bhūpatiḥ vāhyavā hakasambandhaṃ ko na jānāni vai dvija  ViP ṛbhuruvācajānāmyahaṃ yathā brahyaṃs tathā māmavabodhaya adhaḥśabdanigadyaṃ hi kiṃ cordhvamabhidhiyate  ViP brāhmaṇa uvācaityuktaḥ sahasāruhya nidāghaḥ prāha tamṛbhum śrūyatāṃ kathayāmyeṣa yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi  ViP uparyahaṃ yathā rājā tvamadhaḥ kuñjaro yathā avabodhāya te brahmandṛṣṭānto darśito mayā  ViP ṛbhuruvācatvaṃ rājena dvijaśreṣṭha sthitohaṃ gajavadyadi tadetattvaṃ samācakṣva katamastvamahaṃ tathā  ViP brāhmama uvācaityuktaḥ satvaraṃ tasya pragṛhya caramābubhau nidāghastvāha bhagavānācāryastvamṛbhurdhruvam  ViP nānyasyādvaitasaṃskārasaṃskṛtaṃ mānasaṃ tathā yathācāryasya tena tvāṃ manye prāptamahaṃ gurum  ViP ṛburuvācatavopadeśadānāya pūrvaśuśruṣaṇādṛtaḥ gurusnehādṛbhurnāma nidāgha samupāgataḥ  ViP tadetadupadiṣṭaṃ te saṃkṣepeṇa mahāmate paramārthasārabhūtaṃ yad advaitam aśeṣataḥ  ViP brāhma uvācaevamuktvā yayau vidvānnidāghaṃ sa ṛbhurguruḥ nidāghopyupadeśena tenādvaitaparobhavat  ViP sarvabhūtānyabhedena dadṛśe sa tadātmanaḥ yathā brahmaparo muktimavāpa paramāṃ dvijaḥ  ViP tathā tvamapi dharmajña tulyotmarīpubāndhavaḥ bhava sargagataṃ jānannatmānamavanīpate  ViP sitanīlā dibhedena yathaikaṃ dṛśyate nabhaḥ bhrāntadṛṣṭibhir ātmāpi tathaikaḥ sanpṛthakpṛthak  ViP ekaḥ samastaṃ yadihāsti kiñcittadacyuto nāsti paraṃ tatonyat so haṃ sa ca tvaṃ ca sarvametadātmasvarūpaṃ tyaja bhedamoham  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaitīritastena sa rājavarstatyāja bhedaṃ paramārthadṛṣṭiḥ sa cāpi jātismaraṇāptabodhastatraiva janmanyapavargamāpa  ViP iti bharatanarendrasāravṛttaṃ kathayati yaś ca śṛṇoti bhaktiyuktaḥ sa vimalamatireti nātma mohaṃ bhavati ca saṃsaraṇeṇu muktiyogyaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumadṛdvidṛṣoḍaśo dhyāyaḥ iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe dvitīyoṃśaḥ samāptaḥatha śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhyaśrīdharīya vyākhyādvayopete tṛtīyoṃśaḥ prārabhyateśrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥmaitreya uvācakathitā gurūṇāsamyagbhūsamudrādisaṃsthitiḥ sūryādināṃ ca saṃsthānaṃ jyotiṣāṃ cātivistarāt  ViP devādīnāṃ tathā sṛṣṭirṛṣīṇāṃ cāpi varṇitā cāturvarṇyasya cotpattistiryagyonigatasya ca  ViP dhruvaprahlādacaritaṃ vistarācca tvayoditam manvantarāṇyaśeṣāṇi śrotumicchāmyanukramāt  ViP manvantarādhipāṃścaiva śakadevapurogamān bhavatā kathitānetāñchrotumicchāmyahaṃ guro  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaatītānāgatānīha yāni manvantarāṇi vai tānyahaṃ bhavataḥ samyaklathayāmi yathā kramam  ViP svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṃ paraḥ svārociṣas tathā uttamastāmasaścaiva raivataścākṣuṣas tathā  ViP ṣaḍete manavotītāḥsāṃprataṃ tu raveḥsutaḥ vaivasvateyaṃ yastvetatmaptamaṃ vartatentaram  ViP svāyaṃbhuvaṃ tu kathitaṃ kalpādāvantaraṃ mayā devāḥ saptarṣayaś caiva yathāvat kathitā mayā  ViP ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi manoḥsvārociṣasya tu manvantarādhipānsamyagdevarṣiṃstatsutāṃs tathā  ViP pārāvatāḥ satuṣitā devāḥ svārociṣe ntare vipaścattatra devendro maitreyāsīnmahābalaḥ  ViP ūrjastaṃbhas tathā prāṇovātortha pṛṣabhas tathā nirayaś ca parīvāṃś ca tatra saptarṣayo bhavan  ViP caitrakiṃpuruṣādyāś ca sutāḥsvārociṣasya tu dvitīyametadvyākhyātamantaraṃ śṛṇu cottamam  ViP tṛtīyepyantare brahmannuttamo nāma yo manuḥ suśāntirnāma devendro maitreyāsītsutāñchṛṇu  ViP sudhāmānas tathā satyā japāścātha pratardanāḥ vaśavartiś ca pañcaite gaṇā dvādaśakāḥsmṛtāḥ  ViP vasiṣṭhatanayā hyote sapta saptarṣayobhavan ajaḥ paraśudīptādyāstathottamamanoḥsutāḥ  ViP tāmasasyāntare devāḥsupārā harayas tathā satyāś ca sudhiyaścaiva saptaviṃśatikā gaṇāḥ  ViP śivirindras tathā cāsīcchatayajñopalakṣamaḥ saptarṣa yaś ca ye teṣāṃ teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu  ViP jyotirdhāmā puthuḥ kātyaścaitrognirdhanakas tathā pīvaraścarṣayo hyete sapta tatrāpi cāntare  ViP naraḥ khyātiḥ keturūpo jānujaṅghādayas tathā putrāstu tāmasasyāsannājānaḥsumahābalāḥ  ViP pañcame vāpi maitreya raivato nāma nāmataḥ manurvibhuś ca tatrendro devāṃścātrāntare śṛṇu  ViP amitābhā bhūtarayā vaikuṇṭhāḥsusamedhasaḥ ete devagaṇāstatra caturdaśa caturdaśa  ViP hiraṇyaromā vedāśrirūrdhvabāhustathāvaraḥ vedabāhuḥsudhāmā ca parjanyaś ca mahāmuniḥ ete saptarṣayo vipra tatrāsanraivatentare  ViP balabandhuś ca saṃbhāvyaḥsatyakādyāś ca tatsutāḥ narendrāś ca mahāvīryā babhūvurmunisattama  ViP svārociṣaścauttamaś ca tāmaso raivatas tathā priyavratānvayā hyete catvāro manavaḥsmṛtāḥ  ViP viṣṇumārādhya tapasā sa rājarṣiḥ priyavrataḥ manvantarādhipānetāllaṃbdhavānātmavaṃśajān  ViP ṣaṣṭhe manvaṃrate cāsīccākṣuṣākhyas tathā manuḥ manojavastathaivendro devānapi nibodha me  ViP āpyāḥ prasūtā bhavyāś ca pṛthukāścā divaukasaḥ mahānubhāvā lakhāś ca pañcaite hyaṣṭakā gaṇāḥ  ViP sumedhā virajāścaiva haviṣmānuttamo madhuḥ atināmā sahiṣṇuś ca saptāsanniti carṣayaḥ  ViP ūruḥ pūruḥ śatadhyumnapramukhāḥ sumahābalāḥ cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayo bhavan  ViP vivasvataḥsuto vipra śrāddhadevo mahādyutiḥ manuḥsaṃvartate dhīmān sāṃprataṃ saptamentare  ViP ādityavasurudrādyā devāścātra mahāmune purandarastathaivātra maitreya tridaśeśvaraḥ  ViP vaśiṣṭhaḥ kāśyapothātrirjamadagniḥsagautamaḥ viśvāmitrabharadvājau sapta saptarṣayo bhavan  ViP ikṣvākuś ca nṛgaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca nariṣyantaś ca vikhyāto nābhāgoriṣṭa eva ca  ViP karūṣaś ca pṛṣadhraś ca sumahāṃllokaviśrutaḥ manorvaivasvatasyaite nava putrāḥ sudhārmikāḥ  ViP viṣṇuśaktiranaupamyā sattvodriktā sthitau sthitā manvantareṣvaśeṣeṣu devatvenādhitiṣṭhati  ViP aṃśena tasyā jajñe sau yajñaḥsvāyaṃbhuventare ākūtyāṃ mānaso deva utpannaḥ prathamentare  ViP tataḥ punaḥ sa vai devaḥ prāpte svārociṣentare tuṣitāyāṃ samutpanno hyājiṣastuṣitaiḥ saha  ViP auttamapyantare devastuṣitastu punaḥsa vai satyāyāmabhavatsatyaḥ satyaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ  ViP tāmasasyāntare caiva saṃprāpto punareva hi haryāyāṃ haribhiḥ sārdha harireva babhūva ha  ViP raivatepyantare devaḥsaṃbhūtyāṃ mānaso hariḥ saṃbhūto raivataiḥ sārdha devair devavaro hariḥ  ViP cākṣuṣe cāntare devo vaikuṇṭhaḥ puruṣottamaḥ vikuṇṭhāyāmasau jajñe vaikuṇṭhair daivataiḥ saha  ViP manvantaretra saṃprāpte tathā vaivasvatedvija vāmanaḥ kāśyapādviṣṇuradityāṃ saṃbabhūva ha  ViP tribhiḥ kramair imāṃl lokāñ jitvā yena mahātmanā purandarāya trailokyaṃ dattaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam  ViP ityetāstanavastasya saptamanvantareṣu vai saptasvevābhavanvipra yābhiḥ saṃvardhitāḥ prajāḥ  ViP yasmād viṣṭamidaṃ viśvaṃ yasya śaktyā mahātmanaḥ tasmātsa procyate viṣṇurviśordhātoḥ praveśanāt  ViP sarve ca devā manavaḥsamastāḥsaptarṣayo ye manusūnavaś ca indraścayo yaṃ tridaśeśabhūto viṣṇoraśoṣāstu vibhūtayastāḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe prathamo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācaproktānyetāni bhavatā sapta manvantarāṇi vai bhaviṣyāṇyapi viprarṣa mamākhyātuṃ tvamarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasūryasya patnī saṃjñābhūttanayā viśvakarmaṇaḥ manuryamo yamī caiva tadapatyāni vai mune  ViP asahantī tu sā bhartustejaśchāyāṃ yuyoja vai bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇe raṇyaṃsvayaṃ ca tapase yayau  ViP saṃjñeyamityathārkaś ca chāyāyāmātmajatrayam śanaiścaraṃ manuṃ cānyaṃ tapatīṃ cāpyajājanat  ViP chāyāsaṃjñā dadau śāpaṃ yamāya kupitā yadā tadānyeyamasau buddhirityāsīdyamasūryayoḥ  ViP tato vivasvānākhyātāṃ tayaivāraṇyasaṃsthitām samādhidṛṣṭyādadṛśe tāmaśvāṃ tapasi sthitām  ViP vājirūpadharaḥ sotha tasyāṃ devāvathāśvinau janayāmāsa revantaṃ retasoṃte ca bhāskaraḥ  ViP āninye ca punaḥ saṃjñāṃ svasthānaṃ bhagavān raviḥ tejasaḥ śamanaṃ cāsya viśvakarmā cakāra ha  ViP bhramamāropya sūryaṃ tu tasya tejoniśātanam kṛtavānaṣṭamaṃ bhāgaṃ sa vyaśātayadavyayam  ViP yattasmādvaiṣṇavaṃ tejasśātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā jājvalyamānamapatattadbhūmau munisattama  ViP tvaṣṭaiva tejasā tena viṣṇoścakramakalpayat triśūlaṃ caiva śarvasya śibikāṃ dhanadasya ca  ViP śaktiṃ guhasya devānāmanyeṣāṃ ca yadāyudham tatsarvaṃ tejasā tena viśvakarmā vyavardhayat  ViP chāyāsaṃjñāsuto yosau dvitīyaḥ kathito manuḥ pūrvajasyāsavarṇosau sāvarṇistena kathyate  ViP tasya manvantaraṃ hyotatsāvarṇikamathāṣṭamam tacchṛṇuṣva mahābhāga bhaviṣyatkathayāmi te  ViP sāvarṇistu manuryosau maitreya bhavitā tataḥ sutapāścāmitābhāś ca mukhyāścāpi tathā surāḥ  ViP teṣāṃ gaṇāś ca devānāmekaiko viṃśakaḥ smṛtaḥ saptarṣinapi vakṣyāmi bhaviṣyānmunisattama  ViP dīptimān gālavo rāmaḥ kṛpo droṇis tathā paraḥ matputraś ca tathā vyāsa ṛṣyaśṛṅgaś ca saptamaḥ  ViP viṣṇu prasādādanaghaḥ pātālāntaragocaraḥ virocanasutasteṣāṃ balirindro bhaviṣyati  ViP virajāścorvarīvāṃś ca nirmokādyāstathāpare sāvarṇestu manoḥ putrā bhaviṣyanti nareśvarāḥ  ViP navamo dakṣasāvarṇirbhaviṣyati mune manuḥ  ViP pārā marīcigarbhāś ca sudharmāṇas tathā tridhā bhaviṣyanti tathā devā hyokaiko dvādaśo gaṇaḥ  ViP teṣāmidro mahāvīryo bhaviṣyatyadbhuto dvija  ViP savano dyutimān bhavyo vasurmedhātithis tathā jyotiṣmān saptamaḥ satyastatraite ca maharṣayaḥ  ViP dhṛtaketurdīptiketuḥ pañcahastanirāmayau pṛthuśravādyāś ca tathā dakṣamāvarṇikātmajāḥ  ViP dasamo brahmasāvarmirbhaviṣyati mune manuḥ sūdhāmāno viśuddhāś ca śatasaṃkhyās tathā surāḥ  ViP teṣām indraś ca bhavitā śāntir nāma mahābalaḥ saptarṣayo bhaviṣyanti ye tathā tāñchṛṇuṣva ha  ViP haviṣmānsukṛtaḥsatyastapomūrtistathāparaḥ nābhāgo pratimaujāścasatyaketustathaiva ca  ViP sukṣetraścottamaujāścabhūriṣeṇādayo daśa brahmasāvarṇiputrāstu rakṣiṣyanti vasuṃdharām  ViP ekādaśaś ca bhavitā dharmasāvarṇiko manuḥ  ViP vihaṅgamāḥ kāmāgamā nirvāṇā ṛṣayas tathā gaṇāstvete tadā mukhyā devānāṃ ca bhaviṣyatām aikaikastriṃśakasteṣāṃ gaṇaścendraś ca vai pṛṣā  ViP niḥ svaraścāgnitejāś ca vapuṣmānghaṇirāruṇiḥ haviṣmānanaghaścaiva bhāvyāḥ saptarṣayas tathā  ViP sarvatragasśudharmā ca devānīkādayas tathā bhaviṣyanti manostasya tanayāḥ pṛtiviśvarāḥ  ViP rudraputrastu sāvarṇirbhavitā dvādaśo manuḥ ṛkudhāmā ca tatredro bhavitā śṛṇu me surān  ViP haritā rohitā devās tathā mumanaso dvija sukarmāṇaḥ surāpāś ca daśakāḥ pañca vai gaṇāḥ  ViP tapasvī sutapāścaiva tapomūrtistaporatiḥ tapodhṛtirdyutiścānyaḥ saptamastu tapodhanaḥ saptarṣayastvime tasya putrānapi nibodha me  ViP devavānupadevaś ca devaśreṣṭhādayas tathā manostasya mahāvīryā bhaviṣyanti mahānṛpāḥ  ViP trayodaśo rucirnāmā bhaviṣyati mune manaḥ  ViP sutrāmāṇaḥ sukarmāṇaḥ sudharmāṇastathāmarāḥ trayastriṃśadvibhedāsta devānāṃ yatra vai gaṇāḥ  ViP divaspatirmahāvīryasteṣāmindrobhiviṣyati  ViP nirmohastattvadarśi ca niṣprakaṃpyo nirutsukaḥ dhṛtimānavyayaścānyaḥsaptamaḥsutapā muniḥ saptarṣayastvamī tasya putrānapi nibodhe me  ViP citrasenavicitrādyā bhaviṣyanti mahīkṣikaḥ  ViP bhaumaścaturdaśaścātra maitreya bhavitā manaḥ śucirindraḥ suragaṇastatra pañca śṛṇuṣva tān  ViP cākṣuṣāś ca pavitrāś ca kaniṣṭhā bhrājikās tathā vācavṛddhaś ca vai devāḥsaptarṣīnapi me śṛṇu  ViP agnibāhuḥ śuciḥ śukro māgadhognīdhra eva ca yuktas tathā jitaścānyo manuputrānataḥ śṛṇu  ViP ūrugaṃbhīrabuddhyādyā manostasya sutā nṛpāḥ kathitā muniśārdula pālayiṣyanti ye mahīm  ViP caturyugānte vedānāṃ jāyate kila viplavaḥ pravartayanti tānetya bhuvaṃ saptarṣayo divaḥ  ViP kṛtekṛte smṛter vipra praṇetā jāyate manuḥ devā yajñabhujaste tu yāvanmanvantaraṃ tu tat  ViP bhavanti ye manoḥ putrā yāvanmanvaṃrataṃ tu taiḥ tadanvayodbhavaiś caiva tāvadbhūḥ parīpālyate  ViP manuḥsaptarṣayo devā bhūpālāś ca manoḥ sutāḥ manvantare bhavantyete śakraścaivādhikārimaḥ  ViP caturdaśabhir etais tu gatair manvantarair dvija sahasrayugaparyataḥ kalpo niḥśeṣa ucyate  ViP tāvatpramāṇā ca niśā tato bhavati sattama brahmarūpadharaḥ śete śeṣāhāvaṃbusaṃplave  ViP trailokyamakhilaṃ grastvā bhagavānādikṛdvibhuḥ svamāyāsaṃstito vipra sarvabhūto janārdanaḥ  ViP tataḥ prabuddho bhagavān yathā pūrvaṃ tathā punaḥ sṛṣṭiṃ karotyavyayātmā kalpekalpe rajogumaḥ  ViP manavo bhūbhujaḥseṃdrā devāḥsaptarṣayas tathā sāttvikoṃśaḥ sthitikaro jagato dvijasattama  ViP caduryugopyasau viṣṇuḥ sthitivyāpāralakṣamaḥ yugavyavasthāṃ kurute tathā maitreya tacchṛṇu  ViP kṛte yuge paraṃ jñānaṃ kapilādisvarūpadhṛk dadāti sarvabhūtātmā sarvabhūtahite rataḥ  ViP cakravartisvarūpeṇa tretāyāmapi sa prabhūḥ duṣṭānāṃ nigraha kurvanparipāti jagattrayam  ViP vedamekaṃ caturbhedaṃ kṛtvā śākhāśatair vibhuḥ karoti bahulaṃ bhūyo vedavyāsasvarūpadhṛk  ViP vedāṃstu dvāpare vyasya kalerante punarhariḥ kalkisvarūpī durvṛttanmārge sthāpayati prabhuḥ  ViP evametajjagatsarvaṃ śaśvatpāti karoti ca hanti cānteṣvanantātmā nāstyasmavdyatireki yat  ViP bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca sarvabhūtānmahātmanaḥ tadatrānyatra vā vipra sadbhāvaḥ kathitastava  ViP manvantarāṇyaśeṣāṇi kathitāni mayā tavā manvantarādhipāṃścaiva kimanyatkathayāmi te  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe dvitīyo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācajñātametanmayā tvatto yathā sarvamidaṃ jagat viṣṇurviṣṇo viṣṇutaś ca na paraṃ vidyate tataḥ  ViP etattu śrotumicchāmi vyastā vedā mahātmanā vedavyāsasvarūpeṇa yathā tena yugeyuge  ViP yasminyasminyuge vyāso yo ya āsīnmahāmune tantamācakṣva bhagavañchāśābhedāṃś ca me vada  ViP śrīparāśara uvācavedadrumasya maitreya śākhābhedāḥsahasraśaḥ na śakto vistarādvaktuṃ sekṣepeṇa śṛṇuṣva tam  ViP dvāparedvāpare viṣṇurvyāsarūpī mahāmune vedamekaṃ subahudhā kurute jagato hitaḥ  ViP vīryaṃ tejo balaṃ cālpaṃ manuṣyāṇāmavekṣya ca hitāya sarvabhūtānāṃ vedabhedānkaroti saḥ  ViP yayāsau kurute tanvā vedamekaṃ pṛthak prabhuḥ vedavyāsābhidhānā tu sā ca mūrtirmadhrudviṣaḥ  ViP yasminmanvaṃrate vyāsā yeye syustānnibodha me yathā ca bhedaḥ śākhānāṃ vyāsena kriyate mune  ViP aṣṭaviṃśatikṛtvo vai vedo vyasto saharṣibhiḥ vaivasvatentare tasmindvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ  ViP vedavyāsā vyatītā ye hyaṣṭarviśati sattama caturdhā yaiḥ kṛto vedo dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ  ViP dvāpare prathame vyastaḥsvayaṃ vedaḥ svayaṃbhuvā dvitīye dvāpare caiva vedavyāsaḥ prajāpati  ViP tṛtīye cośanā vyāsaścaturthe ca bṛhaspatiḥ savitā pañcame vyāsaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyuḥ smṛtaḥ prabhuḥ  ViP saptame ca tathaivendro vasiṣṭhaścāṣṭame smṛtaḥ sārasvataś ca navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ  ViP ekādaśe tu triśikho bharadvājastataḥ paraḥ trayodaśe cāntarikṣo varṇī cāpi caturdaśe  ViP trayyāruṇaḥ pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe tu dhanañjayaḥ kratuñjayaḥ saptadaśe tadūrdhvaṃ ca jayaḥsmṛtaḥ  ViP tato vyāso bharadvājo bharadvājācca gautamaḥ gautamāduttaro vyāso haryātmā yobhidhīyate  ViP atha haryātmanonte ca smṛto vājaśravāmuniḥ somaśuṣkāyaṇas tasmāt tṛṇabinduriti smṛtaḥ  ViP ṛkṣobhūdbhārgavastasmādvālmīkiryobhidhīyate tasmādasmatpitā śaktirvyāsastasmādahaṃ mune  ViP jātukarṇobhavanmattaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanastataḥ aṣṭaviṃśatirityete vedavyāsāḥ purātanāḥ  ViP eko vedaścaturdhā tu taiḥ kṛto dvāparādiṣu  ViP bhaviṣye dvāpare cāpi drauṇirvyāso bhaviṣyati vyatīte mama putresmin kṛṣṇadvaipāyane mune  ViP dhruvamekākṣaraṃ brahma om ityeva vyavasthitam bṛhatvādbṛṃhaṇatvācca tadbrahyotyabhidhīyate  ViP praṇavāvasthitaṃ nityaṃ bhūrbhuvaḥsvaritīryate ṛgyajuḥsāmātharvāṇo yattasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ  ViP jagataḥ pralayotpattyoryattatkāraṇasaṃjñitam mahataḥ paramaṃ guhyaṃ tasmai subrahmaṇe namaḥ  ViP agādhāpāramakṣayyaṃ jagatsaṃmohanālayam svaprakāśapravṛttibhyāṃ puruṣārthaprayojanam  ViP saṃkhyajñānavatāṃ niṣṭhā gatiḥ śamadamātmanām yattadavyaktamamṛtaṃ pravṛttirbrahma śāśvatam  ViP pradhānamātmayoniś ca guhāsaṃsthaṃ ca śabdyate avibhāgaṃ tathā śukramakṣayaṃ bahudhātmakam  ViP paramabrahmaṇe tasmai nityameva namonamaḥ yadrūpaṃ vāsudevasya paramātmasvarūpiṇaḥ  ViP etadbrahma tridhā bhedamabhedamapi sa prabhuḥ sarvabhedeṣvabhedosaubhidyate bhinnabuddhibhiḥ  ViP sa ṛṅmayaḥsāmamayaḥ sarvātmā sa yajurmayaḥ ṛgyajuḥsāmasārātmā sa evātmā śarīriṇām  ViP sa bhidyate vedamayaḥsvavedaṃ karoti bhedair bahubhiḥ saśākham śākhāpraṇetā sa samastaśākhājñānasvarūpo bhagavānasaṃgaḥ  ViP iti kṣiviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe tṛtīyo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaādyo vedaścatuṣpādaḥ kṛtaḥ sāhasrasaṃmitaḥ tato daśagumaḥ kṛtsno yajñoyaṃ sarvakāmadhuk  ViP tatotra matsuto vyāso aṣṭaviṃśatimentare vedamekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturdhā vyabhajatprabhuḥ  ViP yathā ca tena vai vyastā vedabyāsena dhīmatā vedās tathā samastais tair vyastā vyastais tathā mayā  ViP tadanenaiva vedānāṃ śākhābhedāndvijottama caturyugeṣu paṭhitānsamasteṣvavadhāraya  ViP kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaṃ vyāsaṃ viddhi nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ko hyanyo bhuvi maitreya mahābhāratakṛdbhavet  ViP tena vyastā yathā vedā matputreṇa mahātmanā dvāpare hy atra maitreya tasmiñ śṛṇu yathātatham  ViP brahmaṇā codito vyāso vedānvyastuṃ pracakrame atha śiṣyānprajagrāha caturo vedapāragān  ViP ṛgvedapāṭhakaṃ pailaṃ jagrāha sa mahāmuniḥ vaiśaṃpāyananāmānaṃ yajurvedasya cāgrahīt  ViP jaiminiṃ sāmavedasya tathaivātharvavedavit sumantustasya śiṣyobhūdvedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ  ViP romaharṣaṇanāmānaṃ mahābuddhiṃ mahāmuniḥ sūtaṃ jagrāha śiṣyaṃ sa itihāsapurāṇayoḥ  ViP eka āsīdyajurvedastaṃ caturdhā vyakalpayat cāturhetramabhūttasmiṃstena yajñamathākarot  ViP ādhvaryavaṃ yajurbhis tu ṛgbhir hotraṃ tathā muniḥ audgātraṃ sāmābhiścakre brahmatvaṃ cāpyatharvabhiḥ  ViP tataḥsa ṛca uddhṛtya ṛgvedaṃ kṛtavānmuniḥ yajṛṃṣi ca yajurvedaṃ sāmavedaṃ ca sāmābhaḥ  ViP rājñāṃ cātharvavedena sarvakarmāṇi ca prabhuḥ kārayāmāsa maitreya brahmatvaṃ ca yathāsthiti  ViP soyameko yathā vedastarustena pṛthakkṛtaḥ caturdhātha tato jātaṃ vedapādapakānanam  ViP bibheda prathamaṃ vipra pailo ṛgvedapādapam indrapramitaye prādādbāṣkalāya ca saṃhite  ViP caturdhā sa vibhedātha bāṣkalopi ca saṃhitām bodhādibhyo dadau tāś ca śiṣyebhyaḥ samahāmuniḥ  ViP bodhyāgnimāḍhakau tadūdyājñavalkyaparāśarau pratiśākhāstu śākhāyāstasyāste jagṛhurmune  ViP indrapramitirekāṃ tu saṃhitāṃ svasūtaṃ tataḥ māṇḍukeyaṃ mahātmānaṃ maitreyādhyāpayattadā  ViP tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyebhyaḥ putraśiṣyakramādyayau  ViP vedamitrastu śākalyaḥ saṃhitāṃ tāmadhītavān cakāra saṃhitāḥ pañca śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau ca tāḥ  ViP tasya śiṣyāstu ye pañca teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu mudgalo gomakhaścaiva vātsyaḥ śālīya eva ca śarīraḥ pañcamaścāsīnmaitreya sumahāmatiḥ  ViP saṃhitātritayaṃ cakre śākapūrṇastathetaraḥ niruktamakarottadūccaturthaṃ munisattama  ViP kraiñco vaitālikastadvadbalākaś ca mahāmuniḥ niruktaś ca caturthobhūdvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ  ViP ityetāḥ pratiśākhābhyo hyanuśākhā dvijottama bāṣkalaścāparāstistraḥsaṃhitāḥ kṛtavāndvija śiṣyaḥ kālāyanirgārgyastṛtīyaś ca kathājapaḥ  ViP ityetā bahvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravartitāḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśecaturtho dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācayajurvetadarosśākhāḥsaptaviṃśanmahāmuniḥ vaiśaṃpāyananāmāso vyāsaśiṣyaścakāra vai  ViP śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāś ca jagṛhustepyanukramāt  ViP yājñavalkyastu tatrābhūdbāhyarātasuto dvija śiṣyaḥ paramadharmajño guruvṛttiparaḥsadā  ViP ṛṣiryodya mahāmeroḥ samāje nāgamiṣyati tasya vai saptarātrāttu brahmahattyā bhaviṣyati  ViP pūrvamevaṃ munigaṇaiḥ samayo yaḥ kṛto dvija vaiśaṃpāyana ekastu taṃ vyatikrāntavāṃstadā  ViP svastrīyaṃ bālakaṃ sotha padā spṛṣṭamatāḍayat  ViP śiṣyānāha sa bhoḥ śiṣyā brahmahattyāpahaṃ vratam caradhvaṃ matkṛte sarve na vicāryamidaṃ tathā  ViP athāha yājñavalkyastu kim ebhir bhagavan dvijaiḥ kleśitair alpatejobhiścāriṣyehamidaṃ vratam  ViP tataḥ kruddho guruḥ prāha yājñavalkyaṃ mahāmunim mucyatāṃ yattvayādhītaṃ matto viprāvamānaka  ViP nistejaso vadasyenānyattvaṃ brāhmaṇaṃpuṅgavān tena śiṣyeṇa nārthosti mamājñābhaṅgakāriṇā  ViP yājñavalkyastataḥ prāha bhaktyaitat te mayoditam mamāpyalaṃ tvayādhītaṃ yanmayā tadidaṃ dvija  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityukto rudhirāktāni sarūpāṇi yajūṃṣisaḥ chardayitvā dadau tasmai yayau sa svecchayā muni  ViP yajūṃṣyatha visṛṣṭāni yājñavalkyena vai dvija jagṛhustittirā bhūtvā taittirīyāstu te tataḥ  ViP brahmahattyāvrataṃ cīrṇaṃ guruṇā coditais tu taiḥ cākrurādhvaryavaṃ te tu caraṇānmunisattama  ViP yājñavalkyopi maitreya prāṇāyāmaparāyaṇaḥ tṛṣṭāva prayataḥsūryaṃ yajūṃṣyabhilaṣaṃstataḥ  ViP yājñavalkya uvācanamaḥ savitre dvārāya mukter amitatejase ṛgyajuḥsāmabhūtāya trayīdhāmne ca te namaḥ  ViP namognīṣomabhūtāya jagataḥ kāraṇātmane bhāskarāya paraṃ tejaḥsauṣumṇarucibibhrate  ViP kalākāṣṭhānimeṣādikālajñānātmarūpiṇe dhyeyāya viṣṇurūpāya paramākṣararūpiṇe  ViP bibharti yaḥsuragaṇānāpyāyenduṃ svaraśmibhiḥ svadhāmṛtena ca pitṝṃs tasmai tṛptyātmane namaḥ  ViP himāṃbugharmavṛṣṭīnāṃ kartā bhartā ca yaḥ prabhuḥ tasmai trikālarūpāya namaḥsūryāyavedhase  ViP apahanti tabho yaś ca jagatosya jagatpatiḥ tasya dhāmadharo devo namastasmai vivasvate  ViP satkarmayogyo na jano naivāpaḥ śuddhikāraṇam yasminnanudite tasmai namo devāya bhāsvate  ViP spṛṣṭo yadaṃśubhir lokaḥ kriyāyogyo hi jāyate pavitrakāraṇātmāya tasmai śuddhātmane namaḥ  ViP namaḥ savitre sūryāya bhāskarāya vivasvate ādityāyādibhūtāya devādīnāṃ namo namaḥ  ViP hiraṇmayaṃ rathaṃ yasya ketavomṛtavājinaḥ vahanti bhuvanālokacakṣuṣaṃ taṃ namāmyaham  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityevamādibhis tena stūyamānaḥsa vai raviḥ vājirūpadharaḥ prāha vrīyatāmiti vāñchitam  ViP yājñavalkyastadā prāha praṇipatya divākaram yajūṃṣi tāni me dehi yāni saṃti na me gurau  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevamukto dadau tasmai yajūṃṣi bhagavānraviḥ ayātayāmasaṃjñāni yāni vetti na tadguruḥ  ViP yajūṃṣi yair adhītāni tāni viprair dhijottama vājinaste samākhyātāḥ sūryopyaśvobhavadyataḥ  ViP śākhābhedāstu teṣāṃ vai daśa pañca ca vājinām kāṇvādyāḥsumahābhāgā yājñavalkyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe pañcamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācasāmavedataroḥ śākhā vyāsaśiṣyasya jauminiḥ krameṇa yena maitreya vibhedaśṛṇu tanmama  ViP susaṃtustasya putrobhūtsūtvānaścābhavatsutaḥ adhītavantau caikaikāṃ saṃhitāṃ tau māhamatī  ViP sahasrasaṃhitābhedaṃ sukarmātatsutastataḥ cakāra taṃ ca tacchiṣyau jagṛhāte mahāvratau  ViP hiraṇyanābhaḥ kausalyaḥ pauṣpiṃjiś ca dvijottama udīcyāḥsāmagāḥ śiṣyāstasya pañcaśataṃ smṛtāḥ  ViP hiraṇyanābhāttāvatyaḥsaṃhitā yair dvijottamaiḥ gṛhītāstepi cocyante paṇḍitaiḥ prācyasāmagāḥ  ViP lokākṣirnaidhamiścaiva kakṣivāṃllāṅgalis tathā pauṣpijiśiṣyāstadbhedaiḥ saṃhitā bahulīkṛtāḥ  ViP hiraṇyanābhaśiṣyastu caturviśatisaṃhitāḥ provāca kṛtanāmāsau śiṣyebhyaś ca mahāmuniḥ  ViP taiś cāpi sāmavedo sau śākhābhir bahulīkṛtaḥ atharvaṇāmatho vakṣye saṃhitānāṃ samuccayam atharvavedaṃ sa muniḥsusaṃturamitadyutiḥ  ViP śiṣyamadhyāpayāmāsa kabandhaṃ so pi taṃ dvidhā kṛtvā tudevadarsāya tathā pathyāya dattavān  ViP devadarśasya śiṣyāstu medhobrahmabalis tathā śaulkāyaniḥ pippalādastathānyo dvijasattama  ViP pathyasyāpi trayaḥ śiṣyāḥ kṛtā yair dvija saṃhitāḥ jābāliḥ kumudādiś ca tṛtīyaḥ śaunako dvija  ViP śaunakastu dvidhā kṛtvā dadāvekāṃ tu babhrave dvitīyāṃ saṃhitāṃ prādātsaindhavāya ya saṃjñine  ViP saindhavānmujikeśaś ca dvedhabhinnāstridhā punaḥ nakṣatrakalpo vedānāṃ saṃhitānāṃ tathaiva ca  ViP caturthaḥsyādāṅgirasaḥ śāntikalpaścapañcamaḥ śreṣṭhāstvatharvaṇāmete saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ  ViP ākhyānaiś cāpy upākhyānair gāthābhiḥ kalpaśuddhibhiḥ purāṇasaṃhitāṃ cakrepurāṇārthaviśāradaḥ  ViP prakhyāto vyāsaśiṣyobhūtsūto vai romaharṣaṇaḥ purāmasaṃhitāṃ tasmai dadau vyāso mahāmatiḥ  ViP sumatiścāgnivarcāś ca mitrāyuḥśāṃsapāyanaḥ akṛtavraṇasāvarṇiṣpaṭśiṣyāstasya cābhavan  ViP kāśyapaḥ saṃhitākartā sāvarṇiḥ śāṃsapāyanaḥ romaharṣāṇikācānyā tisṝṇāṃ mūlasaṃhitā  ViP catuṣṭayena bhedena saṃhitānāmidaṃ mune  ViP ādyaṃ sarvapurāṇānāṃ purāṇaṃ brāhmamucyate aṣṭādaśapurāṇāni purāṇajñāḥ pracakṣate  ViP brāhmaṃ pādmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śaivaṃ bhāgavataṃ tathā tathānyaṃ nāradīyaṃ ca mārkaṇḍeyaṃ ca saptamam  ViP āgneyamaṣṭamaṃ caiva bhaviṣyannavamaṃ smṛtam daśamaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ laiṅgamekādaśaṃ smṛtam  ViP vārāhaṃ dvādaśaṃ caiva skāndaṃ cātra trayodaśam caturdaśaṃvāmanaṃ ca kaurmaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā mātsyaṃ ca gāruḍaṃ caiva brahmāṇḍaṃ ca tataḥ param mahāpurāṇānyetāni hyaṣṭādaśa mahāmune  ViP tathā copa purāṇāni munibhiḥ kathitāni ca sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṃśamanvantarāṇi ca sarveṣveteṣu kathyante vaṃśānucārītaṃ ca yat  ViP yadetattava maitreya purāṇaṃ kathyate mayā etadvaiṣṇavasaṃjñaṃ vai pādmasyasamanantaram  ViP sarge ca pratisarge ca vaṃśamanvantarādiṣu kathyate bhagavān viṣṇur aśeṣeṣv iva sattama  ViP aṅgāni vedāścatvāro mīmāṃsānyāyavistaraḥ purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vidyā hyetāścaturdaśa  ViP āyurvedodhanurvedo gāndharvaścaiva te trayaḥ arthaśāstraṃ caturthaṃ tu vidya hyaṣṭādaśaiva tāḥ  ViP jñeyā brahmarṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ tebhyo devarṣayaḥ punaḥ rājarṣayaḥ punastebhya ṛṣiprakṛtayastrayaḥ  ViP iti śākhāḥsamākhyātaḥ śākhābhedāstathaiva ca kartāraścaiva śākhānāṃ bhedahetustathoditaḥ  ViP sarvamanvantareṣvevaṃ śākhābhedāḥsamāḥ smṛtāḥ  ViP prājāpatyā śrutirnityā tadvikalpāstvime dvija  ViP etatte kathitaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭohamihatvayā maitreya vedasaṃbandhaḥ kimanyatkathayāmi te  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśeḥṣṭhodhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācayathā vatkathitaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭosiṃ mayā guro śrotumicchāmyahaṃ tvekaṃ tadbhavānprabravītu me  ViP saptadvīpāni pātālavidhayaś ca mahāmune spatalokāś ca yentasthā brahmāṇḍasyāsya sarvataḥ  ViP sthūlaiḥ sūkṣmais tathā sūkṣmasūkṣmāsūkṣmataraiḥ smṛtā sthūlātsthūlataraiś caiva sarvaṃ prāṇibhir āvṛtam  ViP aṅgulasyāṣṭabhāgopi na sosti munisattama vasaṃti prāṇino yatra karmabandhanibandhanāḥ  ViP sarve caite vaśaṃ yānti yamasya bhagavan kila āyuṣonte tathā yānti yātanāstatpracoditāḥ  ViP yātanābhyaḥ paribhraṣṭā devādyāsvatha yoniṣu jantavaḥ parivartante śāstrāṇāmeṣa nirṇayaḥ  ViP sohamicchāmi tacchrotuṃ yamasya vaśavartinaḥ na bhavantinarā yena tatkarma kathayasva me  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaayameva mune praśro nakulena mahātmanā pṛṣṭaḥ pitāmahaḥ prāha bhīṣmo yattacchṛṇuṣva me  ViP bhīṣṇa uvācapurā mamāgato vatsa sakhā kāliṅgako dvijaḥ sa māmuvāca praṣṭo vai mayā jātismaro muniḥ  ViP tenākhyātamidaṃ sarvamitthaṃ caitadbhaviṣyati tathā ca tadabhūdvatsa yathoktaṃ tena dhīmatā  ViP sa pṛṣṭaś ca mayā bhūyaḥ śraddadhānena vai dvijaḥ yadyadāha na taddṛṣṭamanyathā hi mayā kvacit  ViP ekadā tu mayā pṛṣṭametadyadbhavatoditam prāha kāliṅgako vipraḥsmṛtvā tasya munervacaḥ  ViP jātismareṇa kathito rahasyaḥ paramo mama yamakiṅkarayoryobhūtsaṃvādastaṃ bravīmi te  ViP kāliṅga uvācasvapuruṣamabhivīkṣya pāśahastaṃ vadati yamaḥ kila tasya karṇamūle parihara madhusūdanaprapannānprabhurahamanyanṛṇāmavaiṣṇavānām  ViP ahamamaravarārcitena dhātrā yama iti lokahitāhite niyuktaḥ hariguruvaśagosmi na svatantraḥ prabhavati saṃyamane mamāpi viṣṇuḥ  ViP kaṇṭa kamukuṭakarṇikādibhedaiḥ kanakamabhedamapīṣyate yathaikam surapaśumanujādikalpanābhir harir akhilābhir udīryate tathaikaḥ  ViP kṣititalaparamāṇavonilānte punarupayānti yathaikatāṃ dharitryāḥ surapaśumanujādayastathānte guṇakalaṣeṇa sanātanena tena  ViP harimamaravarārcitāṅghripadmaṃpraṇamati yaḥ paramārthato hi martyaḥ tamapagatasamastapāpabandhaṃ vraja parihṛtya yathāgnimājyasiktam  ViP iti yamavacanaṃ niśamya pāśī yama puruṣastamuvāca dharmarājam kathaya mama vibho samastadhāturbhavati hareḥ khalu yādṛśosya bhaktaḥ  ViP yama uvācana calati nijavarmadharmato yaḥsamamatirātmasuhṛdvipakṣapakṣe na harati na ca hanti kiñciducchaiḥ sthitamanasaṃ tamavehi viṣṇubhaktam  ViP kalikalupamalena yasya nātmā vimalamatemalinīkṛtastamenam manasi kṛtajanārdanaṃ manaṣyaṃ satatamavehi hareratīva bhaktam  ViP kanakamapi rahasyavekṣya buddhyā tṛṇamiva yaḥsamavaiti vai parasvam bhavati ca bhagavatyananyacetāḥ puruṣavaraṃ tamavehi viṣṇubhaktam  ViP sphaṭikagiriśilāmalaḥ kva viṣṇurmanasi nṛṇāṃ kva ca matsarādidoṣaḥ na hi tuhinamayūkharaśmipuñje bhavati hutāśanadīptijaḥ pratāpaḥ  ViP vimalamatiramatsaraḥ praśāntaḥ śucicaritokhilasattvamitrabhūtaḥ priyahitavacano stamānamāyo vasati sadā hṛdi tasya vāsudevaḥ  ViP vasati hṛdisanātane ca tasminbhavati pumāñjagatosya saumyarūpaḥ kṣitirasamatiramyamātmanontaḥ kathayati cārutayaiva sālapotaḥ  ViP yamaniyamavidhūta kalpaṣāṇāmanudinamacyutasaktamānasānām apagatamadamānamatsarāṇāṃ tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa mānavānām  ViP hṛdi yadi bhagavānanādirāste harirariśaṅkhagadādharovyātmā tadaghavighātakartṛbhinnaṃ bhavati kathaṃ sati cāndhakāramarke  ViP harati paradhanaṃ nihanti jantūnvadati tathā nṛtaniṣṭurāṇi yaś ca aśubhajanitaduramadasya puṃsaḥ kaluṣamaterhṛdi tasya nāstyanantaḥ  ViP na sahati parasaṃpadaṃ vinindāṃ kaluṣamatiḥ kurute satāmasādhuḥ nayajati na dadāti yaś ca saṃtaṃ manasi na tasya janārdano dhamasya  ViP paramasuhṛdibāndhave kalatre mutatanayāpitṛmātṛbhṛtyavarge śaṭhamatirupayāti yorthatṛṣṇāṃ tamadhamaceṣṭamavehi nāsya bhaktam  ViP aśubhamatirasatpravṛtti saktaḥsatatamanāryakuśīlasaṃgamattaḥ anudinakṛtapāpabandhayuktaḥ paruṣapaśurna hi vāsudevabhaktaḥ  ViP sakalamidamahaṃ ca vāsudevaḥ paramapumānparameśvaraḥsa ekaḥ iti matiracalābhavatyanante hṛdayagate vrajatānvihāya dūrāt  ViP kamalanayana vāsudeva viṣṇo dharaṇidharācyuta śaṅkhacakrapāṇe bhavaśaraṇamitirayanti ye vai tyaja bhaṭa dūratareṇa tānapāpān  ViP vasati manasi yasya sovyayātmā puruṣavarasya na tasya dṛṣṭipāte tava gatiratha vā mamāsti cakrapratihatavīryabalasya sonyalokyaḥ  ViP kāliṅga uvācaiti nijabhaṭaśāsanāya devo ravita nayasya kilāha dharmarājaḥ mama kathitamidaṃ ca tena tubhyaṃ kuruvara samyagidaṃ mayāpi coktam  ViP śrībhīṣma uvācanakulaitanmamākhyātaṃ pūrvaṃ tena dvijanmanā kaliṅgadeśādeśyetya prītena sumahātmanā  ViP mayāpyetadyathānyāyaṃ samyagvatsa tavoditam yathā viṣṇumṛtenānyattrāṇāṃ saṃsārasāgare  ViP kiṅkarāḥ pāśadaṇḍāś ca na yamo na ca yātanāḥ samarthāstasya yasyātmā keśavālaṃbanaḥsadā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaetanmune samākhyātaṃ gītaṃ vaivasvatena yat tvatpraśnānugataṃ samyakkimanyacchrotumicchasi  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe saptamo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācabhagavanbhagavāndevaḥ saṃsāravijigīṣubhiḥ samākhyāhi jagannātho viṣṇurārādhyate yathā  ViP ārādhitācca govindādārādhanaparair naraiḥ yatprāpyate phalaṃ śrotuṃ taccecchāmi mahāmune  ViP śrīparāśara uvācayatpṛcchati bhavānetatsagareṇa mahātmanā aurvaḥ prāha yathā pṛṣṭastanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu  ViP sagaraḥ praṇipattyainamaurvaṃ papracchabhārgavam viṣṇorārādhanopāyasaṃbandhaṃ munisattama  ViP phalaṃ cārādhite viṣṇo yatpuṃsāmabhijāyate sa cāha pṛṣṭo yatnena tasmai tanmekhilaṃ śṛṇu  ViP aurva uvācabhaumaṃ manorathaṃ svargaṃ svarge ramyaṃ ca yatpadam prāpnotyārādhite viṣṇau nirvāṇamapi cottamam  ViP yadyadicchati yāvacca phalamārādhite cyute tattadāpnoti rājendra bhūri svalpamathāpi vā  ViP yattu pṛcchasi bhūpāla kathāmārādhyate hariḥ tadahaṃ sakalaṃ tubhyaṃ kathayāmi nibodha me  ViP varṇāśramācāravatā puruṣeṇaparaḥ pumān viṣṇurārādhyate panthā nānyastattoṣakārakaḥ  ViP yajanyajñānyajatyenaṃ japantyenaṃ japannṛpa nighnannanyānhinastyenaṃ sarvabhūto yato hariḥ  ViP tasmātsadācāravatā puruṣeṇa janārdanaḥ ārādhyastu svavarṇoktadharmānuṣṭhānakārimā  ViP brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śudraś ca pṛthivīpate svadharmatatparo viṣṇumārādhayati nānyathā  ViP parāpavādaṃ paiśunyamanṛtaṃ ca na bhāṣate anyodvegakaraṃ vāpi toṣyate tenakeśavaḥ  ViP paradāraparadravyaparahiṃsāsu yo ratim na karoti pumānbhūpa toṣyate tena keśavaḥ  ViP na tāḍayati no hanti prāṇino na ca hiṃsakaḥ yo manuṣyo manuṣyendra toṣyate tena keśavaḥ  ViP devādvijagurūṇāṃ ca śuśrūṣāsu sadodyataḥ toṣyate tena govindaḥ puruṣeṇanareśvara  ViP yathātmani ca putre ca sarvabhūteṣu yattathā hitakāmo haristena sarvadā toṣyate sukham  ViP yasya rāgādidoṣeṇa na duṣṭaṃ nṛpa mānasam viśuddhacetasā viṣṇustoṣyate tena sarvadā  ViP varṇāśrameṣu ye dharmāḥ śāstroktā munisattama teṣu tiṣṭhannaro viṣṇumāduṣṭaṃ nṛpa mānasam  ViP sagara uvācatadahaṃ śrotumicchami varṇadharmānaśeṣataḥ tathaivāśramadharmaṃś ca dvijavarya bravīhi tān  ViP aurva uvācabrāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ śudrāṇāṃ ca yathākamam tvamekāgramatirbhūtvā śṛṇu dharmānmayoditān  ViP dānaṃ dadyād yajed devān yajñiḥ svādhyāyatatparaḥ nityodakī bhavedvipraḥ kuryāccāgniparigraham  ViP vṛttyarthaṃ yājayeccānyānanyānadhyāpayettathā kuryātpratigrahādānaṃśuklārthānnyāyato dvijaḥ  ViP sarvabhūtahitaṃ kuryānnāhitaṃ kasyāciddvijaḥ maitrī samastabhūteṣu brāhmaṇasyottamaṃ dhanam  ViP grāvṇiratne ca pārakye samabuddhirbhaveddvijaḥ ṛtāvabhigamaḥ patnyāṃ śastate cāsya pārthiva  ViP dānāni dadyādicchāto dvijebhyaḥ kṣatriyopi vā yajecca vividhair yajñair adhīyīta ca pārthivaḥ  ViP śastrājīvo mahīrakṣā pravarā tasya jīvikā tatrāpi prathamaḥ kalpaḥ pṛthivīparipāranam  ViP dharitrīpālanenaiva kṛtakṛtyā narādhipāḥ bhavanti tṛpateraṃśā yato yajñādikarmaṇām  ViP duṣṭānāṃ śāsanādrājā śiṣṭānāṃ paripālanāt prāpnotyabhimatāṃllokānvarṇasaṃsthāṃ karoti yaḥ  ViP pāśupālyaṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ kṛṣiṃ ca manujeśvara vaiśyāya jīvikāṃ brahmā dadau lokapitāmahaḥ  ViP tasyāpyadhyayanaṃ yajño dānaṃ dharmaś ca śasyate nityanaimittikādīnāmanuṣṭhānaṃ ca karmaṇām  ViP dvijātisaṃśritaṃ karma tādarthyaṃ tena poṣaṇam krayavikrayajair vāpi dhanaiḥ kārūdbhavena vā  ViP śudrasya sannatiḥ śaucaṃ sevā svāminyamāyayā amantrayajño hyasteyaṃ tatsaṃgo viprarakṣaṇam  ViP dānaṃ ca dadyācchūdropi pākayajñair yajeta ca pitryādikaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ śudraḥ kurvīta tena vai  ViP bhṛtyādibharaṇārthāya sarveṣāṃ ca parigrahaḥ ṛtukālebhigamanaṃ svadāreṣu mahīpate  ViP dayā samastabhūteṣu titikṣā nātimānitā satyaṃ śaucamanāyāso maṅgalaṃ priyavāditā  ViP maitryaspṛhā tathā tadvadakārpaṇyaṃnareśvara anusūyā ca sāmānyavarṇānāṃ kathitā guṇāḥ  ViP āśramāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāmete sāmānyalakṣaṇāḥ guṇāṃstathāvaddharmāṃś ca viprādīnāmimāñchṛṇu  ViP kṣāttraṃ karma dvijasyoktaṃ vaiśyaṃ karma tathā padi rājanyasya ca vaiśyoktaṃ śūdrakarma na caitayoḥ  ViP sāmarthye sati tattyājyamubhābhyāmapi pārthiva tadevāpadi kartavyaṃ na kuryātkarmasaṃkaram  ViP ityete kathitā rājanvarṇadharmā mayā tava dharmānāśramiṇāṃ samyagbruvato me niśāmaya  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe ṣṭamodhyāyaḥ aurva uvācabālaḥ kṛtopanayano vedāharaṇatatparaḥ gurugehe vasedbhūpa brahmacārī samāhitaḥ  ViP śaucā cāravrataṃ tatra kāryaṃ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ guroḥ vratāni caratā grāhyo vedaś ca kṛtabuddhinā  ViP ubhe saṃdhye raviṃ bhūpa tathaivāgniṃ samāhitaḥ upatiṣṭhettadā kuryādgurorapyabhivādanam  ViP sthite tiṣṭhedvājedyāte nīcair āsīta cāsati śiṣyo gurornṛpaśreṣṭha pratikūlaṃ na saṃcaret  ViP tenai voktaṃ paṭhedvedaṃ nānyacittaḥ puraḥsthitaḥ anujñātaś ca bhikṣānnamaśnīyādguruṇā tataḥ  ViP avagāhedapaḥ pūrvamācāryeṇāvagāhitaḥ samijjalādikaṃ cāsya kālyaṃ kālyamupānayet  ViP gṛhītagrāhyavedaś ca tato nujñām avāpya ca gārhasthyamāviśet prājño niṣpannaguruṇiṣkṛtiḥ  ViP vidhināvāptadārastu dhanaṃ prāpya svakarmaṇā gṛhasthakāryamakhilaṃ kuryādbhūpāla śaktitaḥ  ViP nivāpena pitṝnarcan yajñair devāṃstathātithīn annair munīṃś ca svādhyāyair apatyena prajāpatim  ViP bhūtāni balibhiścaiva vātsalyenākhilaṃ jagat prāpnoti lokānpuruṣo nijakarmasamārjitān  ViP bikṣābhujaś ca ye kecitparivraḍbrahmacāriṇaḥ tepyatraiva pratiṣṭhante gārhasthyaṃ tena vai param  ViP vedāharaṇakāryāya tīrthasnānāya ca prabho aṭanti vasudhāṃ viprāḥ pṛthivīdarśanāya ca  ViP aniketā hyanāhārā yatra sāyaṅgṛhāś ca ye teṣāṃ gṛhasthaḥ sarveṣāṃ pratiṣṭhā yonireva ca  ViP teṣāṃ svāgatadānādivaktavyaṃ madhuraṃ nṛpa gṛhāgatānāṃ dadyācca śayanāsanabhojanam  ViP atithiryasya bhagnāśo gṛhātpratinivartate sa dattvā duṣkṛtaṃ tasmai puṇyamādāya gacchati  ViP avajñānamahaṅkāro daṃbhaścaiva gṛha sataḥ paritāpopaghātau ca pāruṣyaṃ ca na śasyate  ViP yastu samyakkarotyevaṃ gṛhasthaḥ paramaṃ vidhim sarvabandhavinirmukto lokānāpnotyanuttamān  ViP vayaḥparīṇato rājankṛtakṛtyo gṛhāśramī putreṣu bhāryāṃ nikṣipya vanaṃ gacchetsahaiva vā  ViP parṇamūlaphalāhāraḥ keśaśmaśrujaṭādharaḥ bhūmiśāyī bhavettatra muniḥsarvātithirnṛpa  ViP carmakāśakuśaiḥ kuryātparidhānottarīyake tadvattriṣavaṇaṃ snānaṃ śastamasya nareśvaraḥ  ViP devatābhyarcanaṃ homaḥsarvābhyāgatapūjanam bhikṣābalipradānaṃ ca śastamasya nareśvara  ViP vanyastrehena gātrāṇāmabhyaṅgaścāsya śasyate tapaś ca tasya rājendra śītoṣṇādisahiṣṇutā  ViP yastvetāṃ niyataścaryāṃ vānaprasthaścarenmuniḥ sa dahatyagnivaddoṣāñjayellokāṃś ca śāśvatān  ViP caturthaścāśramo bhikṣoḥ projyate yo manīṣibhiḥ tasya svarūpaṃ gadato mama śrotuṃ nṛpārhasi  ViP putradravyakalatreṣu tyaktastreho narādhipa caturthamāśramasthānaṃ gacchennirdhūtamatsaraḥ  ViP traivargikāṃstyajetsarvānāraṃbhānavanīpate mitrādiṣu samo maitraḥsamasteṣveva jantuṣu  ViP jarāyujāṇḍajādīnāṃ vāḍmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ yuktaḥ kurvīta na drohaṃ sarvasaṃgāṃścavarjayet  ViP ekārātrasthitir grāme pañcarātrasthitiḥ pure tathā tiṣṭhedyathāprītirdveṣo vā nāsya jāyate  ViP prāṇayātrānimittaṃ ca vyaṅgāre bhuktavajjane kāle praśastavarṇānāṃ bhikṣārthaṃ paryaṭedgṛhān  ViP kāmaḥ krodhas tathā darpamohalobhādayaś ca ye tāṃstu sarvānparityajyaparivrāṇnirmamo bhavet  ViP abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo dattvā yaścarate muniḥ tasyāpi sarvabhūtebhyo na bhayaṃ vidyate kvacit  ViP kṛtvāgnihotraṃsvaśarīrasaṃsthaṃ śārīramagniṃ svamukhe juhoti viprastu bhaikṣyopahitair havirbhiścitāgnikānāṃ vrahati sma lokān  ViP mokṣośramaṃ yaścarate yathoktaṃ śuciḥsukhaṃ kalpitabuddhiyuktaḥ anindhanaṃ jyotiriva praśāntaḥsa brahmalokaṃ śrayate dvijātiḥ  ViP itiśrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe navamo dhyāyaḥ sagara uvācakathitaṃ cāturāśramyaṃ cāturvarṇyakriyās tathā puṃsaḥ kriyāmahaṃ śrotumicchāmi dvijasattama  ViP nityanaimittikāḥ kāmyāḥ kriyāḥ puṃsāmaśeṣataḥ samākhyāhi bhṛguśreṣṭha sarvajño hyasi me mataḥ  ViP aurva uvācayadetaduktaṃ bhavatā nityanaimittikāśrayam tadahaṃ kathayiṣyāṃmi śṛṇuṣvaikamanā mama  ViP jātasya jātakarmādikriyākāṇḍamaśeṣataḥ putrasya kurvīta pitā śrāddhaṃ cābhyudayātmakam  ViP yugmāṃstu prāḍmukhānviprānbhojayenmanubheśvara yathā tṛptis tathā kuryāddaivaṃ pitryaṃ dvijanmanām  ViP dadhnā yuktaiḥ sabadarair miśrān piḍān mudā yutaḥ nāndīmukhebhyastīrthena dadyāddaivena pārthiva  ViP prājāpatyena vā sarvamupacāraṃ pradakṣiṇam kurvīta tattathāśeṣavṛddhikāleṣu bhūpate  ViP tataś ca nāma kurvīta pitaiva daśamehani devapūrvaṃ narākhyaṃ hi śarmavarmādisaṃyutam  ViP śarmeti brāhyaṇasyoktaṃ varmeti kṣatrasaṃśrayam guptadāsātmakaṃ nāma praśastaṃ vaiśyaśudrayoḥ  ViP nārthahīnaṃ na cāśastaṃ nāpaśabdayutaṃ tathā nāmaṅgalyaṃ jugupsākaṃ nāma kuryātsamākṣaram  ViP nātidīrghaṃnātihrasvaṃ nātigurvakṣarānvitam sukhoccāryaṃ tu tannāma kuryādyatpraṇavākṣaram  ViP tato nantarasaṃskārasaṃskṛto guruveśmani yathoktavidhimāśritya kuryādvidyāparigraham  ViP gṛhītavidyo gurave dattvā ca gurudakṣiṇām gārhasthyamicchanbhūpāla kuryāddāraparigraham  ViP brahmacaryeṇa vā kālaṃ kuryātsaṃkalpapūrvakam gugoḥ śuśruṣaṇaṃ kuryāttatputrāderathāpi vā  ViP vaikhānaso vāpi bhavetparivrāḍatha vecchayā pūrvasaṃkalpitaṃ yādṛk tādṛkkuryānnarādhipa  ViP varṣair ekaguṇāṃ bhāryāmudvahettrigumaḥsvayam nāti keśāmakeśāṃ vā nātikṛṣṇāṃ na piṅgalām  ViP nisargatodhikāṅgāṃ vā nyūnāṅgāmapi nodvahet nāviśuddhāṃ saromāṃ vākulajāṃ vāpi rogiṇīm  ViP na duṣṭāṃ duṣṭavākyāṃ vā vyaṅginīṃ putṛmātṛtaḥ na śmaśruvyañjanavatīṃ na caiva puruṣākṛtim  ViP na gharvarasvarāṃ kṣāmāṃ tathā kākasvarāṃ na ca nānibandhekṣaṇāṃ tadvadvṛttākṣīṃ nodvahedbudhaḥ  ViP yasyāś ca romaśe jaṅghe gulphau yasyāstathonnatau gaṇḍayoḥ kūparau yasyā hasaṃtyāstāṃ na codvahet  ViP nātirūkṣacchaviṃ pāḍukarajāmaruṇekṣaṇām āpīna hastapādāṃ ca nakanyāmudvahedbudhaḥ  ViP na vāmanāṃ nātidīrghāṃ nodvahetsaṃhatabhruvam na cāti cchidradaśanāṃ na karālamukhīṃ naraḥ  ViP pañcamīṃ mātṛpakṣācca pitṛpakṣācca saptamīm gṛhasthaścodvahetkanyāṃ nyāyena vidhinā nṛpa  ViP brāhmo daivastathaivārṣaḥ prājāpatyastathāsuraḥ gāndharvarākṣayau cānyau paiśācaś cāṣṭamo mataḥ  ViP eteṣāṃ yasya yo dharmo varmasyokto maharṣibhiḥ kurvīta dāragrahaṇaṃ tenānyaṃ parivarjayet  ViP sadharmacāriṇīṃ prāpya gārhasthyaṃ sahitastayā samudvaheddadātyetatsamyagūḍhaṃ mahāphalam  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe daśamo dhyāyaḥ sagara uvācagṛhasthasya sadācāraṃ śrotumicchāmyahaṃ mune lokādasmātparasmācca yamātiṣṭhanna hīyate  ViP aurva uvācaśrūyatāṃ pṛthivīpāla sadācārasya lakṣaṇam sadācāravatā puṃsā jitau lokāvubhāvapi  ViP sādhavaḥ kṣīṇadeṣāstu saccabdaḥ sādhuvācakaḥ teṣāmācaraṇaṃ yastu sadācāraḥsa ucyate  ViP saptarṣayotha manavaḥ prajānāṃ patayas tathā sadācārasya vaktāraḥ kartāraś ca mahīpate  ViP brāhmo muhūrte cotthāya manasā matimātrṛpa prabuddhaścintayeddharmamarthaṃ cāpyavirodhinam  ViP apīḍayā tayoḥ kāmamubhayorapi cintayet dṛṣṭādṛṣṭavināśāya trivarge samadarśinā  ViP parityajedarthakāmau dharmapīḍākarau nṛpa dharmamapyasukhodarkaṃ lokavidveṣṭameva ca  ViP tataḥ kālyaṃ samutthāya kuryānmūtraṃ nareśvara  ViP nairṛtyāmiṣuvikṣepamatītyābhyadhikaṃ bhuvaḥ dvarādāvasathānmūtra purīṣaṃ ca visarjayet  ViP pādāvanejanocchiṣṭe prakṣipenna gṛhāṅgaṇe  ViP ātmacchāyāṃ tarucchāyāṃ gosūryāgnyanilāṃs tathā gurudvijādīṃstu budho nādhimehetkadācana  ViP na kṛṣṭe sasyamadhye vā gauvraje janasaṃsadi na vartmani na nadyāditīrtheṣu puruṣarṣabha  ViP nāpsu naivāṃbhasastīre śmaśāne na samācaret utsargaṃ vai purīṣasya mūtrasya ca visarjanam  ViP udaṅmukho divāmūtraṃ viparītamukho niśi kurvitānāpadi prājño mūtrotsargaṃ ca pārthiva  ViP tṛṇair āstīrya vasudhāṃ vastraprāvṛtamastakaḥ tiṣṭhennāticiraṃ tatra naiva kiñcidudīrayet  ViP valmīkamūṣikodbhūtāṃ mṛdaṃ nāntarjalāṃ tathā śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāccanādadyāllepasaṃbhavām  ViP aṇuprāṇyupapannāṃ ca halotkhātāṃ ca pārthiva parityajenmṛdo hyetāḥsakalāḥ śaucakarmaṇi  ViP ekā liṅge gude tistro dasa vāmakare nṛpa hastadvaye ca spata syurmṛdaḥ parimārjayet  ViP śirṣaṇyāni tataḥ khāni mūrdhānaṃ ca samālabhet bāhū nābhiṃ ca toyena hṛdayaṃ cāpi saṃspṛśet  ViP svācāntastu tataḥ kuryātpumānkeśaprasādhanam ādarśāñjanamāṅgalyaṃ dūrvādyālaṃbhanāni
