ViP nadīnadataṭākeṣu devakhātajaleṣu ca nityakriyārthaṃ snāyīta gīriprastravaṇeṣu ca  ViP kūpeṣūddhṛtatoyena snānaṃ kurvīta vā bhuvi gṛheṣūddhṛtatoyena hyathavā bhuvyasaṃbhave  ViP śucivastradharaḥ snāto devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam teṣāmeva hi tīrthenakurvīta susamāhitaḥ  ViP trirapaḥ prīṇanārthāya devānāmapavarjayet ṛṣīṇāṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ sakṛccāpi prajāpateḥ  ViP pitṝṇāṃ prīṇanārthāya tadapaḥ pṛtivīpate pitāmahebhyaś ca tathā prīmayetprapitāmahān  ViP mātāmahāya tatpitre tatpitre ca samāhitaḥ dadyātpaitreṇatīrthena kāmyaṃ cānyacchṛṇuṣva me  ViP mātre svamātre tanmātre gurupatnyai tathā somārkāgnyaṃbuvāyūnāṃ pūjyānāṃ ca na saṃmukham kuryānniṣṭhīvaviṇmutrasamutsargaṃ ca paṇḍitaḥ  ViP tiṣṭhanna mūtrayettadvatpathiṣvapi na mūtrayet śleṣmaviṇmūtraraktāni sarvadaiva na laṅghayet  ViP maṅgalyapūrvaratnājyapūjyānanabhivādya ca na niṣkramedgṛhātprājñaḥsadācāraparo naraḥ  ViP catuṣpathānnamaskuryātkāle homaparo bhavet dīnānabhyuddharetsādhūnupāsīta bahuśrutān  ViP devarṣipūjakaḥsamyakpitṛpiṇḍojakapradaḥ satkartā cātithīnāṃ yaḥ sa lokānuttamānvrajet  ViP hitaṃ mitaṃ priyaṃ kāle vaśyātmā yobhibhāṣate sa yāti lokānāhlādahetubhūtān nṛpākṣayān  ViP dhīmānhrīpānkṣamāyukto hyāstiko vinayānvitaḥ vidyābhijanavṛddhānāṃ yāti lokānanuttamān  ViP akālagārjitādau ca parvasvāśaucakādiṣu anadhyāyaṃ budhaḥ kuryāduparāgādike tathā  ViP samaṃ nayati yaḥ krudvānsarvabandhuramatsarī bhītāśvāsanakṛtsādhuḥsvargastasyālpakaṃ phalam  ViP varṣātapādiṣu cchatrī daṇḍī rātryaṭavīṣu ca śarīratrāṇakāmo vai sopānatkaḥsadā vrajet  ViP nordhvaṃ na tiryagdūraṃ vā na paśyanparyaṭedbudhaḥ yugamātraṃ mahīṣṭaṣṭhaṃ naro gacchedvilokayan  ViP doṣahetūnaśeṣāṃś ca vaśyātmā yo nirasyati tasya dharmārthakāmānāṃ hānirnālpāpi jāyate  ViP sadācārarataḥ prājño vidyāvinayaśikṣitaḥ pāpepyapāpaḥ paruṣe hyabhidhatte priyāṇi yaḥ maitrīdravāntaḥ karaṇastasya muktiḥ kare sthitā  ViP ye kāmakrodhalobhānāṃ vītarāgā na gocare sadācārasthitāsteṣāmanubhāvair dhṛtā mahī  ViP tasmātsatyaṃ vadetprājño yatparaprītikāraṇam satyaṃ yatparaduḥkhāya tadā maunaparo bhavet  ViP priyamuktaṃ hitaṃ naitaditi matvā na tadvadet śreyastatra hitaṃ vācyaṃ yadyapyatyantamapriyam  ViP prāṇīnāmupakārāya yathaiveha paratra ca karmaṇā manasā vācā tadeva matīmānvadet  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe dvādaśo dhyāyaḥ aurva uvācasacailasya pituḥ snānaṃ jāte putre vidhīyate jātakarma tadā kuryācchrāddhamabhyudaye ca yat  ViP yugmāndevāṃś ca vitryāṃś ca samyaksavyakramāddvijān pūjāyedbhojayeccaiva tanmanā nānyamānasaḥ  ViP dadhyakṣataiḥ sabadaraiḥ prāṅmukhodaṅmukho pi vā devatīrthena vai piṇḍāndadyātkāyena vā nṛpa  ViP nāndīmukhaḥ pitṛgaṇas tena śrāddhena pārthiva prīyate tattu kartavyaṃ puruṣaiḥ sarvavṛddhiṣu  ViP kanyāputravivāheṣu praveśeṣu ca veśmanaḥ nāmakarmaṇi bālānāṃ cūḍākarmādike tathā  ViP sīmantonnayane caiva putrādimukhadarśane nāndīmukhaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ pūjayetprayato gṛhī  ViP pitṛpūjākramaḥ prokto vṛddhāveṣa sanātanaḥ śrūyatāmavanīpāla preta karma kriyāvidhiḥ  ViP pretadehaṃ śabhaiḥ snānaiḥ snāpitaṃ sragvibhūṣitam dagdhvā grāmādbahiḥ snātvā sacailaḥsalilāśaye  ViP yatra tatra sthitāyaitadamukāyeti vādinaḥ dakṣiṇābhimukhā dadyurbāndhavāḥsalilāñjalīn  ViP praviṣṭāś ca samaṃ gobhir grāmaṃ nakṣatradarśane kaṭakarma tataḥ kuryād bhūmau prastaraśāyinaḥ  ViP dātavyonadinaṃ piḍaḥ pretāya bhuvi pārthiva divā ca bhaktaṃ bhoktavyamamāṃsaṃ manujarṣabha  ViP dināni tāni cecchātaḥ kartavya viprabhojanam pretā yānti tathā tṛptiṃ bandhuvargeṇa bhuñjatā  ViP prathamehni tṛtīye ca saptame navame tathā vastratyāgabahiḥsnāne kṛtvā dadyāt tilodakam  ViP caturthehnica kartavyaṃ tasyāsthicayanaṃ nṛpa tadūrdhvamaṅgasaṃsparśaḥsapiṇḍānāmapīṣyate  ViP yogyāḥsarvakriyāṇāṃ tu samanasalilās tathā anulepanapuṣpādibhogād anyatra pārthiva  ViP śayyāsanopabhogaś ca sapiṇḍānāmapīṣyate bhasmāsthicayanādūrdhvaṃ saṃyogo na tu yoṣitām  ViP bāle deśāntarasthe ca patite ca munau mṛte sadyaḥ śaucaṃ tathecchāto jalāgnyudbandhanādiṣu  ViP mṛtabandhordaśāhāni kulasyānnaṃ na bhujyate dānaṃ pratigraho homaḥ svādhyāyaś ca nivartate  ViP viprasyaitaddvādaśāhaṃ rājanyasyāpyaśaucakam ardhamāsaṃ tu vaiśyasya māsaṃ śūdrasya śuddhaye  ViP ayujo bhojayetkāmaṃ dvijānante tato dine dadyāddarbhaṣu piṇḍaṃ ca pretāyocchiṣṭasannidhau  ViP vāryāyudhapratodāstu daṇḍaś ca dvijabhojanāt spraṣṭavyonantaraṃ varṇaiḥ śuddherate tataḥ kramāt  ViP tataḥsarvaṇadharmā ye viprādināsudāhṛtāḥ tānkurvīta pumāñjīvennijadharmārjanais tathā  ViP mṛtāhati ca kartavyamekoddiṣṭamataḥ param āhvānādikriyā daivaniyogarahitena yat  ViP ekordhyastatra itthamāvatsarātsmṛtaḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tasminkāle rājendra catchṛṇu  ViP ekoddiṣṭavidhānena kāryaṃ tadapi pārthiva saṃvatsaretha ṣaṣṭhe vā māse vā dvādaśehni tat  ViP tilagandhodakair yuktaṃ tatra pātracatuṣṭayam  ViP pātraṃ pretasya tatraikaṃ paitraṃ pātratrayaṃ tathā secayetpitṛpātreṣu pretapātraṃ tatastriṣu  ViP tataḥ pitṛtvamāpanne tasminprete mahīpate śrāddhadharmair aśaṣastu tatpūrvānarcayetpitṝn  ViP putraḥ pautraḥ prapautro vā bhrātā vā bhrātṛsaṃtatiḥ sapiṇḍa saṃtatirvāpi kriyārhe nṛpa jāyate  ViP teṣāmabhāve savaiṣāṃ samānodakasatatiḥ mātṛpakṣamapiṇḍena saṃbandhā ye jalena vā  ViP kuladvayepi cocchinne strībhiḥ kāryāḥ kriyā nṛpa pitṛmātṛsapiṇḍais tu samānasalilais tathā  ViP saṃghātāntargatair vāpi kāryāḥ pretasya ca kriyāḥ utsannabandhurikthādvā kārayedavanīpatiḥ  ViP pūrvāḥ kriyā madhyamāś ca tathā caivottarāḥ kriyāḥ triḥprakārāḥ kriyāḥsarvāstāsāṃbhedaṃ śṛṇuṣva me  ViP ādāhādyādaśāhāś ca sparśādyantāstu yāḥ kriyāḥ tāḥ pūrvā madhyamā māsi māsyekoddiṣṭasaṃjñitāḥ  ViP prete pitṛtvamāpanne sapiṇḍikaraṇādanu kriyante yāḥ kriyāḥ pitryāḥ procyante tā nṛpottarāḥ  ViP pitṛmātṛsapiṇḍais tu samānāsalilais tathā saṃghātāntargatair vāpi rājñā māsimāsyasite pakṣe pañcadaśyāṃ nareśvara dathāṣṭakāsu kurvīta kāmyānkālāñchṛṇuṣva me  ViP śrāddhārhamāgataṃ dravyaṃ viśiṣṭamatha vā dvijam śrāddhaṃ kurvīta vijñāya vyatīpāte yate tathā  ViP viṣuve śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe caturdaśo dhyāyaḥ aureva uvācabrāhmaṇānbhojayecchraddhe yadguṇāṃstānnibhodha me  ViP triṇāciketastrimadhustrisuparmaḥṣajaṅgavit vedavicchrotriyo yogī tathā vai jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ  ViP ṛtviksvastreyadauhitrajāmātṛśvaśurās tathā mātulotha taponiṣṭhaḥ pañcāgnyabhiratas tathā śiṣyāḥsaṃbandhinaścaiva mātāpitṛrataś ca yaḥ  ViP etānniyojayecchrāddhe pūrvoktānprathame budhaḥ śastāñchrotriyādīnnimantrayet kathayecca tathaivaiṣāṃ niyogānpitṛdaivikān  ViP tataḥ krodhavyavāyādīnāyāsaṃ tair dhijaiḥ saha yajamāno na kurvīta doṣastatra mahānayam  ViP śrāddhe niyukto tṛptiṃ praṇaśyantu ca yātudhānāḥ  ViP yajñeśvaro havyasamastakavyo bhoktāvyayātmā harirīśvaro tra tatsaṃnidhānādapayāntu sadyo rakṣāṃsyaśeṣaṇyasurāś ca sarve  ViP tṛpteṣveteṣu vikiredannaṃ vipreṣu mātāmahebhyastenaiva piṇḍāṃstīrthena nirvapet  ViP dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu puṣpadhūpādipūjitam svapitre prathamaṃ piṇḍaṃ dadyāducchiṣṭasannidhau  ViP pitāmahāya caivānyaṃ tatpitre ca tathāparam darbhamūle lepabhujaḥ prīṇayellepagharṣaṇaiḥ  ViP piṇḍair mātāmahāṃstadvadgandhamālyādisaṃyutaiḥ pūjāyitvā dvijāgryāṇāṃ dadyāccācamanaṃ tataḥ  ViP pitṛbhyaḥ prathamaṃ bhaktyātanmanaskonareśvara susvadhetyāśiṣā yuktāṃ dadyācchaktyā ca dakṣiṇām  ViP dattvā ca dakṣiṇāṃ tebhyo vācayed vaiśvadevikān prīyantāmihaye viśvedevāstena itīrayet  ViP tatheti cokte tair vipraiḥ prārthanīyāstathāsiṣaḥ paścādvisarjayeddevānpūrvaṃ paitryānmahīpate  ViP mātāmahānāmapyevaṃ saha devaiḥ kramaḥ smṛtaḥ bhojayecca svaśaktyā ca dāne tadvadvisarjane  ViP āpādaśaucanātpūrvaṃ kuryāddevadvijanmasu visarjanaṃ tu prathamaṃ paitraṃ mātāmaheṣu vai  ViP visarjayetprītivacaḥsaṃmānyābhyarthitāstataḥ nivartetābhyanujñāta ādvāraṃ tānanuvrajet  ViP tatastu vaiśvadevākhyaṃ kuryānnityakriyaṃ budhaḥ bhuñjīyācca samaṃ pūjya bhṛtyabandhubhir ātmanaḥ  ViP evaṃ śrāddhaṃ budhaḥ kuryātpaitryaṃ mātāmahaṃ tathā śrāddhair āpyāyitā dadyuḥsarvānkāmanpitāmahāḥ  ViP trīṇi śrāddhe pavitrāṇi dauhitraḥ kutapastilāḥ rajatasya kathā dānaṃ tathā saṃkīrtanādikam  ViP jarjyāni kurvatā śrāddhaṃ krodhodhvagamanaṃ tvārā bhokturapyatra rājendra trayametanna śasyate  ViP viśvedevāḥsapitaras tathā mātāmahā nṛpa kulaṃ cāpyāyate puṃsāṃ sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ prakurvatām  ViP somādhāraḥ pitṛgaṇo yogādhāraś ca candramāḥ śrāddhe yoginiyogastu tasmādbhupālaśasyate  ViP sahasrasyāpi viprāṇāṃ yogī cetpurataḥsthitaḥ sarvān bhoktṝṃs tārayati yajamānaṃ tathā nṛpa  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃse pañcadaśo dhyāyaḥ aurva uvācahaviṣyamatsyamāsais tu śaśasya nakulasya ca sokaracchākalaiṇeyarauravair gavayena ca  ViP aurabhragavyaiś ca tathā māsavṛddhyā pitāmahāḥ prayānti tṛptiṃ māṃsais tu nityaṃ vārdhroṇasāmiṣaiḥ  ViP khaḍgamāṃsamatīvātra kālaśākaṃ tathā madhu śastāni karmaṇyatyantatṛptidāni nareśvara  ViP gayāmupetya yaḥ śrāddhaṃ karoti pṛthivīpate saphalaṃ tasya tajjanma jāyate pitṛtīṣṭidam  ViP praśāntikāḥsamīvārāḥ śyāmākā dvividhās tathā vanyaiṣadhīpradhānāstu śrāddhārhāḥ puruṣarṣabha  ViP yavāḥ priyaṅgavo mudgā godhūmā vrīhayastilāḥ niṣpāvāḥ kovidārāś ca sarṣapāścātra sobhanāḥ  ViP akṛtāgrayaṇaṃ yacca dhānyajātaṃ nareśvara rājamāṣānaṇuṃścaiva masūrāṃś ca visarjayet  ViP alābuṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuṃ piṇḍamūlakam gāndhārakakaraṃvādilavāṇānyauṣarāṇi ca  ViP āraktāścaiva niryāsāḥ pratyakṣalavaṇāni ca varjyānyetāni vai śrāddhe yacca vācā na śasyate  ViP naktāhṛtamanucchinnaṃ tṛpyate na ca yatra gauḥ durghadhiphenilaṃ cāṃbu śrāddhayogyaṃ na pārthiva  ViP kṣiramekasaphānāṃ yadauṣṭramāvikameva ca mārgaṃ ca māhiṣaṃ caiva varjayecchrāddhakameṇi  ViP ṣaṇḍāpaviddhacaṇḍālapāpipāṣaṇḍarogibhiḥ kṛkavākuśvānanagnavānaragrāmasūkaraiḥ  ViP udakyāsūtikāśaucamṛtahāraiś ca vīkṣite śrāddhe surā na pitaro bhuñjante puruṣarṣabha  ViP tasmātparīśrite kuryācchrāddhaṃ śraddhāsamanvitaḥ urvyāṃ ca tilavikṣepādyātudhānānnivārayet  ViP nakhādinā copapannaṃ keśakīṭādibhir nṛpa na caivābhiṣavair miśram annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā  ViP śraddhāsamanvitair dattaṃ pitṛbhyo nāmagotrataḥ yadāhārāstu te jātāstadāhāratvameti tat  ViP śrūyate cāpi pitṛrbhigītā gāthā mahīpate ikṣvākormanuputrasya kalāpopavane purā  ViP api naste bhaviṣyanti kule sanmārgaśīlinaḥ gayāmupetya ye piṇḍāndāsyantyasmākamādarāt  ViP api naḥsa kule jāyādyo no dadyāttrayodaśīm pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca  ViP gaurīṃ vāpyudvahetkanyāṃ nīlaṃ vā vṛṣamutsṛjet yajeta vāśvamedhena vidhivaddakṣiṇāvatā  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe poḍaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaityāha bhagavānaurvaḥsagarāya mahātmane sadācāraṃ purā samyaṅ maitreya paripṛcchate  ViP mayāpyetadaśeṣeṇa tathitaṃ bhavato dvija samullaṅghya sadācāraṃ kaścinnāpnoti śobhanam  ViP śrīmaitreya uvācaṣaṇḍāpaviddhapramukhā viditā bhagavanmayā udakyādyāś ca me samyaṅ nagnamicchāmi veditum  ViP konagnaḥ kiṃ samācāro nagnasaṃjñāṃ naro labhet nagnasvarūpamicchāmi yathāvatkathitaṃ tvāya śrotuṃ dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha na hyastyaviditaṃ tava  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃjñeyaṃ trayī varṇāvṛttirdvija etāmujjhati yo mohātsa nagnaḥ pātakī dvajaḥ  ViP trayī samastavarṇānāṃ dvijasaṃvāraṇaṃ yataḥ nagno bhavatyujjhitāyāṃ yatastasyāṃ na saṃśayaḥ  ViP idaṃ ca śruyatāmanyadyadbhīṣmāya mahātmane kathayāmāsa dharmajño vasiṣṭho smatpitāmahaḥ  ViP mayāpi tasya gadataḥ śrutametanmahātmanaḥ nagnasaṃbandhi maitreya yatpṛṣṭohamiha tvāyā  ViP devāsuramabhūdyuddhaṃ dvivyamabdaśataṃ purā tasminparajitā devā daityair hrādapurogamaiḥ  ViP kṣīrodasyottaraṃ kūlaṃ gatvā tapyanta vai tapaḥ viṣṇorārādhanārthāya jaguścemaṃ stavaṃ tadā  ViP devā ūcuḥārādhanāya lokānāṃ viṣṇorīśasya yāṃ giram vakṣyāmo bhagavānadya tayā viṣṇuḥ prasīdatu  ViP yato bhūtānyaśeṣāṇi prasūtāni mahātmanaḥ yasmiś ca layameṣyanti kastaṃ stotumiheśvaraḥ  ViP tathāpyarātividhvaṃsadhvastavīryā bhayārthinaḥ tvāṃ stoṣyāmastavoktīnāṃ yāthārthyaṃ naiva gocare  ViP tvamurvī salilaṃ vahnirvāyurākāśameva ca samastamantaḥkaraṇaṃ pradhānaṃ tatparaḥ pumān  ViP ekaṃ tavaitadbhūtātmanmūrtamūrtamayaṃ vapuḥ ābrahmastaṃbaparyantaṃ sthānakālavibhedavat  ViP tatraiśaṃ tava yatpūrvaṃ tvannābhikamalodbhavam rūpaṃ viśvopakārāya tasmai brahmātmane namaḥ  ViP śakrārkarudravasvaśvimarutsomādibhedavat vayamekaṃ svarūpaṃ te tasmai devātmane namaḥ  ViP daṃbhaprāyamasaṃbodhi titiśrādamavarjitam yadrūpaṃ tava govinda tasmai daityātmane namaḥ  ViP nātijñānavahā yasminnāḍyastimitatejasi śabdādilobhi yastasmai tubhyaṃ yatrātmane namaḥ  ViP krauryaṃ māyāmayaṃ ghoraṃ yacca rūpaṃ tavāsitam niśācarātmane tasmai namaste puruṣottama  ViP svargasthadharmisaddharmaphalopakaraṇaṃ tava dharmākhyaṃ ca tathā rūpaṃ namastasmai janārdana  ViP harṣaprāyamasaṃsargi gatimadgamanādiṣu siddhākhyaṃ tava yadrūpaṃ tasmai siddhātmane namaḥ  ViP atitikṣāyanaṃ krūramupabhogasahaṃ hare dvijīhvantava yadrūpaṃ tasmai nāgātmane namaḥ  ViP avabodhi ca yacchāntamadoṣamapakalpaṣam ṛṣirūpātmane tasmai viśvarūpāya te namaḥ  ViP bhakṣayatyatha kalpānte bhūtāni yadavāritam tvadrūpaṃ puṇḍharīkākṣa tasmai kālātmane namaḥ  ViP saṃbhakṣya sarvabhūtāni devādīny aviśeṣataḥ nṛtyatyante ca yadrūpaṃ tasmai rudrātmane namaḥ  ViP pravṛttyā rajaso yacca karmaṇāṃ karaṇātmakam janardana namastasmai tvadrūpāya narātmane  ViP aṣṭāviśadvadhopetaṃ yadrūpaṃ tāmasaṃ tava unmārgagāmi sarvātmaṃstasmai vaśyātmane namaḥ  ViP yajñāṅgabhūtaṃ yadrūpaṃ jagataḥ sthitisādhanam vṛkṣādibhedaiḥ ṣaḍbhedi tasmai mukyātmane namaḥ  ViP tiryaṅmanuṣyadevādivyomaśabdādikaṃ ca yat rūpaṃ tavādeḥ sarvasya tasmai suddhātiśuddhaṃ paramarṣidṛśyaṃ rūpāya tasmai bhagavannatāḥ smaḥ  ViP yannaḥ śarīreṣu yadanyadeheṣvaśeṣavastuṣvajamakṣayaṃ yat tasmācca nānyavdyatiriktamasti brahmasvarūpāya natāḥ sma tasmai  ViP sakalamidamajasya yasya rūpaṃ paramapadātmavataḥsanātanasya tamanidhanasaśeṣabījabhūtaṃ prabhumamalaṃ praṇatāḥsma vāsudevam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācastotrasya cāvasāne te dadṛśuḥ parameśvaram śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiṃ garuḍasthaṃ surā harim  ViP tamucuḥsakalā devāḥ praṇipātapuraḥsuram prasīda nātha daityebhyastrāhi naḥ śaraṇārthinaḥ  ViP trelokyayajñabhāgāś ca daityair hlādapurogamaiḥ hṛtā no brahmaṇopyayājñāmullaṅghya paramśvara  ViP yadyapyaśeṣabhū tasya vayaṃ te ca tāvaṃśajāḥ tathāpyavidyābhedena bhinnaṃ paśyāmahe jagat  ViP svavarṇadharmābhiratā vedamārgānusāriṇaḥ na śakyāsterayo hantumasmābhis tapasāvṛtāḥ  ViP tamupāyamaśeṣātmannasmākaṃ dātumarhasi yena tānasurānhantuṃ bhavema bhagavankṣamāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityukto bhagavāṃstebhyo māyāmohaṃ śarīrataḥ samutpādya dadau viṣṇuḥ prāha cedaṃ surottamān  ViP māyāmohoyamakhilāndaityāṃ stānmohayiṣyati tato vadhyā bhaviṣyanti vedamārgabahiṣkṛtāḥ  ViP sthitau sthitasya me vadhyā yāvantraḥ paripanthinaḥ brahmaṇo hyadhikārasya devā daityādikāḥ surāḥ  ViP tadgacchata nabhīḥ kāryā māyāmohoyamagrataḥ gacchannadyopakārāya bhavatāṃ bhavitā surāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktāḥ praṇipatyainaṃ yayurdevā yathāgatam māyāmoho pi taiḥ sārdha yayau yatra mahāsurāḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe saptadaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīpāraśara uvācatapasy abhiratān so tha māyāmoho mahāsurān maitreya dadṛśe gatvānarmadātīrasaṃśritān  ViP tato digaṃbaro muṇḍo barhipicchadharo dvija māyāmoho surān ślakṣṇamidaṃ vacanamabravīt  ViP māyāmoha uvācahe daityapatayo brūta yadartha tapyate tapaḥ aihikārthaś ca pāratryaṃ tapasaḥ phalamiccatha  ViP asurā ūcuḥpāratryaphalalābhāya tapaścaryā mahāmate asmābhir iyam ārabdhā kiṃ vā te tra vivakṣitam  ViP māyāmoha uvācakurudhvaṃ mama vākyāni yadi muktimabhīpsatha arhadhvaṃ dharmametaṃ ca sarve yūyaṃ mahābalāḥ  ViP dharmo vimukterarheyaṃ naitasmādaparo varaḥ atraiva saṃsthitāḥ svargaṃ vimuktiṃ vā gamiṣyatha  ViP arhadhvaṃ dharmametaṃ ca sarve yūyaṃ mahābalāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃprakārair bahubhir yuktidarśanacarcitaiḥ māyāmohena te daityā vedamārgādapā kṛtāḥ  ViP dharmāyaitadadharmāya sadetanna sadityapi vimuktaye tvidaṃ naitadvimuktiṃ saṃprayacchati  ViP paramārthoyamatyarthaṃ paramārtho na cāpyayam kāryametadakāryaṃ ca naitadevaṃ sphuṭaṃ tvidam  ViP digvāsasāmayaṃ dharmo dharmoyaṃ bahuvāsasām  ViP ityanekāntavādaṃ ca māyāmohena naikadhā tena darśayatā daityāḥsvadharmaṃ tyājitā dvija  ViP arhataitaṃ mahādharmaṃ māyāmohena te yataḥ proktāstamāśritā dharmamarhatāstena te bhavan  ViP trayīdharmasamutsargaṃ māyāmohena te surāḥ kārītāstanmayā hyāsaṃstatonye tatpracoditāḥ  ViP tair apy anye pare taiś ca tair apy anye pare ca taiḥ alpair ahobhiḥ saṃtyaktā tair daityaiḥ prāyaśastrayī  ViP punaś ca raktāṃbaradhṛṅ māyāmoho jitendriyaḥ anyānāhāsurān gatvāmṛddhalpamadhurākṣaram  ViP svargārthaṃ yadi vo vāñchā nirvāṇārthamathāsurāḥ tadalaṃ paśughātādiduṣcadharmair nibodhata  ViP vijñānamayamevaitadaśeṣamavagacchata budhyadhvaṃ me vacaḥ samyagbudhair evamihoditam  ViP jagadetadanādhāraṃ bhrāntijñānārthatatparam rāgādiduṣṭamatyarthaṃ bhrāmyate bhavasaṃkaṭe  ViP evaṃ budhyata budhyadhvaṃ budhyataivamitīrayan māyāmohaḥ sa daityeyāndharmamatyāñjayannijam  ViP nānāprakāravacanaṃ sa teṣāṃ yuktiyojanam tathātathā trayīdharmaṃ tatyajuste yathāyathā  ViP tepyanyeṣāṃ tathaivocuranyair anye tathoditā maitreya tatyajurdharmaṃ vedesmṛtyuditaṃ param  ViP anyānapyanyapāṣaṇḍaprakārair bahubirdvija daiteyānmohayāmāsa māyāmohodimohakṛt  ViP svalpenaiva hi kālena māyāmohena te surāḥ mohitāstatyajuḥsarvāṃ trayīmārgāśritāṃ kathām  ViP kecidvinindāṃ vedānāṃ devānāmapare dvija yajñakarmakalāpasya tathānte ca dvijanmanām  ViP nainadyuktisahaṃ vākyaṃ hiṃsādharmāya ceṣyate havīṃṣyanaladaghdhāni phalāyetyarthakoditam  ViP yajñair anekair devatvam avāpyendreṇa bhujyate śamyādi yadi cetkāṣṭhaṃ tadvaraṃ patrabhukpaśu  ViP nihatasya paśorjajñe svargaprāptiryadīṣyate svapitā yajamānena kinnu tasmānna hanyate  ViP tṛptaye jāyate puṃso bhuktamanyena cettataḥ kuryācchrāddhaṃ śramāyānnaṃ na vaheyuḥ pravāsinaḥ  ViP janaśraddheyamityetadavagamya tatotra vaḥ upekṣā śreyase vākyaṃ rocatāṃ yan mayeritam  ViP na hyaptavādā nabhaso nipatanti mahīṃ surāḥ yuktimadvacanaṃ grāhyaṃ mayānyaiś ca bhavadvidhaiḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācamayāmohena te daityāḥ prakārair bahubhis tathā vṛthāpitā yathā naiṣāṃ trayī kaścidarocayat  ViP itthamunmārgayāteṣu teṣu daityeṣu te marāḥ udyogaṃ paramaṃ kṛtvā yuddhāya samupasthitāḥ  ViP tato daivāsuraṃ yuddhaṃ punarevābhavaddvija hatāścate surā daivaiḥ sanmārgaparipanthinaḥ  ViP svadharmakavacaṃ teṣāmabhūdyatprathamaṃ dvija tena rakṣābhavatpūrvaṃ neśurnaṣṭe ca tatra te  ViP tato maitreya tanmārgavartino yebhavañjanāḥ nagnāste tair yatastyakta trayīsaṃvaraṇaṃ tathā kṛtāś ca te surā devair nānā vedavinindakāḥ  ViP brahmacārīgṛhasthaś ca vānaprasthastathāśramī parivrāḍ vā caturthotra pañcamo nopapadyate  ViP vastu saṃtyajya gārhasthyaṃ vānaprastho na jāyate parivrāṭ cāpi maitreya sa nagnaḥ pāpakṛnnaraḥ  ViP nityānāṃ karmaṇāṃ vipra yasya hāniraharniśam akurvanvihitaṃ karma śaktaḥ patati taddine  ViP prāyaścittena mahātā śuddhimāpnotyanāpadi pakṣaṃ nityakriyāhāneḥ kartā maitreya mānavaḥ  ViP saṃvatsaraṃ kriyāhāniryasya puṃsobhijāyate tasyāvalokanātsūryo nirīkṣyaḥsādhubhiḥ sadā  ViP spṛṣṭe snānaṃ sacelasya śuddherheturmahāmate puṃso bhavati tasyoktā na śuddhiḥ pāpakarmaṇaḥ  ViP devarṣipitṛbhītāni yasya viprasya veśmani prayāntyanarcitānyatra loke tasmānna pāpakṛt  ViP saṃbhāṣaṇānupraśnādi sahāsyāṃ caiva kurvataḥ jāyate tulyatā tasya tenaiva dvija vatsarāt  ViP devādinisvāsahataṃ śarīraṃ yasya veśma ca na tena saṃkaraṃ kuryādgṛhāsanaparicchadaiḥ  ViP atha bhuktaṃ gṛhe tasya karotyāsyāṃ tathāsane śete cāpyekaśayane sa sadyastatsamo bhavet  ViP devatāpitṛbhūtāni tathānabhyarcya yo tithīn bhukte sa pātakaṃ bhuṅkte niṣkṛtistasya neṣyate  ViP brāhmaṇādyāstu ye varṇāḥsvadharmādanyatomukhāḥ yānti te nagnasaṃjñāṃ tu hīnakarmasvavasthitaḥ  ViP caturṇāṃ yatra varṇānāṃ maitreyātyantasaṃkaraḥ tatrāsyā sādhuvṛttināmupaghātāya jāyate  ViP anabhyarcya ṛṣīndevānpitṛbhūtātithīs tathā yo bhuṅkte tasya saṃllāpātpatantinarake narāḥ  ViP tasmādetānnaro nagnāṃstrayīsaṃtyāgadūṣitān sarvadā varjayetprājña ālāpasparśanādiṣu  ViP śraddhāvadbhiḥ kṛtaṃ yatnā ddevānpitṛpitāmahān na prīṇayati tacchrāddhaṃ yadyebhir avalokitam  ViP śrūyate ca purākhyāto rājā śatadhanurbhuvi patnī ca śaivyātasyābhūdatidharmaparāyaṇā  ViP pativratā mahābhāgā satyaśaucadayānvitā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpannā vinayena yanena ca  ViP sa tu rājā tayā sārdhaṃ devadevaṃ janārdanam ārādhayāmāsa vibhuṃ parameṇa samādhinā  ViP homair japais tathā dānair upavāsaiś ca bhaktitaḥ pujābhiścānudivasaṃ tanmanā nānyamānasaḥ  ViP ekadā tu samaṃ snātau tau tu bhāryāpatī jale bhāgīrathyāḥsamuttīrṇau kārttikyāṃ samupoṣitau pāṣaṇḍinamapaśyetāmāyāntaṃ saṃmukhaṃ dvija  ViP cāpācāryasya tasyāsau sakhā rājño mahātmanaḥ atastadgauravāttena sakhābhāvamathākarot  ViP na tu sā vāgyatā devī tasya patnī pativratā upoṣitāsmīti raviṃ tasmindṛṣṭe dadarśa ca  ViP samāgamya yathānyāyaṃ daṃpatī tau yathāvidhi viṣṇoḥ pūjādikaṃ sarvaṃ kṛtaṃvatau dvijottama  ViP kālena gacchatā rājā mamārāsau sapatnajit anvāruroha taṃ devī citāsthaṃ bhūpatiṃ patim  ViP sa tu tenāpacāreṇa śvā jajñe vasudhādhipaḥ upoṣitena pāṣaṇḍasaṃllāpo yatkṛto bhavat  ViP sā tu jāti smarā jajñe kāśīrājasutā śubhā sarvavijñānasaṃpūrṇā sarvalakṣaṇapūjitā  ViP tāṃ pitā dātukāmobhūdvarāya vinivāritaḥ tayaiva tanvyā virato vivāhāraṃbhato nṛpaḥ  ViP tataḥsā divyayā dṛṣṭyā dṛṣṭvā śvānaṃ nijaṃ patim vidiśākhyaṃ puraṃ gatvā tadavasthaṃ dadarśa tam  ViP taṃ dṛṣṭvaiva mahābhāgaṃ śvabhūtaṃ tu patiṃ tadā dadau tasmai varāhāraṃ satkārapravaṇaṃ śubhā  ViP bhuñjan dattaṃ tayā so nnam atimṛṣṭam abhīpsitam svajāti lalitaṃ kurvanbahu cāṭu cakāra vai  ViP atīva vrīḍitā balā kurvatā cāṭu tena sā praṇāmapūrvamāhedaṃ dayitaṃ taṃ kuyonijam  ViP smaryatāṃ tanmahārāja dākṣiṇyalalitaṃ tvayā yena śvayonimāpanno mama cāṭukaro bhavān  ViP pāṣaṇḍinaṃ samābhāṣya tīrthasnānādanantaram prāptosi kutsitāṃ yoniṃ kinna smarasi tatprabho  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatayaivaṃ smārīti tasminpūrvajātikṛte tadā dadhyau ciramathā vāra nirvedamatidurlabham  ViP nirviṇṇacittaḥsa tato nirgamya nagarādvahiḥ marutprapatanaṃ kṛtvā sārgālī yonimāgataḥ  ViP sāpi dvitīye saṃprāpte vīkṣya divyena cakṣuṣā jñātvā sṛgālaṃ taṃ draṣṭuṃ yayau kolāhalaṃ girim  ViP tatrāpi dṛṣṭvā taṃ prāha sārgālīṃ yonimāgatam bhartāramapi cārvaṅgī tanayā pṛthivīkṣitaḥ  ViP api smarasi rājendra śvayonisthasya yanmayā proktaṃ te pūrvacaritaṃ pāṣaṇḍālāpasaṃśrayam  ViP punasta yoktaṃ sa jñātvā satyaṃ satyavatāṃ varaḥ kānane sa nirāhārastatyāja svaṃ kalevaram  ViP būyastato vṛko jajñe gatvā taṃ nirjane vane smārayāmāsa bhartāraṃ pūrvavṛttamaninditā  ViP na tvaṃ vṛko mahābhāga rājā śatadhanurbhavān śvā bhūtvā tvaṃ sṛgālo bhūrvṛkatvaṃ sāṃprataṃ gataḥ  ViP smāritena yathā vyaktastenātmā gṛdhratāṃ gataḥ apāpā sā punaścainaṃ bodhayāmāsa bhāmiti  ViP naredra smaryatāmātmā hyalaṃ te gṛdhraceṣṭayā pāṣaṇḍālāpajāto yaṃ doṣo yadgṛdhratāṃ gataḥ  ViP tataḥ kākatvamāpannaṃ samanantarajanmani uvāca tanvī bhartāramupalabhyātmayogataḥ  ViP aśeṣabhūbhṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ vaśyā yasmai baliṃ daduḥ sa tvaṃ kākatvamāpanno jātodya balibhuk prabho  ViP evameva bakatvepi smāritaḥ sa purātanam tat tyāja bhūpatiḥ prāṇān mayūratvamavāpa ca  ViP mayūratve tataḥsā vai cakārānugatiṃ śubhā dattaiḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ bhojyair bālā tajjatibhojanaiḥ  ViP tatastu janako rājā vājimedhaṃ mahākratum cakāra tasyāvabhṛthe snāpayāmāsa taṃ tadā  ViP sasnau svayaṃ ca tanvaṅgī smārayāmāsa cāpi tam yathāsau śvasṛgālādiyoniṃ jagrāha pārthivaḥ  ViP smṛtajanmakramaḥsotha tattyāja svakalevaram jajñe sa janakasyaiva putrosau sumahātmanaḥ  ViP tataḥsā pitaraṃ tanvī vivāhārtham acodayat sa cāpi kāra yāmāsa tasyā rājā svayaṃvaram  ViP svayaṃvare kṛte sā taṃ saṃprāptaṃ patimātmanaḥ varayāmāsa bhūyo pi bhartṛbhāvena bhāminī  ViP bubhuje ca tayā sārdhaṃ saṃbhogānnṛpanandanaḥ pitaryuparate rājyaṃ videheṣu cakāra saḥ  ViP iyāja jajñānsubahūndadau dānāni cārthinām putrānutpādayāmāsa yuyudhe ca sahāribhiḥ  ViP rājyaṃ bhuktvā yathānyāyaṃ pālayitvā vasuṃdharām tattyāja sa priyānprāṇānsaṃgrāme dharmatonṛpaḥ  ViP tataścitāsthaṃ taṃ bhūyo bhartāraṃ sā śubhekṣaṇā anvāruroha vidhivadyathāpūrvaṃ mudānvitā  ViP tato vāpa tayā sārdhaṃ rājaputryā sa pārthivaḥ aindrān atītya vai lokāṃllokānprāpa tadākṣayān  ViP svargākṣayatvamatulaṃ dāṃpatyamatidurlabham prāptaṃ puṇyaphalaṃ prāpya saṃśuddhiṃ tāṃ dvijottama  ViP eṣa pāṣaṇṭasaṃbhāṣāddoṣaḥ prokto mayā dvija tathāśvamedhāvabhṛthasnānamāhātmyameva ca  ViP tasmātpāṣaṇḍibhiḥ pāpair ālāpasparśanaṃ tyajet viśeṣataḥ kriyākāle yajñādau cāpi dīkṣitaḥ  ViP kriyāhānirgṛhe yasya māsamekaṃ prajāyate tasyāvalokanātsūryaṃ paśyeta matimānnaraḥ  ViP kiṃ punaryais tu saṃtyaktā trayī sarṃvātmanā dvija pāṣaṇḍabhojibhiḥ pāpaurvedavādavirodhibhiḥ  ViP sahālāpastu saṃsargaḥ sahāsyā cātipāpinī pāṣaṇḍibhir durācārais tasmāttāṃ parivarjayet  ViP pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthānbaiḍālavratikāñchaṭhān haitukānbakavṛttīṃś ca vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet  ViP dvaratastais tu saṃparkastyājyaścāpyatipāpibhiḥ pāṣaṇḍibhir durājārais tasmāt tān parivarjayet  ViP ete nagnāstavākhyātā dṛṣṭā śrāddho paghātakāḥ yeṣāṃ saṃbhāṣaṇātpuṃsāṃ dinapuṇyaṃ praṇaśyati  ViP ete pāṣaṇḍinaḥ pāpā na hyetānālapedbudhaḥ puṇyaṃ naśyati saṃbhāṣādeteṣāṃ taddinodbhavam  ViP puṃsāṃ jaṭādharaṇamaiṇḍyavatāṃ vṛthaiva moghāśināmakhilaśaucanirākṛtānām toyapradānapitṛpiṇḍabahiṣkṛtānāṃ saṃbhāṣaṇādapi narā narakaṃ prayānti  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśe ṣṭādaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe tṛtīyāṃśaḥsamāptaḥiti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhya śrīdharīyavyākhyādvayopete tṛtīyāṃśaḥ samāptaḥ atha śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhya śrīdharīyavyākhyādvayopete caturthaṃśaḥ prārabhyate śrīmate rāmānujāya nāmaḥmaitreya uvācabhagavanyannaraiḥ kāryaṃ sādhukarmaṇyavasthitaiḥ tanmahyaṃ guruṇākhyātaṃ nityanaimittikātmakam  ViP varmadharmāstathākhyātā dharmā ye cāśrameṣu ca śrotumicchāmyahaṃ vaṃśaṃ rājñāṃ tadbrūhi me guro  ViP śrīparāśara vācamaitreya śrūyatāmayamanekayajśuravīradhīrabhūpālālaṅkṛto brahmādirmānavo vaṃśaḥ  ViP tadasya vaṃśasyanupūrvīmaśeṣavaṃśapāpapraṇāśanāya maitreyaitāṃ kathaṃ śṛṇu  ViP  tadyathā sakalajagatāmādiranādibhūtaḥsa ṛgyajuḥsāmādimayo bhagavān viṣṇustasya brahmaṇo martaṃ rūpaṃ hiraṇyagarbho brahmāṇḍabhūto brahmā bhagavān  prāgbabhūva  ViP  brahmaṇaś ca dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhajanmā dakṣaprajāpatiḥ dakṣasyāpyaditiraditervivasvān vivasvato manuḥ  ViP manorikṣvākunṛgadhṛṣṭaśaryātinariṣyantaprāṃśunābhagadiṣṭakarūṣapṛṣadhrākhyā daśa putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP iṣṭhaṭiṃ ca mitrāvaruṇayor manuḥ putrakāmaścakāra  ViP tatra tāvadahnute hoturapacārādilā nāma kanyā babhūva  ViP saiva ca mitrāvaruṇayoḥ prasādātsudyumno nāma manoḥ putro maitreya āsīt  ViP punaśceśvarakopātstrī satī sā tu somamūnorbudhasyāśramasamīpe babhrāma  ViP sānurāgācca tasyāṃ budhaḥ purūravasamātmajamutpādayāmāsa  ViP jātepi tasminnamitatejobhiḥ paramarṣibhir iṣṭimaya ṛṅmayo yajurmayaḥsāmamayotharvaṇamayaḥsarvavedamayo manomayo jñānamayo na kiñcinmayonnamayo bhagavān yajñapuruṣasvarūpī sudyumnasyapuṃstvamabhilaṣadbhir yathāva diṣṭastatprasādādilā punarapu sudyumno bhavat  ViP tasyāpyutakalagayavinatāstrayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP sudyumnastu strīpūrvakatvādrājyabhāgaṃ na lebhe  ViP tatpitrā tu vasiṣṭhavacanātpratiṣṭhāna nāma nagaraṃ sudyumnāya dattaṃ taccāsau purūravase prādāt  ViP tadanvayāścakṣatriyāḥsarvai dikṣvabhavan pṛṣadhrastu manuputro gurugovadhācchūdratvamagamat  ViP manoḥ putraḥ karūṣaḥ karūṣātkārūṣāḥ kṣatriyā mahābalaparākramababhūvaḥ  ViP diṣṭaputrastu nābhāgo vaiśyatāmagamattasmādbalandhanaḥ putrobhavat  ViP balandhanādvatsaprītirudārakīrtiḥ  ViP vatsaprīteḥ prāṃśurabhavat  ViP prajāpatiś ca prāṃśoreko bhavat  ViP tataś ca khanitraḥ  ViP tasmādapyavikṣit  ViP avikṣitopyatibalaparākramaḥ putro marutto nāmābhavat yasyemāvadyāpi ślokau gīyet  ViP maruttasya yathā yajñas tathā kasyābhavadbhuvi sarvaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ yasya yajñavastvatiśobhanam purīṃ ca kuśasthalīmadhyuvāsa  ViP revatāsyāpi raivataḥ putraḥ kakudmināmā dharmātmā bhrātṛśatasya jyoṣṭho bhavat  ViP tasya revatīnāmakanyābhavat  ViP sa tāmādāya kasyoyamarhatīti bhagavantamabjayoniṃ praṣṭuṃ brahmalokaṃ jagām  ViP tāvacca brahmaṇontike hāhāhūhūsaṃjñābhyāṃ gandharvābhyāmatitānaṃ nāma divyaṃ gāndharvamagīyata  ViP tacca trimārgaparivṛttair anekayugaparivṛttiṃ punaś ca praṇamya bhagavate tasmai yathābhimatānātmanaḥsa varān kathayāmāsa ka eṣāṃ bhagavatobhimata iti yasmai kanyāmimāṃ prayacchāmīti  ViP tataḥ kiñcidavanataśirāḥsasmitaṃ bhagavānabjayoniha  ViP ya ete bhavatobhimatā naiteṣāṃ sāṃprataṃ putrapautrāpatyāpatyasaṃtatirastyavanītale  ViP bahūni tavātraiva gāndharvaṃ śṛṇvataścaturyagānyatītāni  ViP ya ete bhavatobhimatā mahītaleṣṭāviṃśatitamamanoścaturyugamatītaprāyañca vartate  ViP āsanno hi kaliḥ  ViP anyasmai kanyāratnamidaṃ bhavataikākinābhimatāya deyam  ViP bhavatopi putramittrakalatramantribhṛtyabandhubalakośādayaḥsamastāḥ kālenaitenātyantamatītāḥ  ViP tataḥ punarapyutpannasādhvaso rājā bhagavantaṃ praṇamya papraccha  ViP bhagavannevamavasthite ma yeyaṃ kasmai deyeti  ViP tataḥsa bhagavān kiñcidavanamrakandharaḥ kṛtāñjalirbhūtvā sarvalokagururaṃbhojayonirāha  ViP brahmovācana hyādimadhyāntamajasya yasya vidmo vayaṃ sarvamayasya dhātuḥ na ca svarūpaṃ na paraṃ svabhāvaṃ na caiva sāraṃ parameśvarasya  ViP kalāmuhūrttādimayaś ca kālo na yadvibhūteḥ pariṇāmahetuḥ ajmanāśasya sadaikamurtteranāmarūpasya sanātanasya  ViP yasya prasādādahamacyutasya mūrtiḥ prajāsṛṣṭikaro ntakārī krodhācca rudraḥ sthitihetubhūto yasmāc madhye puruṣaḥ parasmāt  ViP tadrūpam āsthāya sṛjaty ajo yaḥ sthitau ca yo sau puruṣasvarūpī rudrasvarūpeṇa ca yotti viśvaṃ dhatte tathānantavapuḥsamastam  ViP pākāya yognitvamupaiti lokānbibhartti pṛthvīvapukhyāyātmā śakrādirūpī paripāti viśvamarkendurūpaś ca tamo hinasti  ViP karoti ceṣṭāḥ śvasanasvarūpī lokasya tṛptiṃ ca jalānnarūpī dadāti viśvasthitisaṃsthitastu sarvāvakāśaṃ ca nabhaḥsvarūpī  ViP yaḥsṛjyate sargakṛdātmanaiva yaḥ pālyate pālayitā ca devaḥ viśvatmakaḥsaṃhṛyatentakārī pṛthak trayasyāsya ca yovyayātmā  ViP yasmiñjagadyo jagadetadādyo yaṃ cāśritosmiñjagati svayaṃbhūḥ sa sarvabhūtaprabhavo dharitryāṃ svāṃśena puṣṇurnṛpa te vatīrṇaḥ  ViP kuśasthalī yā tava bhūpa ramyā purī purābhūdamarāvatīva sā dvārakā saṃprati tatra cāste sa keśavāṃśo baladevanāmā  ViP tasmai tvamenāṃ tanayāṃ naredra prāyaccha māyāmanujāya jāyām śloghyo veresau tanayā taveyaṃ strīratnabhūtā sadṛśo hi yogaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaitīritosau kamalodbhavena bhuvaṃ samāsādya patiḥ prajānām dadarśa hrasvān puruṣān virūpānalpaujasaḥsvalpavivekaviryān  ViP kuśasthaloṃ tāṃ ca puvarīmupetya dṛṣṭvānyarūpāṃ pradadau sa kanyām sīrāyudhāya sphaṭikācalābhavakṣasthalāyātuladhīrnaredraḥ  ViP uccapramāṇāmiti tāmavekṣya svalāṅgalāgreṇa ca tālaketuḥ vinamrayāmāsa tataś ca sāpi babhūva sadyo vanitā yathānyā  ViP tāṃ revatīṃraivatabhūpakanyāṃ sīrāyudho sau vidhinopayeme dattvātha sa nṛpo jagāma hemālayaṃ vai tapase dhṛtātmā  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe caturthāśe prathamodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācayāvacca brahmalokātsa kakudmī raivato nābhyeti tāvatpuṇyajanasaṃjñā rākṣasāstāmasya purīṃ kuśasthalīṃ najaghnuḥ  ViP taccāsya bhrātṛśataṃ puṇyajanatrāsāddiśo bheje  ViP tadanvayāścakṣatriyāḥsarvadikṣvabhavan  ViP vṛṣṭasyāpi vārṣṭakaṃ kṣatramabhavat  ViP nābhāgasyātmajo nābhāgasaṃtrobhavat  ViP tasyāpyaṃbarīṣaḥ  ViP aṃbarīṣasyāpi virūpobhavat  ViP virūpātpṛṣadaśvo jajñe  ViP tataś ca rathītaraḥ  ViP ātrāyaṃ ślokaḥete kṣatraprasūtā vai punaścāṅgirasāḥ smṛtā rathītarāṇāṃ pravarāḥ kṣatropetā dvijātayaḥ  ViP kṣutavataś ca manorikṣvākuḥ putro jajñe ghrāṇataḥ  ViP tasya putraśatapradhānā vikukṣinimidaṇḍākhyāstrayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP pañcāśatputrāḥ uttarātharakṣitāro babhūvuḥ  ViP catvāriṃśadaṣṭau ca dakṣiṇāpathabhūpālāḥ  ViP sa cekṣvākuraṣṭakāyāḥ śrāddhamutpādya śrāddhārhaṃ māṃsamānayeti vikukṣimājñāpayāmāsa  ViP sa tathe ti gṛhītājño vidhṛtaśārāsano vanamabhyetyānekaśo mṛgān hatvā śrāntotikṣutparīto vikukṣirekaṃ śaśamabhakṣayat śeṣaṃ ca māṃsamānīya pitrenivedayāmāsa  ViP ikṣvākukulācāryo vaśiṣṭhastatprokṣaṇāya coditaḥ prāha alamanenāmedhyenāmiṣeṇa durātmanā tava putreṇaitanmāṃsamupahataṃ yato nena śaśo bhakṣitaḥ  ViP tataścāsau vikukṣirgurūṇaivamuktaḥ śaśādasaṃjñāmavāpa pitrā ca parityaktaḥ  ViP pitaryuparate cāsāvakhilāmetāṃ pṛthvīṃ dharmataḥ śāśāsa  ViP śaśādasya tasya purañjayonāma putrobhavat  ViP tasyedaṃ cānyat  ViP purā hi tretāyāṃ devāsurayuddhamatibhīṣaṇamabhavat  ViP tatra cātibalibhir asurair amarāḥ parājitāste bhagavantaṃ viṣṇumārādhayāñcakruḥ  ViP prasannaś ca devānāmanādinidhanokhilajamatparāyaṇo nārāyaṇaḥ prāha  ViP jñātametanmayā yuṣmābhir yadabhilaṣitaṃ tadarthamidaṃ śrūyatām  ViP purañjayo nāma rājarṣeḥ śaśādasya tanayaḥ kṣatriyavaro yastasya śarīrehamaṃśena svayamevāvatīryatānaśeṣanasurānnihaniṣyāmi tadbhavadbhiḥ purañjayo suravadhārthamudyogaṃ kāryatāmiti  ViP etacca śrutvā praṇamya bhagavantaṃ viṣṇumamarāḥ purañjayasakāśamājagmurūcuścainam  ViP bhobhoḥ kṣatriyavaryāsmābhir abhyarthitena bhavatāsmākamarātivadhodyatānāṃ kartavyaṃsāhāyyamicchāmaḥ tadbhavatāsmākamabhyāgatānāṃ praṇayabhaṅgo na kārya ityuktaḥ puṃrajayaḥprāha  ViP  trailokyanātho yoyaṃ yuṣmākamidraḥ śatakraturasya yadyahaṃ skandhādhirūḍho yuṣmākamarātibhaḥsaha yotsye tadahaṃ bhavatāṃ sahāyaḥ syām  ViP ityākarṇya samastadevair indreṇa ca bāḍhamityevaṃ samanvicchitam  ViP  tataś ca śatakratorvṛṣarūpadhārīmaḥ kakudi sthito tiroṣasamanvito bhagavataścarāguroracyutasya tejasāpyāyito devāsurasaṃgrāme samastānevāsurānnijaghāna yataś ca vṛṣabhakakudi sthitena rājñā daiteyabalaṃ niṣūditamataścāsau kakutsthasaṃjñāmavāpa  ViP kakutsthasyāpyanenāḥ putro bhavat  ViP puthunenasaḥ  ViP puthorviṣṭarāśvaḥ  ViP tasyāpi cāndro yuvanāśvaḥ  ViP cāndrasya tasya yuvanāśvasya śāvastaḥ yaḥ purīṃ śāvastīṃ niveśayāmāsa  ViP śāvastasya vṛhadaśvaḥ  ViP tasyāpi kuvālāyāśvaḥ  ViP  yosāvudakasya maharṣerapakāriṇaṃ dundunāmānamasuraṃ vaiṣṇavena tejasāpyāyitaḥ putrasahasrair ekaviṃśadbhiḥ parivṛto javāna dundumārasaṃjñāmavāpa tasya ca tanayāsptamastā eva dundumukhanisvāsāgninā vipluṣṭā vineśuḥ  ViP dṛḍhāśvacandrāśvakapilāśvāś ca trayaḥ kevalaṃ śeṣitāḥ  ViP vṛḍhāśvāddharyaśvaḥ  ViP tasmācca nikuṃbhaḥ  ViP nikuṃbhasyāmitāśvaḥ  ViP tataś ca kṛśāśvaḥ  ViP tasmācca prasenajit  ViP prasenajito yuvanāśvobhavat  ViP tasya cāputrasyātinirvedāmunīnāmāśramamaṇḍale nivasato dayālubhir munibhir apatyotpādanāyeṣṭaḥ kṛtā  ViP tasyāṃ ca madhyārātrau nivṛttāyāṃ mantrapūtajalapūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ vedimadhye nivesya te munayaḥ suṣupuḥ  ViP supteṣu teṣu atīva tṛṭparītaḥsa bhūpālastamāśramaṃ viveśa  ViP tānṛṣīnnaivotthāpayāmāsa  ViP tacca kalaśamaparimeyamāhatmayamantrapūtaṃ papau  ViP prabuddhāś ca ṛṣayaḥ paprachuḥ kenaitaṃ mantrapūtaṃ vāri pītam  ViP atra hi rājño yuvanāsvasya patnī mahābalaparākramaṃ putraṃ janayiṣyati ityākarṇya sa rājā ajānatā mayā pītamityāha  ViP garbhaś ca yuvanāśvasyodare abhavat krameṇa ca vavṛdhe  ViP prāptasamayaś ca dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhena kukṣimavanipaternirbhidya niścakrāma  ViP sa cāsau rājā mamāra  ViP jāto nāmaiṣa kaṃ dhāsyatīti te munayaḥ procuḥ  ViP athāgatya devarājobrajīt māmayaṃ dhāsyatīti  ViP tato mādhātṛnāmā sobhavat vakre cāsya pradeśinī nyastā devendreṇa nyastātāṃ papau  ViP tāṃ cāmṛtastrāviṇīmāsvādyāhnaiva sa vyavardhata  ViP tatastu māndhātā cakravartī saptadvīpāṃ mahīṃ vubhuje  ViP tatrāyaṃ śvokaḥ  ViP yāvatsūrya udetyastaṃ yāvacca pratitiṣṭhati sarvaṃ tadyauvanāśvasya māndhātupaḥ kṣetramucyate  ViP māndhātā śatabindor duhitaraṃ bundumatīmupayem  ViP purukutsamaṃbarīṣaṃ mucukundaṃ ca tasyāṃ putratrayamutpādayāmāsa  ViP pañcāśadduhitarastasyāmeva tasya nṛpaterbabhūvuḥ  ViP ekasminnantare bahūvṛcaścaja saubharirnāma maharṣirantarjale dvādaśābdaṃ kālamuvāsa tatra cāntarjale saṃmado nāmātibabahu prajotimātrapramāṇo mīnādhipatirāsīt    tasya ca putrapautradauhitrāḥ pṛṣṭhato grataḥ pārśvayoḥ pakṣapucchaśirasāṃ copari bhramantastenaiva sadāharniśamatinirvṛttā remire  ViP  sa cāpatyasparśopacīyamānapraharṣaprakarṣo bahuprakāraṃ tasya ṛṣeḥ paśyatastair ātmajaputrapautradauhitrādibhiḥ sahānudinaṃ surāṃ reme  ViP  athāntarjalāvasthitaḥsaubharirekāgrataḥsamādhimapahāyānudinaṃ tasya satsyasyātmajaputrapautradauhitrā dibhiḥ sahātiramaṇīyatāmavekṣyācintayat  aho dhanyoyamīdṛśamanabhimataṃ yonyantaramavāpyaibhir ātmajaputrapautradauhitrādibhiḥ saha ramamāṇodīvāsmākaṃ spṛhāmutpādayati  ViP  vayamapyevaṃ putrādibhiḥ saha lalitaṃ ramiṣyāma ityevamabhikāṅkṣan sa tasmādantarjalānniṣkramya saṃtānāya niveṣṭukāmaḥ kanyārthaṃ māndhātāraṃ  rājānamagacchat  ViP  āgamanaśravaṇasamanantaraṃ cotthāya tena rājñā samyagarghyādinā saṃpūjitaḥ kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ saubhariruvāca rājānam  ViP anyepi saṃtyeva nṛpāḥ pṛthivyāṃ māndhātareṣāṃ prayaccha me mā praṇayaṃ vibhāṅkṣiḥ na hyarthinaḥ kāryavaśādupetāḥ kakutsthavaṃśe vimukhāḥ prayānti  ViP anyepi saṃtyeva nṛpāḥ pṛtivyāṃ māndhātareṣāṃ tanayāḥ prasūtāḥ kiṃ tvarthināmarthitadānadīkṣākṛtavrataślāghyamidaṃ kulaṃ te  ViP śatārdhasaṃkhyā stava saṃti kanyāstāsāṃ mamaikāṃ nṛpate prayaccha yatprārthanābhaṅgabhayādbibhemi tasmādahaṃ rājavarādiduḥkhāt  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti ṛṣivacanamākarṇya sa rājā jarārjaritadehamṛṣimālokya pratyākhyānakātarastasmāccaca śāpabhīto bibhyatkiñcidadhomukhaściraṃ dadhyau ca saubhariruvācanaredrakasmātsumupaiṣi cīntāmahyamuktaṃ na mayātra kiñcit yāvaśyadeyā tanayā tayaiva kṛtārthatā no yadi kiṃ na labdhā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaatha tasya bhagavataḥ śāpabhītaḥsapraśrayastamuvācāsau rājā  ViP rājovācabhagavan asmatkulasthitiriyaṃ ya eva kanyābhir ucito bhijavānvarastasmai kanyā pradīyatebhagavadyācñā cāsmanmanorathānāmapyatigocajaravartinī kathamapyeṣā saṃjātā tadevamupasthitena vidmaḥ kiṃ kurma ityetanmayācintyata ityabhihite ca tena bhūbhujā muniracintayat  ViP  ayamanyo smatpratyākhyānopāyo vṛddhoyamanabhimataḥ strīṇāṃ kimata kanyākānāmityamunā saṃcintyaitadabhihitamevamastu tathā kariṣyāmīti saṃcintya  māndhātāramuvāca  ViP  yadyevaṃ tadādiśyatāmasmākaṃ praveśāya  kaṃnyāntaḥpuraṃ varṣavaro yadi kanyaiva kācinmāmabhilaṣati tadāhaṃ dārasaṃgrahaṃ kariṣyāmi anyathā cettadalamasmākametenātītakālāraṃbhaṇenetyuktvā  virarāma  ViP  tataś ca māndhātrā muniśāpaśaṃ kitena kanyāntaḥpuravarṣadharaḥsamājñaptaḥ  ViP tena saha kanyāntaḥpuraṃ praviśānneva bhagavānakhilasiddhagandharvebhyotiśayena kamanīyaṃ rūpamakarot  ViP praveśya ca tamṛṣimantaḥpure varṣadharastāḥ kanyāḥ prāha  ViP bhavatīnāṃ janayitā mahārājaḥsamājñāpayati  ViP ayamasmān brahmarṣiḥ kanyārthaṃ samabhyāgataḥ  ViP mayā cāsya pratijñātaṃ yadyasmatkanyā yā kācidbhagavantaṃ varayati tatkanyācchandenāhaṃ paripaṃṣathānaṃ kariṣyāmītyākarmya sarvā eva tāḥ kanyāḥ sānurāgāḥ sapramadāḥkeṇava iva mṛgayūthapatiṃ tamṛṣimahamahamikayā varayāṃbabhūvurūcuś ca  ViP alaṃ bhaginyohamimaṃ vṛṇomi vṛṇomyahaṃ naiṣa yadā munis tābhir atīvahārdāddhṛtaḥsa kanyābhir anindyakīrtiḥ tadā sa kanyādhikṛto nṛpāya yathāvajācaṣṭa vinamramūrtiḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatadavagamātkiṅkibhetatkathadhametatkiṃ kiṃ karomi kiṃ mayābhihitamityākulamatiranicchannapi kathamapi rājānumene  ViP kṛtānurūpavivāhaś ca maharṣiḥsakalā eva tāḥ kanyāḥsvamāśramamanayat  ViP  tatra cāseṣaśilpakalpapraṇetāraṃ dhātāramivānyaṃ viśvakarmāṇamāhūya sakalakanyānāmekaikasyāḥ protphullapaṅkajāḥ kūjatkalahaṃsakāraṇḍavādivihaṅgamābhirāmajalāśayāḥsopadhānāḥ sāvakāsāḥsādhuśayyāparicchadāḥ prāsādāḥ kriyantāmityādideśa  ViP tacca tathaivānuṣṭhitamaśeṣaśilpaviseṣācāryastvaṣṭā darśitavān  ViP tataḥ paramarṣiṇā saubhariṇājñaptasteṣu gṛheṣvanivāryānandakundamahānidhirāsāṃcakre  ViP tato navalatena bhakṣyabhojyalehyādyupabhogaurāgatānugatabhṛtyādīnaharniśamaśeṣagṛheṣu tāḥ kṣitiśaduhirato bhojayāmāmuḥ  ViP ekadātu duhitṛsnehākṛṣṭahṛdayaḥsa mahīpatiratiduḥkhitāstā uta sukhitā vā iti vicintyatasya maharṣerāśramasamīpamupetya sphuradaṃśumālālalāmāṃ sphaṭikamayaprāsādamālāmatiramyopavanajalāśayāṃdadarśa  ViP praviśya caikaṃ prāsādamātmajāṃ pariṣvajya kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ pravṛddhasnehanayanāṃbugarbhanayanobravīt  ViP  apyatra vatse bhavatyāḥsukhamuna kiñcidamukhamapi te maharṣiḥsnehavānuta na smaryatesmadguhavāsa ityuktā taṃ tanayā pitaramāha  ViP tātātiramaṇīyaḥ prāsādotrātimanojñamupavanamete kalavākyavihaṅgamābhirutāḥ protphullapadmākarajalāśayāḥmanonurūlabhakṣyabhojyānulepanavastrabhūṣaṇādibhogo mṛdūni śayanāsanāni sarvasaṃpatsametaṃme gārhasthyam  ViP tathāpi kena vā janmabhūmirna smaryate  ViP tvatprasādādidamaśeṣamatiśobhanam  ViP  kiṃ tvekaṃ mamaitadduḥkhakāraṇaṃ yadasmadgṛhānmaharṣirayaṃmadbhartā na viṣkrāmati mamaiva kevalamatiprītyā samīpaparivartinīnāmanyāsāmasmadbhaginīnām  evaṃ ca mama sodaryotiduḥkhitā ityevamatiduḥkhakāraṇamityuktastayā dvitīyaṃ prāsādamupetya svatanayāṃ pariṣvajyopiṣṭastathaiva vṛṣṭavān  tayāpi ca sarvametattatprāsādādyupabhogasukhaṃ bhṛśamākhyātaṃ mamaiva kevalamatiprītyāpārśvaparivartinīnāmanyāsāmasmadbhaginīnāmityevamādiśrutvā samastaprāsādeṣu rājāpraviveśa tanayāṃ tanayāṃ tathaivāvṛcchat  ViP  sarvābhiś ca tābhis tathaivābhihitaḥ paritoṣavismayanirbhavavivaśahṛdayo bhagavantaṃ saubharikekāntāvasthitamupetya kṛtapṛjobravīt  ViP dṛṣṭaste bhagavan sumahāneṣa siddhiprabhāvo naivaṃvidhamanyasya kasyacidasmābhirvibhūtibhir vilāsitamupalakṣitaṃ yadetadbhagavatastapasaḥ phalamityabhipūjya tamṛṣiṃtatraiva tena ṛṣivaryeṇa casaha kiñcitkālamabhimatopabhogān bubhuje svapuraṃ ca jagām  ViP kālena gacchatā tasya tāsu rājatanayāsu putraśataṃ sārdhamabhavat  ViP anudinānurūḍhasnehaprasāś ca sa tatrātīvamamatākṛṣṭahṛdayo bhavat  ViP apyete smatputrāḥ kalabhāṣiṇaḥ pabhdyāṃ gaccheyuḥ apyete yauvanino bhaveyuḥ apikṛtadārānetān paśyeyamapyeṣāṃ putrā bhaveyuḥ apyetatputrānputrasamanvitānpasyāmītyādimanorathānanudinaṃkālasaṃpattipravṛddhānupekṣyaitaccintayāmāsa  ViP aho me mohasyātivistāraḥ  ViP manorathānāṃ na samāptirasti varṣāyutenāpyatha vāpi lakṣaiḥ pūrṇeṣupūrṇeṣu manorathānāmutpattayaḥsaṃti punarnavānām  ViP padbhyāṃ gatā yauvaninaś ca jātā dāraiś ca saṃyogamitāḥ prasūtāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ sutāstattanayaprasūtindraṣṭuṃ punarvāñcchati meṃtarātmā  ViP drakṣyāmi teṣāmiti cetprasūtiṃ manoratho me bhavitā tatonyaḥ purṇopi tatrāpyaparasya janma nivaryate kena manorathasya  ViP āmṛtyuto naiva manorathānāmantosti vijñātamidaṃ mayādya manorthāsaktiparasya cittaṃ na jāyate vai paramārthasaṃgi  ViP sa me samādhirjalavāsamitramatsyasya saṃgātsa hasaiva naṣṭaḥ parigrahaḥsaṃgakṛto mayāyaṃ parigrahotthā ca mamātilipsā  ViP duḥkhaṃ yadaivaikaśarīrajanma śatārdhasaṃkhyākamidaṃ prasūtam parigraheṇa kṣitipātmajānāṃ sutair anekair bahulīkṛtaṃ tata  ViP mutātmajais tattanayaiś ca bhūyo bhūyaś ca teṣāṃ parigraheṇa vistārameṣyatyadiduḥkhahetuḥ parigraho vai mamatābhidhānaḥ  ViP cīrṇaṃ tapo yattu jalāśrayeṇa tasyārdhireṣā tapasoṃtarāyaḥ matsyasya saṃgādabhavacca yo me sutādirāgo muṣitosmi nena  ViP niḥsaṃgatā muktipadaṃ yatīnāṃ saṃgādaśeṣāḥ prabhavanti doṣāḥ ārūḍhayogo vinipātyatedhaḥsaṃgena yogī kimutālpabuddhiḥ  ViP ahaṃ cariṣyāmi tadātmanorthe pariprahagrāhagṛhītabuddhiḥ yadā hi bhūyaḥ parihinadoṣo janasya duḥkhair bhavitā na duḥkhī  ViP sarvasya dhātārama cintyarūpamaṇoraṇīyāṃsamatipramāṇam sitāsitaṃ ceśvaramīśvarāṇāmārādhayiṣye tapasaiva viṣṇum  ViP tasminnaśeṣaujasi sarvarūpaṇyavyaktavispaṣṭatanāvanante mamācalaṃ cittamapetadoṣaṃ sadāstu viṣṇāvamavāya bhūyaḥ  ViP samastabhūtādamalādanantātsarveśvarādanyadanādimadhyāt yasmānna kiñcittamahaṃ gurūṇāṃ paraṃ guruṃ saṃśrayamemi viṣṇumā  ViP śrīparāśara uvāca ityātmānimātmanaivābidāyāsau saubharirapahāya putragṛhāsanaparigrahādikamaśeṣamarthajātaṃ sakalabhāryāsamanvitoṃ vanaṃ praviveśa  ViP  tatrāpyanudinaṃ vaikhānasaniṣpādyamaśeṣakriyākalāpaṃ niṣpādya kṣapitasakalapāpaḥ paripakvamanovṛttirātmanyagnīnsamāropya bhikṣurabhavat   bhagavatyāsajyākhilaṃ karmakalāpaṃ hitvānaṃ śrāvayati dharatyavadhārayatilikhati lekhayati śikṣayatyadhyāpayatyupadiśati vā tasya ṣaṭ janmāni duḥsaṃtatirasaddharmovāḍmanasorasanmārgācaraṇasaśeṣahetuṣu vā mamatvaṃ na bhavati  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe caturthāśe dvitīyo dhyāyaḥ ataś ca mādhātuḥ putrasaṃtatirabhidhīyate  ViP aṃbarīṣasya māndhātṛtanayasya yuvanāśvaḥ putro bhūt  ViP tasmāddhārītaḥ yatoṅgiraso hārītā  ViP rasātale mauneyā nāma gandharvā babhūvuḥṣaṭkoṭisaṃkhyātāstair aśeṣāṇi nāgakulānyapahṛtapradhānaratnādhipatyānyakriyanta  ViP  taiś ca gandharvavīryāvabūtair urageśvaraiḥ stūyamāno bhagavānaśeṣadeveśa āste bhagavānanādinidhanapuruṣottamo yosau yauvanāśvasya māndhātuḥ purukutsanāmā putrastamahāmanupraviśya tānaśeṣān duṣṭagandharvānupaśamaṃ  nayiṣyāmīti  ViP  tadākarṇya bhagavate jalaśāyine kṛtapraṇāmāḥ punarnāgalokamāgatāḥ pannagādhipatayo narmadāñca purukutsānayanāya codayāmāsuḥ  ViP sā cainaṃ rasātalaṃ nītavatī  ViP rasātalagataścāsau yabhagavattejasāpyāyitātmavīryaḥsakalagandharvānnijaghāna  ViP punaś ca svapuramājagāma  ViP sakalapannagādhipatayaś ca narmadāyai varaṃ daduḥ yattenusmaraṇasamavetaṃ nāmagrahaṇaṃ kariṣyati na tasya sarpaviṣabhayaṃ bhaviṣyatīti  ViP atra ca ślokaḥ  ViP narmadāyai namaḥ prātarnarmadāyai namo niśi namostu narmade tubhyaṃ trāhi māṃ viṣasarpataḥ  ViP ityuccāryāharniśamandhakārapraveśe vā sarpair na daśyate na cāpi kṛtānusmaraṇabhujo viṣamapi bhuktamupaghātāya bhavati  ViP purukutsāya saṃtativicchedo na bhaviṣyatītyuragapatayo paraṃ daduḥ  ViP purukutso narmadāyāṃ trasaddasyumajījanat  ViP trasaddasyutaḥsaṃbhūto naraṇyaḥ yaṃ rāvaṇodigvijaye jaghān  ViP anaraṇyasya pṛṣaṭaśvaḥ pṛṣadaśvasya haryaśvaḥ putro bhavat  ViP tasya ca hastaḥ putro bhavat  ViP tataś ca sumanāstasyāpi tridhanvā tridhanvanastrayyāruṇiḥ  ViP trayyāruṇeḥsatyavrataḥ yo sau triśaṅkusaṃjñāmavāpa  ViP sa caṇḍālatāmupagataś ca  ViP dvādaśavarṣikyāmanāvṛṣṭyāṃ viśvāmitrakalatrāpatyapoṣaṇārthaṃ caṇḍālapratigraharaṇāya ca jāhnavītīranyagrodhe mṛgamāṃsamanudinaṃ babandha sa tu parituṣṭena viśvāmitreṇa saśarīraḥsvargamāropitaḥ  ViP triśaṅkorhariścandrastasmācca rohitāśvastataś ca harito haritasya cañcuścañcorvijayavasudevau ruruko vijayādrukasya vṛkaḥ  ViP tato vṛkasya bāhuḥ yo sau haihayatālajaṅghādibhiḥ parājitontarvatnyā mahiṣyā saha vanaṃ praviveśa  ViP tasyāścā sapatnyā garbhastaṃbhanāya garo dattaḥ  ViP tenāsya garbhaḥsaptavarṣāṇi jaṭhara eva tasthau  ViP sa ca bāhurvṛddhabhāvādaurvāśramamamīpe mamāra  ViP sā tasya bhāryā citāṃ kṛtvā tamāropyānuparaṇakṛtaniścayābhūt  ViP athaitāmatītānāgatavartamānakālatrayavedī bhagavānaurvacaḥsvāśramānnirgatyābravīt  ViP tasmādanumaraṇanirbandhādvirarāma  ViP tenaiva ca bhagavatā svāśramamānītā  ViP tatra kativayadinābhyantare ca sahaiva tena gareṇātitejasvī bālako jajñe  ViP tasyaurvo jātakarmādikriyā niṣpādya sagara sarvamevāvocat  ViP tataś ca pitṛrājyapaharaṇādamarṣito haihayatālajaṅghādivadhāya pratijñāmakarot  ViP prāyaśaś ca haihayatālajaṅghāñjaghāna  ViP śakayavanakāṃbhojapāradapaplavāḥ samādhinārādhito varamadāt  ViP  ekā vaṃśakaramekaṃ putramaparā ṣaṣṭiṃ putrasahasrāṇāṃ janayiṣyatīti yasyā yadabhimataṃ tadicchayā gṛhyatāmityukte keśinyekaṃ varayāmāsa  sumatiḥ putrasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭiṃ bhagavantokhilasasāraduḥkhahantāraḥ  ViP na hyetādṛganyadduḥkhamasti yaccharīrātmanorviyoge bhavati  ViP  tadahamicchāmi sakalalokalocaneṣu vastuṃ na punaḥ śarīragrahaṇaṃ kartumityevamuktair devair asāvaśeṣabhūtānāṃ netreṣvavatāritaḥ  ViP tato bhūtānyunmeṣanimeṣaṃ cakruḥ  ViP aputrasya ca tasya bhūbhujaḥ śarīramarājakabhīravo munayo raṇyā mamanthuḥ  ViP tatra ca kumāro jajñe  ViP jananājjanakasaṃjñāṃ cāvāpa  ViP abhūdvidehosya piteti vaidehaḥ mathanānmithiriti  ViP tasyodāvasuḥ putro bhavat  ViP udāvasornadivardhanastataḥsuketuḥ tasmāddevarātastataś ca bṛhadukthaḥ tasya ce mahāvīryastasyāpi sudhṛti  ViP tataścadhṛṣṭaketurajāyata  ViP dhṛṣṭaketorharyaśvastasya ca manuḥ manoḥ patikaḥ tasmātkṛtarathastasya devamīḍhaḥtasya ca vibudhaḥ vibudhasya mahādhṛtistataś ca kṛtarātaḥ tato mahāromā tasya svarṇaromātatputro hrasvaroṇā hrasvaromṇaḥsīradhvajo bhavat  ViP tasya putrarthaṃ yajanabhuvaṃ kṛṣataḥ sīre sītā duhitā samutpannā  ViP sīradhvajasya bhrātā saṃkāśyadhipatiḥ kuśadhvajanāmāsīt  ViP sīradhvajasyāpatyaṃ bhānumān bhānumataḥ śatadyumnaḥ tasya tu śuciḥ tasmāccorjanāmā putro jajñe  ViP tasyāpi śatadhvajaḥ tataḥ kṛtiḥ kṛterañjanaḥ tatputraḥ kurujit tato riṣṭanemiḥ tasmācchutāyuḥśrutāyuṣaḥ supārśvāḥ tasmātsṛṃjayaḥ tataḥ kṣemāvī kṣemāvino nenāḥ tasmādbhaumarathaḥtasya satyarathaḥ tasmādupaguḥ upagor upaguptaḥ tatputraḥ svāgatastasya ca svānandaḥtasmācca suvarcāḥ tasya supārśvaḥ tasyāpisubhāṣaḥ suśrutaḥ tasmāsuśrutājjayaḥ tasyaputro vijayaḥ vijayasya ṛtaḥ ṛtātsunayaḥ sunayādvītahavyaḥ tasmāddhūtiḥ dhṛtervabahulāsvaḥtasya putraḥ kṛtiḥ  ViP kṛtau saṃtiṣṭhatyayaṃ janakavaṃśaḥ  ViP ityete maithilāḥ  ViP prāyeṇaite ātmavidyāśrayiṇo bhūpālā bhavanti  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe caturthāṃse pañcamo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācasūryasya vaṃśyā bhagavankathitā bhavatā mama somasyāpyakhilānvaśyāñchrotumicchāmi pārthivān  ViP kīrtyate sthirakīrtīnāṃ yeṣāmadyāpi saṃtatiḥ prasādasumukhastānme brahmannākhyātumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaśrūyatāṃ muniśārdūla vaṃśaḥ pratithatejasaḥ somasyānukramātkhyātā yatrorvīpatayo bhavan  ViP  ayaṃ hi vaṃśotibalaparākramadyutiśīlaceṣṭavadbhir atiguṇānvitair nahuṣayayātikārtavīryārjunādibhir bhūpālair alaṅkṛtaḥ tamahaṃ kathayāmi śrūyatām akhilajagatstraṣṭurbhagavato nārāyaṇasya nābhikalojasamudbhavābjayonerbrahmaṇaḥ putro triḥ  ViP atreḥsomaḥ  ViP taṃ ca bhagavānabjayoniḥ aśeṣauṣadhīdvijanakṣatrāṇāmādhipatye bhyaṣecayat  ViP sa ca rājasūyamakarot  ViP tatprabhāvādatyutkṛṣṭādhipatyādhiṣṭhātṛtvāccainaṃ mada āviveśa  ViP madāvalepācca sakaladevagurorbṛspatestārāṃ nāma patnīṃ jahāra  ViP bahuśaś ca bṛhaspaticoditena bhagavatā brahmaṇā codyamānasakalaiś ca devarṣibhir yācamāno pi na mumoca  ViP tasya candrasya ca bṛhaspaterdvaṣāduśānā pārṣṇigrāhobhūt  ViP aṅgīrasaś ca sakāśādupalabdhavidyo bhagavānrudro bṛhaspateḥ sahāyyamakarot  ViP yataścośanā tato jaṃbhakuṃbhādyāḥ samastā eva daityadānavanikāyā mahāntamudyamaṃ cakruḥ  ViP bṛhaspaterapi sakaladevasainyayutaḥ sahāyaḥ śakro bhavat  ViP evaṃ ca tayoratīvograsaṃgrāmastārānimittastārakāmayo nāmābhūt  ViP tataś ca samastaśastraṇyamureṣu rudrapurogamā devā deveṣu cāśeṣdānavā mumucuḥ evaṃ devāsurāhavasaṃkṣobhakṣubdhadṛdayamaśeṣameva jagadbrahmaṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagām   tataś ca bhagavānabjayonirapyuśanasaṃ saṃkaramasurāndevāṃś ca nivārya bṛhaspataye tārāmadāpayat  ViP tāṃ cāntaḥprasavāmavalokya bṛhaspatirapyāha  ViP naiṣa mama kṣetre bhavatyānyasya suto dhāryaḥsamutsṛjainamalamalamatidhāṣṭaryeneti  ViP sa ca tenaivamuktātipativratā bhartṛvacanānantaraṃ tamiṣīkāstaṃbe garbhamutsasarja  ViP sa cotsṛṣṭamātra evātitejasā devānāṃ tejāṃsyācikṣepa  ViP bṛhaspatiminduṃ ca tasya kumārasyāticārutayā sābhalāṣau dṛṣṭvā deviḥsamutpannasaṃdehāstārāṃ papracchuḥ  ViP satyaṃ kathayāsmākamiti subhage somasyātha vā bṛhaspaterayaṃ putra iti  ViP evaṃ tair uktā sā tārā hriyā kiñcinnovāca  ViP bahuśopyabhihitā yadāsau devebhyo nāccakṣe tataḥsa kumārastāṃ śaptumudyataḥ prāha  ViP duṣṭeṃba kasmānmama tātaṃ nākhyāsi  ViP adyaiva te vyalīkalajjāvatyās tathā śāstimahaṃ karomi  ViP yathā ca naivamadyāpyatimantharavacanābhaviṣyasīti  ViP athāha bhagavān pitāmahaḥ taṃ kumāraṃ sannivārya svayamapṛcchattāṃ tārām  ViP vatse kasyāyamātmajaḥ somasya vā bṛhaspatervā ityuktā lajjamānāha somasyeti  ViP  tataḥ prasphuraducdhvāsitāmalakapolakāntirbhagavānuḍupatiḥ kumāramāliṅgya sādhu sādhu vatsa prājñosītibudha iti tasya ca nāma cakre  ViP tadākhyātamevaitat sa ca yathelāyāmātmajaṃ purūravamamutpādayāmāsa  ViP  purūravāstvatidānaśīlo tiyajvātitejasvī yaṃ satyavādinamatirūpasvitaṃ manasvinaṃ mitrāvaruṇaśāpānmānuṣe loke mayā vastavyamiti kṛtamatirurvaśī  dadarśa  ViP  dṛṣṭamātre ca tasminnapahāya mānamaśeṣamapāsya svargasukhābhilāṣaṃ tanmanaskā bhūtvā tamevopatasthe  ViP so pi ca tāmatiśayitasakalalokastrīkāntisaukumāryalāvaṇyagativilāsahāsādigumāmavalokya tadāyattacittavṛttirbabhūva  ViP ubhayamapi tanmanaskamananyadṛṣṭi parityaktasa mastānyaprayojanamabhūt  ViP rājā tu prāgalbhyāttāmāha  ViP subhru tvāmahamabhikāmo smi prasīdānurāgamudvahetyuktā lajjāvakhaṇḍitamurvaśī taṃ prāha  ViP bhavatvevaṃ yadi me samayaparipālanaṃ bhavān karotītyākhyāte punapi tāmāha  ViP ākhyāhi me samayamiti  ViP atha pṛṣṭā punarapyabravīt  ViP śayanasamīpe mamoraṇakadvayaṃ putrabhūtaṃ nāpaneyam  ViP bhavāṃś ca mayā na nagnodraṣṭavyaḥ  ViP ghṛtamātraṃ ca mamāhāra iti  ViP evameveti bhūpātirapyāha  ViP  tayā saha sa cāvanipatiralākayāṃ caitrarathādivaneṣvamalapadmakhaṇḍeṣu mānasādisaraḥsvatiramaṇīyeṣu ramamāṇa ekaṣaṣṭivarṣāṇyanudinapravardadhamānapramodo  nayat  ViP  urvaśī ca tadupabhogātpratidinapravardhamānānu rāgā amaralokavāse pi na spṛhāṃ cakāra  ViP vinā corvaśyā suraloko psarasāṃ siddhagandharvāṇāṃ ca nātiramaṇīyo bhavat  ViP tataścorvaśī purūravasoḥsamayavidviśvāsurgandharvasamaveto niśi śayanābhyāśādekamuraṇakaṃ jahāra  ViP tasyākāśe nīyamānasyorvaśī śabdamaśṛṇot  ViP evamuvāca ca mamānāthāyāḥ putraḥ kenāpahriyate kaṃ śaraṇamupayāmīti  ViP tadākarṇya rājā māṃ devī vīkṣyatīti na yayau  ViP athānyamapyuraṇakamādāya gandharvā yayuḥ  ViP tasyāpyapahriyamāṇasyākarṇya śabdamākāśe punarapyanāthāsmyahamabhartṛkā kāpuruṣā śrayetyārtarāviṇī babhūva  ViP rājāpyamarṣavaśādandhakārametaditi khaḍgamādāya duṣṭaduṣṭa hatosīti vyāharannabhyadhāvat  ViP tāvacca gandharvai rapyatīvojjvalā vidyujjanitā  ViP tatprabhayā corvaśī rājānamapagatāṃbaraṃ dṛṣṭvāpavṛttasamayā tatkṣaṇādevāpakrāntā  ViP parityajya tāvapyuraṇakau gandarvāḥsuralokamupagatāḥ  ViP rājāpi ca tau meṣāvādāyātihṛṣṭamanāḥ svaśayanamāyāto norvaśīṃ dadarśa  ViP tāṃ cāpaśyan vyapagatāṃbara evonmattarūpo babhrāma  ViP kurukṣetre cāṃbhojasarasyanyābhiścatasṛbhir apsarobhiḥ samavetāmurvaśīṃ dadarśa  ViP tataśconmattarūpo jāye he tiṣṭha manasi dhore tiṣṭha vacasi kapaṭike tiṣṭhetyevamanekaprakāraṃ sūktamavocat  ViP āha corvaśī  ViP mahārājālamanenāvivekaceṣṭitena  ViP  antarvatnyahamabdānte bhavatātrāgantavyaṃ kumāraste bhabiṣyati ekāṃ ca niśāmahaṃ tvayā saha vatsyāmītyuktaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥsvapuraṃ jagāma  ViP tāsāṃ cāpsarasāmūrvaśī kathayāmāsa  ViP ayaṃ sa puruṣotkṛṣṭo yenāhametāvantaṃ kālamanurāgākṛṣṭamānasā sahoṣiteti  ViP evamuktāstāścāpsarasa ūcuḥ  ViP sādhusādhvasya rūpamapyanena sahāsmākamapi sarvakālamāsyā bhavediti  ViP abde ca pūrṇe sa rājā tatrājagāma  ViP kumāraṃ cāyuṣamasmai corvaśī dadau  ViP dattvā caikāṃ niśāṃ tena rājñā sahoṣitvā pañca putrotpattaye garbhamavāpa  ViP uvāca cainaṃ rājānamasmatprītyā mahārājāya sarva eva gandharvā varadāḥsaṃvṛttāḥ vriyatāṃ ca vara iti  ViP āha ca rājā  ViP vijitasakalārātiravihatendriyasāmarthyo bandhumānamitabalakośo smi nānyadasmākamurvaśīsālokyātprāptavyamastitadahamanayāsahorvaśyā kālaṃ netumabhilaṣāmītyukte gandharvā rājñe gnisthālīṃ daduḥ  ViP  ūcuścainamagnimāmnāyānusārī bhūtvā tridhā kṛtvervaśī salokatāmanorathamuddiśya samyagyajethāḥ tato vasyamabhilaṣitamavāpsyatītyuktastāmagnistālīmādāya  jagāma  ViP  antaraṭavyāmacitayat aho me tīva muḍhatā kimahamakaravam  ViP vahnisthālī mayaiṣānītā norvaśīti  ViP athaināmaṭavyāmevāgnisthālīṃ tatyāja svapuraṃ ca jagām  ViP vyatīterddharātre vinidraścācintayat  ViP mamorvaśīsālokyaprāptayarthamagnisthālī gandharvair dattā sā ca mayāṭavyāṃ parityaktā  ViP tadahaṃ tatra tadāharaṇāya yāsyāmītyutthāya tatrāpyupagato nāgnisthālīmapaśyat  ViP śamīgarbhaṃ cāśvātthamagnisthālīsthāne dṛṣṭvācintayat  ViP mayātrāgnisthālī nikṣiptā sā cāśvatthaḥ śamīgarbho bhūt  ViP tadenamevāhamagnirūpamādāya svapuramabhigamyāraṇīṃ kṛtvā tadutpannāgnerupāstiṃ kariṣyāmīti  ViP evameva svapuramabhigamyāraṇiṃ cakāra  ViP tatpramāṇaṃ cāṅgulaiḥ kurvan gāyatrīmapaṭhat  ViP paṭhataścākṣarasaṃkhyānyevāṅgulānyaraṇyabhavat  ViP tatrāgniṃ nirmathyāgnitrayamāmnāyānusārī bhūtvā juhāva  ViP urvaśīsālokyaṃ phalamabhisaṃdhitavān  ViP tenaiva cāgnividhinā bahuvidhān yajñāniṣṭvā gāndharvalokāna vāpyorvaśyā sahāviyogamavāpa  ViP eko gnirādāvabhavat ekena tvatra manvantare tredhā pravartitāḥ  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe caturthāṃśe ṣaṣṭho dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācatasyāpyāyurdhīmānamāvasurvaniśvāvasuḥśrutāyuḥ śayurayutāyuritisaṃjñāḥ ṣaṭ putrā abhavan  ViP tathāmāvasorbhīmanāmā putro bhavat  ViP bhīmasya kāñcanaḥ kāñcanātsuhotraḥ tasyāpi jahnuḥ  ViP  yo sau yajñavāṭamakhilaṃ gaṅgāṃbhasā plāvitamavalokya krodhasaṃraktalocano bhagavantaṃ yajñapuruṣamātmani parameṇa samādhinā samāropyākhilameva  gaṅgāmapibat  ViP  athainaṃ devarṣayaḥ prasādayāmāsuḥ  ViP duhitṛtve cāsya gaṅgāmanayan  ViP jahnoś ca sumandurnāma putro bhavat  ViP tasyāpyajakastato balākāśvastasmātkuśastasyāpi kuśāṃbukuśanābhādhūrtarajaso vasuśceti catvāraḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP teṣāṃ kuśāṃbaḥ śakratulyo mutro bhavedititapaścakāra  ViP taṃ cogratapasamavalokya mā bhavatvanayo mattulyo vīrya ityātmanaivāsyendraḥ putratvamagacchat  ViP sa gādhirnāma putraḥ kauśiko bhavat  ViP gādhiś ca satyavatīṃ kanyāmajanayat  ViP tāṃ ca bhārgavaḥ ṛcīko vavre  ViP gādhirapyatiroṣaṇāyātivṛddhāya brāhmaṇāya dātumanicchannekataḥ śyāmakarmānāminduvarcasāmanilaraṃhasāmaśvānāṃ sahasraṃ kanyāśulkamayācata tenāpyṛṣiṇā varumasakāśādu palabhyāśvatīrthotpannaṃ tādṛśamaśvasahasraṃ dattam  ViP tatastāmṛcīkaḥ kanyāmupayeme  ViP ṛcīkaś ca tasyāścarumapatyārtaṃ cakāra  ViP tatprasāditaś ca tanmātre kṣatravaraputrotpattaye caramaparaṃ sādhayāmāsa  ViP eṣa carurbhavatyā ayamaparaścarustvanmātrā samya gupayojya ityuktvā vanaṃ jagāma  ViP upayogakāle catāṃ mātā satyavatīmāha  ViP putri sarva evātmaputramatiguṇamabhilaṣati nātmajāyābhrātṛguṇeṣvatīvādṛto bhavatīti  ViP torhasi mamātmīyaṃ caruṃ madīyaṃ carumātmanopayoktum  ViP matputreṇa hi sakalabhūmaṇḍalaparipālanaṃ kāryaṃ kiyadvā brāhmaṇasya balavīryasaṃpadetyuktā sā svacaruṃ mātre dattavatī  ViP atha vanādāgatya satyavatīmṛṣirapaśyat  ViP āha caināmatipāpe kimidamakāryaṃ bhavatyā kṛtam atiraudraṃma te vapurlakṣyate  ViP nīnaṃ tvāyā tvanmātṛsātkṛtaścārurūpayukto na yuktāmetat  ViP mayā hi tatra carau sakalaiśvaryavīryasauryabalasaṃpadāropitā tvadīyacarāvapyakhilaśāntijñānatitikṣādibrāhmamaguṇasaṃpat  ViP  tacca viparītaṃ kurvantyāstavātiraudrāstradhāraṇapālananiṣṭhaḥ kṣatriyācāraḥ putro bhaviṣyati tasyāścopaśamarucirbrāhmaṇācāra ityākarṇyaiva  sā tasya pādau jagrāha  ViP  praṇipatya cainamāha  ViP  bhagavanmayaitadajñānādanuṣṭhitaṃ prasādaṃ me kuru maivaṃvidhaḥ putro bhavatu kāmamevaṃvidhaḥ pautro bhavatvityukte munirapyāha  ViP evamastviti  ViP anantaraṃ ca sā jamadagnimajījanat  ViP tanmātā ca viśvāmitraṃ janayāmāsa  ViP satyavatyapi kauśikī nāma nadyabhavat  ViP jamadagnirikṣvākuvaṃśodbhavasya reṇostanayāṃ reṇukāmupayeme  ViP tasyāṃ cāśeṣakṣatrahantāraṃ paraśurāmasaṃjñaṃ bhagavataḥsakalalokagurornārāyaṇasyāṃśaṃ jamadagnirajījanat  ViP viśvāmītraputrastu bhārgava eva śunaḥśepo daivair dattaḥ tataś ca devarātanāmābhavat  ViP tataścānye madhuśchandodhanañjayakṛtadevāṣṭakakacchapaharirākhyā viśvāmitraputrā babhūvuḥ  ViP teṣāṃ ca bahūni kauśikagotrāṇi ṛṣyantareṣu vivāhyānyabhavat  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe caturthaṃśe saptamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācapurūravaso jyeṣṭhaḥ putro yastvāyurnāmā sa rāhorduhitaramupayeme  ViP tasyāṃ ca pañca putrānutpādayāmāsa  ViP nahuṣakṣatravṛddharaṃbharajisaṃjñāstathaivānenāḥ pañcamaḥ putro bhūt  ViP kṣatravṛddhātsuhotraḥ putro bhavat  ViP kāśyapakāśagṛtsamadāstrayastasya putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP gṛtsamadasya śonakaścāturvarmyapravartayitābhūt  ViP kāśyasya kāśeyaḥ kāśīrājaḥ tasmādrāṣṭraḥ rāṣṭrasya dīrghatapāḥ putro bhavat  ViP dhanvantaristu dīrghatapasaḥ putro bhavat  ViP sa hi saṃsiddhakāryakaramaḥsakalasaṃbhūtiṣvaśeṣajñānavidā bhagavatā nārāyaṇena cātīta saṃbhūtau tasmai varo dattaḥ  ViP kāśīrājagotre vatīrya tvamaṣṭadhā samyagāyurvedaṃ kariṣyasi yajñabhāgabhugbhaviṣyasīti  ViP tasya ca dhanvantareḥ patraḥ ketumān ketumato bhīmarathaḥ tasyāpi divodāsaḥ tasyāpi pratardanaḥ  ViP sa ca bhadraśreṇyavaṃśavināśanādaśeṣaśatravonenajitā iti śatrujidabhavat  ViP tena ca prītimatātmaputro vatsavatsetyabhihito vatso bhavat  ViP satyaparatayā ṛtadhvajasaṃjñāmavāpa  ViP tataś ca kuvalayanāmānamaśvaṃ lebhe tataḥ kuvalayāśva ityasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ prathitaḥ  ViP tasyaca ca vatsasya putro larkanāmābhavat yasyāyamadyāpiśloko gīyate  ViP ṣaṣṭivarṣasahasrāṇi ṣaṣṭivarṣaśatāni ca alarkādaparo nānyo bubhuje medinīṃ yuvā  ViP tasyāpyalarkasya sannatināmābhavadātmaja  ViP sannateḥ sunīthaḥ tasyāpi suketuḥ tasmācca dharmaketurjajñe  ViP tataś ca satyaketuḥ tasmādvibhuḥ tattayaḥsuvibhuḥ tataś ca sukumārastasyāpi dṛṣṭaketuḥtataś ca vītihotraḥ tasmādbhārgaḥ bhārgasya bhārgabhūmiḥ tataścāturvarṇyaṃpravṛttirityetekāśyapabhūbhṛtaḥ kathitāḥ  ViP rajestu saṃtatiḥ śruyatām  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumāhāpurāṇe caturthāṃśe ṣṭamo dhyāya śrīparāśara uvācarajostu pañca putraśatānyatulabalaparākramasārāmāyasan  ViP devāsurasaṃgrāmāraṃbhe ca parasparavadhepsavo devāścāsurāś ca brahmaṇāmupetya papracchuḥ  ViP bhagavannasmākamatra virodhe katamaḥ pakṣo jetā bhaviṣyatīti  ViP athāha bhagavān  ViP yeṣāmarthe rajirātmāttāyudho yotsyati tatpakṣojeteti  ViP atha daityair upetya rajirātmasāhāyyadānāyābhyarthitaḥ prāha  ViP yotsyo haṃ bhavatāmarthe yadyahamamarajayādbhavatāmindro bhaviṣyāmītyākarṇyaitattair abhihitam  ViP na vayamanyathā vadiṣyāmo nyathā kariṣyāmo smākamindraḥ prahlādastadarthamevāyamudyamaityuktvā gateṣvasureṣu devair apyasāvavanipatirevamevoktastenāpi ca tathaivokte devairindrastvaṃ bhaviṣyasīti samanvicchitam  ViP rajināpi devasainyasahāyenānekair mahāstrais tadaśeṣamahāsurabalaṃ niṣūditam  ViP atha jitāripakṣaś ca devendro rajicaramayugalamātmanaḥ śirasā nipīḍyāha  ViP bhayatrāṇādannadānādbhavānasmatpitāseṣalokānāmuttamottamo bhavān yasyāhaṃ putrastrilokendraḥ  ViP sa cāpi rājā prahasyāha  ViP evamastvevamastvanatikramaṇīyāhi vairikṣādapyanekavidhacāṭuvākyagārbhā praṇatirityuktvā svapuraṃ jagāma  ViP śatakraturapīndratvaṃ cakāra  ViP svaryāte tu rajau nāradarṣicoditā rajiputrāḥ śatakratumātmapitṛputraṃ samācārādrājyaṃ yācitavantaḥ  ViP apradānena ca vijityendramatibalinaḥ svayamindratvaṃ cakruḥ  ViP tataś ca bahutithe kāle hyatīte bṛhaspatimekānte dṛṣṭvā apahṛtatrailokyayajñabhāgaḥ śatakraturuvāca  ViP badarīphalamātramapyarhasi mamāpyāyanāya puroḍāśakhaṇḍaṃ dātumityukto bṛhaspatiruvāca  ViP yadyevantvayāhaṃ pūrvameva coditaḥsyāṃ tanmayā tvadarthaṃ kimakartavyamatyilpairevāhobhistvāṃ nijaṃ padaṃ prapayiṣyāmītyabhidhāya teṣāmanudinamābhicārakaṃ buddhimohāyaśakrasya tejobhivṛddhaye juhāva  ViP te cāpi tena buddhimohenābhibhūyamānā brahmadviṣo dharmatyāgino vedavādaparāṅmukhābabhuvūḥ  ViP tatastānapetadharmācāranindro jaghāna  ViP purohitāpyāyitatejāś ca śakro divamākramat  ViP etadindrasya svapadacyavanādārohaṇaṃ śrutvā puruṣaḥ svapadabhraṃśaṃ daurātmayaṃ ca nāpnoti  ViP raṃbhastvapattyo bhavat  ViP kṣatravṛddhasutaḥ pratikṣatro bhavat  ViP tatputraḥ saṃjayaḥ tasyāpi jayaḥ tasyāpi vijayaḥ tasmācca jajñe kṛtaḥ  ViP  tasya ca haryadhanaḥ haryadhanasutaḥsahadevaḥ tasmādadīnastasya jayatseya jayatsenaḥ tataś ca saṃkṛtiḥ tatputraḥ kṣatradharmā ityete kṣatravṛddhasya  vaṃśyāḥ  ViP  tato nahuṣavaṃśaṃ pravakṣyāmi  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumāhāpurāṇe caturthāṃśe navamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācayatiyayātisaṃyātyāyātiviyātikṛtisaṃjñā nahuṣasya ṣaṭ putrā mahābalaparākramā babhūvuḥ  ViP yatistu rājyaṃ naicchat  ViP yayātistu bhūbhṛdabhavat  ViP uśanasaś ca duhitaraṃ devayānīṃ vārṣaparvaṇīṃ śarmiṣṭhāmupayeme  ViP atrānuvaṃśaśloko bhavati  ViP yaduṃ ca durvasuṃ caiva devayānī vyajāyata druhyuṃ cānuṃ ca pūruṃ ca śarmiṣṭhā sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam samadṛṣṭostadā puṃsaḥ sarvāḥsukhamayā diśaḥ  ViP yā dustyajā durmatibhir yā na jīryati jīryataḥ tāṃ tṛṣṇāṃ saṃtyajetprājñaḥsukhenaivābhipūryate  ViP jīryanti jīryataḥ keśā dantā jīryanti jīryataḥ dhanāśā jīvitāśā ca jīryato pi na jīryataḥ  ViP pūrṇaṃ varṣasahasraṃ me viṣayāsaktacetasaḥ tathā pyanudinaṃ tṛṣṇā mama deṣūpajāyate  ViP tasmādetāmahaṃ tyaktvā brahmaṇyādhāya mānasam nirdvandvo nirmamo bhūtvā cariṣyāmi mṛgaiḥ saha  ViP śrīparāśara uvācapuroḥsakāśādādāya jarāṃ dattvā ca yovanam rājyebhiṣicca pūruṃ ca prayayau tapase vanam  ViP diśidakṣiṇapūrvasyāṃ durvasuṃ ca daśamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaataḥ paraṃ yayāteḥ prathamaputrasya yadorvaṃśamahaṃ kathayāmi  ViP yatrāśeṣalokanivāso manuṣyasiddhagandharvayakṣarākṣasaguhyakakiṃpuruṣāpsaroragavihagadaityadānavādityarudravasvaśvimaruddevarṣibhirmumukṣubhir dharmārthakāmamokṣārthibhiś ca tattatphalalābhāya sadābhiṣṭuto sahasrajitkroṣṭunalanahuṣasaṃjñāścātvāro yaduputrā vabhuvuḥ  ViP sahasrajitpuḥ śatajit  ViP tasya haihayahehayaveṇuhayāstrayaḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP haihayaputro dharmaḥ tasyāpi dharmanetraḥ tataḥ  ViP eṣāṃ jyeṣṭhe vītihotrastathānyo bharataḥ  ViP bharatādvṛṣaḥ  ViP vaṣasya putro madhurabhavat  ViP tasyāpi vṛṣṇipramukhaṃputraśatamāsīt  ViP yato vṛṣṇisaṃjñāmetadgotramavāpa  ViP madhusaṃjñāhetuś  ViP tasyāpi rukmakavacastataḥ paravṛt  ViP tasya parāvṛto rukmeṣupṛthujyāmaghavalitaharitasaṃjñāstasya pañcātmajā babhūvuḥ  ViP tasmādyāpi jyāmaghasya śloko gīyate  ViP bhāryāvaśyāstu ye hantītyajānannasāvapi prasenastena kaṇṭhasaktena syamantakenāśvamāruhyāṭavyāṃmṛgayāmagacchat  ViP tatra ca siṃhādvadhamavāpa  ViP sāśvaṃ ca taṃ nihatya siṃhopyamalamaṇiratnamāsyāgreṇādāṃya prasenāśvapadavīmanusasāra  ViP dadarśa cāśvasamavetaṃ prasenaṃ siṃhena vinihatam  ViP akhilajanamadhye siṃhapadadarśanakṛtapariśuddhaḥ siṃhapadamanusasāra  ViP ṛkṣapatinihataṃ ca siṃhamapyalpe bhūmibhāge dṛṣṭvā tataścatadratnagauravādṛkṣasyāpi padānyanuyayau  ViP giritaṭe ca sakalameva tadyadusainyamavasthāpya tatpadānusārī ṛkṣabilaṃ praviveśa  ViP antaḥ praviṣṭaś ca dhātryāḥ sukumārakamullālayantyā vāṇīṃ śuśrāva  ViP siṃhaḥ prasenamavadhītsiṃho jāmbavatā hataḥ sukumārakamā rodīstava hyeṣa syamantakaḥ  ViP  ityākarṇyopalabdhasyamantakontaḥpraviṣṭaḥ kumārakrīḍanakīkṛtaṃ ca dhātryā haste tejobhir jājvacalyamānaṃsyamantakaṃ dadarśa  ViP taṃ ca syamantakābhilaṣitacakṣuṣamapūrvapuruṣamāgataṃ samavekṣya dhātrī trāhitrāhīti vyājahāra  ViP tadārtaravaśravaṇānantaraṃ cāmarṣūrṇahṛdayaḥ sa jāṃbavānājagāma  ViP tayoś ca parasparamuddhatāmarṣayoryuddhamakaviṃśatidinānyabhavat  ViP te ca yadusainikāstatra maptāṣṭādināni tanniṣkrāntimudikṣamāṇāstasthuḥ  ViP aniṣkramaṇe ca madhuripurasāvavaśyamatra bile tyantaṃ nāśamavāpto bhaviṣyatyanyathātasya jīvataḥ kathametāvanti dināni śatrujaye vyākṣepo bhaviṣyatīti kṛtādhyavasāyādvārakāmāgamya hataḥ kṛṣṇa iti kathayāmāsuḥ  ViP tadvāndhavāś ca tatkālocitamakhilamuttarakriyākalāpaṃ cakruḥ  ViP tataścāsya yuddhyamānasyātiśraddhādattaviśiṣṭopapātrayuktānnatoyādinā śrīkṛṣṇasya balaprāṇapuṣṭacirabhūt  ViP itarasyānudinamatigurupuruṣabhedyamānasya atiniṣṭhuraprahārapātapījitākhilāvayavasya nirāhāratayā balahānirabhūt  ViP nirjitaś ca bhagavatā jāṃbavānapraṇipatya vyājahāra  ViP surāsuragandharvayakṣarākṣalasādibhir apyakhilair bhavān na jetuṃ śakyaḥ kimutāvanigocarairalpavīryair narernarāvayavabhūtaiś ca tiryagyonyanusṛtibhiḥ kiṃ punarasmadvidhairavaśyaṃ bhavatāsmatsvāminā rāmeṇena nārāyaṇasya sakalajagatparāyaṇasyāṃśena bhagavatābhavitavyamityuktastasmai bhagavānakhilāvanibhārāvataraṇārthamavataraṇamācacakṣe  ViP prītyabhivyañjitakaratalasparśanena cainamapagatayuddhakhedaṃ cakāra  ViP sa ca praṇipatya punarapyenaṃ prasādya jāṃbavatīṃ nāma kanyāṃ gṛhāgatāyārghyabhūtāṃ grāhayāmāsa  ViP syamantakamaṇiratnamapi praṇipatya tasmai pradadau  ViP acyutopyatipraṇatāttasmādagrāhyamapi tanmaṇiratnamātmasaṃśodhanāyajagrāha  ViP saha jāṃbavatyā sa dvārakāmājagāma  ViP  bhagavadāgamanodbhūtaharṣotkarṣasya dvārakāvāsijanasya kṛṣṇavalokanāttatkṣaṇamevātipariṇatavayaso pi navayauvanamivābhavat  ViP diṣṭyādiṣṭyeti sakalayādavāḥ striyaś ca sabhājayāmāsuḥ  ViP bhagavānapi yathānubhūtamaśeṣaṃyādavasamāje yathāvadāccakṣe  ViP syamantakaṃ ca satrājitāya dattvā mithyābhiśastipariśuddhimavāpa  ViP jāṃbavatīṃ cāntaḥpuraṃ niveśayāmāsa  ViP satrājitopi mayāsyābhūtamalinamāropitamiti jātasaṃtrāsātsvasutāṃ satyabhāmāṃ bhagavate bhāryārthaṃ dadau  ViP tāṃ cākrūrakṛtavarmaśatadhanvapramukhā yādavāḥ prāgvarayāmbabhūvuḥ  ViP tatastatpradānādavajñātamevātmānaṃ manyamānāḥ satrājite vairānubandhaṃ cakruḥ  ViP akrūrakṛtavarmapramukhāś ca śatadhanvānamūcuḥ  ViP ayamatīva durātmā satrājito yo smābhir bhavatā ca prārthito pyātmajāmasmān bhavantaṃ cāvigaṇayya kṛṣṇāya dattavān  ViP tadalamanena jīvatā ghātayitvainaṃ tanmahāratnaṃ syamantakākhyaṃ tvayā kiṃ na gṛhyatevayamabhyupapatsyāmo yadyacyutastavopari vairānubandhaṃ kariṣyatītyevamuktastathetyasāvapyāha  ViP  jatugṛhadagdhānāṃ pāṇḍutanayānāṃ viditaparamārtho pi bhagavān duryodhanaprayatnaśauthilyakaraṇārtha pārthānukūlyakaraṇāya vāraṇāvataṃ gataḥ gate ca tasmin suptameva satrājitaṃ śatadhanvā jaghāna maṇiratnaṃ cādadāt  ViP pitṛvadhāmarṣapūrṇā ca satyabhāmā śīghraṃ syandanamārūḍhā vāraṇāvataṃ gatvā bhagavatehaṃ pratipāditetyakṣāntimatā śatadhanvanāsmatpitā vyāpāditaḥ tacca syaṃmantakamaṇiratnamapahṛtaṃyasyāvabhāsanenāpahṛtatimiraṃ trailokyaṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP tadīyaṃ tvadīyāpahāsanā tadālocya yadatra yuktaṃ tatkriyatāmiti kṛṣṇamāha  ViP tayā caivamuktāḥ parītuṣṭāntaḥ karaṇo pi kṛṣṇaḥ satyabhāmāmamarṣatāmranayanaḥ prāha  ViP satye mamaivaiṣāpahāsanā nāhametāṃ tasya durātmanaḥsahiṣye  ViP na hyanullaṅghya parapādapaṃ tatkṛtanīḍāśrayiṇo vihaṅgamā vadhyante tadalamamunāsmatpurataḥsaukaproritavākyaparikareṇetyuktvā dvārakāmabhyetyai kānte baladevaṃ vāsudevaḥ prāha  ViP mṛgayāgataṃ prasenamaṭavyāṃ mṛgapatirjaghāna  ViP satrājito pyadhunā śatadhanvanā nidhanaṃ prāpitaḥ  ViP tadubhayavināśāttanmaṇiratnamāvābhyāṃ sāmānyaṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP taduttiṣṭhāruhyatāṃ rathaḥ śatadhanvanidhanāyodyamaṃ kurvityabhihitastatheti samanvicchitavān  ViP kṛtodyamau ca tāvubhāvupalabhya śatadhanvā kṛtavarmāṇamupetya pārṣṇipūramakarmanimittamacodayat  ViP āha cainaṃ kṛtavarmā  ViP nāhaṃ baladevavāsudevābhyāṃ saha virodhāyālamityuktaścākrūramacodayat  ViP asāvapyāha  ViP na hi kaścidbhagavatā pādaprahāraparikaṃpitajagattrayeṇa surariṣuvanitāvaidhavyakāriṇāprabalaripucakrāpratihatacakreṇa cakriṇā madamuditanayanāvalokanākhilaniśātanenātiguruvairivāraṇāpakarṣaṇāvikṛtamahimorusīreṇasīriṇā ca saha sakalajagadvandyānāmamaravarāṇāmapi yoddhuṃ samarthaḥ  ViP kimutāhaṃ tadanyaḥ śaraṇamabhilaṣyatāmityuktaḥ śatadhanurāha  ViP yadyasmatparitrāṇāsamarthaṃ bhavānātmanamadhigacchati tadayamasmattastāvanmaṇiḥ saṃgṛhya rakṣyatāmiti  ViP ekamuktaḥ so pyāha  ViP yadyantyayāmapyavasthāyāṃ na kasmaicidbhavān kathayiṣyati tadahametaṃ grahīṣyāmīti  ViP tathetyukte cākrūrastanmaṇiratnaṃ jagrāha  ViP śatadhanurapya tulavegāṃ śatayojanavāhinīṃvaḍavāmāruhyapakrāntaḥ  ViP śaivyasugrīvamghapuṣpabalāhakāśvacatuṣṭayayuktarathasthitau baladevavāsudevai tamanuprayātau  ViP sā ca vaḍavā śatayojanapramāṇamārgamatītā punarapi vāhyamānā mithilāvanoddeśe prāṇānutsasarja  ViP śatadhanurapi tāṃ parityajya padātirevādravat  ViP kṛṣṇopi balabhadramāha  ViP tāvadatra syandane bhavatā stheyamahamenamadhamācāraṃ padātireva padātimanugamyayāvaddhātayāmi atra hi bhūbhāge dṛṣṭadoṣāḥsabhayā ato naiteśvā bhavatemaṃ bhūmibhāgamullaṅghanīyāḥ  ViP tathetyuktva baladevo ratha eva tasthau  ViP kṛṣṇopi dvikrośamātraṃ bhūmibhāgamanusṛtya dūrasthitasyaiva cakraṃ kṣiptvā śatadhanuṣaḥ śiraściccheda  ViP taccharīrāṃbarādiṣu ca bahuprakāramanvicchannapi syamantakamaṇiṃ nāvāpa padā tadopagamya balabhadramāha  ViP  vṛthaivāsmābhiḥ śatadhanurghātitaḥ na prāptamaśilajagatsārabhūtaṃ tanmahāratnaṃ syamantakākhyamityākarṇyodbhūtakopo baladevo vāsudevamāha  dhiktvāṃ yastvamevamarthalipsuretacca te bhrātṛtvānmayā kṣāntaṃ tadayaṃ panthāḥsvecchayāgamyatāṃ na me dvārakayā na tvayā na cāśeṣabandhubhiḥ kāryamalamalamebhir mamāgratolīkaśapathair ityākṣipya tatkathāṃ kathañcitprasādyamānopi na tasthau  ViP sa videhapurīṃ praviveśa  ViP janakarājaścārghyapūrvakamenaṃ gṛhaṃ praveśayāmāsa  ViP sa tatraiva ca tasthau  ViP vāsudevo pi dvārakāmājagāma  ViP yāvacca janakarājagṛhe balabhadro vatasthe tāvaddhārtarāṣṭro duryodhanastatsakāśādgadāśikṣāmaśikṣayat  ViP  varṣatrayānte ca babhrūgrasenaprabhṛtibhir yādavair na tadratnaṃ kṛṣṇenāpahṛtamiti kṛtāvagatibhir videhanagarīṃ gatvā baladevaḥsaṃpratyāyya  dvārakāmānītaḥ  ViP  akrūropyuttamamaṇisamudbhutasuvarṇena bhagavaddhyānaparo navarataṃ yajñāniyāja  ViP savanagatau hi kṣatriyavaiśyau nighnanbrahyāhā bhavatītyevaṃprakāraṃ dīkṣākavacaṃ praviṣṭaḍa eva tasthau  ViP dviṣaṣṭivarṣāṇyeva tanmaṇiprabhāvāttatropasargadurbhikṣamārikāmaraṇādikaṃ nābhūt  ViP athākrūrapakṣīyair bhojaiḥ śatrughne sātvatasya prapautre vyāpādite bhojaiḥ sahākrūro dvārakāmapahāyāpakrāntaḥ  ViP tadapakrāntidinādārabhya tatropasargadurbhikṣavyālānāvṛṣṭimārikādyupadravā babhūvuḥ  ViP atha yādavā balabhadrograsenasamavetā mantramamantrayan  ViP bhagavānuragāriketanaḥ kimidamekadaiva pracuropadravāgamanametadālocyatāmityuktendhakanāmā yaduvṛddhaḥ prāha  ViP asyākrūrasya pitṛśvaphalko yatra yatrābhūttatratatra durbhikṣamārikānāvṛṣṭyādikaṃ nābhūt  ViP kāśīrājasya viṣaye tvanāvṛṣṭyā ca śvaphalko nītaḥ tataś ca tatkṣaṇāddevo vavarṣa  ViP kāśīrājapatnyāś ca garbhe kanyāratnaṃ pūrvamāsīt  ViP sā ca kanyā pūrṇepi prasūtikāle naiva niścakrāma  ViP evaṃ ca tasya garbhasya dvādaśavarśaṇyaniṣkrāmato yayuḥ  ViP kāśīrājaś ca tāmātmajāṃ garbhasthāmāha  ViP  putri kasmānna jāyase niṣkramya tāmāsyaṃ te draṣṭumicchāmi etāṃ ca mātaraṃ kimiticiraṃ kleśayiṣyasītyuktā garbhasthaiva vyājahāra  ViP tāta yadyekaikāṃ gāṃ dinedine brāhmaṇāya prayacchasi tadahamanyais tribhir varṣairasmādgarbhāttato vaśyaṃ niṣkramiṣyāmītyedvacanamākarṇya rājā dinedine brāhmaṇāyagāṃ prādāt  ViP sāpi tāvatā kālena jātā  ViP tatastasyāḥ pitā gāndinīti nāma cakāra  ViP tāṃ ca gāndinīṃ kanyāṃ śphalakāyopakāriṇe gṛhamāgatāyārghya bhūtāṃ prādāt  ViP tasyāmayamakrūraḥ śvaphalakājjajñe  ViP tasyaivaṅguṇamithunādutpattiḥ  ViP tatkathamasminnapakrānte atra durbhikṣamārikādyupadravā na bhaviṣyanti  ViP tadayamātrānīyatāmalamatiguṇavatyaparādhānveṣaṇeneti yaduvṛddhasyāndhakasyaitadvacanamākarmyakeśavograsenabalabhadrapurogamair yadubhiḥ kṛtāparādhatitikṣubhir abhayaṃ dattvāśvaphalakaputraḥśvapumānītaḥ  ViP tatra cāgatamātra eva tasya syamantakamaṇeḥ prabhāvādanāvṛṣṭimārikādurbhikṣavyālādyupadravopaśamā babhūvuḥ  ViP kṛṣṇaścintayāmāsa  ViP svalpametatkāraṇaṃ yadayaṃ gāndinyāṃ śvaphalakenākrūro janitaḥ  ViP sumahāṃścāyamanāvṛṣṭidurbhikṣamārikādyupadravāpratiṣedhakārī prabhāvaḥ  ViP tannṛna masya sarāśe sa mahāmaṇiḥ syamantakākhyastiṣṭhati  ViP tasya hyovaṃvidhāḥ prabhāvāḥ śruyante  ViP ayamapi ca yajñādanantaramanyatkratvantaraṃ tasyānantaramanyadyajñāntaraṃ cājastramavicchinnaṃ yajatīti  ViP  analpopādānaṃ cāsyāsaṃśayamatrasau maṇivarastiṣṭhitīti kṛtādhyavasāyo nyatprayojanamuddiśya sakalayādavasamājamātmagṛha evācīkarat  ViP  tatra copaviṣṭoṣvakhileṣu yaduṣu pūrvaṃ prayojanamupanyasya paryavasite ca tasmin prasaṃgāntaraparihāsakathāmakrūreṇa kṛtvā janārdanastamakrūramāha dānapate jānīma eva vaya yathā śatadhanvanā tadidamakhilajagatsārabhūtaṃ syamantakaṃratnaṃ bhavataḥ tadaśeṣarāṣṭropakarakaṃ bhavatsakāśe tiṣṭhati tiṣṭhatu sarva evavayaṃ tatprabhāvaphalabhujaḥ kiṃ tveṣa balabhadro smānāśaṅkitavāṃśtadasmatprītayedarśayasvetyabhidāya joṣaṃ sthite bhagavati vāsudeve saratnaḥsocintayat  ViP kimatrānuṣṭheyamanyathā cedbravīmyahaṃ tatkevalāṃbaratirodhānamanviṣyanto ratnametedrakṣyanti ativirodho na kṣama iti saṃcintya tamakhilajagatkāraṇabhūtaṃ nārāyaṇamāhakrūraḥ  ViP bhagavanmamaitatsyamantakaratnaṃ satadhanuṣā samarpitamapagate ca tasminnadya śvaḥparaśvo vā bhagavān yācayiṣyatīti kṛtamatiratikṛcchreṇaitāvantaṃ kālamadhārayam  ViP tasya ca dhāraṇaśeklenāhamaśeṣopabhogeṣvasaṃgimānaso na vedbhisvasukhakalāmapi  ViP etāvanmātramapyaśeṣarāṣṭropakārī dhārayituṃ na śaknoti bhavānmanyata ityātmanā na coditavān  ViP tadīdaṃ syamantakaratnaṃ gṛhyatāmicchayā yasyābhimataṃ tasya samarpyatām  ViP tataḥ svodaravastranigopitamatisaghukanakasamudgakagataṃ prakaṭīkṛtavān  ViP tataś ca niṣkrāmya syamantakamaṇiṃ tasminyadukulasamāje mumoca  ViP muktamātre ca tasminnatikāntyā tadakhilamāsthānamudyotitam  ViP athāhākruraḥ sa eṣa maṇiḥ śatadhanvanāsmākaṃ samarpitaḥ yasyāyaṃ sa enaṃ gṛhṇātu iti  ViP tamālokyasarvayādavānāṃ sādhusādhviti vismitamanasāṃ vāco śrūyanta  ViP tamālokyātīva balabhadro mamāyamacyutenaiva sāmānyaḥsamanvicchita iti kṛtaspṛho bhūt  ViP mamaivāyaṃ pitṛdhanamityatīva ca satyabhāmāpi spṛhayāñcakāra  ViP balasatyāvalokanātkṛṣṇopyātmānaṃ gocakrāntarāvasthitamivamene  ViP sakalayādavasamakṣaṃ cākrūramāha  ViP  etaddhi maṇiratnamātmasaṃsodhanāya eteṣāṃ yadūnāṃ mayā darśitam etacca mama balabhadrasya ca sāmānyaṃ pitṛdhanaṃ caitatsatyabhāmāyā nānyasyaitat etacca sarvakālaṃ śucinā brahmacaryādiguṇavatā dhriyamāmamaśeṣarāṣṭrasyopakārakamaśucinā dhrayamāṇamādhārameva hanti  ViP atohamasya ṣoḍaśastrīsahasraparigrahādasamartho dhāraṇe kathametatsatyabāmā svīkaroti  ViP ārbalabhadreṇāpi madirāpānādyaśeṣopabhogaparityāgaḥ karyaḥ  ViP tadalaṃ yadulokoyaṃ balabhadraḥ ahaṃ ca satyā ca tvāṃ dānapate prārthayāmaḥ  ViP tadbhavāneva dhārayituṃ samarthaḥ  ViP  tvaddhṛtaṃ cāsya rāṣṭrasyopakārakaṃ tadbhavānaśeṣarāṣṭranimittametatpūrvavaddhārayatvanyanna vaktavyamityukto dānapatistathetyāha jagrāha ca  tanmahāratnam  ViP  tataḥprabhṛtyakrūraḥ prakaṭenaiva tenātijājjvalyamnenātmakaṇṭhāvasaktenāditya ivāṃśumālī cacāra  ViP  ityetadbhagavato mithyābhiśastikṣālanaṃ yaḥ smarati na tasya kadācidalpāpi mithyābhiśastirbhavati avyāhatāśilendriyaścākhilapāpamokṣamavāpnoti iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe caturthāṃśe trayodaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaanamitrasya putraḥ śinirnāmābhavat  ViP tasyāpi satyakaḥ satyakātsātyakiryuyudhānāparanāmā  ViP tasmādapi saṃjayaḥ tatputraś ca kuṇiḥ kuṇeryugandharaḥ  ViP ityete śaineyāḥ  ViP anamitrasyānvaye vṛṣṇiḥ tasmāt ścaphalkaḥ tatprabhāvaḥ kāthena eva  ViP śvaphalkasyānyaḥ kanīyāṃścitrakonāma bhrātā  ViP śvaphalkādakrūro gāndinyāmabhavat  ViP tathopamadgaḥ  ViP upamadgormṛdāmṛdaviśvārimejayagirikṣatropakṣatraśataghnārimardanadharmadṛgdṛṣṭadharmagandhamojavāhaprativāhākhyāḥ putrāḥsutārākhyā kanyā cadevavānupadevaścākrūraputrau  ViP pṛthuvivṛthupramukhāścitrakasya putrā bahavo babhūvuḥ  ViP kukurabhajamānaśucikaṃbalabarhiṣākhyāstathāndhakasya catvāraḥ putrāḥ  ViP kukurāddhṛṣṭaḥ tasmācca kapotaromā tataś ca vilomā tasmādapi tuṃburasakho bhavadanusaṃjñaś ca  ViP anorānakadundabhiḥ tataścā bhijit abhijitaḥ punarvasuḥ  ViP tasyāpyāhukaḥ āhukī ca kanyā  ViP āhukasya devakograsenau dvau putrau  ViP devavānupadevaḥ sahadevo devarakṣitā ca devakasya catvāraḥ putrāḥ  ViP teṣāṃ vṛkadevopadevā devarakṣitā śrīdevā śāntidevā sahadevā devakī ca saptabhaginyaḥ  ViP tāś ca sarvā vasudeva upayeme  ViP ugrasenasyāpi kaṃsanyagrodhasunāmānakāhvaśaṅkusubhūmirāṣṭrapālayuddhatuṣṭisutuṣṭiṃmatsaṃjñāḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP kaṃsākaṃsavatīsutanūrāṣṭrapalikāhvāścograsenasya tanūjāḥ kanyāḥ  ViP bhajamānācca vidūrathaḥ putro bhavat  ViP vidūrathācchūraḥ śurācchamī śaminaḥ pratikṣatraḥ tasmātsvayaṃbhojaḥ tataś ca hṛdikaḥ  ViP tasyāpi kṛtavarmaśatadhanurdavārhadevagarbhādyāḥ putrā babhūvuḥ  ViP devagarbhasyāpi śuraḥ  ViP śurasyāpi mārīṣā nāma patnyabhavat  ViP tasyāṃ cāsau daśaputrānajanayadvasudevarūrvān  ViP vasudevasya jātamātrasyaiva tadgṛhe bhagavadaṃśāvatāramavyāhatadṛṣṭyā paśyadbhir devair divyānakadundubhayo
