ekarāśau sameṣyanti tadā bhavati vai kṛtam  ViP atītā vartamānāś ca tathaivānāgatāś ca ye ete vaṃśeṣu bhūpālāḥ kathitā munisattama  ViP yāvatparīkṣito janma yāvannandābhiṣecanam etadvarṣasahasraṃ tu jñeyaṃ pañcāśaduttaram  ViP saptarṣīṇāṃ tu yau pūrvau dṛśyete hyuditau divi tayostu madhye nakṣatraṃ dṛśyate yatsamaṃ niśi  ViP tena saptarṣayo yuktāstiṣṭhantyabdaśataṃ nṛṇām te tu pārīkṣite kāle maghāsvāsandvijottama  ViP tadā pravṛttaś ca kalirdvādaśābdaśatātmakaḥ  ViP yadaiva bhagavānviṣṇoraṃśo yāto divaṃ dvija vasudevakulodbhūtastadaivātrāgataḥ kaliḥ  ViP yāvatsapādapadmābhyāṃ pasparśemāṃ vasuṃdharām tāvatputhvīpariṣvaṅge samartho nābhavatkaliḥ  ViP gate sanātanasyāṃśe viṣṇostatra bhuvo divam tatyāja sānujo rājyaṃ dharma putro yudhiṣṭhiraḥ  ViP viparītāni dṛṣṭvā ca nimittāni hi pāṇḍavaḥ yāte kṛṣṇe cakārātha so bhiṣekaṃ parīkṣitaḥ  ViP prayāsyanti yadā caite pūrvāṣāḍhāṃ maharṣayaḥ tadā nandātprabhṛtyeṣa gativṛddhiṃ gamiṣyati  ViP yasmin kṛṣṇo divaṃ yātastasminneva tadā hani pratipannaṃ kaliyugaṃ tasya saṃkhyāṃ nibodha me  ViP trīṇi lakṣāṇi varṣāṇāṃ dvija mānuṣyasaṃkhyayā ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi bhaviṣyatyeṣa vai kaliḥ  ViP śātāni tāni divyānāṃ sapta pañca ca saṃkhyayā niḥśeṣeṇa gate tasminbhaviṣyati punaḥ kṛtam  ViP brāhmaṇāḥ kṣittriyā vaiśyāḥ śudrāś ca dvijasattama yugeyuge mahātmānaḥ samatītāḥsahasraśaḥ  ViP bahutvānnāmadheyānāṃ parisaṃkhyā kulekule paunaruktyāddhi sāmyāc ca na mayā parikīrtitā  ViP devāpiḥ poravo rājā puruścekṣākuvaṃśajaḥ mahāyogabalopetau kalāpagramasaṃśritau  ViP kṛte yuge tvihāgamya kṣatraprāvartakau hi tau bhaviṣyato manorvaśabījabhūtau vyavasthitau  ViP etena kramayogena manuputraurvasuṃdharā kṛtatretādvāparāṇi yugāni trīṇi bhujyate  ViP kalau te bījabhūtā vai kecittiṣṭhanti vai mune yathaiva devāpipurū sāṃprataṃ samadhiṣṭhitau  ViP eṣa tūddeśato vaṃśastavokto bhūbhujāṃ mayā nikhilo gadituṃ śakyo naiṣa varṣaśatair api  ViP ete cānye ca bhūpālā yair atra kṣitimaṇḍale kṛtaṃ mamatvaṃ mohāndhair nityaṃ heyakalevare  ViP kathaṃ mameyamacalā matputrasya kathaṃ mahī madvaṃśasyeticintārtā jagmurantamime nṛpāḥ  ViP tebhyaḥ pūrvatarāścānye tebhyastebhyas tathā pare bhaviṣyāścaiva yāsyanti teṣāmanye ca ye pyanu  ViP vilokyātmajayodyogaṃ yātrāvyagrānnarādhipān puṣpaprahāsaiḥ śaradi hasaṃtīva vasuṃdharā  ViP maitreya pṛthivīgītāñchlokāṃścātra nibodha me yānāha dharmadhvajine najakāyāsito muniḥ  ViP pṛthivyuvācakathameṣa naredrāṇāṃ moho buddhimatāmapi yena kena sadharmāṇopyativiśvastacetasaḥ  ViP pūrvamātmajayaṃ kṛtvā jetumicchanti mantriṇaḥ tato bhṛtyāṃś ca paurāṃś ca jigīṣante tathā ripūn  ViP krameṇānena jeṣyāmo vayaṃ pṛthvīṃ sasāgarām ityāsaktadhiyo mṛtyuṃ na paśyantyavidvaragam  ViP samudrāvaraṇaṃ yāti bhūmaṇḍalamatho vaśam kiyadātmajayasyaitanmuktirātmajayephalam  ViP utsṛjya pūrvajā yātā yāṃ nādāya gataḥ pitā tāṃ māmatīva mūḍhatvājjetumicchanti pārthivāḥ  ViP matkṛte pitṛ putrāṇāṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ cāpi vigrahaḥ jāyatetyantamohena mamatvādṛtacetasām  ViP pṛthvī mameyaṃ sakalā mamaiṣā madanvayasyāpi ca śāśvatīyam yoyo mṛte nyatra babhūva rājā kubuddhirā sīditi tasyatasya  ViP dṛṣṭvā mamatvādṛtacittamekaṃ vihāya māṃ mṛtyuvaśaṃ vrajantam tasyānuyastasya kathaṃ mamatvaṃ hṛdyāspadaṃ matprabhavaṃ karoti  ViP pṛthvī mamaiṣāśu parityajaināṃ vadanti ye dūtamukhaiḥ svaśatrūn narādhipāsteṣu mamātihāsaḥ punaś ca mūḍheṣu dayābhyupaiti  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityete dharaṇīgītaḥ ślokā maitreya yaiḥ śrutāḥ mamatvaṃ vilayaṃ yāti tapatyarke yathā himam  ViP ityeṣa kathitaḥ samyaṅmanorvaśo mayā tava yatra sthitipravṛttasya viṣṇoraṃśāṃśakā nṛpāḥ  ViP śṛṇoti ya imaṃ bhaktyā manorvaśamanukramāt tasya pāpamaśeṣaṃ vai praṇaśyatyamalātmanaḥ  ViP dhanadhānyardhimatulāṃ prāpnotyavyāhatendriyaḥ śrutvaivamakhilaṃ vaṃśaṃ praśastaṃ śaśīsūryayoḥ  ViP ikṣvākujahnumāndhātṛsagarāvikṣitānraghūn yayātinahuṣādyāṃś ca jñātvā niṣṭhāmupāgatān  ViP mahābalānmahāvīryānanantadhanasaṃcayān kṛtānkālena balinā kathāśeṣānnarādhipān  ViP śrutvā na putradārādau gṛhakṣetrādike tathā dravyādau vā kṛtaprajño mamatvaṃ kurute naraḥ  ViP taptaṃ tapo yaiḥ puruṣapravīrair udvāhubhir varṣagaṇānanekān iṣṭvā suyajñair balinotivīryāḥ kṛtānukālena kathāvaśeṣāḥ  ViP pṛthuḥsamastānvicacāra lokānavyāhato yovijitāricakraḥ sa kālavātābhihataḥ praṇaṣṭaḥ kṣiptaṃ yathā śālmalitūlamagnau  ViP yaḥ kārtavīryo bubhuje samastāndvīpānsamākramyahatāricakraḥ kathāprasaṃgeṣvabhidhīyamānaḥsa eva saṃkalpavikalpahetuḥ  ViP daśānanāvikṣatarāghavāṇāmaiśvaryamudbhāsitadiṅmukhānām bhasmāpi śiṣṭaṃ na kathaṃ kṣaṇena bhrūbhaṅgapātena dhigantakasya  ViP kathāśarīratvamavāpa yadvai māndhātṛnāmā bhuvi cakravartī śrutvāpi tatkohi karoti sādhurmamatvamānmanyapi mandacetāḥ  ViP bhagīrathādyāḥsagaraṃ kakutstho daśanano rāghavalakṣmaṇau ca yudhiṣṭhirādyāś ca babhūvurete satyaṃ na mithyā kva nu te na vidmaḥ  ViP ye sāṃprataṃ ye ca nṛpā bhaviṣyāḥ proktā mayā vipravarogravīyāḥ ete tathānye ca tathābhidheyāḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti yathaiva pūrve  ViP eta dviditvā na nareṇa kāryaṃ mamatvamātmanyapi paṇḍitena tiṣṭhantu tāvattanayātmajāyāḥ kṣetrādayo ye ca śarīriṇo nye  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumāhapurāṇe caturthāṃśe caturviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīviṣṇumāhapurāṇe catuthāsaḥ samāptaḥiti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhya śrīdharīyavyākhyādvayopete caturthośaḥ samāptaḥ ata śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhya śrīdharīyavyākhyādvayopete pañcamāśaḥ prārabhyateśrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥmaitreya uvācanṛpāṇāṃ kathitaḥsarvo bhavatā vaṃśavistaraḥ vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva yathāvadanuvarṇitam aṃśāvatāro brahmarṣe yo yaṃ yadukulodbhavaḥ viṣṇostaṃ vistareṇāhaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ  ViP cakāra yāni karmāṇi bhagavān puruṣottamaḥ aṃśāṃśenāvatīryorvyāṃ tatra tāni mune vada  ViP śrīpāraśara uvācamaitreya śrūyatāmetadyatpṛṣṭo hamiha tvayā viṣṇoraṃśāṃśasaṃbhūticaritaṃ jagato hitam  ViP devakasya sutāṃ pūrvaṃ vasudevo mahāmune upayeme mahābhāgāṃ devakīṃ devatopamām  ViP kaṃsastayorvararathaṃ codayāmāsa sārathiḥ vasudevasya devakyā saṃyoge bhojanandanaḥ  ViP āthāntarikṣe vāguccaiḥ kaṃsamābhāṣya sādaram meghagaṃbhīranirghoṣaṃ samābhāṣyedamabravīt  ViP yāmetāṃ vahase mūḍha saha bhartrā rathe sthitām asyās tavāṣṭamo garbhaḥ prāṇān apahariṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityākarṇyaṃ samutpāṭya khaḍgaṃ kaṃso mahābalaḥ devakīṃ hantumārabdho vasudevo bravīdidam  ViP na hantavyā mahābhāga devakī bhavatānagha samarpayiṣye sakalāngarbhānasyodarodbhavān  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatathetyāha tataḥ kaṃso vasudevaṃ dvijottama na ghātayāmāsa ca tāṃ devakīṃsatyagauravāt  ViP etasminnevakāle tu bhūribhārāvapīḍitā jagāma dharaṇī merau samājaṃ tridivaukasām  ViP sa brahmakānsurānsarvānpraṇipatyātha medini kathayāmāsa tatsarvaṃ khedātkaruṇabhāṣiṇī  ViP bhūmiruvācaagniḥsuvarṇasya gururgavāṃ sūryaḥ paro guruḥ mamāpyakhilalo kānāṃ kururnārāyaṇo garuḥ  ViP prajāpatipatirbrahma pūrveṣāmapi pūrvajaḥ kalākāṣṭhānimeṣātmā kālaścāvyaktamūrtimān  ViP tadaṃśabhūtaḥsarvaiṣāṃ samūho vaḥsurottamāḥ  ViP ādityā sarutaḥsādhyā rudrā vasvaśvivahnayaḥ pitaro ye ca lokānāṃ sraṣṭāro tripurogamāḥ  ViP ete tasyāprameyasya viṣṇo rūpaṃ mahātmanaḥ  ViP yakṣarākṣasadaiteyapiśācoragadānavāḥ gandharvāpsarasaścaivarūpaṃ viṣṇormahātmanaḥ  ViP graharkṣatārakācitragaganāgnijalānilāḥ ahaṃ ca viṣayāścaiva sarva viṣṇumayaṃ jagat  ViP tathā cānekarūpasya yasya rūpāṇya harniśam bādhyabādhakatāṃ yānti kallolā iva sāgare  ViP tatsāṃpratamamī daityāḥ kālanemipurogamāḥ martyalokaṃ samākramya bādhante harniśaṃ prajāḥ  ViP kālanemirhato yo sau viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā ugrasenasutaḥ kaṃsaḥsaṃbhūtaḥsa mahāsuraḥ  ViP āriṣṭo dhenukaḥ keśī pralaṃbo narakas tathā suṃdo surastathātyugro bāṇaścāpi baleḥsutaḥ  ViP tathānye ca mahāvīryā nṛpāṇāṃ bhavaneṣu ye samutpannā durātmānastānna saṃkhyātumutsahe  ViP akṣohiṇyotra bahulā divyamūrtidharāḥsurāḥ mahābalānāṃ dṛptānāṃ daityendraṇāṃ mamopari  ViP tadbhūribhāra pīḍārtā na śaknomyamareśvarāḥ bibhartumātmānamahamiti vijñāpayāmi vaḥ  ViP kriyatāṃ tanmahābhāgā mama bhārāvatāraṇam yathā rasātalaṃ nāhaṃ gaccheyamativihvalā  ViP ityākarṇya dharāvākyamaśeṣais tridaśeśvaraiḥ bhuvo bhārāvatārārthaṃ brahmā prāha pracoditaḥ  ViP brahmovācayathāha vasudhā sarvaṃ satyameva divaukasaḥ ahaṃ bhavo bhavantaś ca sarve nārāyaṇātmakāḥ  ViP vibhūtayaś ca yāstasya tāsāmeva parasparam ādhikyanyūnatābādhyabādhakatvena vartate  ViP tadāgacchata gacchāmaḥ kṣīrābdhestaṭamuttamam tatrārādhya hariṃ tasmai sarvaṃ vijñāpayāma vai  ViP sarvathaiva jagatyarthe sa sarvātmā jaganmayaḥ sattvāṃśenāvatīryorvyāṃ dharmasya kurute sthitim  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā prayayo tatra saha devaiḥ pitāmahaḥ samāhitamanāścaivaṃ tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam  ViP brahmovācadve vidye tvamanāmnāyaparā caivāparā tathā ta eva bhavato rūpe mūrtāmūrtātmike prabho  ViP dve brahmaṇī tvaṇīyotisthūlātmansarva sarvavit śabdabrahmaparaṃ caiva brahma brahmamayasya yat  ViP ṛgvedastvaṃ yajurvedaḥsāmavedastvatharvaṇaḥ śikṣākalpo niruktaṃ ca cchando jyotiṣameva ca  ViP itihāsapurāṇe ca tathā vyākaraṇaṃ prabho mīmāṃsā nyāyaśāstraṃ ca dharmaśāstrāṇyadhokṣaja  ViP ātmātmadehaguṇavadvicārācāri yadvaca tadapyādyapate nānyadadhyātmātmasvarūpavat  ViP tvamavyaktamanirdeśyamacintyānāmavarmavat apāṇipādarūpaṃ ca śuddhaṃ nityaṃ parātparam  ViP śṛṇoṣyakarṇaḥ paripaśyasi tvamacakṣurūpo bahurūparūpaḥ apādahasto javano grahītā tvaṃ vetsi sarvaṃ ca sarvavedyaḥ  ViP aṇoraṇīyāṃ samasatsvarūpaṃ tvāṃ paśyato jñānanivṛttiragryā dhīrasya dhīrasya bibharti nānyadvareṇyarūpātparataḥ parātman  ViP tvaṃ viśvanābhir bhuvanasya goptā sarvāṇi bhūtāni tavāntarāṇi yadbhūtabhavyaṃ yadaṇoraṇīyaḥ pumāṃs tvam ekaḥ prakṛteḥ parastāt  ViP ekaścaturdhā bhagavānhutāśo varcovibhūtaṃ jagato dadāsi tvaṃ viśvataścakṣuranantamūrte tredhā padaṃ tvaṃ nidadhāsi dhātaḥ  ViP yathāgnireko bahudhā samidhyate vikārabhedair avikārarūpaḥ tathā vyaktāvyaktasvarūpastvaṃ samaṣṭivyaṣṭirūpavān sarvajñaḥsarvanitsarvaśaktijñānabalardhimān  ViP anyūnaścāpyavṛddhiś ca svādhīno nādimānvaśī klamatandrī bhayakrodhakāmādibhir asaṃyutaḥ  ViP niravadyaḥ paraḥ prāpterniradhiṣṭho kṣaraḥ kramaḥ sarveśvaraḥ parādhāro dhāmnāṃ dhāmātmako kṣayaḥ  ViP sakalāvaraṇānītanirālaṃbanabhāvana mahāvibhūtisaṃsthāna namaste puruṣottama  ViP nākāraṇātkāraṇādvā kāraṇākāraṇānna ca śarīragrahaṇaṃ vāpi dharmatrāṇāya kevalam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityevaṃ saṃstavaṃ śrutvā manasā bhagavānajaḥ brahmāṇamāha prītena viśvarūpaṃ prakāśayan  ViP śrībhagavānuvācabhobho brahmaṃstvayā mattaḥsaha devair yadiṣyate taducyatāmaśeṣaṃ ca siddhamevāvadhāryatām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatato brahmā harerdivya viśvirūpamavekṣya tat tuṣṭāva bhūyo deveṣu sādhvasāvanatātmasu  ViP brahmovācanamo namastestu sahasrakṛtvaḥsahasrabāho bahuvaktrapāda namonamaste jagataḥ pravṛttivināśasaṃsthānakarāprameya  ViP sūkṣmātisūkṣmātibṛhatpramāma garīyasāmapyatigauravātman pradhānabuddhīndriyavatpradhānamūlātparātmanbhagavanprasīda  ViP eṣā mahī deva mahīprasūtair mahāsuraiḥ pīḍitaśailabandhā parāyaṇaṃ tvāṃ jagatāmupaiti bhārāvatārārthamapārasāra  ViP ete vayaṃ vṛtraripustathāyaṃ nāsatyadastrau varuṇastathaiva ime ca rudrā vasavaḥsasūryāḥsamīraṇāgniprasukhāstathānye  ViP surāḥsamastāḥsuranāthakāryamebhir mayā yacca tadīśa sarvām ājñāpayājñāṃ paripālayantastavaiva tiṣṭhāma sadāstadoṣāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ saṃstūyamānastu bhagavānparameśvaraḥ ujjahārātmanaḥ keśau sitakṛṣṇau mahāmune  ViP uvāca ca surānetau matkeśau vasudhātale avatīrya bhuvo bhārakleśahāniṃ kariṣyataḥ  ViP surāś ca sakalāḥsvāṃśair avatīrya mahītale kurvantu yuddhamunmattaiḥ pūrvotpannair mahāsuraiḥ  ViP tataḥ kṣayamaśeṣāste daiteyā dharamītale prayāsyanti na saṃdeho maddṛpātavicūrṇitāḥ  ViP vasudevasya yā patnī devakī devatopamā tatrāyamaṣṭamo garbho matkeśo bhavitā surāḥ  ViP avatīrya ca tatrāyaṃ kaṃsaṃ ghātayitā bhuvi kālanemīṃ samudbhūtamityuktvāntardadhe hariḥ  ViP adṛśyāya tatastasmai praṇipatya mahāmune merupṛṣṭhaṃ surā jagmuravateruś ca bhūtale  ViP kaṃsāya cāṣṭamo garbho devakyā dharaṇīdharaḥ bhaviṣyatītyāca cakṣe bhagavānnārado muniḥ  ViP kaṃso pi tadupaśrutya nāradātkupitastataḥ devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca gṛhe guptāvadhārayat  ViP vasudevena kaṃsāya tenaivoktaṃ yathā purā tathaiva vasudevo pi putram arpitavān dvija  ViP hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāḥṣaḍgarbhā iti viśrutāḥ viṣṇuprayuktā stānnidrākramādgarbhānayojayat  ViP yoganidrā mahāmāyā vaiṣṇavī mohitaṃ yayā avidyayā jagatsarvaṃ tāmāha bhagavānhariḥ  ViP śrībhagavānuvācanidre gaccha mamādeśātpātālātalasaṃśrayān ekaikatvena ṣaḍgarbhāndevakījaṭharaṃ naya  ViP hateṣu teṣu kaṃsena śeṣākhyoṃśastato mama aṃśāṃśonādare tasyāḥsaptamaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati  ViP gokule vasudevasya bhāryānyā rohiṇī sthitā tasyāḥsa saṃbhūtisamaṃ devi neyastvayodaram  ViP saptamo bhojarā jasya bhayādrodhoparodhataḥ devakyāḥ pitito garbha iti loko vadiṣyati  ViP garbhasaṃkarṣaṇātso tha loke saṃkarṣaṇeti vai saṃjñāmavāpsyate vīraḥ śvetādriśikharopamaḥ  ViP tato haṃ saṃbhaviṣyāmi devakījaṭhare śubhe bhargaṃ tvayā yaśodāyā gantavyamavilaṃbitam  ViP prāvṛṭkāle ca nabhasi kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāmahaṃ niśi utpatsyāmi navamyāṃ tu prasūtiṃ tvamavāpsyasi  ViP yaśodāśayane māṃ tu devakyāstvāmanindite macchaktiproritamatirvasudevo nayiṣyati  ViP kaṃsaś ca tvāmupādāya devi śailaśilātale prakṣepsyatyantārikṣe ca saṃsthānaṃ tvamavāpsyasi  ViP tatastvāṃ śatadṛkchakraḥ praṇamya mama gauravāt praṇipātānataśirā bhaginītve grahīṣyati  ViP tvaṃ ca śuṃbhaniśuṃbhādīnhatvā daityānsahasraśaḥ sthānair anekaiḥ pṛthivīmaśeṣāṃ maṇḍayiṣyasi  ViP tvaṃ bhūtiḥ sannatiḥ kṣāntiḥ kāntirdyauḥ pṛthivī dhṛtiḥ lajjāpuṣṭī ruṣā yā tu kācidanyā tvameva sā  ViP ye tvāmāryeti durgeti vedagarbhāṃbiketi ca bhadreti bhadrakālīti kṣemadā bhagyadeti ca  ViP prātaścaivāparāhne ca stoṣyantyānamramūrtayaḥ teṣāṃ hi prārthitaṃ sarvaṃ matprasādādbhaviṣyati  ViP surāmāṃsopaharaiś ca bhakṣyabhojyaiś ca pūjitā nṝṇāmaśeṣasāmāṃstvaṃ prasannā saṃpradāsyasi  ViP te sarve sarvadā bhadre matprasādādasaṃśayam asaṃdigdhā bhaviṣyanti gaccha devi yathoditam iti viṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe prathamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācayathoktaṃ sā jagaddhātrā devadevena vai tathā ṣaḍgarbhagarbavinyāsaṃ cakre cānyasya karṣaṇam  ViP saptame rohiṇīṃ garbhe prāpte garbhaṃ tato hariḥ lokatra yopakārāya devakyāḥ praviveśa ha  ViP yoganidrā yaśodāyāstasminneva tathā dine saṃbhūtā jaṭhare tadvadyathoktaṃ parameṣṭhinā  ViP tato grahagaṇaḥsamyakpracacāra divi dvija viṣṇoraṃśe bhuvaṃ yāte ṛtavaścābabhuḥ śubhāḥ  ViP na sehe devakīṃ draṣṭaṃ kaśtidapyatitejasā jājvalyamānāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā manāṃsi kṣobhamāyayuḥ  ViP adṛṣṭāḥ puruṣaiḥ strībhir devakīṃ devatāgaṇāḥ bibhrāṇāṃ vapuṣā viṣṇuṃ tuṣṭuvustāmaharniśam  ViP devatā ūcuḥprakṛtistvaṃ parā sūkṣmā brahmagarbhābhavatpurā tato vāṇī jagaddhāturvedagarbhāsi śobhane  ViP sṛjyasvarūpagarbhāsi sṛṣṭibhūtā sanātane bījabhūtā tu sarvasya yajñabhūtā bhavastrayī  ViP phalagarbhā tvamevejyā vahnigarbhā tathāraṇiḥ aditirdevagarbhā tvaṃ daityagarbhā tathā ditiḥ  ViP jyotsnā vāsaragarbhā tvaṃ jñānagarbhāsi sannatiḥ nayagarbhā parā nītirlajjā tvaṃ praśrayodvahā  ViP kāmagarbhā tathecchā tvaṃ tuṣṭiḥ saṃtoṣagarbhiṇī medhā ca bodhagarbhasi dhairyagarbhodvahā dhṛtiḥ  ViP graharkṣatārakāgarbhā dyaurasyākhilahaitukī etā vibhūtayo devi tathānyāś ca sahasraśaḥ  ViP tathā saṃkhyā jagaddhātrī sāṃprataṃ jaṭhare tava samudrādrinadīdvīpavanapattanabhūṣaṇā grāmakharvaṭakheṭāḍhyā samastā pṛtivī śubhe  ViP samastavahnayoṃbhāṃsi sakalāś ca samīraṇāḥ mahoragās tathā yakṣā rākṣasāḥ pretagudyakāḥ  ViP graharkṣatārakācitravimānaśatasaṃkutam avakāśamaśeṣasya yaddadāti nabhasthalam  ViP bhūlokaś ca bhuvarlokaḥsvarloko tha maharjanaḥ tapaś ca brahmalokaś ca brahmāṇḍamakhilaṃ śubhe  ViP tadantare sthitā devā daityagandharvacāraṇāḥ mahoragās tathā yakṣā rākṣasāḥ pretaguhyakāḥ  ViP manuṣyāḥ paśavaścānye ye ca jīvā yaśasvini tair antasthair ananto sau sarvagaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ  ViP rūpakarmasvarūpāṇi na paricchedagocare yasyākhilapramāṇāni sa viṣṇur garbhagas tava  ViP tvaṃ svāhā tvaṃ svadhā vidyā svadhā tvaṃ jyotiraṃbare tvaṃ sarvalokarakṣārthamavatīrṇā mahītale  ViP prasīda devi sarvasya jagataḥ śaṃ śubhe kuru prītyā taṃ dhārayeśānaṃ dhṛtaṃ yenākhilaṃ jagat  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe dvitīyo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ saṃstūyamānā sā devair devamadhārayat garbheṇa puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ jagatastrāṇakāraṇam  ViP tato khilajagatpadmabodhāyācyutabhānunā devakīpūrvasaṃdhyāyāmāvirbhūtaṃ mahātmanā  ViP tajjanmadinamatyarthamāhlādyamaladiṅmukham babhūva karvalokasya kaumudī śaśino yathā  ViP saṃtaḥsaṃtoṣamadhakaṃ praśamaṃ cañjamārutāḥ prasādaṃ nimnagā yātā jāyamāne janārdane  ViP siṃdhavo nijaśabdena vādyaṃ cakrurmanoharam jagurgandharvapatayo nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ  ViP sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi devā bhuvyantarikṣagāḥ jajvaluścāgnayaḥ śāntā jāyamāne janārdane  ViP madaṃ jagurjurjaladāḥ puṣpavṛṣṭimuco dvija ardharātre khilādhāre jāyamāne janārdane  ViP phullendīvarapatrābhaṃ caturbāhumudīkṣya tam śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ jātaṃ tuṣṭāvānakadundubhiḥ  ViP abhiṣṭraya ca taṃ vāgbhiḥ prasannābhir mahāmatiḥ vijñāpayāmāsa tadā kaṃsādbhīto dvijottama  ViP vasudeva uvācajātosi devadeveśa śaṅkhacakragadādharam divyarūpamidaṃ deva prasādenopasaṃhara  ViP adyaiva deva kaṃsoyaṃ kurute mama ghātanam avatīrma iti jñātvā tvamasminmamamandire  ViP devakyuvācayo nantarūpo khilaviśvarūpo garbhepi lokānvapuṣā bibharti prasītadāmeṣa sa devadevo yo māyayāviṣkṛtabālarūpaḥ  ViP upasaṃhara sarvātmanrūpametaccaturbhujam jānātu māvatāraṃ te kaṃsoyaṃ ditijanmajaḥ  ViP śrībhagavānuvācastuto haṃ ya ttvayā pūrvaṃ putrārthinyā tadadya te saphalaṃ devi saṃjātaṃ jāto haṃ yattavodarāt  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā bhagavāṃstūṣṇīṃ babhūva munisattama vasudevopi taṃ rātrāvādāya prayayau bahiḥ  ViP mohitāścābhavestatra rakṣiṇo yoganidrayā mathurādvārapālāś ca vrajatyānakadundubhau  ViP varṣatāṃ jaladānāṃ ca toyamātyulbaṇaṃ niśi saṃvṛtyānuyayau śeṣaḥ phaṇair ānakadundubhim  ViP yamunāṃ cātigaṃbhīrāṃ nānāvartaśatākulām vasudevo vahanviṣṇuṃ jānumātravahāṃ yayau  ViP kaṃsasya karadānāya tatraivābyāgatāstaṭe nandādīngopavuddhāṃś ca yamunāyā dadarśa saḥ  ViP tasminkāle yaśodāpi mohitā yoganidrayā tāmeva kanyāṃ maitreya prasūtā mohite jane  ViP vasudevopi vinyasya bālamādāya dārikām yaśodāśayanāttūrṇamājagāmāmitadyutiḥ  ViP dadṛśe ca prabuddhā sā yaśodā jātamātmajam nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ tatotyarthaṃ mudaṃ yayau  ViP ādāya vasudevo pi dārikāṃ nijamandire devakīśayane nyasya yathāpūrvamatiṣṭhata  ViP tato bāladhvaniṃ śrutvā rakṣiṇaḥ sahasotthitāḥ kaṃsāyāvedayāmāsurdevakīprasavandvija  ViP kaṃsastūrṇamupetyaināṃ tato jagraha bālikām muñcamuñceti devakyā sannakaṇṭhyā nivāritaḥ  ViP cikṣepa ca śilāpṛṣṭhe sā kṣiptā viyati sthitā avāpa rūpaṃ uvācakaṃsastatodvignamanāḥ prāha sarvānmahāsurān pralaṃbakeśipramukhānāhūyāsurapuṅgavān  ViP kaṃsa uvācahe pralaṃba mahābāho keśin dhenuka pūtane ariṣṭādyāstathaivānye śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama  ViP māṃ ViP vasudevopi taṃ prāha diṣṭyādiṣṭyeti sādaram vārdhake pi samutpannastanayo yaṃ tavādhunā  ViP datto hi vārṣikaḥsarvo bhavadbhir nṛpateḥ karaḥ yadarthamāgatāstasmānnātra stheyaṃ mahādhanaiḥ  ViP nṛsiṃharūpī sarvatra rakṣatu tvāṃ janārdanaḥ  ViP vāmano rakṣatu sadā bhavantaṃ yaḥ kṣaṇādabhūt trivikramaḥ kramākrāntatrailokyaḥ sphuradāyudhaḥ  ViP śiraste pātu govindaḥ kaṇṭhaṃ rakṣatu keśavaḥ śāyitaḥ śakaṭasyādho bālaparyaṅkikātale  ViP te ca gopā mahaddṛṣṭvā pūtanāyāḥ kalevaram mṛtāyāḥ paramaṃ trāsaṃ vismayaṃ ca tadā yayuḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe pañcamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara hāhākṛtaḥ sarvo goparopījano dvija ājagāmātha dadṛśe bālamutānaśāyinam  ViP gopāḥ keneti kenedaṃ śakaṭaṃ parivartitam tatraiva bālakāḥ procurbālenānena pātitam  ViP rudatā dṛṣṭamasmābhiḥ pādavikṣepapātitam śakaṭaṃ parivṛttaṃ vai naitadanyasya ceṣṭitam  ViP tataḥ punaratīvāsangopā vismayacetasaḥ nandagopopi jagrāha bālamatyantavismitaḥ  ViP yaśodā śakaṭārūḍhabhagnabhāṇḍakapālikā  ViP pūtanāyā vināśaś ca śakaṭasya viparyayaḥ vinā vātādidoṣeṇa drumayoḥ patanantathā  ViP vṛndāvanamitaḥsthānāttasmādgacchāma mā ciram yāvadbhaumamahotpātadoṣo nābhibhavevdrajam  ViP iti kṛtvā matiṃ dravyāvayavanirdhūtaṃ kṣaṇamātreṇa tattathā kākabhāsasamākīrṇaṃ vrajasthānamabhūddūja  ViP vṛndāvanaṃ bhagavatā kṛṣṇenā kliṣṭakarmaṇā śubhena manasā dhyātaṃ gavaṃ siddhimabhīpsatā  ViP tatastatrātirūkṣe pi gharmakāle dvijottama prāvṛṭkāla ivodbhūtaṃ navaśaṣpaṃ samantataḥ  ViP sa samāvāsitaḥ sarvo vrajo vṛndāvane tataḥ śakaṭāvāṭaparyantaścandrārdhākārasaṃsthitaḥ  ViP vatsapālau ca mārakatīvāsītpadmarāgavibhūṣitā  ViP ūhurunmārgavāhīni nimnagāṃbhāṃsi sarvataḥ manāṃsi durvinītānāṃ prāpya lakṣmīṃ navāmiva  ViP na rejentaritaścandro nirmalo malinair ghanaiḥ sadvādivādo mūrkhaṇāṃ pragalbhābhir ivoktibhiḥ  ViP nirguṇenāpi cāpena śakrasya gagane padam avāpyatāvivekasya nṛpasyaiva parigrahe  ViP meghapṛṣṭhe balākānāṃ rarāja vimalā tatiḥ durvatte vṛttaceṣṭeva kulīnasyātiśaubhanā  ViP na ba bandhāṃbare sthairyaṃ vidyudatyantacañcalā maitrīva pravare puṃsi durjanena prayojitā  ViP mārgā babhūvur aspaṣṭās tṛṇaśaṣpacayāvṛtāḥ arthāntaramanuprāptāḥ prajaḍānāmivoktayaḥ  ViP unmattaśikhisāraṅge tasminkāle mahāvane kṛṣṇarāmau mudāyuktau gopālaiś ceratuḥ saha  ViP kvicidgobhiḥ samaṃ ramyaṃ goyatānaratāvubhau ceratuḥ kvacidatyarthaṃ śītavṛkṣatalāśritau  ViP kvacitkadaṃbasrakcitrau mayūrasragvirājitau viliptau kvacidāsātāṃ vividhair giridhātubhiḥ  ViP parṇaśayyāsu saṃsuptau kvacinnidrāntaraiṣiṇau kvacidgarjati jīmūte hāhākāraravākulau  ViP gāyatāmanya gopānāṃ praśaṃsāparamau kvacit mayūrakekānugatau gopaveṇupravādakau  ViP iti nānāvidhair bhāvair uttamaprītisaṃyutau krīḍantau tau vane tasmiñceratustuṣṭamānasau  ViP vikāle ca samaṃ gobhir gopavṛndasamanvitau vihṛtyātha yathāyogaṃ vrajametya mahābalau  ViP gopaiḥ samānaiḥ sahitau krīḍantāvamarāviva evaṃ tāvūṣatustatra rāmakṛṣṇau mahādyutī  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe ṣaṣṭhodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaekadā tu vinā rāmaṃ kṛṣṇo vṛndāvanaṃ yayau vicacāra vṛto gopair vanyapuṣpasragujjvalaḥ  ViP sa jagāmātha kālindīṃ lola kallolaśālinīm tīrasaṃlagnaphenaughair hasantīm iva sarvataḥ  ViP tasyāścatimahābhīmaṃ viṣāgniśritavāriṇam hradaṃ kālīyanāgasya dadarśativibhīṣaṇam  ViP viṣāgninā prasaratā dagdhatīraṃmahīruham vātāhatāṃbuvikṣepasparśadagdhavihaṅgamam  ViP tamatīva mahā raudraṃ mṛtyuvakramivāparam vilokya cintayāmāsa bhagavānmadhusūdanaḥ  ViP asminvasati duṣṭātmā kālīyo sau viṣāyudhaḥ yo mayā nirjitastyaktvā duṣṭo gacchetpayonidhim  ViP teneyaṃ dūṣitā sarvā yamunā sāgaraṅgamā na naraigodhanaiś cāpi tṛṣārtair upabhujyate  ViP tadasya nāgarājasya kartavyo nigraho mayā nistrāsāstu sukhaṃ yena careyurvrajavāsinaḥ  ViP etadarthaṃ tu lokesminnavatāraḥ kṛto mayā yadeṣāmutpathasthānāṃ kāryā śāntirdurātmanām  ViP tadetaṃ nātidūrasthaṃ kadaṃbamuruśākhinam adirudya patiṣyāmi hrade sminnanilāśinaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaitthaṃ vicintya baddhā ca gāḍhaṃ parikaraṃ tataḥ nipapāta hrade tatra nāgarājasya vegataḥ  ViP tenātipatatā tatra kṣobhitaḥsa mahāhradaḥ atyarthaṃ dūrajātāṃstu samasiṃcanmahīruhān  ViP te hi duṣṭaviṣajvālātaptāṃbupavanokṣitāḥ jajvaluḥ pādāpāḥsadyo jvālāvyāptadigantarāḥ  ViP āsphoṭayāmāsa tadā kṛṣṇo nāgahrane bhujam tacchabdaśravaṇāccāśu nāgarājo bhyupāgamat  ViP ātāmranayanaḥ kopādviṣajvālākulair mukhaiḥ vṛto mahāviṣaiś cānyair uragair anilāśanaiḥ  ViP nāgapatnyaś ca śataśo hārihāropaśobhitāḥ prakaṃpitatanukṣepacalatkuntasakāntayaḥ  ViP tataḥ praveṣṭitaḥsarpaiḥ sa kṛṣṇe bhogabandhanaiḥ dadaṃśuste pi taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ viṣajvālākulair mukhaiḥ  ViP taṃ tatra patitaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarpabhogaurnipīḍitam gopā vrajamupāgamya cukruśuḥ śokalālasāḥ  ViP gopā ūcuḥeṣa mohaṃ gataḥ kṛṣṇo magnau vai kāliyahrade bhakṣyate nāgarājena tamāgacchata paśyata  ViP tacchutvā tatra te gopā vajrapā topamaṃ vacaḥ gopyaś ca tvarītā jagmuryaśodāpramukhā hradam  ViP hāhā kvāsāviti jano gopīnāmativihvalaḥ yaśodayā samaṃ bhrānto drutapraskhalitaṃ yayau  ViP nandagopaś ca gopāś ca rāmaścādbhutavikramaḥ tvaritaṃ yamunāṃ jagmuḥ kṛṣṇadarśanalālāsāḥ  ViP dadṛśuścāpi te tatra sarparājavaśaṅgatam niṣprayatnīkṛtaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ sarpabhogaviveṣṭitam  ViP nandagopopi niśceṣṭo nyasya putramukhe dṛśam yaśodā ca mahābhāgā babhūva munisattama  ViP gopyas tvanyā rudantyaś ca dadṛśuḥ śokakātarāḥ procuś ca keśavaṃ prītyā bhayakātaryagadgadam  ViP gopya ūcuḥsarvā yaśodayā sārdha viśāmotra mahāhradam sarparājasya no gantumasmābhir yujyate vrajam  ViP divasaḥ so vinā sūryaṃ vinā candreṇa kā niśā vinā vṛṣeṇa kā gāvo vinā kṛṣṇena ko vrajaḥ  ViP vinākṛtā na yāsyāmaḥ kṛṣṇenānena gokulam aramyaṃ nātisevyaṃ ca vārihīnaṃ yathā saraḥ  ViP yatra nendīvaraśyāmakāyakāntirayaṃ hariḥ tenāpi pāturvāsena ratirastīti vismayaḥ  ViP utphullapaṅkajadalaspaṣṭakāntivilocanam apaśyanto hariṃ dīnāḥ kathaṃ goṣṭhe bhaviṣyatha  ViP atyanta madhurālāpahṛtāśeṣamanoratham na vinā puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ yāsyāmo nandagokulam  ViP bhogenāviṣṭitasyāpi sarparājasya paśyata smitaśobhimukhaṃ gopyaḥ kṛṣṇasyāsmadvilokane  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti gopīvacaḥ śrutvā rauhiṇeyo mahābalaḥ gopāṃś ca trāsavidhurānvi lokya stimitekṣaṇān  ViP nandaṃ ca dīnamatyarthaṃ nyastadṛṣṭiṃ sutānane mūrchākulāṃ yaśodaṃ ca kṛṣṇamāhātmasaṃjñayā  ViP kimidaṃ devadeveśa bhāvo yaṃ mānuṣastvayā vyajyatetyantamātmānaṃ kimanantaṃ na votsi yat  ViP tvameva jagato nābhir arāṇāmiva saṃśrayaḥ kartāpahartā pātā ca traulokyaṃ tvaṃ trayīmayaḥ  ViP sendrai rudrāgnivasubhir ādityair marudaśvibhiḥ cintyase tvamacintyātman samastaiś caiva yogibhiḥ  ViP jagatyarthaṃ jagannātha bhārāvataraṇecchayā avatīrṇo si martyeṣu tavāṃśaścāhamagrajaḥ  ViP manuṣyalīlāṃ bhagavan bhajatā bhavatā surāḥ viḍambayantastvallīlāṃ sarva eva sahā sate  ViP avatārya bhavānpūrvaṃ gokule tu surāṅganāḥ krīḍārthamātmanaḥ paścādavartīrṇo si śāśvata  ViP atrāvatīrṇayoḥ kṛṣṇa gopā eva hi bāndhavāḥ gopyaś ca sīdataḥ kasmādetānbandhūnupekṣase  ViP darśito mānuṣo bhāvo darśitaṃ bālacāpalam tadayaṃ damyatāṃ kṛṣṇa duṣṭatmā daśanāyudhaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti saṃsmāritaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ smitabhinnoṣṭhasaṃpuṭaḥ āsphoṭya mocayāmāsa svadehaṃ bhogibandhanāt  ViP ānamya cāpi hastābhyāmubhābhyāṃ madhyamaṃ śiraḥ āruhyābhugnaśirasaḥ praṇanartoruvikramaḥ  ViP prāṇāḥ phaṇe bhavaṃścāsya kṛṣṇasyāṅghrinikuṭṭanaiḥ yatronnatiṃ ca kurute nanāmāsya tataḥ śiraḥ  ViP mūrchāmupāyayau bhrāntyā nāgaḥ kṛṣṇasya recakaiḥ daṇḍapātanipātena vavāma rudhiraṃ bahu  ViP taṃ vibhigraśirogrīvamāsyebhyasmutaśoṇitam vilokya karuṇaṃ jagmustatpatnyo madhusūdanam  ViP nāgapatnya ūcuḥjñāto si devadeveśa sarvajñastvamanuttamaḥ paraṃ jyotiracintyaṃ yattadaṃśaḥ parameśvaraḥ  ViP na samarthāḥ surāḥstotuṃ yamananyabhavaṃ vibhum svarūpavarṇanaṃ tasya kathaṃ yoṣitkariṣyati  ViP yasyākhilamahīrvyomajalāgnipavanātmakam brahmāṇḍamalpakālpāṃśaḥ stoṣyāmastaṃ kathaṃ vayam  ViP yamato na vidurnityaṃ yatsvarūpaṃ hi yoginaḥ paramārthamaṇoralpaṃ sthūlātsthūlaṃ natāḥ sma tam  ViP na yasya janmane dhātā yasya cāntāya nāntakaḥ sthitikartā na cānyosti yasya tasmai namaḥsadā  ViP kopaḥ svalpo pi te nāsti sthitipālanameva te kāraṇaṃ kāliya syāsya damane śruyatāṃ vacaḥ  ViP striyonukaṃpyāḥsādhūnāṃ mūḍhā dīnāś ca jantavaḥ yatastatosya dīnasya kṣamyatāṃ kṣamatāṃvara  ViP samasta jagadāvāro bhavānalpabalaḥ phaṇī tvatpādapīḍito jahyānmuhūrtārdhana jīvitam  ViP kva pannago lpavīryo yaṃ kva bhavānbhuvanāśrayaḥ prītidveṣau samotkṛṣṭagocarau bhavato vyaya  ViP tataḥ kuru jagatsvāminprasādamavasīdataḥ prāṇāṃstyajati nāgo yaṃ bhartṛbhikṣā pradīyatām  ViP bhuvaneśa jagannātha mahāpuruṣapūrvaja prāṇāṃstyajati nāgo yaṃ bhartṛbhikṣāṃ prayaccha naḥ  ViP vedāntavedya deveśa duṣṭadaityanibarhama prāṇāṃstyajati nāgo yaṃ bhartabhikṣā pradīyatām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityukte tābhir āśvasya klāntadehopi pannagaḥ prasīda devadeveti prāha vākyaṃ śanaiḥ śanaiḥ  ViP kāliya uvācatavāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ nātha svābhāvikaṃ param nirastātiśayaṃ yasya tasya stoṣyāmi kitrvaham  ViP tvaṃ parastvaṃ parasyādyaḥ paraṃ tvattaḥ parātmaka parasmātparamo yas tvaṃ tasya stoṣyāmi kinnv aham  ViP yasmādbahmāca rudraś ca candredramarudaśvinaḥ vasavaś ca sahādityais tasya stoṣyāmi kitrvaham  ViP ekāvayavasūkṣmāṃśo yasyaitadakhilaṃ jagat kalpanāvayavasyāṃśastasya stoṣyāmi kitrvaham  ViP sadasadrūpiṇo yasya brahmādyās tridaśeśvarāḥ paramārthaṃ na jānanti tasya stoṣyāmi kitrvaham  ViP brahmādyaurarcite yastu gandhapuṣpānulepanaiḥ nandanādisamudbhūtaiḥ sorcyate vā kathaṃ mayā  ViP yasyāvatārarūpāṇi devarājaḥsadārcati na vetti paramaṃ rūpaṃ sorcyate vā kathaṃ mayā  ViP viṣayebhyaḥ samāvṛttya sarvākṣāṇi ca yoginaḥ yamarcayanti dhyānena sorcyate vā kathaṃ mayā  ViP hṛdi saṃkalpya yadrūpaṃ dhyānenārcanti yoginaḥ bhāvapuṣpādinā nāthaḥ sorcyate vā kathaṃ mayā  ViP so haṃ te devadeveśa nārcanādau stutau na ca sāmarthyavān kṛpāmātramanovṛttiḥ prasīda me  ViP sarpajātiriyaṃ krurā yasyāṃ jātosmi keśava tatsvabhāvo yamatrāsti nāparādho mamācyuta  ViP sṛjyate bhavatā sarvaṃ tathā saṃhrīyate jagat jātirūpasvabhāvāś ca sṛjyante sṛjatā tvayā  ViP yathāhaṃ bhavatā sṛṣṭo jātyā rūpeṇa ceśvara svabhāvena ca sādhutvaṃ tathedaṃ ceṣṭitaṃ mayā  ViP yadyanyathā pravarteyaṃ devadeva tato mayi nyāyo daṇḍanipāto vai tavaivavacanaṃ yathā  ViP tathāpyajñe jagatsvāmindaṇḍaṃ pātitavānmayi sa ślāghyo yaṃ paro daṇḍas tvatto me nānyato varaḥ  ViP hatavīryo hataviṣo damito haṃ tvayācyuta jīvitaṃ dīyatāmekamājñāpaya karomi kim  ViP śrībhagavānuvācanātra stheyantvayā sarpa kadācidyamunājale saputraparivārastvaṃ samudrasalilaṃ vraja  ViP matpadāni ca te sarpa dṛṣṭvā mūrdhani sāgare garuḍaḥ pannagaripustvayi na prahariṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā sarparājaṃ taṃ mumoca bhagavānhariḥ praṇamya so pi kṛṣṇāya jagāma payasāṃ nidhim  ViP paśyatāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ sabhṛtyasutabāndhavaḥ samastabhāryāsahitaḥ parityajya svakaṃ hradam  ViP gate sarpe pariṣvajya mṛtaṃ punarivāgatam gopā mūrdhani hārdena siṣicur netrajair jalaiḥ  ViP kṛṣṇāmākliṣṭakarmāṇamanye vismitacetasaḥ tuṣṭuvurmuditā gopā dṛṣṭvā śivajalāṃ nadīm  ViP gīyamānaḥ sa gopībhiścāritaiḥ sādhuceṣṭitaiḥ saṃstūyamāno gopaiś ca kṛṣṇo vrajamupāgamat  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe saptamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācagāḥ pālayantau ca punaḥ sahitau balakeśavau bhramamāṇau vane tasminramyaṃ tālavanaṃ gatau  ViP tattu tālavanaṃ divyaṃ dhenuko nāma dānavaḥ mṛgamāṃsakṛtāhāraḥ sadādhyāste kharākṛtiḥ  ViP tattu tālavanaṃ pakvaphalasaṃpatsamanvitam dṛṣṭvā spṛhānvitā gopā phalādāne bruvanvacaḥ  ViP gopā ūcuḥhe rāma he kṛṣṇa sadā dhenukenaiṣa rakṣyate bhūpradeśo yatastasmātpakvānīmāni saṃti vai  ViP phalāni paśya tālānāṃ gandhāmoditadiṃśi vai vayametānyabhīpsāmaḥ pātyantāṃ yadi rocate  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti gopakumārāṇāṃ śrutvā saṃkarṣaṇo vacaḥ etatkartavyamityuktvā pātayāmāsa tāni vai kṛṣṇaś ca pātayāmāsa bhuvitāni phalāni vai  ViP phalānāṃ patatāṃ śabdamākarṇya sudurāsadaḥ ājagāma sa duṣṭātmā kopāddaiteyagardabhaḥ  ViP padbhyāmubhābhyāṃ sa tadā paścimābhyāṃ balaṃ balī jaghānorasi tābhyāṃ ca sa ca tenābhyagṛhyata  ViP gṛhītvā bhrāmayāmāsa soṃbare gatajīvitam tasminneva sa cikṣepa vegena tṛṇarājani  ViP tataḥ phalānyanekāni tālāgrānnipatankharaḥ pṛthivyāṃ pātayāmāsa mahāvāto ghanāniva  ViP anyā natha sajātīyānāgatāndaityagardabhān kṛṣṇaścikṣepa tālāgre balabhadraś ca līlayā  ViP kṣaṇenālaṅkṛtā pṛthvī pakvais talaphalais tadā daitya gardabhadehaiś ca maitreya śuśubhe dhikam  ViP tato gāvo nirābādhāstasmiṃstalavane dvija navaśaṣvaṃ sukhaṃ ceruryanna bhuktamabhūtpurā  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe ṣṭamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācatasminrāsabhadaiteye sānuge vinipātite saumyaṃ tadgopagopīnāṃ ramyaṃ tālavanaṃ babhau  ViP tatastau jātaharṣau tu vasudevasutāvubhau hatvā dhenukadaiteyaṃ bhāṇḍīravaṭam āgatau  ViP kṣvelamānau pragāyantau vicinvantau ca tajjātiguṇayuktābhiḥ kriḍābhiśceraturvanam  ViP tatastvāndolikābhiś ca niyuddhaiś ca mahābalau vyāyāmaṃ cakratustatra kṣepaṇīyais tathāśmabhiḥ  ViP tallipsurasurastatra hyubhayo ramamāṇayoḥ ājagāma pralaṃbākhyo gopaveṣatirohitaḥ  ViP so vagāhata niḥśaṅkasteṣāṃ madhyamamānuṣaḥ mānuṣaṃ vapurāsthāya pralaṃbo dānavottamaḥ  ViP tayośichdrāntaraprepsuraviṣahyamamanyata kṛṣṇaṃ tato rauhiṇeyaṃ hantuṃ pupluvustataḥ  ViP śrīdāmānaṃ tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pralaṃbaṃ rohiṇīsutaḥ jitavānkṛṣṇapakṣīyair gopair anye parājitāḥ  ViP te vāhayantastvanyonyaṃ bhāṇḍīraṃ vaṭametya vai punarnivavṛtuḥsarve yeye tatra parijitāḥ  ViP saṃkarṣaṇaṃ tu skandhena śīghramutkṣipyadānavaḥ nabhaḥsthalaṃ jagāmāśu sacandra iva vāridaḥ  ViP asahanrauhiṇeyasya sa bhāraṃ dānavottamaḥ vavṛdhe sa mahākāyaḥ prāvṛṣīva balāhakaḥ  ViP saṃkarṣaṇastu taṃ dṛṣṭvā dagdhaśailopamākṛtim sragdāmalaṃbābharaṇaṃ makuṭāṭopamastakam  ViP raudraṃ śakaṭacakrākṣaṃ pādanyāsa calatkṣitim abhītamanasā tena rakṣasā rohiṇīsutaḥ hriyamāmastataḥ kṛṣṇamidaṃ vacanamabravīt  ViP kṛṣṇākṛṣṇa hriyāmyeṣa parvatodagramūrtinā kenāpi paśya daityena gopālacchadmarūpiṇā  ViP yadatra sāṃprataṃ kāryaṃ mayā madhuniṣūdana tatkathyatāṃ prayātyeṣa durātmātitvarānvitaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatamāha rāmaṃ govindaḥsmitabhinnoṣṭhasaṃpuṭaḥ mahātmā rauhiṇeyasya balavīryapramāmāvit  ViP śrīkṛṣṇa uvācakimayaṃ mānuṣo bhāvo vyaktamevāvalaṃbyate sarvātman sarvaguhyānāṃ guhyaguhyātmanā tvayā  ViP smarāśeṣajagadbījakāraṇaṃ kāraṇāgraja ātmānamekaṃ tadvacca jagatyekārṇave ca yat  ViP kiṃ na vetsi yathāhaṃ ca tvaṃ caikaṃ kāraṇaṃ bhuvaḥ bhārāvatāraṇārthāya martyalokamupāgatau  ViP nabhaśiśrasteṃbuvahāś ca keśāḥ pādau kṣitirvatrkramanantavahni somo manaste śvasitaṃ samīraṇo diśaścatasro vyaya bāhavaste  ViP sahasrabatrkro bhagavānmahātmā sahasrahastāṅghriśarīrabhedaḥ sahasrapadmodbhavayonirādyaḥsahasraśastvāṃ munayo gṛṇanti  ViP divyaṃ hi rūpaṃ tava vetti nānyo devair aśeṣair avatārarūpam tadarcyate vetsi na kiṃ yadante tvayyeva viśvaṃ layamabhyupaiti  ViP tvayā dhṛteyaṃ dharaṇī bibharti carācaraṃ viśvamanantamūrte kṛtādibhedairaja kālarūpo nimeṣapūrvo jagadetadatsi  ViP attaṃ yathā vaḍāvavahnināṃbu himasvarūpaṃ parigṛhya kāstam himācale bhānumatoṃśusaṃgājjalatvamabhyeti punastadeva  ViP evaṃ tvayā saṃharaṇe ttametajjagatsamastaṃ tvadadhīnakaṃ punaḥ tavaiva sargāya samudyatasya jagattvamabhyetyasukalpamīśa  ViP bhavānahaṃ ca viśvātmannekameva ca kāraṇam jagatosya jagatyarthe bhedenāvāṃ vyavasthitau  ViP tatsmaryatāmameyātmastvayātmā jahi dānavam mānuṣyamevāvalaṃbya bandhūnāṃ kriyatāṃ hitam  ViP śrī parāśara uvācaiti saṃsmārito vipra kṛṣṇena sumahātmanā vihasya pīḍayāmāsa pralaṃbaṃ balavānbalaḥ  ViP muṣṭinā sohananmūrdhni kopasaṃraktalocanaḥ tena cāsya prahāreṇa bahiryāte vilocane  ViP sa niṣkāsitamastiṣko mukhācchoṇitamudvaman nipapāta mahīpṛṣṭhe datya varyo mamāra ca  ViP pralaṃbaṃ nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā balenādbhutakarmaṇā prahṛṣṭāstuṣṭuvurgaupāḥsādhusādhviti cābruvan  ViP saṃstūyamāno gopais tu rāmo daitye nipātite pralaṃbaṃ saha kṛṣṇena punargokulamāyayau  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe navamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācatayorviharatorevaṃ rāmakeśavayorvraje prāvṛḍ vyatītā vikasatsarojā cābhavaccharat  ViP avāpustāpamatyarthaṃ śapharyaḥ palvalodake putrakṣetrādisaktena mamatvena yathā gṛhī  ViP mayurā maunamātasthuḥ parityaktamadā vane asāratāṃ parijñāya saṃsārasyeva yoginaḥ  ViP utsṛjya jalasarvasvaṃ vimalāḥsitamūrtayaḥ tatyajuścāṃbaraṃ meghā gṛhaṃ vijñānino yathā  ViP śaratsūryāṃśutaptāni yayuḥ śoṣaṃ sarāṃsi ca bahvālaṃbamamatvena hṛdayānīva dehinām  ViP kumudaiḥ śaradaṃbhāṃsi yogyatālakṣaṇaṃ yayuḥ avabodhair manāṃsīva samatvamamalātmanām  ViP tārakāvimale vyomni rarājākhaṇḍamaṇḍalaḥ candraścaramadehātmā yogī sādhukule yathā  ViP śanakaiḥ śanakais tīraṃ tatyajuś ca jalāśayāḥ mamatvaṃ kṣetraputrādirūḍhamuccair yathā budhāḥ  ViP pūrvaṃ tyaktaiḥ saroṃbhobhir haṃsā yogaṃ punar yayuḥ kleśaiḥ kuyogino śeṣair antarāyahatā iva  ViP nibhṛto bhavadatyarthaṃ samudraḥstimitodakaḥ kramāvāptamahāyogo viścalātmā yathā yatiḥ  ViP sarvatrātiprasannāni salilāni tathābhavan jñāte sarvagate viṣṇau manāṃsīva sumedhasām  ViP babhūva nirmalaṃ vyoma śaradā dhvastatoyadam yogāgnidagdhakleśaughaṃ yogināmiva mānasam  ViP sūryāṃśujanitaṃ tāpaṃ nitye tārāpatiḥ śamam ahaṃmānodbhavaṃ duḥkhaṃ vivekaḥ sumahāniva  ViP nabhasobdaṃ bhuvaḥ paṅkaṃ kāluṣyaṃ dadarśedro mahāraṃbhāyodyatāṃstānvrajaukasaḥ  ViP kṛṣṇastānutsukāndṛṣṭvā gopānutsavalālasān kautūhalādidaṃ vākyaṃ prāha vṛddhānmahāmatiḥ  ViP ko yaṃ śakramaho nāma yena vo harṣa āgataḥ prāha taṃ vartayāmopayuñjānāstarpayāmaś ca devatāḥ  ViP kṣīravatya imā gāvo vatsavatyaś ca nirvṛtāḥ tena saṃvardhitaiḥ sasyais tuṣṭāḥ puṣṭāḥ bhavanti vai  ViP nāsasyā nātṛṇā bhūmirna bubhukṣārdito janaḥ dṛśyate sureśamarcanti vayamanye ca mānavāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācanandagopasya vacanaṃ śrutvetthaṃ śakrapūjane roṣāya tridaśendrasya prāhadāmodarastadā  ViP na vayaṃ kṛṣikartāro vāṇijyājīvino na ca ca saiva tasyopakārikā  ViP yo yasya phalamaśranvai pūjayatyaparaṃ naraḥ iha ca pretya caivāsau na tadāpnoti śobhanam  ViP kṛṣyāntā prathitā sīmā mīmāntaṃ ca punarvanam vanāntā girayaḥsarve te cāsmākaṃ parā gatiḥ  ViP na dvārabandhāvaraṇā na gṛhakṣetriṇas tathā sukhinastvakhile loke yathā vai cakracāriṇaḥ  ViP śrūyante girayaścaiva vanesminkāmarūpiṇaḥ tattadrūpaṃ samāsthāya ramante sveṣu  ViP mantrayajñaparā viprāḥsīrayajñāś ca karṣakāḥ girigoyajñaśīlāś ca vayamadrivanāśrayāḥ  ViP tasmādgovardhanaḥ śailo bhavadbhir vividhārhaṇaiḥ arcyatāṃ pūjyatāṃ medhyānpaśunhatvā vidhānataḥ  ViP sarvaghoṣasya saṃdoho gṛhyatāṃ mā vicāryatām bhojyantāṃ tena vai viprās tathā ye cābhivāñchakāḥ  ViP tatrārcite kṛte home bhojiteṣu dvijātiṣu śaratpuṣpakṛtāpīḍāḥ parigacchantu gogaṇāḥ  ViP etanmama mataṃ gopāḥsaṃprītyā kriyate yadi tataḥ kṛtā bhavetprītirgavāmadres tathā mama  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā vandādyāste vrajaukasaḥ prītyutphullamukhā gopāḥsādhusādhvityathābruvan  ViP śobhanaṃ te mataṃ vatsa yadetadbhavatoditam tatkariṣyāmahe sarvaṃ giriyajñaḥ pravartyatām  ViP tathā ca kṛtavantaste giriyajña vrajaukasaḥ dadhipāyasamāṃsādyair daduḥ śailabaliṃ tataḥ  ViP dvijāṃś ca ViP so dhiruhya mahānāgam airāvatam amitrajit govardhanagirau kṛṣṇaṃ dadarśa tridaśeśvaraḥ  ViP cārayantaṃ mahāvīryaṃ gāstu gopavapurdharam kṛtsnasya jagato gopaṃ vṛtaṃ gopakumārakaiḥ  ViP garuḍaṃ ca śrībhagavānuvācamatsaṃbandhena vo gopā yadi lajjā na jāyate ślāghyo vāhaṃ tataḥ kiṃ vo vicāreṇa prayojanam  ViP yadi vo sti mayi prītiḥ ślāghyo haṃ bhavatāṃ yadi tadātmabandhusadṛśī buddhirvaḥ kriyātāṃ mayi  ViP nāhaṃ devo na gāndharvo na yakṣo na ca dānavaḥ ahaṃ vo bāndhavo jāto naitaccintyamito nyathā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaiti śrutvā harervākyaṃ baddhamaunāstato vanam yayurgopā mahābhāga śanaiḥ śanair jagau gopī kācittasya layānugam dattāvadhānā kācicca tameva manasāsmarat  ViP kācitkṛṣṇetikṛṣṇeti proktvā lajjāmupāyayau yayau ca kācitpremāndhā tatpārśvamavilaṃbitam  ViP parabrahmasvarūpiṇam nirucchvāsatayā muktiṃ gatānyā gopakanyakā  ViP gopīparivṛto rātriṃ śaraccandramanoramām mānayāmāsa govindo rāsāraṃbharasotsukaḥ  ViP gopyaś ca vṛndaśaḥ kṛṣṇaceṣṭāsvāyattamūrtayaḥ anyadeśaṃ gate kṛṣṇe cerurvṛndāvanāntaram  ViP kṛṣṇe nibaddhahṛdayā idamūcuḥ parasparam  ViP kṛṣṇo hameṣa lalitaṃ vrajāmyālokyatāṃ gatiḥ anyā bravīnti kṛṣṇasya mama gītirniśamyatām  ViP duṣṭakāliya tiṣṭhātra kṛṣṇohamiti cāparā bāhumāsphoṭya kṛṣṇasya līlayā sarvamādade  ViP anyā bravīti bho gopā niḥśaṅkaiḥ sthīyatāmiti alaṃ vṛṣṭibhayenātra dhṛto govardhano mayā  ViP dhenuko yaṃ mayākṣipto vicarantu yathecchayā gāvo bravīti caivānyā kṛṣṇalīlānusāriṇī  ViP evaṃ nānāprakārāsu kṛṣṇaceṣṭa su tāstadā gopyo vyagrāḥsamaṃ cerū ramyaṃ vṛndāvanāntaram  ViP vilokyaikā bhuvaṃ prāha gopī gopavarāṅganā pulakāñcitasarvāṅgī vikāsinayanotpalā  ViP dhvajabajrāṅkuśābjāṅkarekhāvantyāli paśyata padānyetāni kṛṣṇasya līlālalitagāminaḥ  ViP kāpi tena samāyātā kṛtapuṇyā madālasā padāni tasyāścaitāni ghanānyalpatanūni ca  ViP puṣpāpacayamatroccaiś cakre dāmodare dhruvam yenāgrākrāntamātrāṇi padānyatra mahātmanaḥ  ViP atropaviśya vai tena kācitpuṣpair alaṅkṛtā anyajanmani sarvātmā viṣṇur abhyarcitas tayā  ViP puṣpabandhanasaṃmānakṛtamānāmapāsya tām nandagopasuto yāto mārgeṇānena paśyata  ViP anuyātainamatrānyā nitaṃbabharamantharā yā gantavye drutaṃ yāti nimnapādāgrasaṃsthitiḥ  ViP hastanyastāgrahasteyaṃ tena yāti tathā sakhī anāyattapadanyāsā lakṣyate padapaddhatiḥ  ViP hastasaṃsparśamātreṇa dhūrtenaiṣā vimānitā nairāśyānmandagāminyā nivṛttaṃ lakṣyate padam  ViP nūnamuktā nirāśāḥ kṛṣṇadarśane yamunātīramāsādya jagustaccaritaṃ tathā  ViP tato dadṛśurāyāntaṃ vikāsimukhapaṅkajam gopyas trailokyagoptāraṃ kṛṣṇamakliṣṭaceṣṭitam  ViP kācidālokya govindamāyāntamatiharṣitā dhyāyantī yogārūḍheva sā babhau  ViP tataḥ kāñcit priyālāpaiḥ kāñcid bhrūbhaṅgavīkṣitaiḥ ninye nunayamanyāṃ ca karasparśena mādhavaḥ  ViP tābhiḥ prasannacittābhir gopībhiḥ saha sādaram rarāsa ātmasvarūparūpo sau vyāpī vāyuriva sthitaḥ  ViP yathā samastabhūteṣu nabhogniḥ pṛthivī jalam vāyuścātmā tathaivāsau vyāpya sarvamavasthitaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe trayodaśodhyāyaḥ āyāntaṃ daityavṛṣabhaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇo mahābalaḥ na cacāla tadāsthānādavajñāsmitalīlayā  ViP āsannaṃ caiva jagrāha grāhavanmadhusūdanaḥ jaghāna jānunā kukṣau viṣāṇagrahaṇācalam  ViP tasya darpabalaṃ tridaśādhipatvaṃ manvantaraṃ pūrṇamapetaśatrum  ViP apyeṣa māṃ kaṃsaparigraheṇa doṣāspadībhūtamadoṣaduṣṭam kartāmānopahataṃ dhigastu tajjanma yatsādhubahiṣkṛtasya  ViP jñānātmakasyāmalasattvarāśerapetadoṣasya sadā sphuṭasya kiṃ vā jagatyatra samastapuṃsāmajñātamasyāsti hṛdi sthitasya  ViP tasmādahaṃ bhaktivinamracetā vrajāmi sarveśvamīśvarāṇām aṃśāvatāraṃ puruṣottamasya hyanādimadhyāntamajasya viṣṇoḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe saptaśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācacintayannitigovindamupagamya sa yādavaḥ akrurosmīti caraṇau nanāma śirasā hareḥ  ViP so pyenaṃ dhvajavajrābjakṛtacihnena pāṇinā saṃspṛśyākṛṣya ca prītya sugāḍhaṃ pariṣasvaje  ViP kṛtasaṃvandanau tena yathāvadbalakeśavau tataḥ pravīṣṭau saṃhṛṣṭau tamādāyātmamandiram  ViP saha tābhyāṃ tadākrūraḥ kṛtasaṃvandanādikaḥ bhuktabhojyo yathānyāyyamācacakṣe tatastayoḥ  ViP yathā nirbhatsitastena kaṃsenānakadundubhiḥ yathā ca devakī devī dānavena durātmanā  ViP ugrasene yathā kaṃsaḥsa durātmā ca vartate yaṃ caivārthaṃ samuddiśya kaṃsena tu visarjitaḥ  ViP tatsarvaṃ vistarācchutvā bhagavāndevakīsutaḥ uvācākhilamapyetajjñātaṃ dānapate mayā  ViP kariṣye tanmāhabhāga yadatraupayikaṃ matam vicintyaṃ nānyathaitatte viddhi kaṃsaṃ hataṃ mayā  ViP ahaṃ rāmaś ca mathurāṃ śvo yāsyāvaḥsaha tvayā gopavṛddhāś ca yāsyanti hyādāyopāyanaṃ bahu  ViP niśeyaṃ nīyatāṃ vīra na cintāṃ kartumarhasi trirātrābhyantare kaṃsaṃ nihanaṣyāmi sānugam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasamādiśya tato gopānakrūro pi ca keśavaḥ suṣvāpa balabhadraś ca nandagopagṛhe tataḥ  ViP tataḥ prabhāte vimale kṛṣṇarāmau mahādyutī akrūreṇa samaṃ gantumudyatau mathurāṃ purīm  ViP dṛṣṭvā gopījanaḥsāsraḥ ślathadvalayabāhukaḥ niśaśvasātiduḥkhārtaḥ prāha parasparam  ViP mathurāṃ prāpya govindaḥ kathaṃ gokulameṣyati nagarastrīkalālāpamadhu śrotreṇa pāsyati  ViP vilāsivākyapāneṣu nāgarīṇāṃ kṛtāspadam cittamasya kathaṃ bhūyo grāmyagopīṣu yāsyati  ViP sāraṃ samastagoṣṭhasya vidhinā haratā harim prahṛtaṃ gopayoṣitsu nirghṛṇena durātmanā  ViP bhāvargabhasmitaṃ vākyaṃ vilāsalalitā gatiḥ nāgarīṇāmatīvaitatkaṭākṣekṣitameva ca  ViP grāmyo harirayaṃ tāsāṃ vilāsanigaḍair yutaḥ bhavatīnāṃpunaḥ pārśvaṃ kayā yuktyā sameṣyati  ViP eṣaiṣa rathamāruhya mathurāṃ yāti keśavaḥ krūreṇākrūrakeṇātra nirghṛṇena pratāritaḥ  ViP kiṃ na vetti nṛśaṃsoyamanurāgaparaṃ janam yenaivamakṣṇorāhlādaṃ nayatyanyatra no harim  ViP eṣa rāmeṇa sahitaḥ prayātyatyantanirghṛṇaḥ rathamāruhya govindastvaryatāmasya vāraṇe  ViP gurūṇāmagrato vaktuṃ viṃ bravītha na naḥ kṣamam guravaḥkiṃ kariṣyanti dagdhānāṃ virahāgninā  ViP nadaṅgopamikhā gopā gantumete samudyatāḥ nodyamaṃ kurute kaścidgovindavinivartane  ViP suprabhātādya rajanī mathurāvāsayoṣitām pāsyantyacyutavaktrābjaṃ yāsāṃ netrālipaṅktayaḥ  ViP dhanyāste pathi ye kṛṣṇamito yāntyanivāritāḥ udvahiṣyanti paśyantaḥ svadehaṃ pulakāñcitam  ViP mathurānagarīpauranayanānāṃ mahotsavaḥ govindāvayavair dṛṣṭair atīvādya bhaviṣyati  ViP ko nu svapraḥsabhāgyābhir dṛṣṭastābhir adhokṣajam vistārikāṃ tinayanā yā drakṣyantyanivāritāḥ  ViP aho gopījanasyāsya darśayitvā mahānidhim utkṛttānyatra netrāṇi vidhinā karuṇātmanā  ViP anurāgeṇa śaithilyamasmāsu vrajite harauḥ śaithilyamupayāntyāśu kareṣu valayānyapi  ViP akrūraḥ krūrahṛdayaḥ śīvraṃ prerayate hayān eva mārtāsu yoṣitsu kṛpā kasya na jāyate  ViP eṣa kṛṣṇarathasyoccaiś cakrareṇur nirīkṣyatām dūrībhūto hariryena so pi reṇurnalakṣyate  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityevamatihārdena gopījananirīkṣitaḥ tatyāja vrajabhūbhāgaṃ saha rāmeṇa keśavaḥ  ViP gacchanto javanāśvena rathena yamunātaṭam praptamadhyāhnasamaye rāmākrūrajanārdanāḥ  ViP athāha kuṣmamakrūro bhavadybhāṃ tāvadāsyatām yāvatkaromi kālindyā āhnikārhaṇamaṃbhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatathetyuktastatasnātaḥsvācāntaḥsa mahāmatiḥ dadhyau brahma paraṃ vipra graviṣṭo yamunājale  ViP phaṇāsahasramālāḍhyaṃ balabhadraṃ dadarśa saḥ kundamālāṅgamunnidrapadmapatrāyatekṣaṇam  ViP vṛtaṃ vāsukiraṃbhādyair mahadbhiḥ pavanā śibhiḥ saṃstūyamānamudgandhivanamālāvibhūṣitam  ViP dadhānamasite vastre cārurūpāvataṃsakam cārukuṇḍalinaṃ bhāntamantarjalatale sthitam  ViP tasyotsaṃge ghanaśyāmamātāmrāyatalocanam caturbāhumudārāṅgaṃ cakrādyāyudhabhūṣaṇam  ViP pīte vasānaṃ vasane citramālyopaśobhitam śakracāpataḍinmālāvicitramiva toyadam  ViP śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ cāru sphuranmakarakuṇḍalam dadarśa kṛṣṇamakliṣṭaṃ puṇḍarīkāvataṃsakam  ViP sanandanādyair munibhiḥ saddhayogair akalmaṣaiḥ saṃcintyamānaṃ tatrasthair nāsāgranyastalocanaiḥ  ViP balakṛṣṇau tathākrūraḥ pratyabhijñāya vismitaḥ acintayadrathācchīghraṃ kathamatrāgatāviti  ViP vivakṣostaṃbhayāmāsa vācaṃ tasya janārdanaḥ tato niṣkramya salilādrathamabhyāgataḥ punaḥ  ViP dadarśa tatra caivobhau rathasyopari niṣṭhitau rāmakṛṣṇau yathāpūrvaṃ manuṣyavapuṣānvitau  ViP nimagnaś ca punas toye dadarśa ca tathaiva tau saṃstūyamānau gandharvair munisiddhamahoragaiḥ  ViP tato vijñātasadbhāvaḥsa tu dānapatistadā tuṣṭāva sarva vijñānamayamacyutamīśvaram  ViP akrūra uvācasanmātrarūpiṇetintyamahimre paramātmane vyāpine naikarūpaikasvarūpāya namo namaḥ  ViP sarvarūpāya te cintyahavirbhūtāya te namaḥ namo vijñānapārāya parāya prakṛteḥ prabhoḥ  ViP bhūtātmā cendriyātmā ca pradhānātmā tathā bhavān ātmā ca paramātmā ca tvamekaḥ pañcadhā sthitaḥ  ViP prasīda sarva sarvātmna kṣarākṣaramayeśvara brahmaviṣṇuśivākhyābhiḥ kalpanābhir udīritaḥ  ViP anākhyeyasvarūpātmannanākhyeyaprayojana anākhyena bhidhānaṃ tvāṃ natosmi parameśvara  ViP na yatra nātha vidyante nāmajātyādikalpanāḥ tadbrahma paramaṃ nityamavikāri bhavānajaḥ  ViP na kalpanāmṛterthasya sarvasyādhigamo yataḥ tataḥ kṛṣṇacyutānantaviṣṇusaṃjñābhiriḍyate  ViP sarvārthastvamaja vikalpanābhir etair vādyair bhavati hi yair anantaviśvam viśvātmā tvamiti vikārahīnametatsarvasminna hi bhavatosti kiñcidanyat  ViP tvaṃ brahmā paśupatiryamā vidhātā dhātā tvaṃ tridaśapatiḥsamīraṇo gniḥ toyeśo dhanapatiṃratakastvameko bhinnārthair jagadabhipāsiśaktibhedaiḥ  ViP viśvaṃ bhavānsṛjati sūryagabhastirūpo viśveśa te guṇamayoyamataḥ prapañcaḥ rūpaṃ paraṃ saditi vācakamakṣaraṃ yajjñānātmane sadasate praṇato smi tasmai  ViP oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥsaṃkarṣaṇāya ca pradyumnāya namastubhyamaniruddhāya te namaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe ṣṭāśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaevamantarjale viṣṇumabhiṣṭūya sa yādavaḥ arcayāmāsa sarveśaṃ dhūpapuṣpair manomayaiḥ  ViP parityaktānyaviṣayo manastatra niveśya saḥ brahmabhūte ciraṃ sthitvā virarāma samādhinaḥ  ViP kṛtakṛtyamivātmānaṃ manyamāmau mahāmatiḥ ājagāma rathaṃ bhūyo nirgamya yamunāṃbhasaḥ  ViP dadarśa rāmakṛṣṇau ca yathāpurvamavasthitau vismitākṣastadākrūrastaṃ ca kṛṣṇo bhyabhāṣata  ViP śrīkṛṣṇa uvācanūnaṃ te dṛṣṭamāścaryamakrūra yamunājale vismayotphullanayano bhavānsaṃlakṣyate yataḥ  ViP akrūra uvācaantarjale yadāścaryaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ tatra mayācyuta tadatrāpi hi paśyāmi mūrtimatpurataḥ sthitam  ViP jagadetanmahāścaryarūpaṃ yasya mahātmanaḥ tenāścaryapareṇāhaṃ bhavatā kṛṣṇa saṃgataḥ  ViP tatkimetena mathurāṃ yāsyāmo madhusūdana bibhemi kaṃsāddhigjanma paripiṇḍopajīvinām  ViP ityuktvā codayāmāsa sa hayān vātaraṃhasaḥ saṃprāptaścāpi sāyāhne so krūro mathurāṃ purīm  ViP vilokya mathurāṃ kṛṣṇaṃ rāmaṃ cāha sa yādavaḥ padybhāṃ yātaṃ mahāvīrau rathenaiko viśāmyaham  ViP gantavyaṃ vasudevasya no bhavadybhāṃ tathā gṛham yuvayorhi kṛte vṛddhaḥsa kaṃsena nirasyate  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā praviveśātha so krūro mathurāṃ purīm praviṣṭau rāmakṛṣṇau ca rājamārgamupāgatau  ViP strībhir naraiś ca sānandaṃ lotanair abhivīkṣitau jagmaturlīlayā vīrau mattau bālagajāviva  ViP bhramamāṇau tato dṛṣṭvā rajakaṃ raṅgakārakam ayocetāṃ sūrūpāṇi vāsāṃsi rucirāṇi tau  ViP kaṃsasya rajakaḥ so tha prasādārūḍhavismayaḥ bahūnyākṣepavākyāni prāhoccai rāmakeśavau  ViP tatastalaprahāreṇa kṛṣṇastasya durātmanaḥ pātayāmāsa roṣeṇa rajakasya śiro bhuvi  ViP hatvādāya ca vastrāṇi pītanīlāṃbarau tataḥ kṛṣṇarāmau mudā yuktau mālākāragṛhaṃ gatau  ViP vikāsinetrayugalo mālākārotivismitaḥ etau kasya sutau yātau maitreyācintayattadā  ViP pītanīlāṃbaradharau tau dṛṣṭvātimanoharau sa tarkayāmāsa tadā bhuvaṃ devāvupāgatau  ViP vikāsimukhapadmābhyāṃ tābhyāṃ puṣpāṇi yācitaḥ bhivaṃ viṣṭabhya hastābhyāṃ pasparśa śirasā mahīm  ViP prasādaparamau nāthau mama gehamupāgatau dhanyo hamarcayiṣyāmītyāha tau mālyajīvanaḥ  ViP tataḥ prahṛṣṭavadanastayoḥ puṣpaṇi kāmataḥ cārūṇyetānyathaitāni pradadau sa pralobhayan  ViP punaḥpunaḥ praṇamyobhau mālākāro narottamau dadau puṣpāṇi cārūṇi gandhavantyamalāni ca  ViP mālākārāya kṛṣṇo pi prasannaḥ pradadau varān śrīstvāṃ matsaṃśrayā bhadra na kadācittyajiṣyati  ViP balahānirna te saumya dhanahānirathāpi vā yāvaddināni tāvacca na naśiṣyati saṃtatiḥ  ViP bhuktvā ca vipulānbhogāṃstvamante matprasādataḥ mamānusmaraṇaṃ prāpyadivyaṃ lokamavāpsyasi  ViP dharme manaś ca te bhadra sārvakālaṃ bhaviṣyati yuṣmatsaṃtatijātānāṃ dhīrghamāyurbhaviṣyati  ViP nopasargādikaṃ doṣaṃ yuṣmatsaṃtatisaṃbhavaḥ avāpsyati mahābhāgā yāvatsūryo bhaviṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaatyuktvā tadgṛhātkṛṣṇo baladevasahāyavān nirjagāma muniśreṣṭha mālākāreṇa pūjitaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśa ekonaviśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācarājamārge tataḥ kṛṣṇaḥsānulepanabhājanām dadarśa kubjāmāyāntīṃ navayovanagocarām  ViP tāmāha lalitaṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kasyedamanulepanam bhavatyā nīyate satyaṃ vadendīvaralocane  ViP sakāmeneva sā proktā sānurāgā hariṃ prati prāha sā lalitaṃ kubjā taddarśanabalātkṛtā  ViP kānta kasmānna jānāsi kaṃsena viniyojitām naikavakreti vikhyātāmanulepanakarmaṇi  ViP nānyapiṣṭaṃ hi kaṃsasya prītaye hyanulepanam bhavāmyahamatīvāsya prasādadhanabhājanam  ViP śrīkṛṣṇa uvācasugandhametadrājārhaṃ ruciraṃ rucirānane āvayorgātra sadṛśaṃ dīyatāmanulepanam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaśrutvaitadāha sā kubjā gṛhyatāmiti sādaram anulepanaṃ ca pradadau gātrayogyamathobhayoḥ  ViP bhakticchedānuliptāṅgau tatastau puruṣarṣabhau seṃdracāpau vyarājetāṃ sitakṛṣṇāvivāṃbudau  ViP tatastāṃ cubuke śaurirullāpana vidhānavit utpāṭya tolayāmāsa vdyaṅgulenāgrapāṇinā  ViP cakarṣa padybhāṃ ca tadā ṛjutvaṃ keśavo nayat tataḥsā ṛjutāṃ prāptāyoṣitamabhavadvarā  ViP vilāsalilitaṃ prāha premagarbhabharālasam vastre pragṛhya govindaṃ mama gehaṃ vrajeti vai  ViP evamuktastayā śaurī rāmasyālokya cānanam prahasya kubjāṃ tāmāha naikavakrāmaninditām  ViP āyāsye bhavatīgehamiti tāṃ prahasanhariḥ visasarja jahāsoccai rāmasyālokya cānanam  ViP bhaktibhedānuniptāṅgau nīlapītāṃbarau tu tau dhanuḥśālāṃ tato yātau citramālyopasobhitau  ViP āyāgaṃ taddhanūratnaṃ tābhyāṃ pṛṣṭais tu rakṣibhiḥ ākhyāte sahasā kṛṣṇo gṛhītvā pūrayaddhanuḥ  ViP tataḥ pūrayatā tena bhajyamānaṃ balāddhanuḥ cakāra sumahacchabdaṃ mathurā yena pūritā  ViP anuyuktau tatastau tu bhagre dhanuṣi rakṣibhiḥ rakṣisainyaṃ nihatyobhau niṣkrāntau kārmukālayāt  ViP akrūrāgamavṛttāntamupalabhya mahaddhanuḥ bhagnaṃ śrutvā ca kaṃso pi prāha cāṇūramuṣṭikau  ViP kaṃsa uvācagopāladārakau prāptau bhavadybhāṃ tu mamāgrataḥ mallayuddhena hantavyau mama prāṇaharau di tau  ViP niyuddhe tadvināśena bhavadbhyāṃ toṣito hy aham dāsyāmyabhimatānkāmānnānyathaitau mahābalau  ViP nyāyatonyāyato vāpi bhavadybhāṃ tau mamāhitau hantāvyau tadvadhādrājyaṃ sāmānyaṃ vāṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP ityādiśya sa tau mallau tataścāhūya hastipam provācoccais tvayā mallasamājadvāri kuñjaraḥ  ViP sthāpyaḥ kuvalayāpīḍastena tau gopadārakau ghātanīyau niyuddhāya raṅgadvāramupāgatau  ViP tamapyājñāpya dṛṣṭvā ca sarvānmañcānupākṛtān āsannamaraṇaḥ kaṃsaḥ sūryodayamudaikṣata  ViP tataḥ samastamañceṣu nāgaraḥsa tadā janaḥ rājamañceṣu cārūḍhāḥsaha bhṛtyair narādhipāḥ  ViP mallaprāśrikavargaś ca raṅgamadhyasamīpagaḥ kṛtaḥ kaṃsena kaṃso pi tuṅgamañce vyavasthitaḥ  ViP antaḥpurāṇāṃ mañcāś ca tathānye parikalpitāḥ anye ca vāramukhyānāmanye nāgarayoṣitām  ViP nandagopādayo gopā mañceṣv anyeṣv avasthitāḥ akrūravasudevau ca mañcaprānte vyavasthitau  ViP nāgarīyoṣitāṃ madhye devakīputragardhinī antakāle pi putrasya drakṣyāmīti mukhaṃ sthitā  ViP vādyamāneṣu turyeṣu cāṇūre cātivalgati hāhākārapare loke hyāsphoṭayati muṣṭike  ViP īṣaddhasaṃtau tau vīrau balabhadrajanārdanau gopaveṣadhārau vālau raṅgadvāramupāgatau  ViP tataḥ kuvalayāpīḍo mahāmātrapracoditaḥ abhyadhāvata vegena hantuṃ gopakumārakau  ViP hāhākāro mahāñjajñe raṅgamadhye dvijottama baladevo nujaṃ dṛṣṭvā vacanaṃ cedam abravīt  ViP hantavyo hi mahābhāga nāgo yaṃ śatrucoditaḥ  ViP ityuktaḥso grajenātha baladevena vai dvija siṃhanādaṃ tataścakre mādhavaḥ paravīrahā  ViP kareṇa karamakṛṣya tasya keśiniṣūdanaḥ bhramayāmāsa taṃ śairir airāvatasamaṃ bale  ViP īśopi sarvajagatāṃ bālalīlānusārataḥ krīḍitvā suciraṃ kṛṣṇaḥ kadirantapadāntare  ViP utpāṭya vāmadantaṃ tu dakṣiṇenaiva pāṇinā tāḍayāmāsa yantāraṃ tasyāsīcchatadhā śiraḥ  ViP dakṣiṇa dantamutpāṭya balabhadro pi tatkṣaṇāt sa roṣastena pārśvasthān gajapālānapothayat  ViP tatastūtplutya vegena rauhiṇeyo mahābalaḥ jaghāna vāmapādena mastake hastinaṃ ruṣā  ViP sa papāta hatastena balabhadreṇa līlayā sahasrākṣeṇa vajreṇa tāḍitaḥ parvato yathā  ViP hatvā kuvalayāpīḍaṃ hastyārohapracoditam madāsṛganuliptāṅgau hastidantavarāyudhau  ViP mṛgamadhye yathā siṃhau garvalīlāvalokinau praviṣṭau sumahāraṅgaṃ balabhadrajanārdanau  ViP hāhākāro mahāñjajñe mahāraṅge tvanantaram kṛṣṇo yaṃ balabhadbhoyamiti lokasya vismayaḥ  ViP so yaṃ yena hatā ghorā pūtanā bālaghātinī kṣiptaṃ tu śakaṭaṃ yena bhagnau tu yamalārjunau  ViP soyaṃ yaḥ kāliyaṃ nāgaṃ mamardāruhya vālakaḥ dhṛto govardhano yena saptarātraṃ mahāgiriḥ  ViP ariṣṭo dhenukaḥ keśī līlayaiva mahātmanā nihatā yena durvṛttā dṛśyatāmeṣa so cyutaḥ  ViP ayaṃ cāsya mahābāhurbalabhadro grato grajaḥ prayāti līlayā yoṣinmanonayananandanaḥ  ViP ayaṃ sa kathyate prājñaiḥ purāṇārthaviśāradaiḥ gopālo yādavaṃ vaṃśaṃ magnamabhyaddhariṣyati  ViP ayaṃ hi sarvalokasya viṣṇorakhilajanmanaḥ avatīrṇo mahīmaṃśo nūnaṃ bhāraharo bhuvaḥ  ViP ityevaṃ varṇite paurai rāme kṛṣṇe ca tatkṣaṇāt urastatāpa devakyāḥ snehasnutapayodharam  ViP mahotsavam ivāsādya putrānanavilokanāt yuvave vasudevo bhūdvihāyābhyāgatāṃ jarām  ViP vistāritākṣiyugalo rājāntaḥpurayoṣitām nāgārastrīsamūhaś ca draṣṭuṃ na virarāma tam  ViP sakhyaḥ paśyata kṛṣṇasya mukhamatyaruṇekṣaṇam gajayuddhakṛtāyāsasvedāṃbukaṇikacitam  ViP vikāsiśaradaṃbhojamapaśyāmajalokṣitam paribhūyaṃ sthitaṃ janma saphalaṃ kriyatāṃ dṛśaḥ  ViP śrīvatsāṃkaṃ mahaddhāma bālasyaitadvilokyatām vipakṣakṣapaṇaṃ vakṣo bhujayugyaṃ ca bhāmīni  ViP kiṃ na paśyasi dugdhendumṛṇāladhavalākṛtim balabhadramimaṃ nīlaparidhānamupagatam  ViP valgatāmuṣṭikenaiva cāṇūreṇa tathā sakhi krīḍatobalabhadrasya harerhāsyaṃ vilokyatām  ViP sakhyaḥ paśyata cāṇūraṃ niyuddhārthamayaṃ hariḥ samupaiti na saṃtyatra kiṃ vṛddhā muktakārimaḥ  ViP kva yauvanonmukhībhūtamukumāratanurhariḥ kva vajrakaṭhinābhogaśarīro yaṃ mahāsuraḥ  ViP imau sulalitair aṅgair vartete navayauvanau daiteyamallāścāṇūrapramukhāstvatidāruṇāḥ  ViP niyuddhaprāśnikānāṃ tu mahāneṣa vyatikramaḥ yadbālabalinor yuddhaṃ madhyasthaiḥ samupekṣyate  ViP śrīpāraśara uvācaitthaṃ purastrīlokasva vadataścālayanbhuvam vavalga baddhakakṣyontarjanasya bhagavānhariḥ  ViP balabhadro pi cāsphoṭya vavalgalalitaṃ tathā padepade tathā bhūmiryanna śīrṇā tadadbhutam  ViP cāṇūreṇa tataḥ kṛṣṇo yayudhe mitavikramaḥ niyuddhakuśalo daityau balabhadreṇa muṣṭikaḥ  ViP sannipātāvadhūtais tu cāṇūreṇa samaṃ hariḥ prakṣepaṇair muṣṭibhiś ca kīlavajranipātanaiḥ  ViP pādoddhūtaiḥ pramṛṣṭaiś ca tayoryuddham abhūn mahat  ViP aśastramatighoraṃ tat tayor yuddhaṃ sudāruṇam balaprāṇaviniṣpādyaṃ samājotsavasannidhau  ViP yāvadyāvacca cāṇūro yuyudhe hariṇā saha prāmahānimavāpāgryāṃ tāvattavallavāllavam  ViP kṛṣṇopi yuyudhe tena līlayaiva jaganmayaḥ khedāccālayatā kopānnijakesaraśekharam  ViP balakṣayaṃ vivṛddhiṃ ca dṛṣṭvā cāṇūrakṛṣṇayoḥ vārayāmāsa tūryāṇi kaṃsaḥ kopaparāyaṇaḥ  ViP mṛdaṅgādiṣu tūryeṣu pratiṣiddheṣu tatkṣaṇāt khe saṃgatānyavādyanta devatūryāṇyanekaśaḥ  ViP jaya govinda cāṇūraṃ jahi keśava dānavam antardhānagatā devāstamūcuratiharṣitāḥ  ViP cāṇūreṇa ciraṃ kālaṃ pīḍitvā madhusūdanaḥ utpāṭya bhramayāmāsa tadvadhāya kṛto dyamaḥ  ViP bhrāmayitvā śataguṇaṃ daityamallamamitrajit bhūbhāvātphoṭayāmāsa gagane gatajīvitam  ViP bhūmāvāsphoṭitastenacāṇūraḥ śatadhābhavat raktasrāvamahāpaṅkāṃ cakāra ca tadā bhavam  ViP baladevo pi tatkālaṃ muṣṭikena mahābalaḥ yayudhe daityamallena cāṇūreṇa yathā hariḥ  ViP so pyenaṃ muṣṭinā mūrdhni vakṣasyāhatya jānunā pātayitvā dharāpṛṣṭhe niṣpipeṣa gatāyuṣam  ViP kṛṣṇa stośalakaṃ bhūyo mallarājaṃ mahābalam vāmamuṣṭiprahāreṇa pātayāmāsa bhūtale  ViP cāṇūre nahate malle muṣṭeke vinipātite nīte kṣayaṃ tośalake sarve mallāḥ pradudruvuḥ  ViP vavalgatustato raṅge kṛṣṇasaṃkarṣaṇāvubhau samānavayaso gopānbalādākṛṣyaharṣitau  ViP kaṃso pi koparaktākṣaḥ prāhoccair vyāyatānnarān gopāvetau samājaughānniṣkrāmyetāṃ balāditaḥ  ViP nando pi gṛhyatāṃ pāpo nirgalair āyasair iha avṛddhārhaima daṇḍena vasudevo pi badhyatām  ViP valganti gopāḥ kṛṣṇena ye ceme sahitāḥ purāḥ gāvo nigṛhya tāmeṣāṃ yaccāsti vasu kiñcana  ViP evamājñāpayānaṃ tu prahasya madhusūdanaḥ utplutyāruhya taṃ mañcaṃ kaṃsaṃ jagrāha vegataḥ  ViP keśeṣvā kṛṣya vigalatkirīṭamavanītale saṃ kaṃsaṃ pātayāmāsa tasyopari papāta ca  ViP aśeṣajagadādhāraguruṇā patatopari kṛṣṇena tyājitaḥ prāṇānugrasenātmajo nṛpaḥ  ViP mṛtasya keśeṣu tadā gṛhītvā madhusūdanaḥ cakarṣa dehaṃ kaṃsasya raṅgamadhye mahābalaḥ  ViP gauravemātipatatā parighātena kṛṣyatā kṛtā kaṃsasya dehena vegeneva mahāṃbhasaḥ  ViP kaṃse gṛhīte kṛṣṇena tadbhrātābhyāgato ruṣā sunāmā bala bhadreṇa līlayaiva nipātitaḥ  ViP tato hāhākṛtaṃ sarvamāsīttadraṅgamaṇḍalam avajñayā hataṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇena mathureśvaram  ViP kṛṣṇe pi vasudevasya pādau jagrāha satvaraḥ devakyāś ca mahābāhurbaladevasahāyavān  ViP utthāpya vasudevastaṃ devakī ca janārdanam smṛtajanmoktavacanau tāve va praṇatau sthitau  ViP śrīvasudeva uvācaprasīda sīdatāṃ datto devānāṃ yo varaḥ prabho tathāvayoḥ prasādena kṛtoddhāraḥsa keśava  ViP ārādhito yadbhagavānavatīrṇo gṛhe mama durvṛttanidhanārthāya tena naḥ pāvitaṃ kulam  ViP tvamantaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvabhūtamayasthitaḥ pravartete samastātmaṃstvatto bhūtabhaviṣyati  ViP yajñais tvam ijyase cintya sarvadevamayācyuta tvameva yajño yaṣṭā ca yajvanāṃ parameśvaraḥ  ViP samudbhavaḥsamastasya jagatastvaṃ janārdana  ViP sāpahnavaṃ mama mano yadetattvayi jāyate devakyāścātmajaprītyā tadatyantaviḍaṃbanā  ViP tvaṃ kartā sarvabhūtānāmanādinidhano bhavān tvaṃ manuṣyasya kasyaiṣā jihvā putrete vakṣyati  ViP jagadetajjagannātha saṃbhūtamakhilaṃ yataḥ kayā yuktyā vinā māyāṃ so smattaḥ saṃbhaviṣyati  ViP yasminpratiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam sa koṣṭhotsaṃgaśayane mānuṣo jāya te katham  ViP sa tvaṃ prasīda paramśvara pāhi viśvamaṃśāvatārakaraṇair na mamāsi putraḥ ābrahyapādapamidaṃ jagadetadīśa tvatto vimohayasi kiṃ puruṣottamāsmān  ViP māyāvimohitadṛśā tanayo mameti kaṃsādbhāyaṃ kṛtamapāstabhayo titīvram nito si gokulamarātibhayā kulena vṛddhiṃ gato si mama nāsti mamatvamīśa  ViP karmāṇi rudramarudaśviśatakratūnāṃ sādhyāni yasya na bhavanti nirīkṣitāni tvaṃ viṣṇurīśa jagatāmupakārahetoḥ prāptosi naḥ parigato vigato hi mohaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe viṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācatau samutpannavijñānau bhagavatkarmadarśanāt devakī vasudevau kudṛṣṭvā māyāṃ punarhariḥ mohāya yaducakrasya vitatāna sa vaiṣṇavīm  ViP uvāca cāṃba he tāta cirādutkaṇṭhitena me bhavantau kaṃsabhītena dṛṣṭau saṃkarṣaṇena ca  ViP kurvatāṃ yāti yaḥ kālo mātāpitrorapūjanam tatkhaṇḍamāyuṣo vyarthamasādhūnāṃ hi jāyate  ViP gurudevadvijātīnāṃ mātāpitroś ca pūjanam kurvatāṃ saphalaḥ kālo dehināṃ tāta jāyate  ViP tatkṣantavyamidaṃ sarvamatikramakṛtaṃ pitaḥ kaṃsavīryapratāpābhyāmāvayoḥ paravaśyayoḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvātha praṇamyobhau yaduvṛddhānanukramāt yathāvadabhipūjyātha cakratuḥ pauramānanam  ViP kaṃsapatnyastataḥ kaṃsaṃ parivārya hataṃ bhuvi vilepurmātaraścāsya duḥkhaśokapariplutāḥ  ViP bahuprakāramasvasthāḥ paścāttāpāturo hariḥ tāḥsamāśvāsayāmāsa svayamasrāvilekṣamaḥ  ViP ugrasenaṃ tato bandhāmumoca madhusūdanaḥ abhyasiṃcattadaivainaṃ nijarājye hatātmajam  ViP rājyobhiṣiktaḥ kṛṣṇena yadusiṃhaḥsutasya saḥ cakāra pretakāryāṇi ye cānye tatra ghātitāḥ  ViP kṛtaurdhadaihikaṃ cainaṃ siṃhāsanagataṃ hariḥ uvācājñāpaya vibho yatkāryamaviśaṅkitaḥ  ViP yayātiśāpādvaṃśoyamarājyārhepi sāṃpratam mayi bhṛtye sthite devanājñāpayatu kiṃ nṛpaiḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā so smaradvāyumājagāma ca tatkṣaṇāt uvāca cainaṃ bhagavānkeśavaḥ kāryamānuṣaḥ  ViP gacchedaṃ brūhi vāyo tvamalaṃ garvoṇa vāsava dīyatāmugrasenāya sudharmā bhavatā sabhā  ViP kṛṣṇo bravīti rājārhametadratnamanuttamam sūdharmākhyasabhāyuktamasyāṃ yadubhir āsitum  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktaḥ pavano gatvā sarvamāha śacīpatim dadau so pi sudharmākhyāṃ sabhāṃ vāyoḥ purandaraḥ  ViP vāyunā cāhṛtāṃ divyāṃ sabhāṃ te yadupuṅgavāḥ bubhujuḥsarvaratnāḍhyāṃ govindabhujasaṃśrayāḥ  ViP viditākhilavijñānau sarvajñānamayāvapi śiṣyācāryakramaṃ vīrau khyāpayantau sadūttamau  ViP tataḥsāṃdīpaniṃ kāśyamavantīpuravāsinam vidyārthaṃ jagmaturbālau kṛtopanayanakramau  ViP vedābhyāsakṛtaprīti saṃkarṣaṇajanārdanau tasya śiṣyatvamabhyetya guruvṛttipurau hi tau darśayāñcakratur vīrā vācāramakhile jane  ViP sarahasyaṃ dhanurvedaṃ sasaṃgrahamadhīyatām ahorātracatuḥṣaṣṭyā tadadbhutamabhūddvūja  ViP sāṃdīpanirasaṃbhāvyaṃ tayoḥ karmātimānuṣam vicintya tau tadā mene prāptau candradivākarau  ViP sāṃgāṃś ca caturo vedānsarvaśāstrāṇi caiva hi astragrāmamaśeṣaṃ ca proktamātramavāpya tau  ViP ūcuturvriyatāṃ yā te dātavyā gurudakṣimā  ViP so py atīndriyamālokya tayoḥ karma mahāmati ayācata sṛtaṃ putraṃ prabhāse lavaṇārṇave  ViP gṛhītāstrau tatastau tu sārghyahasto mahodadhiḥ uvāca na mayā putro hṛtaḥsāṃdīpaneriti  ViP daityaḥ pañcajano nāma śaṅkharūpaḥ sa bālakam jagrāha yosti salile mamaivā surasūdana  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvontarjalaṃ gatvā hatvā pañcajanaṃ ca tam kaṣṇo jagrāha tasyāsthiprabhavaṃ śaṅkhamuttamam  ViP yasya nādena daityānāṃ balahānirajāyata devānāṃ vavṛdhe tejo yātyadharmaś ca saṃkṣayam  ViP taṃ pāñcajanyamāpūrya gatvā yamapuraṃ hariḥ baladevaś ca balavāñjitvā vaivasvataṃ yamam  ViP taṃ bālaṃ yātanāsaṃstha yathāpūrvaśarīriṇam pitre pradattavānkṛṣṇo balaś ca balināṃ varaḥ  ViP mathurāṃ ca punaḥ prāptābugrasenena pālitām prahṛṣṭapuruṣastrīkāmubhau rāmajanārdanau  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśa evaviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācajarāsaṃdhamute kasa upayeme mahābalaḥ astiṃ prāptiṃ ca maitreya cayorbhartṛhaṇaṃ harim  ViP mahā balaparīvāro magadhādhipatirbalī hantumabhyāyayau kopājjarāsaṃdhaḥsayādavam  ViP upetya mathurāṃ so tha rurodha magadheśvaraḥ akṣauhiṇībhiḥ sainyasya trayoviṃśatibhir vṛtaḥ  ViP niṣkramyālpaparīvārāvubhau rāmajanārdanau yuyudhāte samaṃ tasya balinau balisainikaiḥ  ViP tato rāmaś ca kṛṣṇaś ca matiṃ cakraturañjasā āyudhānāṃ purāṇānāmādāne munisattama  ViP anantaraṃ hareḥ śārṅgaṃ tūṇī cākṣayasāyakau ākāśādāgatau vipra tathā kaumodakī gadā  ViP halaṃ ca balabhadrasya gaganādāgataṃ mahat manaso bhimataṃ vipra sānandaṃ musalaṃ tathā  ViP tato yuddhe parājitya sasainyaṃ sagadhādhipam purīṃ viviśaturvīrāvubhau rāmajanārdanau  ViP jite tasminsudurvṛtte jarāsaṃdhe mahā mune jīvamāne gate kṛṣṇastenāmanyata nājitam  ViP punarapyājagāmātha jarāsaṃdho balānvitaḥ jitaś ca rāmakṛṣṇābhyāmapakrānto dvijottama  ViP daśa cāṣṭau ca saṃgramānevamatyantadurmadaḥ yadubhir māgadho rājā cakre kṛṣṇapurogamaiḥ  ViP sarveṣveteṣu yuddheṣu yādavaiḥ sa parājitaḥ apakrāñco jarāsaṃdhaḥsvalpasainyair balādhikaḥ  ViP na tadbalaṃ yādavānāṃ vijitaṃ yadanekaśaḥ tat tu saṃnidhimāhātmyaṃ viṣṇor aṃśasya cakriṇaḥ  ViP manuṣyadharmaśīlasya līlā sā jagatīpateḥ astrāṇyanekarūpāṇi yadarātiṣu muñcati  ViP manasaiva jagatsṛṣṭiṃ saṃhāraṃ ca karoti yaḥ tasyāpipakṣakṣapaṇe kiyānudyamavistaraḥ  ViP tathāpi yo manuṣyāṇāṃ dharmastamanuvartate kurvanbalavatā saṃdhiṃ hīnair yuddhaṃ karotyasau  ViP sāma copapradānaṃ ca tathā bhedaṃ ca darśayan karoti daṇḍapātaṃ ca kvacideva palāyanam  ViP manuṣyadehināṃ ceṣṭāmityevamanuvartate līlā jagatpatestasya cchandataḥ parivartate  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāśe dvāviṃśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācagārgyaṃ goṣṭhyāṃ dvijaṃ śyālaḥṣaṇḍa ityuktavāndvija yadūnāṃ sannidhau sarve jahasuryādavāstadā  ViP tataḥ kopaparītātmā dakṣiṇāpathametya saḥ sutamicchaṃstapastepe yaducakrabhayāvaham  ViP ārādhayanmahādevaṃ lohacūrṇamabhakṣayat dadau varaṃ ca tuṣṭo smai varṣe tu dvādaśe haraḥ  ViP saṃtoṣayāmāsa ca taṃ yavaneśo hyanātmajaḥ tadyoṣitsaṃgamāccāsya putro bhūdalisannibhaḥ  ViP taṃ kālayavanaṃ nāma rāye sve yavaneśvaraḥ abhiṣicya vanaṃ yāto vajragrakaṭhinorasam  ViP sa tu vīryamadonmattaḥ pṛthivyāṃ balino nṛpān apṛcchannāradastasmai kathayāmāsa yādavān  ViP mlecchakoṭisahasrāṇāṃ sahasraiḥ so bhisaṃvṛtaḥ gajāśvarathasaṃpannaiś cakāra paramodyamam  ViP prayayau sa vyavacchinnaṃ chinnayāno dinedine yādavānprati sāmarṣo maitreya mathurāṃ purīm  ViP kṛṣṇo pi cintayāmāsa kṣapitaṃ yādavaṃ balam yavanena raṇe gamyaṃ māgadhasya bhaviṣyati  ViP māgadhasya balaṃ kṣīṇaṃ sa kālayavano balī hantaitadevamāyātaṃ yadūnāṃ vyasanaṃ dvidhā  ViP tasmāddurgaṃ kariṣyāmi yadūnāmaridurjayam striyo pi yatra yuddheyuḥ kiṃ punarvṛṣṇipuṅgavāḥ  ViP mayi matte pramatte vā supte pravasite pi vā yādavābhibhavaṃ duṣṭā mā kurvaṃstvarayodhikāḥ  ViP iti saṃcintya govindo yojanānāṃ mahodadhim yayāce dvādaśapurīṃ dvārakāṃ tatra nirmame  ViP mahodyānāṃ mahāvaprāṃ taṭākaśataśobhitām prāsādagṛhasaṃbādhāmindrasyevāmarāvatīm  ViP mathurāvāsinaṃ lokaṃ tatrānīya janārdanaḥ āsanne kālayavane mathurāṃ ca svayaṃ yayau  ViP bahirāvāsite sainye mathurāyā nirāyudhaḥ nirjagāma ca govindo dadarśa yavanaś ca tam  ViP sa jñātvā vāsudevaṃ taṃ bāhupraharaṇaṃ nṛpaḥ anuyāto mahāyogī cetobhiḥ prāpyate na yaḥ  ViP tenānuyātaḥ kṛṣṇo pi praviveśa mahāguhām yatra śete mahāvīryo mucukundo nareśvaraḥ  ViP so pi praviṣṭo yavano dṛṣṭvā śayyāgataṃ nṛpam pādena tāḍayāmāsa matvā kṛṣṇaṃ sudurmatiḥ  ViP utthāya mucukundo pi dadarśa yavanaṃ nṛpaḥ  ViP dṛṣṭamātraś ca tenāsau jajvāla yavanogninā tatkrodhajena maitreya bhasmībhūtaś ca tatkṣaṇāt  ViP sa hi devāsure yuddhe gato hatvā mahāsurān nidrārtaḥsumahākālaṃ nidrāṃ vavre varaṃ surān  ViP proktaś ca devaiḥ saṃsuptaṃ yastvāmutthāpayiṣyati dehajenāgninā sadyaḥsa tu bhasmībhaviṣyati  ViP evaṃ dagdhvā sa taṃ pāpaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca madhusūdanam kastvamityāha so pyāha jātohaṃ śaśinaḥ kule vasudevasya tanayo yadorvaṃśasamudbavaḥ  ViP mucukundo pi tatrāsau vṛddhagargyāvaco smarat  ViP saṃsmṛtya praṇipatyainaṃ sarvaṃ sarveśvaraṃ harim prāha jñāto bhavān viṣṇor aṃśastvaṃ parameśvara  ViP purā gārgyeṇa kathitamaṣṭāviṃśatime yuge dvāparānte harerjanma yaduvaṃśe bhaviṣyati  ViP sa tvaṃ prāpto na saṃdeho martyānāmupakārakṛt  ViP tathāhi sumahattejo nālaṃ soḍhumahaṃ tava tathāhi sajalāṃbhodanādadhīrataraṃ tava vākyaṃ namati caivorvī yuṣmatpādaprapīḍitā  ViP devāsuramahāyuddhe daityasainyamahābhaṭāḥ na sehurmama te jaste tvattejo na sahāmyaham  ViP saṃsārapatitasyaiko jantostvaṃ śaraṇaṃ param prasīda tvaṃ prapannārtihara nāśaya me śubham  ViP tvaṃ payo nidhayaḥ śailasaritastvaṃ vanāni ca medinī gaganaṃ vāyurāpognistvaṃ tathā manaḥ  ViP buddhiravyākṛtaprāṇāḥ prāṇeśastvaṃ tathā pumān puṃsaḥ parataraṃ yacca vyāpya janma vikāravat  ViP śabdādihīnamajaramameyaṃ kṣayavarjitam avṛddhināśaṃ tadbrahma tvamādyantavivarjitam  ViP tvatto marāḥsapitaro yakṣagandharvakinnarāḥ siddhāścāpsarasastvatto manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ khagāḥ  ViP sarīsṛpā mṛgāḥsarve tvattaḥsarve mahīruhāḥ yacca bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca kiñcidatra carācaram  ViP mūrtāmūrtaṃ tathā cāpi sthūlaṃ sūkṣmataraṃ tathā tatsarvaṃ tvaṃ jagatkartā nāsti kiñcittvā yā vinā  ViP mayā saṃsāracakre sminbhramatā bhagavaṃstadā tāpatrayābhibhūtena na prāptā nirvṛtiḥ kvicit  ViP duḥkhānyeva sukhānīti mṛgatṛṣṇājalāśayāḥ mayā nātha gṛhītāni tāni tāpāya me bhavan  ViP rājyamurvī balaṃ kośo mitrapakṣastathātmajāḥ bhāryā bhṛtya jano ye ca śabdādya viṣayāḥ prabho  ViP sukhabuddhyā mayā sarvaṃ gṛhītamidamavyayam pariṇāme tadeveśa tāpātmakamabhūnmama  ViP devalokagatiṃ prāpto nātha devagaṇo pi hi mattaḥsāhāyyakāmobhūcchāśvatī kutra nirvṛtiḥ  ViP tvāmanārādhya jagatāṃ sarveṣāṃ prabhavāspadam śāśvatī prāpyate kena parameśvara nirvṛtiḥ  ViP tvanmāyāmūḍhamanaso janmamṛtyujarādikān avāpya tāpānpaśyanti pretarājamanantaram  ViP tato nijakriyāsūtinarakeṣvatidāruṇam prāpnuvanti narā duḥkhamasvarūpavidastava  ViP ahamatyantaviṣayī mohitastava māyayā mamatvagarvagartāntarbhramāmi parameśvara  ViP so haṃ tvāṃ śaraṇamapāramaprameyaṃ saṃprāptaḥ paramapadaṃ yato na kiñcit saṃsārabhramaparitāpataptacetānirvāṇe pariṇatadhāmni sābhilāṣaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇeca pañcamāṃśe trayoviṃśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaitthaṃstutastadā tena mucukundena dhīmatā prāheśaḥ sarvabhūtānāmanādinidhano hariḥ  ViP śrībhagavānuvācayathābhivāñchitāndivyāngacchalokānnarādhipa avyāhataparaiśvaryo matprasādopabṛṃhitaḥ  ViP bhuktvā divyanmahā bhogānbhaviṣyasi mahākule jātismaro matprasādāttatomokṣamavāpsyasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktaḥ praṇipatyeśaṃ jagatāmacyutaṃ nṛpaḥ guhāmukhādviniṣkrāntataḥsa dadarśālpakānnarān  ViP tataḥ kaliyugaṃ matvā prāptaṃ taptuṃ nṛpastapaḥ naranārāyaṇasthānaṃ prayayau gandhamādanam  ViP kṛṣṇopi ghātayitvārimupāyena hi tadvalam jagrāha mathurāmetya hastyaśvasyandanojjvalam  ViP ānīya cograsenāya dvāravatvāṃ nyavedayat parābhibhavaniḥ śaṅkaṃ babhūva ca yadoḥ kulam  ViP baladevo pi maitreya praśāntākhilavigrahaḥ jñātidarśanasotkaṇṭhaḥ prayayau nandagokulam  ViP tato gopāś ca gopyaś ca yathā pūrvam amitrajit tathaivābhyavadatpramṇā bahumānapuraḥsaram  ViP sa kaiścit saṃpariṣvaktaḥ kāṃścicca pariṣasvaje hāsyaṃ cakre samaṃ kaiścid gopair gopījanais tathā  ViP priyāṇyanekānyavadan gopāstatra halāyudham gopyaś ca premakupitāḥ procuḥserṣyamathāparāḥ  ViP gopyaḥ papracchuraparā nāgarījanavallabham kaccidāste sukhaṃ kṛṣṇaścalapremalavātmakaḥ  ViP asmacceṣṭāmapahasanna kaccitpurayoṣitām saubhāgyamāna madhikaṃ karoti kṣaṇasauhṛdaḥ  ViP kaccitsmarati naḥ kṛṣṇo gītānugamanaṃ kalam apyasau mātaraṃ draṣṭu sakṛdapyāgamiṣyati  ViP atha vā kiṃ tadālāpaiḥ kriyantāmaparāḥ kathāḥ yasyāsmabhir vinā tena vināsmākaṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP pitā mātā tathā bhrātā bhartā bandhujanaś ca kim saṃtyaktastatkṛtesmābhir akṛtajñadhvajo hi saḥ  ViP tathāpi kaccidālāpamihāgamanasaṃśrayam karoti kṛṣṇo vaktavyaṃ bhavatā rāma nānṛtam  ViP dāmodaro sau govindaḥ purastrīsaktamānasaḥ apetaprītirasmāsu durdarśaḥ pratibhāti naḥ  ViP āmantritaś ca kṛṣṇeti punardāmodareti ca jahasuḥsasvaraṃ gopyo hariṇā hṛtacetasaḥ  ViP saṃdeśaiḥ sāmamadhuraiḥ premagarbhair agarvitaiḥ rāmeṇāśvāsitā gopyaḥ kṛṣṇasyātimanoharaiḥ  ViP gopaiś ca pūrvavadrāmaḥ parihāsamanoharāḥ kathāścakāra reme ca saha tair vrajabhūmiṣu  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe caturviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācavane vicaratas tasya saha gopair mahātmanaḥ mānuṣacchadmarūpasya śeṣasya dharaṇīdhṛtaḥ  ViP niṣpādito rukāryasya kāryoṇorvīpracāriṇaḥ upabhogārthamatyarthaṃ varuṇaḥ prāha vāruṇīm  ViP abhīṣṭā sarvadā yasya madire tvaṃ mahaujasaḥ anantasyopabhogāya tasya gaccha mude śubhe  ViP ityuktā vāruṇī tena sannidhānamathākaret vṛndāvanasamutpannakadaṃ batarukoṭare  ViP vicaran baladevo pi madirāgandhamuttamam āghrāya madirātarṣamavāpātha varānanaḥ  ViP tataḥ kadaṃbātsahasāmadyadhārāṃ sa lāṅgalī patantīṃ vīkṣya maitreya prayayau paramāṃ mudam  ViP papau ca gopagopībhiḥ samupeto mudānvitaḥ pragīyamāno lalītaṃ gītavādyaviśāradaiḥ  ViP sa mattotyantagharmāṃbhaḥkaṇikāmauktikojjvalaḥ āgaccha yamune snātumicchāmītyāha vihvalaḥ  ViP tasya vācaṃ nadī sā tu mattoktāmavamatya vai nājagāma tataḥ ktruddho halaṃ jagrāha lāṅgalī  ViP gṛhītvā tāṃ halāntena cakarṣa madavihvalaḥ pāpe nāyāsi nāyāsi gamyatāmicchayānyataḥ  ViP sākṛṣṭā sahasā tena mārgaṃ saṃtyajya nimragā yatrāste balabhadro sau plāvayāmāsa tadvanam  ViP śorīriṇī tadābhyetya trāsavihvalalocanā prasīdetyabravīdrāmaṃ muñca māṃ musalāyudha  ViP tatastasyāḥ suvacanamākarṇya sa halā yudhaḥ so bravīdavajānāsi mama śauryabale nadi so haṃ tvāṃ halapātena nayiṣyāmi sahasradhā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktayāti saṃtrāsāttayā nadya prasāditaḥ bhūbhāge plāvite tasminmumoca yamunāṃ balaḥ  ViP tataḥ snātasya vai kāntir ajāyata mahātmanaḥ  ViP avataṃsotpalaṃ cāru gṛhītvaikaṃ ca kuṇḍalam varuṇaprahitāṃ cāsmai mālāmamlānapaṅkajām samudrābhe tathā vastre nīle lakṣmīrayacchata  ViP kṛtāvataṃsaḥ sa tadā cārukuṃḍalabhūṣitaḥ nīlāṃbaradharaḥsragvī śuśubhe kāntisaṃyutaḥ  ViP itthaṃ vibhūṣito reme tatra rāmas tathā vraje māsadvayena yātaś ca sa punardvārakāṃ purīm  ViP revatīṃ nāma tanayāṃ raivatasya mahīpateḥ upayeme balastasyāṃ jajñāte niśitolmukau  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe pañcaviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācabhīṣmakaḥ kuṇḍine rājā vidarbhaviṣaye bhavat rukmītasyabhavatputro rukmiṇī ca varānanā  ViP rukmiṇīṃ cakame kṛṣṇaḥsā ca taṃ cāruhīsini na dadau yācate caināṃ rukmī dveṣeṇa cakriṇe  ViP dadau ca śiśupālāya jarāsandhapracoditaḥ bhīṣmako rukmiṇā sārdha rukmiṇīmuruvikramaḥ  ViP vivāhāryaṃ tataḥ sarve jarāsaṃdhamukhā nṛpāḥ bhīṣmakasya puraṃ jagmuḥ śiśupālapriyaiṣiṇaḥ  ViP kṛṣṇo pi balabhadrādyair yadubhiḥ parivāritaḥ prayayau kuṇḍinaṃ draṣṭuṃ vivāhaṃ caidyabhūbhṛtaḥ  ViP śvo bhāvini vivāhe tu tāṃ kanyāṃ hṛtavānhariḥ vipakṣabhāram āsajya rāmādiṣv atha bandhuṣu  ViP tataś ca paiṇḍrakaśrśrīmāndantavakro vidūrathaḥ śiśupālajarāsaṃdhaśālvādyāś ca mahībhṛtaḥ  ViP kupitāste hariṃ hantuṃ cakrurudyogamuttamam nirjitāś ca samāgamya rāmādyoryadupuṅgavaiḥ  ViP kuṇḍinaṃ na pravekṣyāmi hyahatvā yudhi keśavam kṛtvā pratijñāṃ rukmī ca hantuṃ kṛṣṇamanudrutaḥ  ViP hatvā balaṃ sanāgāśvaṃ pattisyandanasaṃkulam nirjitaḥ pātitaścorvyāṃ līlayaiva sa cakriṇā  ViP nirjitya rukmiṇaṃ samyagupayeme ca rukmiṇīm rākṣasena vivāhena saṃprāptāṃ madhusudanaḥ  ViP tasyāṃ jajñe ca pradyumno madanāṃśaḥsavīryavān jahāra śaṃbaro yaṃ vai yo jaghāna ca śaṃbaram  ViP iti śriviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe ṣaḍviśodhyāyaḥ śrīmaitreya uvācasaṃbareṇahṛto vīraḥ pradyumnaḥ sa kathaṃ mune śaṃbaraḥ sa mahāvīryaḥ pradyumnena kathaṃ hataḥ  ViP yastenāpahṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ sa kathaṃ vijaghāna tam etadvistarataḥ śrotumicchāmi saralaṃ guro  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaṣaṣṭhehni jātamātraṃ tu pradyumnaṃ sūtikāgṛhāt mamaiṣa hanteti mune hṛtavānkālaśaṃbaraḥ  ViP hṛtvā cikṣepa caivainaṃ grāhogre lavaṇārṇave kallolajanitāvarte sughore makārālaye  ViP pātitaṃ tatra caivaiko matsyo jagrāha bālakam na mamāra ca tasyāpi jaṭharāgnipradīpitaḥ  ViP matsyabandhaiś ca matsyo sau matsyair anyaiḥ saha dvaja ghātito sūravaryāya śaṃbarāya niveditaḥ  ViP tasya māyā vatī nāma patnī sarvagṛheśvarī kārayāmāsa sūdānāmādhipatyamaninditā  ViP dārite matsyajaṭhare sā dadarśātiśobhanam kumāraṃ manmathatarordagdhasya prathamāṅkuram  ViP ko yaṃ kathamayaṃ matsyajaṭhare praviveśitaḥ ityevaṃ kaunupāviṣṭāṃ nanvīṃ prāhātha nāradaḥ  ViP ayaṃ samastajagataḥ sthitisaṃhārakāriṇaḥ śaṃbareṇa hṛto viṣṇostanayaḥ sūtikāgṛhāt  ViP kṣiptaḥsamudre matsyena nigīrṇaste gṛhaṃ gataḥ nararatnamidaṃ subhru visrabdhā paripālaya  ViP śrīparāśara uvācanāradenaivam uktā sā pālayāmāsa taṃ śiśum bālyādevātirāgeṇarūpātiśayamohitā  ViP sa yadā yauvanābhogabhūṣito bhūnmahāmate sābhilāṣā tadā sāpi babhūva gajagāmini  ViP māyāvatī dadau tasmai māyāḥ sarvā mahāmune pradyumnāyānurāgāndhā tatryastahṛdayekṣaṇā  ViP prasājjantīṃ tu tāṃ prāha sa kārṣṇiḥ kamalebhaṇām mātṛtvamapahāyādya kimevaṃ vartase nyathā  ViP sā tasmai kathayāmāsana putrastvaṃ mameti vai tanayaṃ tvāmayaṃ viṣṇorhṛtavānkālaśaṃbaraḥ  ViP kṣiptaḥ samudre matsyasya saṃprāpto jaṭharānmayā sā hi roditite mātā kāntādyāpyativatsalā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktaḥ śaṃbaraṃ yuddhe pradyumnaḥ sa samāhvayat krodhākulīkṛtamanā yuyudhe ca mahā balaḥ  ViP hatvā sainyamaśeṣaṃ tu tasya daityasya yādavaḥ saptamāyā vyatikramya māyāṃ prayuyuje ṣṭamīm  ViP tayā jaghāna taṃ daityaṃ māyayā kālaśaṃbaram utpattya ca tayā sārdhamājagāma pituḥ puram  ViP antaḥpure nipatitaṃ māyāvatyā samanvitam taṃ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇa saṃkalpā babhūvuḥ kṛṣṇayoṣitaḥ  ViP rukmiṇī sābhavatpremṇā sāsradṛṣṭiraninditā dhanyāyā khalv ayaṃ putro vartate navayauvane  ViP asminvayasi putro me pradyumno yadi jīvati sabhāgyā jananī vatsa sā tvāyā kā vibhīṣitā  ViP atha vā yādṛsaḥ sneho mama yādṛgvapustava harerapatyaṃ suvyaktaṃ bhavānvatsa bhaviṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaetasminnantare prāptaḥsaha kṛṣṇena nāradaḥ antaḥpuracarāṃ devīṃ rukmiṇīṃ prāha harṣayan  ViP eṣa te tanayaḥ subhru hatvā śaṃbaramāgataḥ hṛto yenābhavadbālo bhavatyāḥsūtikāgṛhāt  ViP iyaṃ māyāvatī bhāryā tanayasyāsya te satī śaṃbarasya na bhāryeyaṃ śrūyatāmatra kāraṇam  ViP manmathe tu gate nāśaṃ tadudbhavaparayaṇā śaṃbaraṃ mohayāmāsa māyārūpeṇa rūpiṇī  ViP vihārādyupabhogeṣu rūpaṃ māyāmayaṃ śubham darśayāmāsa daityasya tasyeyaṃ madirekṣaṇā  ViP kāmo vatīrṇaḥ putraste tasyeyaṃ dayitā ratiḥ viśaṅkā nātra kartavyā snuṣeyaṃ tava śobhane  ViP tato harṣasamāviṣṭau rukmiṇī keśavautadā nagarī ca samastā sā sādhusādhvityabhāṣata  ViP ciraṃ naṣṭena putreṇa saṃgatāṃ prekṣya rukmiṇīm avāpa vismayaṃ sarvo dvāravatyāṃ tadā janaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcasāṃśe spataviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācacārudeṣṇaṃ sudeṣṇaṃ ca cārudehaṃ ca vīryavān suṣeṇaṃ cāruguptaṃ ca bhadracāruṃ tathā param  ViP cāruvindaṃ sucāruṃ ca cāruṃ cabalināṃ varam rukmiṇyajanayatputrānkanyāṃ cārumatīṃ tathā  ViP anyāś ca bhāryāḥ kṛṣṇasya babhūvuḥ sapta śobhanāḥ kālidī mitravindā ca satyā cāgnajitī tathā  ViP devī jāmbavatī cāpi rohiṇī kāmarūpiṇī madrarājasutā cānyā suśīlā śīlamaṇḍanā  ViP satrājitī satyabhāmā lakṣmaṇā cāruhāsinī ṣoḍaśāsan sahasrāṇi strīṇāmanyāni cakriṇaḥ  ViP pradyumnapi mahāvīryo rukmiṇastanayāṃ śubhām svayaṃbare tāṃ jagrāha sā ca taṃ tanayaṃ hareḥ  ViP tasyāmasyābhaktaputro mahābalaparākramaḥ aniruddho raṇe ruddhavīryodadhirarindamaḥ  ViP tasyāpi rukmiṇaḥ pautrīṃ varayāmāsa keśavaḥ dauhitrāya dadau rakmī tāṃ spardhannapi cakriṇā  ViP tasyā vivāhe rāmādyā yādavā hariṇā saha kalyāṇārthaṃ tataḥsarve ye cānye bhūbhṛtas tathā rukmiṇī nagaraṃ jagmurnāmnā bhojakaṭaṃ dvija  ViP vivāhe tatra nirvṛtte pradyumnasya mahātmanaḥ kaliṅgarājapramukhā rukmiṇaṃ vākyamabruvan  ViP anakṣajño halī dyute tathāsya vyasanaṃ mahat tajjayāmo balaṃ kasmāddyutenainaṃ mahābalam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatatheti tānāha nṛpānrukmī balamadānvitaḥ sabhāyāṃ saha rāmeṇa cakre dyūtaṃ ca vai tadā  ViP sahasramekaṃ niṣkāṇāṃ rukmiṇā vijito balaḥ dvitīye pipaṇe cānyatsahasraṃ rukmiṇā jitaḥ  ViP tato daśasahasrāṇi niṣkāṇāṃ paṇamādade balabhadro jayattāni rukmī dyutavidāṃ varaḥ  ViP tato jahāsa svanavatkaliṅgādhipatirdhija dantān vidarśayan mūḍho rukmī cāha madoddhataḥ  ViP avidyo yaṃ mayā dyūte balabhadraḥ parājitaḥ bhudhaivākṣāvalepāndho yo vamene kṣakovidān  ViP dṛṣṭvā kaliṅgarājānaṃ prakāśadaśanānanam rikmiṇaṃ cāpi durvākyaṃ kopaṃ cakre halāyudhaḥ  ViP tataḥ kopaparītātmā niṣkakoṭiṃ samādade glahaṃ jagrāha rukmī ca tadarthekṣānapātayat  ViP ajayadbaladevastaṃ prāhoccair vijitaṃ mayā mayeti rukmī prāhoccair alīkokter alaṃ bala  ViP tvayokto yaṃ glahaḥsatyaṃ na mayaiṣonumoditaḥ evaṃ tvayā cedvijitaṃ vijitaṃ na mayā katham  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaathāntarikṣe vāgucceḥ prāha gaṃbhīranādinī baladevasya taṃ kopaṃ vardhayantī mahātmanaḥ  ViP jitaṃ balena dharmeṇa rukmiṇā bhāṣitaṃ mṛṣā anuktvāpi vacaḥ kiñcit kṛta bhavati karmaṇā  ViP tato balaḥ samutthāya kopasaṃrakkalocanaḥ jaghānāṣṭapadenaiva rikmiṇaṃ sa mahābalaḥ  ViP kaliṅgarājaṃ cādāya visphurantaṃ balādbalaḥ babhañja dantānkupito yaiḥ prakāśair jahāsa saḥ  ViP ākṛṣya ca mahāstaṃbhaṃ jātarūpamayaṃ balaḥ jaghāna tānye tatpakṣe bhūbhṛtaḥ kupito bhṛśam  ViP tato hāhākṛtaṃ sarvaṃ palāyana paraṃ dvija tadrājamaṇḍalaṃ bhītaṃ babhūva kupite bale  ViP balena nihataṃ dṛṣṭvā rukmiṇaṃ madhusūdanaḥ novāca kiñcinmaitreya rukmiṇī balayorbhayāt  ViP tatoniruddhamādāya kṛtadāraṃ dvijottama dvārakāmājagāmātha yaducakraṃ ca keśavaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe ṣṭāviṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācadvāravatyāṃ sthite kṛṣṇe śakrastribhuvaneśvaraḥ ājagāmātha maitreya mattairāvatapṛṣṭhagaḥ  ViP praviśya dvārakāṃ so tha sametya hariṇā tataḥ kathayāmāsa daityasya narakasya vicoṣṭitam  ViP tvayānāthena devānāṃ manaṣyatvepi tiṣṭhatā praśamaṃ sarvaduḥkhāni nītāni madhusūdana  ViP tapasvivyamanārthāya soriṣṭo dhenukas tathā pravṛtto yas tathā keśīte sarve nihatāstvayā  ViP kaṃsaḥ kuvalayāpīḍaḥ pūtanā bālaghātinī nāśaṃ nītāstvayā sarve ye nye jagadupadravāḥ  ViP yuṣmaddordaḍasaṃbhūtiparitrāte jagattraye yajvayajñāṃśasaṃprāptyā tṛptiṃ yānti divaukasaḥ  ViP so haṃ sāṃpratamāyāto yannimittaṃ janārdana tacchutvā tatpratīkāraprayatnaṃ kartumarhasi  ViP bhaumo yaṃ narako nāma prāgjyotiṣapureśvaraḥ karoti sarvabhūtānām upaghātam arindama  ViP devasiddasurādīnāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca najārdana hṛtvā tu so suraḥ kanyā rurudhe nijamandire  ViP chatraṃ yatsalilasrāvi tajjahāra pracetasaḥ madaṃrasya tathā śṛṅgaṃ hṛtavānmaṇiparvatam  ViP amṛtastrāviṇī divye manmātuḥ kṛṣṇakuñjale jahāra so suro dityā vāñchatyairāvataṃ gajam  ViP durnītametadgovindamayā tasya niveditam yadatra
