cakradhārāgninirdagdhāṃścakāra śalabhāniva  ViP hatvāsuraṃ hayagrīvaṃ tathā pañcajanaṃ dvija prāgjyotiṣapuraṃ dhīmāṃstvārāvānsamupādravat  ViP narakeṇāsya tatrābhūnmahāsainyena saṃyugam kṛṣṇasya yatra gṛhāma kuṇḍale ceme pālayāsya ca saṃtatim  ViP bhārāvataraṇārthāya mamaiva bhagavānimam aṃśena lokamāyātaḥ prasādasumukhaḥ prabho  ViP tvaṃ kartā ca vikartā ca saṃhartā prabhavo pyayaḥ jagatāntvaṃ ratnāni narakāvāsājjagrāha munisattama  ViP kanyāpure sa kanyānāṃ ṣoḍaḥśātulavikramaḥ śatādhikāni dadṛśe sahasrāṇi mahāmune  ViP caturdaṃṣṭrāngajāṃścāgryān ṣaṭsahasrāṃś ca dṛṣṭavān kāṃbhojānāṃ yuddamabhūdbrahyannuṣārthe harakṛṣṇayoḥ kathaṃ kṣayaṃ ca bāṇasya bāhūnāṃ kṛtavānhariḥ  ViP etatsarvaṃ mahābhāga mamākhyātuṃ tvamarhasi mahatkautūhalaṃ jātaṃ kathāṃ śrotumimāṃ hareḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācauṣā bāṇasutā vipra pārvatīṃ saha śaṃbhunā krīḍantīmupalakṣyoccaiḥ spṛhāṃ cakre tadāśrayām  ViP tataḥsakalacittajñā gaurī tāmāha bhāminīm alamatyarthatāpena bhartrā tvamapi raṃsyase  ViP ityuktā sā tayā cakre kadeti matimātmanaḥ ko vā bhartā mametyāha punastāmāha pārvatī  ViP pārvatyuvācavaiśākhaśukladvādaśyāṃ svapne yobhibhavaṃ tava kariṣyati sa te bhartā rājaputri bhaviṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatasyāṃ tithābuṣāsvapne yathā devyā samīritam tathaivā bhibhavaṃ cakre kaścidrāgaṃ ca tatra sā  ViP tataḥ prabuddhā puruṣamapaśyantī samutmukā kva gatesīti nirlajjā maitreyoktavatī sakhim  ViP bāṇasya mantrī kuṃbhāṇḍaṃ citrarekhā ca tatsutā tasyāḥsakhyabhavatsā ca prāha koyaṃ tvayocyate  ViP yadā lajjākulā nāsyai kathayāmāsa sā sakhī tadā viśvāsamānīya sarvamevābhyavādayat  ViP viditārthāṃ tu tāmāha punaścoṣā yathoditam devyā tathaiva tatprāptau yo hyupāyaḥ kuruṣva tam  ViP citralekhovācadurvijñeyamidaṃ vaktuṃ prāptuṃ vāpi na sakyate tathāpi kiñcatkartavyamupakāraṃ priye tava  ViP saptāṣṭadinaparyantaṃ tāvatkālaḥ pratīkṣyatām ityuktvābhyantaraṃ gatvā upāyaṃ tamathākarot  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ pade surāndaityangandharvāṃś ca pradhānataḥ manuṣyāṃś ca vilikhyāsyai citralekhā vyadarśayat  ViP apāsya sā tu gandharvāṃs tathoragasurāsurān manuṣyeṣu dadau dṛṣṭiṃ teṣv apy andhakavṛṣṇiṣu  ViP kṛṣṇarāmau vilokyāsīt subhrūr lajjājaḍeva sā pradyumnadarśane vrīḍedṛṣṭiṃ ninyenyato dvija  ViP dṛṣṭamātre tataḥ kānte pradyumnatanaye dvija dṛṣṭatyarthavilāsinyā lajjā kvāpi nirākṛtā  ViP soyaṃsoyamitītyukte tayā sā yogagāminī citralekhābrajīdenāmuṣāṃ bāṇasurāṃ tadā  ViP citralekhovācaayaṃ kṛṣṇasya pautraste bhartā devyā prasāditaḥ aniruddha iti khyātaḥ prakhyātaḥ priyadarśanaḥ  ViP prāpnoṣi yadi bhartāramimaṃ prāptaṃ tvayākhilam duṣpraveśā purī pūrvaṃ dvārakā kṛṣṇapālitā  ViP tathāpi yatnādbhartāramānayiṣyāmi te sakhi rahasyametadvaktavyaṃ na kasyacidapi tvayā  ViP acirādāgamiṣyāmi sahasva virahaṃ mama yayau dvāravatīṃ coṣāṃ samāśvāsya tataḥ sakhīm  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe dvātriṃśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācabāṇopi praṇipatyāgre maitreyāha trilocanam deva bāhusahasreṇa nirviṇṇosmyāhavaṃ vinā  ViP kaccinmamaiṣāṃ bāhūnāṃ sāphalyajanako varadaṃ śaṃbhumabhyāgato gṛham sabhagnaṃ dhvajamālokya hṛṣṭo harṣaṃ punaryayau  ViP etasminneva kāle tu yogavidyābalena tam aniruddhamathāninye citralekhā varāpsarāḥ  ViP kanyāntaḥpuramabhyetya ramamāṇaṃ sahoṣayā vijñāya rakṣiṇo gatvā śaśaṃsurdaityabhūpate  ViP vyādiṣṭaṃ kiṅkarāṇāṃ tu sainyaṃ tena mahātmanā jaghāna parighaṃ ghoramādāya paravīrahā  ViP hateṣu teṣu bāṇopi balapradyumnasahito bāṇasya prayayau puram  ViP purapraveśe pramathair yuddhamāsīnmahātmanaḥ yayau bāṇapurābhyāśaṃ nītvā tānsaṃkṣayaṃ hariḥ  ViP tatastripādastriśirā jvaro māheśvaro mahān bhagavānmadhusūdanaḥ  ViP jvara uvācamama tvāya samaṃ yuddhaṃ ye smarīṣyanti mānavāḥ vijvarāste bhaviṣyantī tyuktvā cainaṃ yayau jvaraḥ  ViP tatognīnbhagavānpañca jitvā nītvā tathā kṣayam dānavānāṃ śastrāstrāṃśupratāpitiḥ  ViP pralayoyamaśeṣasya jagato nūnamāgataḥ menire tridaśāstatra vartamāne mahāraṇe  ViP jṛṃbha kāstreṇa govindo jṛṃbhayāmāsa śaṅkaram tataḥ praṇemurdaiteyāḥ pramathāś ca samantataḥ  ViP jṛṃbhābhibhūtasyu haro rathopastha upāviśat na śaśāka tato yoddhuṃ kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā  ViP garujakṣatavāhaś ca pradyumnāstreṇa pīḍitaḥ kṛṣṇahuṅkāranirdhūtaśaktiścāpayayau guhaḥ  ViP jṛṃbhite śaṅkare naṣṭe daityasainye guhe jite nīte pramathasainye ca saṃkṣayaṃ śārṅgadhanvanā  ViP nandinā saṃgṛhītāśvamadhirūḍho mahāratham bāṇastatrāyayau yoddhuṃ kṛṣṇakārṣṇibalaiḥ saha  ViP balabhadro mahāvīryo bāṇasainyamanekadhā vivyādha bāṇaiḥ prabhraśya dharmataścāpalāyata  ViP ākṛṣya lāṅgalāgreṇa mukalenāśu tāḍitam balaṃ balena dadṛśe bāṇo bāṇaiś ca cakriṇā  ViP tataḥ kṛṣṇena yanmayā vyāhṛtaṃ vacaḥ  ViP asmatsaṃśrayadṛptoyaṃ nāparādhī tavāvyaya mayā dattavaro daityastatastvāṃ kṣamayāmyaham  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktaḥ prāha govidaḥ śulapāṇimumāpatim prasannapadano bhūtvā trayastriṃśo dhyāyaḥ maitreya uvācacakre karma mahacchaurirbībhraṇo mānuṣīṃ tanum jigāya śakraṃ śarvaṃ ca sarvāndevāṃś ca līlayā  ViP yac cānyad akarot karma divyaceṣṭavighātakṛt tatkathyatāṃ avatīrmastvamityukto janair ajñānamohitaiḥ  ViP sa mene vāsudevohamavatīrṇo mahītale naṣṭasmṛtistataḥsarvaṃ viṣṇucihnamacīkarat  ViP dūtaṃ ca preṣayāmāsa kṛṣṇāya sumahātmane tyaktvā cakrādikaṃ cihnaṃ śrīparāśara uvācaityuktepagate dūte saṃsmṛtyābhyāgataṃ hariḥ garutmantamathāruhya tvaritastatpuraṃ yayau  ViP tatastu keśavodyogaṃ śrutvā kāśīpatistadā sarvasainyaparivāraḥ pārṣṇigrāha upāyayau  ViP tato balena mahatā kāśīrājabalena ca paiṇḍrako vāsudevo sau keśavābhimukho yayau  ViP taṃ dadarśa harirdūrādudārasyandane sthitam cakrahastaṃ gadāśārṅgabāhuṃ pāṇigatāṃbujam  ViP sragdharaṃ pītavasanaṃ ViP ūcuś ca kupitāḥsarve bāhlikādyāś ca kauravāḥ arājyārhaṃ yadorvaśamavekṣya musalāyudha  ViP bhobhoḥ kimetadbhavatā balabhadreritaṃ vacaḥ ājñāṃ kurukulotthānāṃ yādavaḥ kaḥ pradāsyati  ViP ugraseno pi yadyājñāṃ kauravāṇāṃ pradāsyati tadalaṃ pāṇḍuraiś chatrair nṛpayogyair viḍaṃbanaiḥ  ViP tadgaccha bala mā vā tvaṃ sāṃbamanyāyaceṣṭitam vimokṣyāmo na bhavataścograsenasya śāsanāt  ViP praṇatiryā kṛtāsmākaṃ mānyānāṃ kukurāndhakaiḥ na nāma sā kṛtā keyamājñā svāmini bhṛtyataḥ  ViP garvamāropitā yūyaṃ samānāsanabhojanaiḥ ko doṣo bhavatāṃ nītiryatprītyā nāvalokitā  ViP asmābhir argho bhavato yoyaṃ bala niveditaḥ premṇaitannaitadasmākaṃ kulādyuṣmatkulocitam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā kuravaḥ sāṃbaṃ muñcāmo na hareḥsutam kṛtaitaniścayastūrṇaṃ viviśurgajasāhvayam  ViP mattaḥ kopena cāghūrmastatodhikṣepajanmanā utthāya pārṣṇyā vasudhāṃ jaghāna sa halāyudhaḥ  ViP tato vidāritā pṛthvī pārṣṇighātānmahātmanaḥ āsphoṭayāmāsa tadā diśaḥ śabdena pūrayan  ViP uvāca cātitāmrākṣo bhṛkuṭīkuṭilānanaḥ  ViP aha madāvalepoyamasārāṇāṃ durātmanām kauravāṇāṃ mahīpatvamasmākaṃ kila kālajam ugrasenasya yenājñāṃ manyante dyapi laṅghanam  ViP ugrasenaḥ samadhyāste sudhārmā na śacīpatiḥ dhiṅmānuṣaśatocchiṣṭe tuṣṭireṣāṃ nṛpāsane  ViP pārijātataroḥ puṣpamañjarīrvanitājanaḥ bibharti yasya bhatyānāṃ so pyeṣāṃ na mahīpatiḥ  ViP samastabhūbhṛtāṃ nātha ugrasenaḥ sa tiṣṭhatu adya niṣkauravāmurvī kṛtvā yāsyāmi tatpurīm  ViP karṇaṃ duryodhanaṃ droṇamadya bhīṣmaṃ sabāhlikam duḥśasanādīnbhūriṃ ca bhūriśravasameva ca  ViP somadattaṃ śalaṃ caiva bhīmārjunayudhiṣṭhirān yamau ca kauravāṃścānyānhatvā sāśvarathadvipān  ViP vīramādāya taṃ sāṃbaṃ sapatnīkaṃ tataḥ purīm dvārakāmugrasenādīngatvā drakṣyāmi bāndhavān  ViP atha vā kauravāvāsaṃ samastaiḥ kurubhiḥ saha bhāgīrathyāṃ kṣipāmyāśu nagaraṃ nāgasāhvayam  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā madaraktākṣaḥ karṣaṇādhomukhaṃ halam prākāravapradurgasya cakarṣa musalāyudhaḥ  ViP āghūrṇitaṃ tatsahasā tato vai hāstinaṃ puram dṛṣṭvā saṃkṣubdhahṛdayāścukṣubhuḥsarvakauravāḥ  ViP rāmarāma mahābāho kṣamyatāṃ kṣamyatāṃ tvayā upasaṃhriyatāṃ kopaḥ prasīda musalāyudha  ViP eṣa sāṃbaḥsapatnīkastavaniryātito balāt avijñātaprabhāvāṇāṃ kṣmayatāmaparādhinām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatato niryātayāmāsuḥsāṃbaṃ patnīsamanvitam niṣkramya svapurāttūrṇaṃ kauravā munipuṅgava  ViP bhīṣmadroṇakṛpādīnāṃ praṇamya vadatāṃ priyam kṣāntameva mayetyāha balo balavatāṃ varaḥ  ViP adyāpyāghūrṇitākāraṃ lakṣyate tatpuraṃ dvija eṣa prabhāvo rāmasya balaśauryopalakṣaṇaḥ  ViP tatastu kauravāḥsāṃbaṃ saṃpūjya bali nā saha preṣayāmāsurudvāhadhanabhāryāsamanvitam  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe pañcatriṃśo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācamaitreyaitadbalaṃ tasya balasya balaśālinaḥ kṛtaṃ yadanyattenābhūttadapi śrūyatāṃ savanāndeśānpuragramāntarāṇi ca kvacicca parvatākṣepergramādīnsamacūrṇayat  ViP śailānutpāṭya toyeṣu mumocāṃbunidhau tathā punaścārmavamadhyasthaḥ kṣobhayāmāsa sāgaram  ViP tena vikṣobhitaścābdhirudvelo dvija jāyate plāvayaṃstīrajāngramānpurādīnativegavān  ViP kāmarūpī mahārūpī kṛtvā sasyānyaśeṣataḥ luṭhanbhramaṇasaṃmardaiḥ saṃcūrmayati vānaraḥ  ViP tena viprakṛtaṃ sarvaṃ jagadetaddurātmanā niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāraṃ maitreyāsītsuduḥkhitam  ViP ekadāraivatodyāne papau pānaṃ halā yudhaḥ revatī ca mahābhāgā tathaivānyā varastriyaḥ  ViP udgīyamāno vilasallalanāmaulimadhyagaḥ reme yadukulaśreṣṭhaḥ kubera iva nandane  ViP tataḥsa vānaro bhyetya gṛhītvā sīriṇo halam musalaṃ ca cakārāsya saṃmukhaṃ ca viḍaṃbanam  ViP tathaiva yoṣitāṃ tāsāṃ jahāsābhimukhaṃ kapiḥ pānapūrmāś ca karakāñcikṣepāhatya vai tadā  ViP tataḥ kopaparītātmā bhartsayāmāsa taṃ halī tathāpi tamavajñāya cakrekilakiladhvanim  ViP tataḥ smayitvā sa balo jagrāha musalaṃ ruṣā so pi śailaśilāṃ bhīmāṃ jagrāha plavagottamaḥ  ViP cikṣepa sa ca tāṃ kṣiptāṃ musalena sahasradhā vibheda yādavaśreṣṭhaḥsā papāta mahītale  ViP atha tanmusalaṃ cāsau samullaṅghya plavaṅgamaḥ vegenāgatya roṣeṇa kareṇorasyatāḍayat  ViP tato balena kopena muṣṭinā mūrdhni tāḍitaḥ papāta rudhirodgārī dvividaḥ kṣīṇajīvitaḥ  ViP patatā taccharīreṇa gireḥ śṛgamaśīryata maitreya śatadhā vajrivajremeva vidāritam  ViP puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ tato devā rāmasyopari cikṣipuḥ praśaśaṃsustato bhyetya sādhvetatte mahatkṛtam  ViP anena duṣṭakapinā daityapakṣopakāriṇā jagannirākṛtaṃ vīra diṣṭyā sa kṣayamāgataḥ  ViP ityuktvā divamājagmurdevā hṛṣṭaḥsaguhyakāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃvidhānyanekāni baladevasya dhīmataḥ karmāṇyaparimeyāniśeṣasya dharaṇībhṛtaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe pañcamāṃśe ṣaṭtriṃśodhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaevaṃ daityavadhaṃ kṛṣṇe baladeva sahāyavān cakre duṣṭakṣitīśānāṃ tathaiva jagataḥ kṛte  ViP kṣiteś ca bhāraṃ bhagavānphālgunena samanvitaḥ avatārayāmāsa vibhuḥsamastākṣohiṇīvadhāt  ViP kṛtvā bhārāvataramaṃ bhuvo hatvākhilānnṛpān śāpavyājena viprāṇāmupasaṃhṛtavānkulam  ViP utsṛjya dvārakāṃ kṛṣṇastyaktvā mānuṣyamātmanaḥ sāṃśo viṣṇumayaṃ sthānaṃ praviveśa mune nijam  ViP maitreya uvācasa vipraśāpavyājena bhāvikāryapracoditāḥ sāṃbaṃ jāṃbavatīputraṃ bhūṣayitvā striyaṃ yathā  ViP praśritāstānmunīnūcuḥ praṇipātapuraḥsaram iyaṃ strī putrakāmā vai brūta kiṃ janayiṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācadivyajñānopapannāste vipralabdhāḥ kumārakaiḥ munayaḥ kupitāḥ procurmusalaṃ janayiṣyati  ViP sarvayādavasaṃhārakāraṇaṃ bhuvanottaram yenākhilakulotsādau yādavānāṃ bhaviṣyati  ViP ityuktāste kumārāstu ācacakṣuryathātatham ugrasenāya musalaṃ jajñe sāṃbasya codarāt  ViP tadugraseno musalamayaścūrṇamakārayat jajñe taderakāyūrṇaṃ prakṣiptaṃ tair mahodadhau  ViP musalasyātha lohasya pūrṇitasya tu yādavaiḥ khaṇḍaṃ cūrṇitaśeṣaṃ tu tato yattomarākṛti  ViP tadapyaṃbunidhau kṣiptaṃ matsyo jagrāha jālibhiḥ ghātitasyodarāttasya lubdho jagraha tajjārāḥ  ViP vijñātaparamārthopi bhagavānmadhusūdanaḥ naicchattadanyathā kartuṃ vidhinā yatsamīhitam  ViP devaiś ca prahito vāyuḥ praṇipattyāha keśavam rajasyevamahaṃ dūtaḥ prahito bhagavansuraiḥ  ViP vasvaśvimarudādityarudrasādhyādibhiḥ saha vijñāpayati śakrastvāṃ tadidaṃ śrūyatāṃ vibho  ViP bhārāvataraṇārthāya varṣāṇāmadhikaṃ śatam bhagavānavatīrṇotra tridaśeḥsaha coditaḥ  ViP durvṛttā nihatā daityā bhuvo bhāro vatāritaḥ tvayā manāthāstridaśā bhavantu tridive sadā  ViP tadatītaṃ jagannātha varṣāṇāmadhikaṃ śatam idānīṃ gamyatāṃ svargo bhavatā yadi rocate  ViP devair vijñāpyate deva tathātraiva ratistava tatsthīyatāṃ karomyetat saptarātreṇa satvaraḥ  ViP yathā gṛhītamaṃbhodherdattvāhaṃ dvārakābhuvam yādavānupasaṃhṛtya yāsyāmi tridaśālayam  ViP manuṣyadehamutsṛjya saṃkarṣamasahāyavān prāpta evāsmi mantavyo devendreṇa tathāmaraiḥ  ViP jarāsaṃdhādayo ye nye nihatā bhārahetavaḥ kṣitestebhyaḥ kumāro pi yadūnāṃ nāpacīyate  ViP tadetaṃ sumahābhāram avatārya kṣiter aham yāsyāmyamaralokasya pālanāya bravīhi tān  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityukto vāsudevena devadūtaḥ praṇamya tam maitreya divyayā gatyā devarājāntikaṃ yayau  ViP bhagavānapyathotpātāndivyabhaumāntarikṣajān dadarśa dvārakāpuryāṃ vināśāya divāniśam  ViP tāndṛṣṭvā yādavānāha paśyadhvamatidāruṇān mahotpātāñchamāyaiṣāṃ prabhāsaṃ yāma mā ciram  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaevamukte tu kṛṣṇena yādavapravārastataḥ mahābhāgavataḥ prāha praṇipatyoddhavo harim  ViP bhagavanyanmayā kāryaṃ tadājñāpaya sāṃpratam manye kulamidaṃ sarvaṃ bhagavānsaṃhariṣyati  ViP nāśāyāsya nimittāni kulasyācyuta lakṣaye  ViP śrībhagavānuvācagaccha tvaṃ divyayā gatyā ViP dvārakāṃ ca mayā tyaktāṃ samudraḥ plāvayiṣyati madveśma caikaṃ muktvātu bhayānmatto jalāśaye tatra sannihitaścāhaṃ bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktaḥ praṇipatyainaṃ jagāmāśu cakrustatra mahāpānaṃ vāsudevena coditāḥ  ViP pibatāṃ tatra caiteṣāṃ saṃgharṣeṇa parasparam ativādendhano jajñe kalahāgniḥ kṣayāvahaḥ  ViP maitreya uvācasvaṃsvaṃ vai bhuñjatāṃ teṣāṃ kalahaḥ kridhasaṃraktalocanāḥ jaghnuḥ parasparaṃ te tu śastrair daivabalātkṛtāḥ  ViP kṣīṇaśastrāś ca jagṛhuḥ pratyāsannāmathairakām  ViP erakā tu gṛhītā vai vajrabhūteva lakṣyate tayā parasparaṃ jaghnuḥsaṃprahāre sudāruṇe  ViP pradyumnasāṃbapramukhāḥ kṛtavarmātha sātyakiḥ aniruddhādayaścānye pṛthurvipṛthureva ca  ViP cāruvarmā cārukaś ca tathākrūrādayo dvija erakārūpibhir vajrais te nijaghnuḥ parasparam  ViP nivārayāmāsa hariryādavāṃste ca keśavam sahāyaṃ menirerīṇāṃ prāptaṃ jaghnuḥ parasparam  ViP kṛṣṇo pi kupitasteṣāmerakāmuṣṭimādade vadhāya so pi musalaṃ muṣṭarlauhamabhūttadā  ViP jaghāna tena niḥśeṣānyādavānātatāyinaḥ jaghnuste sahasābhyetya tathānyepi parasparam  ViP tataścārṇavamadhyena jaitro sau cakriṇo rathaḥ paśyato dārukasyātha prāyādaśvair dhṛto dvija  ViP cakraṃ gadā tathā śārṅga tūṇīśaṅkhosireva ca pradakṣiṇaṃ hariṃ kṛtvā jagmurādityavartmanā  ViP kṣaṇena nābhavatkaścidyādavānāmaghātitaḥ ṛte kṛṣṇaṃ mahātmānaṃ dārukaṃ ca mahāmune  ViP caṅkramyamāṇau tau rāmaṃ vṛkṣamūle kṛtāsanam dadṛśāte mukhāccāsya niṣkrāmantaṃ mahoragam  ViP niṣkramya sa makhāttasya mahābhogo bhujaṅgamaḥ prayayāvarṇavaṃ siddhaiḥ pujyamānastathoragaiḥ  ViP tatorghyamādāya tadā tathā kṣayam yogo sthitvāhamapyetatparityakṣye kalevaram  ViP vācyaś ca dvārakāvāsī janaḥ sarvas tathāhukaḥ yathomāṃ nagarīṃ sarvāṃ samudraḥ plāvayiṣyati  ViP tasmādbhavadbhiḥ sarvais tu pratīkṣyo āyayau sa jarānāma tadā tatra sa lubdhakaḥ musalāvaśeṣalohaikasāyakanyastatomaraḥ  ViP sa tatpādaṃ mṛgākaramavekṣyārādavisthitaḥ tale vivyādha tenaiva tomareṇa dvijottama  ViP tataś ca dadṛśe tatra cadurbāhudharaṃ naram praṇipatyāha caivainaṃ prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ  ViP ajānatā kṛtamidaṃ mayā hariṇaśaṅkayā kṣamyatāṃ mama pāpena dagdhaṃ māṃ trātumarhasi  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatatastaṃ bhagavānāha tasminsabhagavānsaṃyojyātmānamātmani brahmabhūte vyayecintye vāsudevamaye male  ViP ajanmanyamare viṣṇavāprameye khilātmani tatyāja mānuṣaṃ dehamatītya trividhāṃ gatim  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viviśustā hutāśanam  ViP revatī cāpi rāmasya dehamāśliṣya sattamā viveśa jvalitaṃ vāhniṃ tatsaṃgāhlādaśītalam  ViP ugrasenastu tacchutvā tathaivānakadundubhiḥ devakī rohiṇī caiva viviśurjātavedasam  ViP tatorjunaḥ pretakāryaṃ kṛtvā teṣāṃ yathāvidhi niścakrāma janaṃ sarve gṛhītvā vajrameva ca  ViP dvāravatyā viniṣkrāntāḥ kṛṣṇapatnyaḥ sahasraśaḥ vajraṃ janaṃ ca kauteyaḥ pālayañchanakair yayau  ViP sabhā sudharmā kṛṣṇena kartyaloke samujjhite svargaṃ jagāma maitreya pārijātaś ca pādapaḥ  ViP yasmindine hariryāto divaṃ saṃtyajya medinīm tasminnevāvatīrṇo yaṃ kālakāyo balī kaliḥ  ViP plāvayāmāsa tāṃ śūnyāṃ dvārakāṃ ca mahodadhiḥ vāsudevagṛhaṃ tvekaṃ na plāvayati sāgaraḥ  ViP nātikrāntumalaṃ brahmaṃstadadyāpi mahodadhiḥ nityaṃ sannihitastatra bhagavānkeśavo yataḥ  ViP tadatīva mahāpuṇyaṃ sarvapātakanāśanam viṣṇuśriyānvitaṃ sthānaṃ dṛṣṭvā pāmādvimucyate  ViP pārthaḥ pañcanade deśe bahudhānyadhanānvite cakāra vāsaṃ sarvasya janasya munisattamaḥ  ViP tato lobhaḥsamabhavatpārthenaikena dhanvinā dṛṣṭvāstriyo nīyamānā dasyūnāṃ nihateśvarāḥ  ViP tataste pāpakamāṇo lobhopahṛtacetasaḥ ābhīrā mantrayāmāsuḥsametyānyantadurmadāḥ  ViP ayamekorjuno dhanvī strījanaṃ nihateśvaram nayatyasmānatikramya dhigetadbhavatāṃ balam  ViP hatvā garvasamārūḍho bhīṣmadromajayadrathān karṇādīṃś ca na jānāti balaṃ grāmanivāsinām  ViP yaṣṭihastānavekṣyāsmāndhanuṣpāṇiḥsa durmatiḥ sarvānevāvajānāti kiṃ vo bāhubhir unnataiḥ  ViP tato yaṣṭipraharaṇādasyavo loṣṭadhāriṇaḥ sahasraśobhyadhāvanta taṃ janaṃ nihateśvaram  ViP tato nirbhartsya kauteyaḥ prāhābhīrānhasanniva nivartadhvamadharmajñā yadi na stha mumūrṣavaḥ  ViP avajñāya vacastasya jagṛhuste tadā dhanam strīdhanaṃ caiva maitreya viṣvaksena piragraham  ViP tatorjuno dhanurdivyaṃ gāṇḍīvamajaraṃ yudhi āropayitumārebhe na śaśāka ca vīryavān  ViP cakāra sajyaṃ kṛcchrāccataccābhūcchithilaṃ punaḥ na sasmāra tatostrāṇi cintayannapi pāṇḍavaḥ  ViP śarānmumoca caiteṣu pārthā vairiṣvamarṣitaḥ tvagbhedaṃ de paraṃ cakrurastā gāṇḍīvadhanvinā  ViP vahninā ye kṣayā dattāḥ śarāstepi kṣayaṃ yayuḥ yuddhyataḥsaha gopālair arjunasya bhavakṣaye  ViP acintayacca kainteyaḥ kṛṣṇasyaiva hi tadbalam yanmayā śarasaṃghātaiḥ sakalā bhūbhṛto hatāḥ  ViP miṣataḥ pāṇḍuputrasya tatastāḥ pramadottamāḥ ābhīrair apakṛṣyanta kāmaṃ cānyāḥ pradudruvuḥ  ViP tataḥ śareṣu kṣīṇeṣu dhanuṣkoṭyā dhanañjayaḥ jaghāna dasyūṃste cāsya prahārāñjahasurmune  ViP prekṣatastasya pārthasya puṣṇyandhakavarastriyaḥ jagmurādāya te mlecchāḥ samastā munisattama  ViP tataḥsuduḥkhito jiṣṇuḥ kaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭamiti bruvan aho bhagavatānena muṣṭosmīti ruroda vai  ViP taddhanustāni śastrāṇi sa rathaste ca vājinaḥ sarvamekapade naṣṭaṃ dānamaśrotriye yathā  ViP ahotibalabaddaivaṃ vinā tena mahātmanā yadasāmarthyayuktepi nicavarge jayapradam  ViP tau bāhū sa ca me muṣṭiḥ sthānaṃ tatsosmi cārjunaḥ puṇyenaiva vinā tena gataṃ sarvamasāratām  ViP mamārjunatvaṃ bhīmasya bhīmatvaṃ tatkṛte dhruvam vinā tena yadā bhīrair jitohaṃ rathināṃ varaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaitthaṃ vadanyayau jiṣmuridraprasthaṃ purottamam cakāra tatra rājānaṃ vajraṃ yādavanandanam  ViP sa dadarśa tato vyāsaṃ phālgunaḥ kānanāśrayam tamupetya mahābhāgaṃ vinayenābyavādayat  ViP taṃ vandamānaṃ caraṇāvavalokya muniściram uvāca vākyaṃ vicchāyaḥ kathamadya tvamīdṛśaḥ  ViP avīrajonugamanaṃ brahmahatyā kṛtātha vā dṛḍhāśābhaṅgaduḥkhīva bhraṣṭacchāyo si sāṃpratam  ViP sāṃtānikādayo vāte yācamānā nirākṛtāḥ agamyastrīratirvā tvaṃ yenāsi vigataprabhaḥ  ViP bhuṅte pradāyaviprebhyo mṛṣṭamekotha vā bhavān kiṃ vā kṛpaṇavittāni hṛtāni bhavatārjuna  ViP kacinnu śurpavātasya gocaratvaṃ gatorjuna duṣṭacakṣurhato vāsi niḥśrīkaḥ kathamanyathā  ViP spṛṣṭo nakhāṃbhasā vātha ghaṭavāryukṣitopi vā kena tvaṃ vāsi vicchāyo nyūnair vā yudhi nījātaḥ  ViP śrīparāśarauvācatataḥ pārtho viniśvāsya śrūyatāṃ bhagavanniti proktvā yathāvadācaṣṭe vyāsāyātmaparābhavam  ViP arjuna uvācayadbalaṃ yacca mattejo yadvīryaṃ yaḥ parākramaḥ yā śrīśchāyā ca naḥ sosmānparityajya harirgataḥ  ViP īśvareṇāpi mahatā smitapūrvābhibhāṣiṇā hīnā vayaṃ mune tena jātāstṛṇamayā iva  ViP astrāṇāṃ sāyakānāṃ ca gāṇḍīvasya tathā mama sāratā yābhavanmūrtiḥsa gataḥ puruṣottamaḥ  ViP yasyāvalokanādasmāñchrīrjayaḥ saṃpadunnatiḥ na tatyāja sa govindastyaktvāsmānbhagavāngataḥ  ViP bhīṣmadroṇāṅgarājādyā s tathā duryodhanādayaḥ yatprabhāvena nirdagdhāḥ sa kṛṣṇastyaktavānbhuvam  ViP niryauvanā gataśrīkā naṣṭacchāyeva medinī vibhāti tāta naikohaṃ virahe tasya cakriṇaḥ  ViP yasya prabhāvādbhīṣmādyair mayy agnau śalabhāyatam vinā tenādya kṛṣṇena gopālaurasmi nirjitaḥ  ViP gāṇḍīvastriṣu lokeṣu khyātiṃ yadanubhāvataḥ gatastena vinābhīralaguḍaiḥ sa tiraskṛtaḥ  ViP strīsahasrāṇyanekāni mannāthāni mahāmune yatato mama nītāni dasyubhir laguḍāyudhaiḥ  ViP ānīyamānamābhīraiḥ kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇāvarodhanam hṛtaṃ yaṣṭipraharaṇaiḥ paribhūya balaṃ mama  ViP niḥśrīkatā na me citraṃ yajjīvāmi tadadbhutam nīcāvamānapaṅkāṅkī nirlajjosmi pitāmaha  ViP vyāsa uvācaalaṃ te vrīḍayā pārtha na tvaṃ śocitum arhasi avehi sarvabhūteṣu kālasya gatirīdṛśī  ViP kālo bhavāya bhūtānāmabhavāya ca pāṇḍava kālamūlam idaṃ jñātvā bhava sthairyaparo rjuna  ViP nadyaḥ samudrā girayaḥsakalā ca vasuṃdharā devā manuṣyāḥ paśavastaravaś ca sarīsṛpāḥ  ViP sṛṣṭāḥ kālena kālena punar yāsyanti saṃkṣayam kālātmakamidaṃ sarvaṃ jñātvā śamamavāpnuhi  ViP kālasvarūpī bhagavānkṛṣṇaḥ kamalalocanaḥ yaccāttha kṛṣṇamāhātmyaṃ tattathaiva dhanañjaya  ViP bhārāvatārakāryārthamavatīrṇasya medinīm bhārākrāntā dharā yātā devānāṃ samitiṃ purā  ViP tadarthamavatīrṇo sau kālarūpī janārdanaḥ tacca niṣpādinaṃ kāryamaśeṣā bhūbhujo hatāḥ  ViP vaṣṇyandhakakulaṃ sarvaṃ tathā pārthopasaṃhṛtam na kiñcidanyatkartavyaṃ tasya bhūmitale prabhoḥ  ViP ato gataḥsa bhagavānkatakṛtyo yathecchayā sṛṣṭiṃ sarge karotyeṣa devadevaḥ sthitau sthitim antentāya samarthoyaṃ sāṃprataṃ vai yathā gataḥ  ViP tasmātyārtha na saṃtāpastvayā kāryaḥ parābhave bhavanti bhāvāḥ kāleṣu puruṣāṇāṃ yataḥ stutiḥ  ViP tvayaikena hatā bhīṣmadroṇakarmādayo raṇe teṣāmarjuna kālotthaḥ kiṃ nyūnābhibhavo na saḥ  ViP viṣṇostasya prabhāveṇa yathā teṣāṃ parābhavaḥ kṛtastathaiva bhavato dasyubhyaḥ sa parābhavaḥ  ViP sa deveśaḥ śarīrāṇi samāviśya jagatsthitim karoti sarvabhūtānāṃ nāśamante jagatpatiḥ  ViP bhagodaye te kainteya sahāyo bhūjjanārdanaḥ tathānte tadvipakṣāste keśavena vināśitāḥ  ViP kaḥ śraddaddhyātsagāṅgoyānhanyāstvaṃ kauravāniti ābhīrebhyaś ca bhavataḥ kaḥ śraddadhyātparābhavam  ViP pārthaitatsarvabhūtasya harerlīlāvicoṣṭitam tvayā yatkaurāvā dhvastā yadābhīrair bhavāñjitaḥ  ViP gṛhītā dasyubhir yāś ca bhavāñchocati tāḥstriyaḥ etasyāhaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ kathayāmi tavārjuna  ViP aṣṭāvakaḥ purā vipro jalavāsarato bhavat bahūnvarṣagaṇānpārtha gṛṇanbrahma sanātanam  ViP jiteṣvasurasaṃghaṣu merupṛṣṭhe mahotsavaḥ babhūva tatra gacchantyo dadṛśustaṃ surastriyaḥ  ViP raṃbhātilottamādyāstu śataśo tha sahasraśaḥ tuṣṭuvustaṃ mahātmānaṃ praśaśaṃsuś ca pāṇḍava  ViP ākaṇṭhamagnaṃ salile jaṭābhāravahaṃ munim vinayāvanatāścainaṃ praṇemustotratatparāḥ  ViP yathāyathā prasanno sau tuṣṭuvustaṃ tathātathā sarvāstāḥ kauravaśreṣṭha taṃ variṣṭhaṃ dvijanmanām  ViP aṣṭāvakra uvācaprasanno haṃ mahābhāgā bhavatīnāṃ yadiṣyate mattastadvrayatāṃ sarvaṃ pradāsyāmyatidurlabham  ViP raṃbhātilottamādyāstaṃ vaidikyopsarasobruvan prasanne tvayyaparyāptaṃ kimasmākamiti vakramaṣṭadhā  ViP taṃ dṛṣṭvā gūhamānānāṃ yāsāṃ hāsaḥ sphuṭo bhavat tāḥ śaśāpa muniḥ kopamavāpya kurunandana  ViP yasmādvikṛtarūpaṃ māṃ matvā hīsā vamānanā bhavatībhiḥ kṛtā tasmādetaṃ śāpaṃ dadāmi vaḥ  ViP matprasādena bhartāraṃ labdhvā tu puruṣottamam macchāpopahatāḥsarvā dasyuhastaṃ gamiṣyatha  ViP vyāsa uvācaityudīritamākarṇya munistābhiḥ prasāditaḥ punaḥsuredralokaṃ vai prāha bhūyo gamiṣyatha  ViP evaṃ tasya muneḥ śāpādaṣṭāvakrasya cakriṇam bhartāraṃ prāpya tā yātā dasyuhastaṃ surāṅganāḥ  ViP tattvāya nātra kartavyaḥ śoko lpopi hi pāṇḍava tenaivākhilanāthena sarvaṃ tadupasaṃhṛtam  ViP bhavatāṃ copasaṃhāra āsannastena pāṇḍava balaṃ lejas tathā vīryaṃ māhātmyaṃ copasaṃhṛtam  ViP jātasya niyato mṛtyuḥ patanaṃ ca tathonnateḥ viprayogāvamānastu saṃyogaḥ saṃcaye kṣayaḥ  ViP vijñāya na budhāḥ śokaṃ na harṣamupayānti ye teṣāmevetare ceṣṭāṃ śikṣantaḥsaṃti tādṛśāḥ  ViP tasmāt tvayā naraśreṣṭha jñātvaitadbhrātṛbhiḥ saha parityajyākhilaṃ tantraṃ gantavyaṃ tapase vanam  ViP tadraccha dharmarājāya nivedyautadvaco mama paraśvo bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdha yathā yāsi tathā kuru  ViP ityuktobhyetya pārthābhyāṃ yamābhyāṃ ca sahārjunaḥ dṛṣṭaṃ caivānubhūtaṃ ca sarvamākhyātavāṃs tathā  ViP vyāsavākyaṃ ca te sarve śrutvārjunamukheritam rājye parīkṣitaṃ kṛtvā yayuḥ pāṇḍusutā vanam  ViP ityetattava maitreya vistareṇa mayoditam jātasya yadyadorvaśe vāsudevasya ceṣṭitam  ViP yaścaitaccaritaṃ śrīdharīyavyākhyādvayopete pañca māṃśaḥ samāptaḥ atha śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe viṣṇucittyātmaprakāśākhyaśrīdharīya vyākhyādvayopete ṣaṣṭhāṃśaḥ prārabhyate śrīmate rāmānujāya namaḥmaitreya uvācavyākhyātā śrūyatāṃ matto yathāvadupasaṃhṛtiḥ kalpānte prākṛte caiva pralayo jāyate yathā  ViP ahorātraṃ pitṝṇāṃ tu māso bdastridivaukasām caturyugamahasre tu brahmaṇo vai dvijottama  ViP kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliśceti caturyugam divyair varṣasahasrais tu taddvādaśabhir ucyate  ViP caturyugāṇy aśeṣāṇi sadṛśāni svarūpataḥ ādyaṃ kṛtayugaṃ muktvā maitreyāntyaṃ tathā kalim  ViP ādye kṛtayuge sargo brahmaṇā uvācakaleḥsvarūpaṃ maitreya yadbhavāñchrotu micchati tannibodha samāsena vartate yanmahāmune  ViP varṇāśramācāravatī pravṛttirna kalau nṛṇām na sāmaṛgyajurdharmaviniṣpādanahaitukī  ViP vivāhā na kalau copakṣayaṃ gate kalau striyo bhaviṣyanti tadā keśair alaṅkṛtāḥ  ViP parityakṣyanti bhartāraṃ vittahīnaṃ tathā striyaḥ bhartā bhaviṣyati kalau vittavāneva yoṣitām  ViP yo vai dadāti bahulaṃ svaṃ sa ViP arakṣitāro hartāraḥ śulkavyājena pārthivāḥ hāriṇo janavittānāṃ saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge  ViP yoyo śvarathanāgāḍhyaḥsa sa rājā bhaviṣyati yaś ca yaścābalaḥ sarvaḥ sa sa bhṛtyaḥ kalau yuge  ViP vaiśyāḥ kṛṣivaṇijyādi saṃtyajya nijakarma yat śūdravṛttyā pravartsyanti kārukarmopajīvinaḥ  ViP bhaikṣavrataparāḥ śūdrā pravrajyāliṅgino dhamāḥ pāṣaṇḍasaṃśrayāṃ vṛttimāśrayiṣyanti satkṛtāḥ  ViP durbhikṣakarapīḍābhir atīvopadrutā janāḥ godhūmānnayavānnāḍhyāndeśānyāsyanti duḥkhitāḥ  ViP vedamārge pralīne ca pāṣaṇḍāḍhye tato jane adharmavṛddhyā lokānāmalpamāyurbhaviṣyati  ViP aśāstravihitaṃ ghoraṃ tapyamāneṣu vai tapaḥ nareṣu nṛpadoṣeṇa bālye mṛtyurbhaviṣyati  ViP bhavitā yoṣitāṃ sūtiḥ pañcaṣaṭmaptavārṣikī navāṣṭadaśavarṣāṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ tathā kalau  ViP palitodbhavaś ca bhavitā tathā dvādaśavārṣikaḥ nātijīvati vai kaścitkalau varṣāṇi viṃśatiḥ  ViP alpaprajñā vṛthāliṅgā duṣṭāntaḥkaraṇāḥ kalau yatastato vinaṅkṣyanti kālenālpena mānavāḥ  ViP yadāyādā hi maitreya hānirdharmasya lakṣyate tadātadā kalervṛddhiranumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ  ViP yadāyadā hi pāṃṣaḍavṛddhirmaitreya lakṣyate tadātadā kalervṛddhiranumeyā mahātmabhiḥ  ViP yadāyadā satāṃ hīnirvedamārgānusāriṇām tadātadā tadā jñeyaṃ kaler balam  ViP na prītirvedavādeṣu pāṣaṇḍeṣu yadā ratiḥ kalervṛddhistadā prājñair anumeyā vicakṣaṇaiḥ  ViP kalau jagatpatiṃ viṣṇuṃsarvasraṣṭāramīśvaram nārcayiṣyanti maitreya pāṣaṇḍopahatā janāḥ  ViP kiṃ devaiḥ kiṃ dvijair vedaiḥ kiṃ śauce nāṃbujanmanā ityevaṃ vipravakṣyanti pāṣaṇḍopahatā janāḥ  ViP svalpāṃbuvṛṣṭiḥ parjanyaḥ sasyaṃ svalpaphalaṃ tathā phalaṃ tathālpasāraṃ ca vipra prāpte kalau yuge  ViP śāṇīprāyāṇi vastrāṇi śamīprāyā mahīruhāḥ śūdraprāyās tathā varṇā bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge  ViP aṇuprāyāṇi dhānyāni cājyaprāyaṃ tathā payaḥ bhaviṣyati kalau prāpte hyauśīraṃ cānulepanam  ViP śvaśrūśvaśurabhūyiṣṭhā guravaś ca nṛṇāṃ kalau śyālādya hāribhāryāś ca sṛhṛdo munisattama  ViP kasya mātā pitā kasya yathā karmānugaḥ pumān iti codāhariṣyanti śvaśurānugatānarāḥ  ViP vāṅmanaḥkāyagair doṣair abhibhūtāḥ punaḥ punaḥ narāḥ pāpānyanudinaṃ kariṣyantyalpamedhasaḥ  ViP niḥsattvānāmaśaucānāṃ nihrīkāṇāṃ tathā nṛṇām yadyadduḥkhāya tatsarvaṃ kalikāle bhaviṣyati  ViP niḥsvādhyāyavaṣaṭkāre svadhāsvāhāvivarjite tadā praviralo dharmaḥ kvacilloke nivatsyati  ViP tatrālpenaiva yatnena puṇyaskandhamanuttamam karotiyaḥ kṛtayuge kriyate tapasā hi saḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe prathamo dhyāyaḥśrīparāśara uvācavyāsaścāha mahābuddhiryadatraiva hi vastuni tacchrūyatāṃ mahābhāgā gadato mama tattvataḥ  ViP kasminkāle lpako dharmo dadāni sumahatphalam munīnāṃ puṇyavādo bhūtkaiś cāsau kriyate sukham  ViP saṃdehanirṇayārthāya vedavyāsaṃ mahāmunim yayuste saṃśayaṃ praṣṭuṃ maitreya munipuṅgavāḥ  ViP dṛdṛśuste muniṃ tatra jāhnavīsalile dvija vedavyāsaṃ mahābhāgamardhasnātaṃ sutaṃ mama  ViP snānāvasānaṃ te tasya pratīkṣanto maharṣayaḥ tasthus tīre mahānadyās taruṣaṇḍam upāśritāḥ  ViP magno tha jāhnavītoyādutthāyāha suto mama śudraḥsādhuḥ kaliḥsādhurityevaṃ śṛṇvatāṃ vacaḥ teṣāṃ munīnāṃ bhūyaś ca mamajja sa nadījale  ViP sādhusādhviti cotthāya śūdra dhanyosi cābravīt  ViP nimagnaś ca samutthāya punaḥ prāha mahāmuniḥ yoṣitaḥ sādhu dhanyāstāstābyo dhanyatarostikaḥ  ViP tataḥ snātvā yathānyāyamācāntaṃ ca kṛtakriyam upatasthurmahābhāgaṃ munayaste sutaṃ mama  ViP kṛtasaṃvandanāṃścāha kṛtāsanaparigrahān kimartha māgatā yūyamiti satyavatīsutaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatamūcuḥsaṃśayaṃ praṣṭaṃ bhavantaṃ vayamāgatāḥ alaṃ tenāstu tāvannaḥ kathyatāmaparaṃ tvayā  ViP kaliḥsādhviti yatproktaṃ śūdraḥ sādhviti yoṣitaḥ yadāha bhagavāntsādhu dhanyāśceti punaḥ punāḥ  ViP tat sarvaṃ śrotum icchāmo na ced guhyaṃ mahāmune tatkathyatāṃ tato hṛtsthaṃ pṛcchāmastvāṃ prayojanam  ViP śrīparāśa uvācaityukto munibhir vyāsaḥ prahasyedamathābravīt śrūyatāṃ bho muniśreṣṭhā yaduktaṃ sādhusādhviti  ViP vyāsa uvācayatkṛte daśabhir varṣais tretāyāṃ hāyanena tat dvāpare tacca māsena hyahorātreṇa tatkalau  ViP tapaso brahmacaryasya japādeś ca phalaṃ dvijāḥ prāpnoti puraṣastena kaliḥsādhviti bhāṣitam  ViP dhyāyankṛte yajanyajñais tretāyāṃ dvāparercayan yadāpnoti tadāpnoti kalau saṃkīrtya keśavam  ViP dharmotkarṣamatīvātra prāpnoti puruṣaḥ kalau alpāyāsena dharmajñāstena tuṣṭosmyahaṃ kaleḥ  ViP vratacaryāparair grāhyā vedāḥ pūrvaṃ dvijātibhiḥ tataḥsa dharmasaṃprāptair yaṣṭavyaṃ vidhivad dhanaiḥ  ViP vṛthā kathā vṛthā bhojyaṃ vṛthejyā ca dvijanmanām patanāya tato bhāvyaṃ tais tu saṃyamibhiḥ sadā  ViP asamyakkaraṇe doṣasteṣāṃ sarveṣu vastuṣu bhojyapeyādikaṃ caiṣāṃ necchāprāptikaraṃ dvijāḥ  ViP pāratantryaṃ samasteṣu teṣāṃ kāryeṣu vai yataḥ jayanti te nijāṃllokānkleśena mahatādvijāḥ  ViP dvijaśuśrūṣayaivaiṣa pākayajñādhikāravān nijāñjayati vai lokāñchūdro dhanyatarastataḥ  ViP bhakṣyābhakṣyeṣu nāsyāsti peyāpeyeṣu vai yataḥ niyamo muniśārdūlāstenāsau sādhvitīritaḥ  ViP svadharmasyāvirodhena narair labdhaṃ dhanaṃ sadā pratipādanīyaṃ pātreṣu yaṣṭavyaṃ ca yathāvidhi  ViP tasyārjane mahākleśaḥ pālane ca dvijottamāḥ tathāsadviniyogena vijñātaṃ gahanaṃ nṛṇām  ViP evamanyais tathā kleśaiḥ puruṣā dvijasattamāḥ nijāñjayanti vai lokānprājāpatyādikānkramāt  ViP yoṣicchuśrūṣaṇādbhartuḥ karmaṇā manasā girā taddhitā śubhamāpnoti tatsālokyaṃ yato dvijāḥ  ViP nātikleśena mahatā tāneva puruṣo yathā tṛtīyaṃ vyāhṛtaṃ tena mayā sādhviti yoṣitaḥ  ViP etadvaḥ kathitaṃ viprāyannimittamihāgataḥ tatpṛcchataḥ yathākāmaṃ sava bakṣyāmi vaḥ sphuṭam  ViP ṛṣayaste tataḥ procuryatpraṣṭavyaṃ mahāmune asminneva ca tatpraśne yathāvatkathitaṃ tvayā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ prahasya tānāha kṛṣṇadvaipāyanomuniḥ vismayotphullanayanāṃstāpasāṃstānupāgatān  ViP mayaiṣa bhavatāṃ praśro jñāto divyena cakṣuṣā tatohaṃ vaḥ prasaṃgena sādhusādhviti bhāṣitam  ViP svalpena hi pratyanenadharmaḥsidhyati vai kalau narair ātmaguṇāṃbhobhiḥ kṣalitākhilakilbiṣaiḥ  ViP śudraiś ca dvijaśuśrūṣātatparair dvijasattamāḥ tathā strībhir anāyā sātpatiśuśrūṣayaiva hi  ViP tatastritayamapyetanmama dhanyataraṃ matam dharmasaṃpādane kleśo dvijātīnāṃ kṛtādiṣu  ViP bhavadbhir yad abhipretaṃ tadetatkathitaṃ mayā apṛṣṭenāpi dharmajñāḥ kimanyatkriyatāṃ dvijāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥsaṃpūjya te vyāsaṃ praśaśaṃsuḥ punaḥ punaḥ yathāgatandvijā jagmurvyāsoktikṛtaniścayāḥ  ViP bhavato pi mahābhāga rahasyaṃ kathitaṃ mayā atyantaduṣṭasya kalerayameko mahānmuṇaḥ  ViP yaccāhaṃ bhavatā pṛṣṭo jagatāmupasaṃhṛtim prākṛtāmantarālāṃ ca tāmapyeṣa vadāmi te  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumāhapurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe dvitīyo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācasarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ trividhaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ naimittikaḥ prākṛtikaḥ tathaivātyantiko layaḥ  ViP brāhmo naimittikasteṣāṃ kalpānte pratisaṃcaraḥ ātyantikastu mokṣākhyaḥ prākṛto dviparārdhakaḥ  ViP maitreya uvācaparārdhasaṃkhyāṃ bhagavanmamācakṣva yayā tu saḥ dviguṇīkṛtayā jñeyaḥ prākṛtaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācasthānātsthānaṃ daśaguṇamekasmādraṇyate dvija tatoṣṭādaśame bhāge parārdhamabhidhīyate  ViP parārdhadviguṇaṃ yattu prākṛtaḥsa layo dvija tadāvyaktekhilaṃ vyaktaṃ svahetau layameti vai  ViP nimeṣo mānuṣo yo sau mātrāmātrāpramāṇataḥ taiḥ pañcadaśabhiḥ kāṣṭhā triṃśatkāṣṭha kalā smṛtā  ViP nāḍikā tu pramāṇena sā kalā daśa pañca ca  ViP unmānenāṃbhasaḥsā tu palānyardhatrayodaśa māgadhena tu mānena jalaprasthastu sa smṛtaḥ hemamāṣaiḥ kṛtacchidracaturbhiścāturaṅgulaiḥ  ViP nāḍikābhyāmatha dvābhyāṃ muhūrto dvijasattama ahorātraṃ muhurtāstu triṃśanmāso dinais tathā  ViP māsair dvādaśabhir varṣamahorātraṃ tutaddivi tribhir varṣaśatair varṣaṃ ṣaṣṭyā caivāsuradviṣām  ViP tais tu dvādaśasāhastraiś caturyugamudāhṛtam caturyugasahasraṃ tu kathyate brahmaṇo dinam  ViP sa kalpastatra manavaścaturdaśa mahāmune tadante caiva maitreya brāhmo nemittiko layaḥ  ViP tasya svarūpamatyugraṃ maitreya gadato mama śṛṇuṣva prākṛtaṃ bhūyastava vakṣyāmyahaṃ layam  ViP caturyugasahasrānte kṣīṇaprāye mahītale anāvṛṣṭiratīvogrā jāyate śatavārṣikī  ViP tato yānyalpasārāṇi tāni sattvānyaśeṣataḥ kṣayaṃ yānti muniśreṣṭha pārthivānyanupījanāt  ViP tataḥ sabhagavānviṣṇu rudrarūpadharo vyayaḥ kṣayāya yatate kartumātmasthāḥsakalāḥ prajāḥ  ViP tataḥ sa bhagavān viṣṇur bhānoḥ saptasu raśmiṣu sthitaḥ pibatyaśeṣāṇi jalāni munisaptama  ViP pītvāṃbhāṃsi samastāni prāṇibhūmigatānyapi śoṣaṃ nayati maitreya samastaṃ pṛthivītalam  ViP samudrānsāritaḥ śailanadīprasravaṇāni ca pātāleṣu ca yattoyaṃ tatsarvaṃ nayati kṣayam  ViP tatastasyānubhāvena toyāhāropabṛṃhitāḥ ta eva raśmayaḥsapta jāyante sapta bhāskarāḥ  ViP adhaścordhvaṃ ca te dīptā stataḥsapta divākarāḥ dahantyaśaṣaṃ trailokyaṃ sapātālatalaṃ dvija  ViP dahyamānaṃ tu tair dīptais trailokyaṃ dvija bhāskaraiḥ sādrinadyarṇavābhogaṃ nisnehamabhijāyate  ViP tato nirdagdhavṛkṣāṃbutrailokyamākhitaṃ dvija bhavatyeṣā ca vasudhā kūrmapṛṣṭhopamākṛtiḥ  ViP tataḥ kālāgnirudro sau bhūtvā sarvaharo nalaḥ śeṣāhiśvāsasaṃbhūtaḥ pātālāni dahatyadhaḥ  ViP pātālāni samastāni sa dagdhvā jvalano mahān bhūmimabhyetya sakalaṃ babhasti vasudhātalam  ViP bhuvarlokaṃ tataḥsarvaṃ svarlokaṃ ca sudāruṇaḥ jvālāmālāmahāvartastatraiva parivartate  ViP aṃbarīṣamivābhāti trailokyamakhilaṃ tadā jvālāvartaparivāramupakṣīṇacarācaram  ViP tatastāpaparītāstu lokadvayanivāsinaḥ kṛtādhikārāgacchanti maharlokaṃ mahāmune  ViP tasmādapi mahātāpataptā lokāttataḥ param gañcchanti janalokaṃ te daśāvṛttyā paraiṣiṇaḥ  ViP tato dagdhvā jagatsarvaṃ rudrarūpījanārdanaḥ mukhaniśvāsajānmeghānkaroti munisattama  ViP tato gajakulaprakhyāstaḍitvanto tinādinaḥ uttiṣṭhanti tathā vyomnighorāḥsaṃvartakā ghanāḥ  ViP kecinnīlotpalaśyāmāḥ kecitkumudasannibhāḥ dhūmravarṇā ghanāḥ kecitkecitpītāḥ payo dharāḥ  ViP kecidrāsabhavarṇābhā lākṣārasanibhās tathā kecidvaiḍūryasaṃkāśā indranīlanibhāḥ kvacit  ViP śaṅkhakundanibhāś cānye jātyaṃ jananibhāḥ pare indragopanibhāḥ kecit tataḥ śakhinibhās tathā  ViP manaḥśilābhāḥ kecid vai haritālanibhāḥ pare cāṣapatranibhāḥ keciduttiṣṭhante mahāghanāḥ  ViP kecitpuravarākārāḥ kecitparvatasannibhāḥ kūṭāgāranibhāścānye kecitsthalanibā ghanāḥ  ViP mahārāvā mahākāyāḥ pūrayanti nabhaḥsthalam varṣantaste mahāsārāstamagnimatibhairavam śamayantyakhilaṃ vipra trailokyāntaradhiṣṭhitam  ViP naṣṭe cāgnau ca satataṃ varṣamāṇā hyaharniśam plāvayanti jagat sarvam aṃbhobir munisattama  ViP dhārābhir atimātrābhiḥ plāvayitvākhilāṃ bhuvam bhuvarlokaṃ tathevordhū plāvayanti hi te dvija  ViP andhakārīkṛte loke naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame varṣati te mahāmeghā varṣāṇāmadhikaṃ śatam  ViP evaṃ bhavati kalpānte samastaṃ munisattama vāsudevasya māhātmyānnityasya paramātmanaḥ  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe tṛtīyo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācasaptarśisthānāmākramya sthiteṃbhasi mahāmune ekārṇavaṃ bhavatyetattrailokyamakhilaṃ tataḥ  ViP mukhaniśvāsajo viṣṇorvāyustāñjaladāṃstataḥ nāśayanvāti maitreya varṣāṇāmaparaṃ śatam  ViP sarvabhūtamayo cintyo bhagavānbhūtabhāvanaḥ anādirādirviśvasya pītvā vāyumaśeṣataḥ  ViP ekārṇave tatastasmiñcheṣaśayyāgataḥ prabhuḥ brahmarūpadharaḥ śete bhagavānādikṛddhariḥ  ViP janalokagataiḥ siddhaiḥ samakādyair abhiṣṭutaḥ brahmalokagataiś caiva cintyamāno mumukṣubhiḥ  ViP ātmamāyāmayīṃ divyāṃ yoganidrāṃ samāsthitaḥ ātmānaṃ vāsudevākhyaṃ cintayanmadhusūdanaḥ  ViP eṣa naimittiko nāma maitreyaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ nimittaṃ tatra yacchete brahmarūpadharo hariḥ  ViP yadā jāgarti sarvātmā sa tadā ceṣṭate jagat nimīlatyetadakhilaṃ māyāśayyāṃ gate cyute  ViP padmayonerdinaṃ yattu caturyugasahasravat ekārṇavīkṛte loke tāvatī rātririṣyate  ViP tataḥ prabuddho rātryante punaḥsṛṣṭiṃ karotyajaḥ brahmasvarūpadhṛgviṣṇuryathā te kathitaṃ purā  ViP ityeṣa kalpasaṃhāro vāntarapralayo dvija naimittikaste kathitaḥ prākṛtaḥ śṛṇvataḥ param  ViP anāvṛṣṭyādisaṃparkāt kṛte saṃkṣālane mune samasteṣveva lokeṣu pātāleṣvakhileṣu ca  ViP mahadādervikārasya viśeṣāntasya saṃkṣaye kṛṣṇecchākārite tasminpravṛtte pratisaṃcare  ViP āpo grasaṃti vai pūrvaṃ bhūmergandhātmakaṃ guṇam āttagandhā tato bhūmiḥ pralayatvāya kalpate  ViP praṇaṣṭe gandhatanmātre bhavatyurvī jalātmikā āpastadā pravṛddhāstu vegavatyo mahāsvanāḥ  ViP sarvamāpūrayantīdaṃ tiṣṭhanti vicaranti ca salilenormimālena ālokāntātsamantataḥ  ViP apāmapi guṇo yastu jyotiṣā pīyate tu saḥ naśyantyāpastatastāś ca rasatanmātrasaṃkṣayāt  ViP tataścāpo hṛtarasājyotiṣaṃ prāpnuvanti vai agnāvasthe tu salile tejasā sarvato vṛte  ViP sa cāgniḥ sarvato vyāpya cādatte tajjalaṃ tathā sarvamāpūryatercirbhis tadā jagadidaṃ śanaiḥ  ViP arcirbhiḥ saṃvṛte tasmiṃstiryagūrdhvamadhastadā jyotiṣo pi paraṃ rūpaṃ vāyuratti prabhākaram  ViP pralīne ca tatastasminvāyubhūte khilātmani pranaṣṭe rūpatanmātre hṛtarūpo vibhāvasuḥ  ViP praśāmyati tadājyotirvāyurdedhūyate mahān nirā loke tathā loke vāyvavasthe ca tejasi  ViP tatastu mūlamāsādya vāyuḥsaṃbhavamātmanaḥ ūrdhvaṃ cādhaś ca tiryakca dodhavīti diśo daśa  ViP vāyorapi guṇaṃ sparśamākāśo grasate tataḥ praśāmyati tato vāyuḥ khaṃ tu tiṣṭhatyanāvṛtam  ViP arūparasamasparśamagandhaṃ na ca mūrtimat sarvamāpūrayaccaiva sumahāttatprakāśate  ViP bhūtendriyeṣu yugapadbhūtādau saṃsthiteṣu vai abimānātmako hyeṣa bhūtādistāmasaḥsmṛtaḥ  ViP bhītādiṃ grasate cāpi mahānve buddhilakṣaṇaḥ  ViP urvī mahaṃś ca jagataḥ pratintarbāhyatas tathā  ViP evaṃ sapta mahābuddhe kramātprakṛtayaḥsmṛtāḥ pratyāhāre tu tāḥsarvāḥ praviśanti parasparam  ViP yenedamāvṛtaṃ sarvamaṇḍamapsu pralīyate saptadvīpasamudrāntaṃ saptalokaṃ saparvatam  ViP udakāvaraṇaṃ yattu jyotiṣā pīyate tu tam jyotirvāyau layaṃ yāti yātyākāśe samīramaḥ  ViP ākāśaṃ caiva bhūtādirgrasate taṃ tathā mahān mahāntamebhiḥ sahitaṃ prakṛtirgrasate dvija  ViP gumasāmyamanudriktamanyūnaṃ ca mahāmune procyate prakatirhetuḥ pradhānaṅkāraṇaṃ param  ViP ityeṣā prakṛtiḥsarvā vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇī vyaktasvarūpamavyakte tasmānmaitreya līyate  ViP ekaḥ śuddho kṣaro nityaḥsarvavyāpī tathā pumān so py aṃśaḥsarvabhūtasya maitreya paramātmanaḥ  ViP na saṃti yatra sarveśe nāmajātyādikalpanāḥ sattāmātratmake jñeye jñānātmanyātmanaḥ pare  ViP tadbrahma paramaṃ dhāma paramātmā sa ceśvaraḥ sa viṣṇuḥsarvamevedaṃ yato nāvartate yatiḥ  ViP prakṛtiryā mayākhyātā vyaktāvyaktasvarūpiṇī puruṣaścāpyubhāvetau liyate paramātmani  ViP paramātmā ca sarveṣāmādhāraḥ parameśvaraḥ viṣṇunāmā sa vedeṣu vedānteṣu ca gīyate  ViP pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca dvividhaṅkarma vaidikam tābhyāmubhābhyāṃ puruṣaiḥ sarvamūrtiḥsa ijyate  ViP ṛgyajuḥsāmabhir mārgaiḥ pravṛtterijyate hyasau yajñeśvaro yajñapumānpuruṣaiḥ puruṣottamaḥ  ViP jñānātmā jñānayogena jñānamūrtiḥ sa cejyate nivṛtte yogibhir mārge viṣṇurmuktiphalapradaḥ  ViP hrasvadīrghaplutair yattu kiñcidvastvabhidhīyate yacca vācāmaviṣayaṃ tatsarvaṃ viṣṇuravyayaḥ  ViP vyaktaḥsa eva cāvyaktaḥsa eva puruṣottamaḥ paramātmā ca viśvātmā viśvarūpadharohariḥ  ViP vyaktāvyaktātmikā tasminprakṛtiḥsaṃpralīyate puruṣaścāpi maitreya vyāpinyavyāhatātmani  ViP dviparārdhātmakaḥ kālaḥ kathito yo mayā tava tadahastasya maitreya viṣṇorīśasya kathyate  ViP vyakte ca prakṛtau līne prakṛtyāṃ puruṣe tathā tatra sthite niśā cāsya tatpramāṇā mahāmune  ViP naivāhastasya na niśā nityasya paramātmanaḥ upacārastathāpyeṣa tasyeśasya dvijocyate  ViP ityeṣa tava maitreya kathitaḥ prākṛto layaḥ ātyantikamatho brahmannibodha pratisaṃcaram  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe caturtho dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaādhyātmikādi maitreya jñātvā tāpatrayaṃ budhaḥ utpannajñānavairāgyaṃ prāpnotyātyantikaṃ layam  ViP ādhyātmikopi dvividhaḥ śarīro mānasas tathā śarīro bahubhir bhedair bhidyate śruyatāṃ ca saḥ  ViP śirorogapratiśyāyajvaraśūlabhagandaraiḥ gulmārśaḥ śvayayuśvāsacchardyādibhir anekadhā  ViP tathākṣirogātīsārakuṣṭhāṅgāmayasaṃjñitaiḥ bhidyate dehajastāpo mānasaṃ śrotumarhasi  ViP kāmakrodhabhayadveṣalobhamohaviṣādajaḥ śokāsūyāvamānerṣyāmātsaryādimayas tathā  ViP mānaso pi dvijaśreṣṭha tāpo bhavati naikadhā ityevamādibhir bhedais tāpo hyādhyātmikaḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP mṛgapakṣimanuṣyādyaiḥ piśācoragarākṣasaiḥ sarīsṛpādyaiś ca nṛṇāṃ jāyate cādhibhautikaḥ  ViP śītavā toṣṇavārṣābubaidyutādisamudbhavaḥ tāpo dvijavaraśreṣṭhaiḥ kathyate cādhidaivikaḥ  ViP garbhajanmajarājñānamṛtyunārakajaṃ tathā duḥkhaṃ sahasraśo bhedair bhidyate munisattama  ViP sukumāratanurgarbhe janturbahumalāvṛte ulvasaṃveṣṭito bhugnapṛṣṭhagrīvāsthisaṃhatiḥ  ViP atyamlakaṭutīkṣmoṣṇalavaṇair mātṛbhojanaiḥ atyantatāpair atyarthaṃ vardhamānātivedanaḥ  ViP prasāraṇākuñcanādau nāṅgānāṃ prabhurātmanaḥ śakṛnmūtramahāpaṅkaśāyī sarvatra pīḍitaḥ  ViP nirucchvāsaḥ sacaitanyaḥ smarañ janmaśatāny atha āste garbhe tiduḥkhena nijakarmanibandhanaḥ  ViP jāyamānaḥ purīṣāsṛṅmūtraśukrāvilānanaḥ prājāpatyena vātena pīḍyamānāsthibandhanaḥ  ViP adhomukho vai kriyate prabalaiḥ sūtimārutaiḥ kleśānniṣkrāntimāpnoti jaṭharānmāturāturaḥ  ViP murchāmavāpya mahatīṃ saṃspṛṣṭo bāhyavāyunā vijñānabhraṃśamāpnoti jātaś ca munisattama  ViP kaṇṭakair iva tunnāṅgaḥ krakacair iva dāritaḥ pūtivraṇānnipatito dharaṇyāṃ krimiko yathā  ViP kaṇḍūyane pi cāśaktaḥ parivartepyanīśvaraḥ snānapānādikāhāram apy āpnoti parecchayā  ViP aśuciprastare suptaḥ kīṭadraṃśādibhis tathā bhakṣyamāṇo pi naivaiṣāṃ samartho vinivāraṇe  ViP janmaduḥkhānyanekāni janmanonantariṇī ca bālabhāve yadā pnoti hyādhibhautādikāni ca  ViP ajñānatamasācchanno mūḍhāntaḥkaraṇo naraḥ na jānāti kutaḥ kohaṃ kvāhaṃ gantā kimātmanaḥ  ViP kenabandhena baddhohaṃ kāraṇaṃ kimakāraṇam kiṃ kāryaṃ kimakāryaṃ vā kiṃ vācyaṃ kiṃ ca nocyate  ViP ko dharmaḥ kaś ca vādharmaḥ kasminvarte tha vā katham kiṃ kartavyamakartavyaṃ kiṃ vā kiṅguṇadoṣavat  ViP evaṃ paśusamair muḍhair ajñānaprabhavaṃ mahat avāpyate narair duḥkhaṃ śiśrodaraparāyaṇaiḥ  ViP ajñānaṃ tāmaso bhāvaḥ kāryāraṃbhapravṛttayaḥ ajñānināṃ pravartante karmalopāstato dvija  ViP narakaṃ karmaṇāṃ lopātphalamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ tasmādajñānināṃ duḥkhamiha cāmutra cottamam  ViP jarājarjaradehaś ca śithilāvayavaḥ pumān vicalacchīrṇadaśano valisnāyuśirāvṛtaḥ  ViP dūrapranaṣṭanayano vyomāntargatatārakaḥ nāsāvivalaniryātalomapuñjaścaladvapuḥ  ViP prakaṭībhūtasarvāsthirnatapṛṣṭhāsthisaṃhatiḥ utsannajaṭharāgnitvād alpāhāro placeṣṭitaḥ  ViP kṛcchrāccaṅkramaṇotthānaśayanāsanaceṣṭitaḥ mandībhavacchrotranetraḥsravallālāvilānanaḥ  ViP anāyattaiḥ samastaiś ca karaṇermaraṇonmukhaḥ tatkṣaṇepyanubhūtānāmasmartakhilavastunām  ViP sakṛduccārite vākye samudbhūta mahāśramaḥ śvāsakāśasamudbhūtamahāyāsaprajāgaraḥ  ViP anyenotthāpyate nyena tathā saṃveśyate jarī bhṛtyātmaputradārāṇāmavāmānāspadī kṛtaḥ  ViP prakṣīṇākhilaśaucaś ca vihārāhārasaspṛhaḥ hāsyaḥ parijanasyāpi nirviṇṇāśeṣabāndhavaḥ  ViP anubhūtamivānyasmiñjanmanyātmaviceṣṭitam saṃsmaranyauvane dīrghaṃ niśvasatyabhitāpitaḥ  ViP evamādīni duḥkhāni jarāyāmanubūya vai maraṇe yāni duḥkhāni prāpnoti śṛṇutānyapi  ViP ślathadgrīvāṅghrihaste tha vyāpto vepathunā bhṛśam muhurglāniḥ paravaśo muhurjñānalavānvitaḥ  ViP hiraṇyadhānyatanayabhāryābhṛtyagṛhādiṣu ete kathaṃ bhaviṣyantītyatīva mamatākulaḥ  ViP marmabhidbhir bhahārogaiḥ krakacair iva dāruṇaiḥ śarair ivāntakasyograiś chadyamānāsubandhanaḥ  ViP parivartitatārākṣo hastapādaṃ muhuḥ kṣipan saṃśuṣyamāṇatālvoṣṭhapuṭo ghuraghurāyate  ViP niruddhakaṇṭho doṣaughair udānaśvasāpīḍitaḥ tāpena mahatā vyāptastṛṣā cārtas tathā kṣudhā  ViP kleśādutkrāntimāpnoti yamakiṅkarapīḍitaḥ tataś ca yātanādehaṃ kleśena pratipadyate  ViP etānyanyāni cogrāṇi duḥkhāni maraṇe nṛṇām śṛṇuṣva narake yāni prāpyante puruṣair mṛtaiḥ  ViP yāmyakiṅkarapāśādigrahaṇaṃ daṇḍatāḍanam yamasya darśanaṃ cogramugramārgavilokanam  ViP karaṃbhavālukāvahniyantraśastrāsibhīṣaṇe pratyekaṃ narakeyāś ca yātanā dvija duḥsahāḥ  ViP krakacaiḥ pāṭyamānānāṃ mūṣāyāṃ cāpi dahyatām kuṭhāraiḥ kṛtyamānānāṃ bhūmau cāpi nikhanyatām  ViP śūleṣvāropyamāṇānaṃ vyāghravaktre praveśyatām gṛdhraiḥ saṃbhakṣyamāṇānāṃ dvīpibhiścopabhūjyatām  ViP kvāthyatāṃ tailamadhye ca klidyatāṃ kṣārakardame uccānnipātyamānānāṃ kṣipyatāṃ kṣepayantrakaiḥ  ViP narake yāni duḥkhāni pāpahetūdbhavāni vai prāpyante nārakair vipra teṣāṃ saṃkhyā na vidyate  ViP na kevalaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha narake duḥkhapaddhatiḥ svagaṃpi pātabhītasta kṣayiṣṇornāsti nirvṛtiḥ  ViP punaś ca garbhe bhavati jāyate ca punaḥ punaḥ garbhe vilīyate bhūyo jāyamāno stameti vai  ViP jātamātraś ca mriyate bālabhāve tha yauvane madhyamaṃ vā vayaḥ prāpya vārdhake vātha vā mṛtiḥ  ViP yāvajjīvati tāvacca duḥkhair nānāvidhaiḥ plutaḥ taṃ tu kāraṇapakṣmaughair āste kārpāsabījavat  ViP dravyanāśe tathotpattau pālane ca sadā nṛṇām bhavantyanekaduḥkhāni tathaiveṣṭavipattiṣu  ViP yadyatprītikaraṃ puṃsāṃ vastu maitreya jāyate tadeva duḥkhavṛkṣasya bījatvamupagacchati  ViP kalatraputramitrārthagṛhakṣetradhanādikaiḥ kriyate na tathā bhūri sukhaṃ puṃsāṃ yathā sukham  ViP iti saṃsāraduḥkhārkatāpatāpitacetasām vimuktipādapacchāyāmṛte kutra sukhaṃ nṛṇām  ViP tadasya trividhastapi duḥkhajātasya vai mama garbhajanmajarādyeṣu sthāneṣu prabhaviṣyataḥ  ViP nirastātiśayāhlādasukhabhāvaikalakṣaṇā bheṣajaṃ bhagavatprāptirekāntātyantikī matā  ViP tasmāt tatprāptaye yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ paṇḍitair naraiḥ tatprāptiheturjñānaṃ ca karma coktaṃ mahāmune  ViP āgamotthaṃ vivekācca dvidhā jñānaṃ tad ucyate śabdabrahmāgamamayaṃ paraṃ brahma vivekajam  ViP andhaṃ tama ivājñānaṃ dīpavaccendriyodbhavam yathā sūryas tathā jñānaṃ yadviprarṣe vivekajam  ViP manurapyāha vedārthaṃ smṛtvā yanmunisattama tadetacchrūyatāmatra saṃbandhe gadato mama  ViP dve brahmaṇī veditavye śabdabrahma paraṃ ca yat śabdabrahmaṇi niṣṇātaḥ paraṃ brahmādhigacchati  ViP dve vai vidye veditavye iti cātharvaṇī śrutiḥ parayā tvakṣaraprāptirṛgvedādimayāparā  ViP yat tad avyaktam ajaram acintyam ajam avyayam anirdeśyamarūpaṃ ca pāṇipādādyasaṃyutam  ViP vibhu sarvagataṃ nityaṃ bhūtayonirakāraṇam vyāpya vyāptaṃ yataḥ sarvaṃ yad vai paśyanti sūrayaḥ  ViP tadbrahma tatparaṃ dhāma tad dhyeyaṃ mokṣakāṃkṣibhiḥ śrutivākyoditaṃ sūkṣmaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam  ViP tadeva bhagavadvācyaṃ svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ vācako bhagavacchabdastasyādyasvākṣayātmanaḥ  ViP evaṃ nigaditārthasta tattattvaṃ tasya tattvataḥ jñāyate yena tajjñānaṃ paramanyattrayīmayam  ViP aśabdagocarasyāpi tasya vai brahmaṇo dvija pūjāyāṃ bhagavacchabdaḥ kriyate hyupacārataḥ  ViP śuddhe mahāvibhūtvākhye pare brahmaṇi śabdite maitreya bhagavacchabdaḥsarvakāraṇakāraṇe  ViP saṃbharteti tathā bhartā bhakārorthadvayānvitaḥ netā gamayatā sraṣṭā gakārārthas tathā mune  ViP aiśvaryasya samagrasya vīryasya yaśasaḥ śriyaḥ jñānavairāgyayoścaiva ṣaṇṇāṃ bhaga itīraṇā  ViP vasaṃti tatra bhūtāni bhūtātmanyakhilātmani sa ca bhūteṣvaśeṣeṣu vakārārthastato vyayaḥ  ViP evameṣa mahāñchabdo maitreya bhagavāniti paramabrahmabhūtasya vāsudevasya nānyagaḥ  ViP tatra pūjyapadārthoktiparibhāṣāsamanvitaḥ śabdo yaṃ nopacāreṇa tvanyatra hy upacārataḥ  ViP utpattiṃ pralayaṃ caiva bhūtānāmāgatiṃ gatim vetti vidyāmāvidyāṃ ca sa vācyo bhagavāniti  ViP jñānaśaktibalaiśvayavīryatejāṃsyaśeṣataḥ bhagavacchabdavācyāti vinā heyair guṇādibhiḥ  ViP sarvāṇi tatra bhūtāni vasāṃti paramātmani bhūteṣu ca sa sarvātmā vāsudevastataḥ smṛtaḥ  ViP khāṇḍikyajanakāyāha pṛṣṭaḥ keśidhvajaḥ purā nābhavyākhyāmanantasya vāsudevasya tattvataḥ  ViP bhūteṣu vasate soṃtarvasaṃtyatra ca tāni yat dhātā vidhātā jagatāṃ svaśaktileśāvṛtabhūtavargaḥ icchāgṛhītābhimatorudehaḥsaṃsādhitāśeṣajagadvito yaḥ  ViP tejobalaiśvaryamahāvabodha suvīryaśaktyādiguṇaikarāśiḥ paraḥ parāṇāṃ sakalā na yatra kleśādayaḥsaṃti parāvareśe  ViP sa īśvaro vyaṣṭisamaṣṭirūpo vyaktasvarūpaḥ sarveśvaraḥsarvadṛk sarvavicca samastaśaktiḥ parameśvarākhyaḥ  ViP saṃjñāyate yena tadastadoṣaṃ śuddhaṃ paraṃ nirmalamekarūpam saṃdṛśyate vāpyavagamyate vā tajjñānamajñānamatonyaduktam  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe pañcamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācasvādhyāyasaṃyamābhyāṃ sa dṛśyate puruṣottamaḥ tatprāptikāraṇaṃ brahma tad etad iti paṭhyate  ViP svādhyāyādhyogamāsīta yogātsvādhyāyamāvaset svādhyāyayogasaṃpattyā paramātmā prakāśate  ViP tadīkṣaṇāya svādhyāyaścakṣuryogas tathā param na māṃ sa cakṣuṣā draṣṭuṃ brahmabhūtaḥsa śakyate  ViP maitreya uvācabhagavaṃstamahaṃ yogaṃ jñātumicchāmi taṃ vada jñāte yatrākhilādhāraṃ paśyeyaṃ parameśvaram  ViP śrīparāśara uvācayathā keśidhvajaḥ prāha khāṇḍikyāya mahātmane najakāya purā yoga tamahaṃ kathayāmi te  ViP maitreya uvācakhāṇḍikya ko bhavadbrahmanko vā keśidhvajaḥ kṛtī kathaṃ tayoś ca saṃvādo yogasaṃbandhakāraṇāt  ViP śrīparāśara uvācadharmadhvajo vai janaka stasya putro mitadhvajaḥ kṛtadhvajaś ca nāmnāsītsadādhyātmaratirnṛpaḥ  ViP kṛtadhvajasya putro bhūtkhyātaḥ keśidhvajo nṛpaḥ putromitadhvajasyāpi khāṇḍikyajanako bhavat  ViP karmamārgeṇa khāṇḍikyaḥ pṛtivyāmabhavatpatiḥ keśidhvajo pyatīvāsīdātmavidyāviśāradaḥ  ViP tāvubhāvapi caivāstāṃ vijigīṣū parasparam keśidhyajena khāṇḍikyaḥsvarājyādavaropitaḥ  ViP purodhasā mantribhiś ca samaveto lpasādhanaḥ rājyānnirākṛtaḥso tha durgāraṇyacaro bhavat  ViP iyāha so pi subahūnyajñāñjñānavyapāśrayaḥ brahmavidyāmadhiṣṭhāya tarttu mṛtyumavidyayā  ViP ekadā varttamānasya yāgo yogavidāṃ vara gharmadhenuṃ jaghānograḥ śārdulo vijane vane  ViP tato rājā hatāṃ śrutvā dhanuṃ vyāghreṇa cartvijaḥ prāyaścitaṃ sa papraccha kimatreti vidhīyatām  ViP tepyūcurna vayaṃ vidma kaśeruḥ pṛcchatāmiti kaśerurapi tenoktastathaiva prāha bhārgavam  ViP śunakaṃ pṛccha rājaindra nāhaṃ vedmi sa vetsyati sa gatvā kamapṛcchacca so py āha śṛṇu yanmune  ViP na keśarurna caivāhaṃ na caikaḥsāṃprataṃ bhuvi vettyeka eva tvacchatruḥ khāṇḍikyo yo jitastvayā  ViP sa cāha taṃ vrajāmyeṣa praṣṭumātmarīpuṃ mune prāpta eva mahāyajño yadi māṃ sa haniṣyati  ViP prāyaścittamaśeṣeṇa sa cetpṛṣṭo vadiṣyati tataścāvikalo yogo muniśreṣṭha bhaviṣyati  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā rathamāruhya kṛṣṇājinadharo nṛpaḥ vanaṃ jagāma yatrāste sa khāṇḍikyo mahāmatiḥ  ViP tamāpatantamālokya khāṇḍikyo ripumātmanaḥ provāca krodhatāmrākṣaḥsamāropitakārmukaḥ  ViP khāṇḍikya uvācakṛṣṇājinaṃ tvaṃ kavacamābadhyāsmānhaniṣyasi kṛṣṇājinadhare vetsi na mayi prahariṣyati  ViP mṛgāṇāṃ vada pṛṣṭheṣu mūḍha kṛṣṇājinaṃ na kim yeṣāṃ mayā tvāya cogrāḥ prahitāḥ śitasāyakāḥ  ViP sa tvāmahaṃ haniṣyāmi na me jīvanvimokṣyase ātatāyyasi durbuddhe mama rājyaharo ripuḥ  ViP keśidhvaja uvācakhāṇḍikya saṃśayaṃ praṣṭuṃ bhavantamahāmāgataḥ na tvāṃ hantuṃ vicāryaitatkopaṃ bāṇaṃ vimuñca vā  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥsa mantribhiḥ sārdhamekānte sapurohitaḥ mantrayāmāsa khāṇḍikyaḥsarvair eva mahāmatiḥ  ViP tamūcurmatriṇo vadhyo ripureṣa vaśaṃ gataḥ hate smin pṛthivī sarvā tava vaśyā bhaviṣyati  ViP khāṇḍikyaścāha tānsarvānevametanna saṃśayaḥ hatesminpṛtivī sarvā mama vaśyā bhaviṣyati  ViP paralokajayastasya pṛthivī sakalā mama na hanmi cellokajayo mama tasya vasuṃdharā  ViP nāhaṃ manye lokajayādadhikā syādvasuṃdharā paralokajayo nantaḥsvalpakālo mahījayaḥ  ViP tasmānnainaṃ haniṣyāmi yatpṛcchati vadāmi tat  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatatastamabyupetyāha khāṇḍikyajanako ripum praṣṭavyaṃ yattvāya sarvaṃ tatpṛcchasva vadāmyaham  ViP śrīparāśara uvācatataḥ sarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ gharmadhenuvadhaṃ dvija kathāṃyatvā sa papraccha prāyaśtittaṃ hi tadgatam  ViP sa cācaṣṭa yathānyāyaṃ dvija keśidhvajāya tat prāyaścittamaśeṣeṇa yaddhai tatra vidhīyate  ViP viditārthaḥsa tenaiva hyanujñāto mahātmanā yāgabhūmim upāgamya cakre sarvāḥ kriyāḥ kramāt  ViP krameṇa vidhivadyāgaṃ nītvā so vabhṛthāplutaḥ kṛtakṛtyastato bhūtvā cintayāmāsa pārthivaḥ  ViP pūjitāś ca dvijāḥsarve sadasyā mānitā mayā tathaivārthijano py arthair yo rjito bhimatair mayā  ViP yathārhamasya lokasya mayā sarvaṃ viceṣṭitam aniṣpannakriyaṃ cetastathāpi mama kiṃ yathā  ViP itthaṃ saṃcintayannaiva sasmāra sa mahīpatiḥ khāṇḍikyāya na datteti mayā vai gurudakṣiṇā  ViP sa jagāma tadā bhūyo rathamāruhya pārthivaḥ maitreya durgagahanaṃ khāṇḍikyo yatra saṃsthitaḥ  ViP khāṇḍikyo pi punardṛṣṭvā tamāyāntaṃ dhṛtāyudham tasthau hantuṃ kṛtamatistamāha sa punarnṛpaḥ  ViP bho nāhaṃ te parādhāya prāptaḥ khāṇḍikya mā kruddhāḥ gurornikrayadānāya māmavehi tvamāgatam  ViP niṣpādito mayā yāgaḥ samyaktvadupadeśataḥ so haṃ te dātumicchāmi vṛṇīṣva gurudakṣiṇām  ViP śrīparāśara uvācabhūyasya mantribhiḥ sārdhaṃ mantrayāmāsa pārthivaḥ guruniṣkrayakāmo yaṃ kiṃ mayā prārthyatāmiti  ViP tamūcurmatriṇo rājyamaśaṃṣaṃ prārthyatāmayam śatribhiḥ prārthyate rājyamanā yāsitasainikaiḥ  ViP prahasya tānāha nṛpaḥsa khāṇḍikyo mahāmatiḥ svalpakālaṃ mahīpālyaṃ mādṛśaiḥ prārthyate katham  ViP evametadbhavanto tra hyarthasādhanamantriṇaḥ paramārthaḥ kathaṃ ko tra yūyaṃ nātra vicakṣaṇāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaityuktvā samupetyainaṃ sa tu keśidhvajaṃ nṛpaḥ uvāca kimavaśyaṃ tvaṃ dadāsi gurudakṣiṇām  ViP bāḍhamityeva tenoktaḥ khāṇḍikyastamathābravīt bhavānadyātma vijñānaparamārthavicakṣaṇaḥ  ViP yadi ceddīyate mahyaṃ bhavatā guruniṣkrayaḥ tatkleśapraśamāyālaṃ yatkarma tadudīraya  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe ṣaṣṭhodhyāyaḥ keśidhvaja uvācana prārthitaṃ tvayā kasmādasmadrājyamakaṇṭakam rājyalābhādvinā nānyatkṣatriyāṇā matipriyam  ViP khāṇḍikya uvācakeśidhvaja nibodha tvaṃ mayā na prārthitaṃ yataḥ rājyametadaśeṣaṃ te yatra gṛdhnantyapaṇḍitāḥ  ViP kṣatriyāṇāmayaṃ dharmo yatprajāparipālanam vadhaś ca dharmayuddhena svarājyaparipanthinām  ViP tatrāśaktasya me doṣo naivāstyapahṛte tvayā bandhāyaiva bhavatyeṣā hyavidyāpyakramojjhitā  ViP alpopabhogalipsārtham iyaṃ rājyaspṛhā mama anyeṣāṃ doṣaja saiva dharmaṃ vai nānurudhyate  ViP na yācñā kṣatrabandhūnāṃ dharmayaitatsatāṃ matam ato na yācitaṃ rājyamavidyāntargataṃ tava  ViP rājye gṛdhnantyavidvāṃso mamatvāhṛtacetasaḥ ahaṃmānamahāpānamadamattā na mādṛśāḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaprahṛṣṭaḥsādhviti tataḥ prāha keśidhvajo nṛpaḥ khāṇḍikyajanakaṃ prītyā śrūyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama  ViP keśidhvaja uvācaahaṃ hyavidyayā kṛtyuṃ tartukāmaḥ karomi vai rājyaṃ yāgāṃś ca vividhānyogaiḥ puṇyakṣayaṃ tathā  ViP tadidaṃ te mano diṣṭyā vivekaiśvaryatāṃ gatam tacchrūyatāmavidyāyāḥsvarūpaṃ kulanandana  ViP anātmanyātmabuddhiryā cāsve svamiti yā matiḥ saṃsāratarusaṃbhūtibījametaddvidhā sthitam  ViP pañcabhūtātmake dehe dehī mohatamovṛtaḥ ahaṃ mamaitadityuccaiḥ kurute kumatirmatim  ViP ākāśavāyvagnijalapṛthivībhyaḥ pṛthak sthite ātmanyātmamayaṃ bhāvaṃ kaḥ karoti kalevare  ViP kalevaropabhogyaṃhi gṛhakṣetrādikaṃ ca kaḥ adehe hyātmani prājñe mamedamiti manyate  ViP itthaṃ ca puttrapauttreṣu taddehotpāditeṣu kaḥ karoti paṇḍitaḥsvāmyamanātmani kalevare  ViP sarvaṃ dehopabhogāya kurute karma mānavaḥ dehaścānyo yadā puṃsastadā bandhāya tatparam  ViP mṛṇmayaṃ hi yathā gehaṃ lipyate vai mṛdaṃbhasā pārthivo yaṃ tathā deho mṛdaṃbvālepanasthitaḥ  ViP pañjabhūtatmakair bhogoḥ pañcabhūtātmakaṃ vapuḥ āpyāyate yadi tataḥ puṃso bhogo tra kiṃ kṛtaḥ  ViP anekajanmasāhasrīṃ saṃsārapadavīṃ vrajan mohaśramaṃ prayāto sau vāsanaremukuṇṭhitaḥ  ViP prakṣālyate yadā sosya reṇujñānoṣṇavāriṇā tadā saṃsārapānthasya yāti mohaśramaḥ śamam  ViP mohaśrame śamaṃ yāte svasthāntaḥkaraṇaḥ pumān ananyātiśayābādhaṃ paraṃ nirvāṇamṛcchati  ViP nirvāṇamaya evāyam ātmā jñānamayo malaḥ duḥkhājñānamayā dharmāḥ prakṛtes te tu nātmanaḥ  ViP jalasya nāgnisaṃsargasthālīsaṃgāttathāpi hi śabdodrekādikāndharmāṃstatkaroti yathā nṛpa  ViP tathātmā prakṛteḥsaṃgādahaṃmānādidūṣitaḥ bhajate prākṛtān dharmān anyas tebhyo hi so vyayaḥ  ViP tadetatkathitaṃ bījamavidyāyā mayā tava kleśānāṃ ca kṣayakaraṃ yogādanyanna vidyate  ViP khāṇḍikya uvācataṃ bravīhi mahābhāga yogaṃ yogaviduttama vijñātayogaśāstrārthastvamasyāṃ nimisaṃtatau  ViP keśidhvaja uvācayogasvarūpaṃ khāṇḍikya śrūyatāṃ gadato mama yatra sthito na cyavate prāpya brahmalayaṃ muniḥ  ViP mana eva manuṣyāṇāṃ kāraṇaṃ bandhamokṣayoḥ bandhāya viṣayāsaṃgi muktyai nirviṣayaṃ manaḥ  ViP viṣayebhyaḥ samāhṛtya vijñānātmāmano muniḥ cintayenmuktaye tena brahmabhūtaṃ pareśvaram  ViP ātmabhāvaṃ nayatyenaṃ tadbahya dhyāyinaṃ munim vikāryamātmanaḥ śaktyā lohamākarṣako yathā  ViP ātmaprayatnasāpekṣā viśiṣṭā yā manogatiḥ tasya brahmaṇi saṃyogo yoga ityabhidhīyate  ViP evamatyantavaiśiṣṭyayuktadharmopalakṣaṇaḥ yasya yogaḥsa vai yogī mumukṣurabhidhīyate  ViP yogayuk prathamaṃ yogī yuñjāno hyabhidhīyate viniṣpannasamādhistu paraṃ brahmopalabdhimān  ViP yadyantarāyadoṣeṇa dūṣyate cāsya mānasam janmāntarair abhyasato muktiḥ purvasya jāyate  ViP viniṣpannasamādhistu muktiṃ tatraiva janmani prāpnoti yogī yogāgnidagdhakarmacayo cirāt  ViP brahmacaryamahiṃsāṃ ca satyāsteyāparigrahān seveta yogī niṣkāmo yogyatāṃ svamano nayan  ViP svādhyāyaśaucasaṃtoṣatapāṃsi niyatātmavān kurvīta brahmaṇi tathā parasminpravaṇaṃmanaḥ  ViP ete yamāḥsaniyamāḥ pañca pañca ca kīrtitāḥ viśiṣṭaphaladāḥ kāmyā niṣkāmānāṃ vimuktidāḥ  ViP ekaṃ bhadrāsanādīnāṃ samāsthāya guṇair yutaḥ yamākhyair niyamākhyaiś ca yuñjīta niyato yatiḥ  ViP prāṇākhyamanilaṃ vaśyamabhyāsātkurute tu yat prāṇāyāmaḥsavijñeyaḥsabījo bīja eva ca  ViP paraspareṇābhibhavaṃ prāṇāpānau yathānilau kurutaḥsadvidhānena tṛtīyaḥsaṃyamāttayoḥ  ViP tasya cālaṃbanavataḥ sthūlarūpaṃ dvijottama ālaṃbanamanantasya yogino bhyasataḥ smṛtam  ViP śabdādiṣvanuraktāni nigṛhyākṣāṇi yogavit kuryāccittānukārīṇi pratyāhāraparāyaṇaḥ  ViP vaśyatā paramā tena jāyateti calātmanām indriyāṇāmavaśyais tair na yogī yogasādhakaḥ  ViP prāṇayāmena pavane pratyāhāreṇa cendriye vaśīkṛte tataḥ kuryātsthitaṃ cetaḥ śubhāśraye  ViP khāḍikya uvācakathyatāṃ me mahābhāgā cetaso yaḥ śubhāśrayaḥ yadādhāramaśeṣaṃ taddhanti doṣamalodbhavam  ViP keśidhvāja uvācaāśrayaścetaso brahma dvidhā taccasvabhāvataḥ bhūpa mūrtamamūrtaṃ ca paraṃ cāparameva ca  ViP trividhā bhāvanā bhūpa viśvametannibodhatām brahmākhyā karmasaṃjñā ca tathā caivobhayātmikā  ViP karmabhāvātmikā hyekābrahmabhāvātmikā parā ubhayātmikā tathaivānyā trividhā bhāvabhāvanā  ViP sanandanādayo ye tu brahmabhāvanayā yutāḥ karmabhāvanayā cānye devādyāḥ sthāvarāvarāḥ  ViP hiraṇyagarbhādiṣu ca brahmakarmātmikā dvidhā bodhādhikārayukteṣu vidyate bhāvabhāvanā  ViP akṣīṇeṣu samasteṣu viśeṣajñānakarmasu viśvametatparaṃ cānyadbhedabhinnadṛśāṃ nṛṇām  ViP pratyastamitabhedaṃ yatsattāmātramagocaram vacasāmātmasaṃvedyaṃ tajjñānaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam  ViP tacca viṣṇoḥ paraṃ rūpamarūpākhyamanuttamam viśvasvarūpavairūpyalakṣaṇaṃ paramātmanaḥ  ViP na tadyogayujā śakyaṃ nṛpa cintayituṃyataḥ tataḥsthūlaṃ hare rūpaṃ cintayedviśvagocaram  ViP hiraṇyagarbho bhagavānvāsudevaḥ prajāpatiḥ maruto vasavo rudrā bhāskarāstārakā grahāḥ  ViP gandharvayakṣadaityādyaḥsakalā devayonayaḥ manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ śailāḥsamudrāḥsarito drumāḥ  ViP bhūpa bhūtānyaśeṣāṇi bhūtānāṃ ye ca hetavaḥ pradhānādiviśeṣāntaṃ cetanācetanātmakam  ViP ekapādaṃ dvipādaṃ ca bahupādamapādakam mūrtametaddhare rūpaṃ bhāvanātritayātmakam  ViP etatsarvamidaṃ viśvaṃ jagadetaccarācaram parabrahmasvarūpasya viṣṇoḥ śaktisamanvitam  ViP viṣṇuśaktiḥ parā proktā kṣetrajñākhyā tathāparā avidyākarmasaṃjñānyā tṛtīyā śaktiriṣyate  ViP yayā kṣetrajñaśaktiḥsā veṣṭitā nṛpasarvagā saṃsāratāpānakhilānavāprotyatisaṃtatān  ViP tayā tirohitatvācca śaktiḥ kṣetrajñasaṃjñitā sarvabhūteṣu bhūpāla tāratamyenalakṣyate  ViP aprāṇavatsusvalpā sā sthāvareṣu tato dhikā sarīsṛpeṣu tebhyopi hyatiśaktyā patattriṣu  ViP pātattriṃbhyo mṛgāstebhyastacchaktyā paśavo dhikāḥ paśubhyo manujāścātiśaktyā puṃsaḥ prabhāvitāḥ  ViP tebhyopi nāgagandharvayakṣādyā devatā nṛpa  ViP śakraḥsamastadevebhyastataścātiprajāpatiḥ hiraṇyagarbho pi tataḥ puṃsaḥ śaktyupalakṣitaḥ  ViP etānyaśeṣarūpāṇi tasya rūpāṇi pārthiva yatastacchaktiyogena yuktāni nabhasā yathā  ViP dvitīyaṃ viṣṇusaṃjñasya yogidhyeyaṃ mahāmate amūrtaṃ brahmaṇo rūpaṃ yat sad ityu cyate budhaiḥ  ViP samastāḥ śaktayaścaitā nṛpa yatra pratiṣṭhitāḥ tadviśvarūpavairūpyaṃ rūpam anyad dharer mahat  ViP samastaśaktirūpāṇi tatkaroti janeśvara devatiryaṅmanuṣyādiceṣṭāvanti svalīlayā  ViP jagatāmupakārāya na sā karmanimittajā ceṣṭā tasyāprameyasya vyāpinyavyāhatātmikā  ViP tadrūpaṃ viśvarūpasya tasya yogayujā nṛpa cintyamātmaviśuddhyarthaṃ sarvakilbiṣanāśanam  ViP yathāgniruddhataśikhaḥ kakṣaṃ dahati sānilaḥ tathā cittasthito viṣṇuryogināṃ sarvakilbiṣam  ViP tasmātsamastaśaktīnāmādhāre tatra cetasaḥ kurvīta saṃsthitiṃ sā tu vijñeyā śuddhadhāraṇā  ViP śubhāśrayasya cittasya sarvagasyācalātmanaḥ tribhāvabhāghanātīto muktaye yogino nṛpa  ViP anye tu puruṣavyāghra cetaso ye vyāpāśrayāḥ aśuddhāste samastāstu devādyāḥ karmayonayaḥ  ViP mūrtaṃ bhagavato rūpaṃ sarvāpāśrayanispṛham eṣā vai dhāraṇa proktā yaccittaṃ tatra dhāryate  ViP yacca mūrtaṃ hare rūpaṃ yādṛkcintyaṃ narādhipa tacchrūyatāmanādhārā dhāramā nopapadyate  ViP prasannavadanaṃ cārupadmapatropamekṣaṇam sukapolaṃ suvistīrṇalalāṭaphalakojjvalam  ViP samakarṇāntavinyastacārukuṇḍalabhūṣaṇam kaṃbugrīvaṃ suvīstīrṇaśrīvatsāṃkitavakṣasam  ViP valitribhaṅginā magnanābhinā hyudareṇa ca pralaṃbāṣṭabhujaṃ viṣṇumathavāpi caturbhujam  ViP samasthitorujaṅghaṃ ca susthitāṅghrivarāṃbujam cintayedbrahmabhūtaṃ taṃ pītanirmalavāsasam  ViP kirīṭahārakeyūrakaṭakādivibhūṣitam  ViP śārṅgaśaṅkhagadākhaḍgacakrākṣavalayānvitam varadābhayahastaṃ ca mudrikāratnabhūṣitam  ViP cintayettanmayo yogī samādhāyātmamānasam tāvadyāvadṛḍhībhūtā tatraiva nṛpa dhāraṇā  ViP vrajatastiṣṭhatonyadvā svecchayā karma kurvataḥ nāpayāti yadā cittatsiddhāṃ manyeta tāṃ tadā  ViP tataḥ śaṅkhagadācakraśarṅgīdirahitaṃ budhaḥ cintayedbhagavadrūpaṃ praśāntaṃ sākṣasūtrakam  ViP sā yadā dhāraṇā tadvadavasthānavatī tataḥ kiriṭakeyūramukhair bhūṣaṇai rahitaṃ smaret  ViP tadekāvayavaṃ devaṃ cetasā hi punarbudhaḥ kuryāttato vayavini praṇidhānaparo bhavet  ViP tadrūpapratyayā caikā saṃtatiścānyaniḥspṛhā taddhyānaṃ prathamair aṅgaiḥ ṣaḍbhir niṣpādyate nṛpa  ViP tasyaiva kalpanāhīnaṃ svarūpagrahaṇaṃ hiyat manasā dhyānaniṣpādyaṃ samādhiḥso bhidhīyate  ViP vijñānaṃ prāpakaṃ prāpye pare brahmaṇi pārthiva prāpaṇīyastathaivātmā prakṣīṇāśeṣabhāvanaḥ  ViP kṣetrajñaḥ karaṇī jñānaṃ karaṇaṃ tasya tena tat niṣpādya muktikāryaṃ vai kṛtakṛtyaṃ nivartate  ViP tadbhāvabhāvamāpannastato sau paramātmanā bhavatyabhedī bhedaś ca tasyājñānakṛto bhavet  ViP vibhedajanake jñāne nāśamātyantikaṃ gate ātmano brahmaṇo bhedama saṃtaṃ kaḥ karīṣyati  ViP ityuktaste mayā yogaḥ khāṇḍikya paripṛcchataḥ saṃkṣepavistarābhyāṃ tu kimanyatkriyatāṃ tava  ViP khāṇḍikya uvācakathite yogasadbhāve sarvameva kṛtaṃ mama tavopadeśenāśeṣo naṣṭaścittamalo yataḥ  ViP mameti yanmayā coktamasadetanna cānyathā naredra gadituṃ śakyamapi vijñeyavedibhiḥ  ViP ahaṃ mametyavidyeyaṃ vyavahārastathānayoḥ paramārthastvasaṃlāpo gocare vacasāṃ na yaḥ  ViP tadgaccha śreyase sarvaṃ mamaitadbhavatā kṛtam yadvimuktiprado yogaḥ proktaḥ keśidhvajāvyayaḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācayathārhaṃ pūjayā tena khāṇḍikyena sa pūjitaḥ ājagāma puraṃ brahmaṃstataḥ keśidhvajo nṛpaḥ  ViP khāṇḍikyo pi sutaṃ kṛtvā rājānaṃ yogasiddaye vanaṃ jagāma govinde viniveśitamānasaḥ  ViP tatraikāntamatirbhūtvā yamādiguṇasaṃyutaḥ viṣṇvākhye nirmale brahmaṇy avāpa nṛpatir layam  ViP keśidhvajo vimuktyarthaṃ svakarmakṣapaṇonmukhaḥ bubhuje viṣayānkarma cakre cānabhisaṃhitam  ViP akalyāṇopabhogaiś ca kṣīṇapāpo malas tathā avāpa siddhimatyantāṃ tāpakṣayaphalāṃ dvija  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe saptamo dhyāyaḥ śrīparāśara uvācaityeṣa kathitaḥsamyak tṛtīyaḥ pratisaṃcaraḥ ātyantiko vimuktiryā layo brahmaṇi śāśvate  ViP sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṃśamanvantarāṇi ca vaṃśānucaritaṃ caiva bhavato gaditaṃ mayā  ViP purāmaṃ baiṣṇavaṃ caitatsarvakilbiṣanāśanam viśiṣṭaṃ sarvaśāstrebhyaḥ puruṣārthopapādakam  ViP tubhyaṃ yathāvanmaitreya proktaṃ śuśruṣave vyayam yadanyadapi vaktavyaṃ tṛtpṛcchādya vadāmi te  ViP maitreya uvācabhagavankathitaṃ sarvaṃ yatpṛṣṭosi mayā mune śrutaṃ caitanmayā bhaktyā nānyatpraṣṭavyamasti me  ViP vicchinnāḥsarvasaṃdehā vaimalyaṃ manasaḥ kṛtam tvatprasādānmayā jñātā utpattisthitisaṃkṣayāḥ  ViP jñātaś ca trividho rāśiḥ śaktiś ca trividhā guro vijñātā sā ca kārtsnyena trividhā bhāvabhāvanā  ViP tvatprasādānmayā jñātaṃ jñeyamanyair alaṃ dvija yadetadakhilaṃ viṣṇorjaganna vyatiricyate  ViP kṛtārthohamasaṃdehastvatprasādānmahāmune varṇadharmādayo dharmā viditā yadaśeṣataḥ  ViP pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca jñānaṃ karmamayākhilam prasīda viprapravara nānyatpraṣṭavyamasti me  ViP yadasya kathanāyāsair yo rjito si mayā guro tatkṣamyatāṃ viśeṣosti na satāṃ putraśiṣyayoḥ  ViP śrīparāśara uvācaetatte yanmayākhyātaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmatam śrute sminsarvadoṣotthaḥ pāparāśiḥ praṇaśyati  ViP sargaś ca pratisargaś ca vaṃśamanvantarāmi ca vaṃśānucaritaṃ kṛtsnaṃ mayātra tava kīrtitam  ViP atra devās tathā daityā gandharvoragarākṣasāḥ yakṣavidyādharāḥsiddhāḥ kathyante psarasas tathā  ViP munayo bhāvitātmānaḥ kathyante tapasānvitāḥ cāturvaṇyaṃ tathā puṃsā viśiṣṭacaritānica  ViP puṇyāḥ pradeśā medinyāḥ puṇyā nadyo tha sāgarāḥ parvatāś ca mahāpuṇyāścaritāni ca dhīmatām  ViP varṇadharmādayo dharmāvedaśāstrāṇi kṛtsnaśaḥ yeṣāṃ saṃsmaramātsadyaḥsarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  ViP utpattisthitināśānāṃ heturyo jagato vyayaḥ sa sarvabhūtaḥsarvātmā kathyate bhagavānhariḥ  ViP avaśenāpi yannāmni kīrtite sarvapātakaiḥ pumānvimanacye sadyaḥsiṃhatrastair mṛgair iva  ViP yannāmakīrtanaṃ bhaktyā vilāyanamanuttamam maitreyāseṣapāpānāṃ dhātūnāmiva pāvakaḥ  ViP kalikalmaṣamatyugraṃ narakārttipradaṃ nṛṇām prayāti vilayaṃ sadyaḥsakṛdyatra ca saṃsmṛte  ViP hiraṇyagarbhadevendrarudrādityāśvivāyubhiḥ pāvakair vasubhiḥ sādhyair viśvedevādibhiḥ suraiḥ  ViP yakṣarakṣoragaiḥ siddhair daityagandharvadānavaiḥ apsarobhis tathā tārānakṣatraiḥ sakalair grahaiḥ  ViP saptarṣibhis tathā dhiṣṇyair dhiṣṇyādhipatibhis tathā brahmaṇādyair manuṣyaiś ca tathaiva paśubhir mṛgaiḥ  ViP sarīsṛpair vihaṅgaiś ca palāśādyair mahīruhaiḥ vanāgnisāgarasaritpātālaiḥ sasurāgnibhiḥ  ViP śabdādibhiścasahitaṃ brahmāṇḍamakhilaṃ dvija merorivāṇuryasyaitadyanmayaṃ ca dvijottama  ViP sa sarvaḥ sarvavitsarvasvarūpo rūpavarjitaḥ bhagavānkīrtito viṣṇuratra pāpapraṇāśanaḥ  ViP yadaśvamedhāvabhṛthe snātaḥ prāpnoti vai phalam mānavastadavāpnoti śrutvaitanmunisattama  ViP prayāge puṣkarecaiva kurukṣetre tathārṇave kṛtopavāsaḥ prāpnoti tadasya śravaṇānnaraḥ  ViP yadagnihotre suhute varṣeṇāpnoti mānavaḥ mahāpuṇyaphalaṃ vipra tadasya śravaṇātsakṛt  ViP yajjyeṣṭhasukladvādaśyāṃ snātvā vai yamunājale mathurāyāṃ hariṃ dṛṣṭvā prāpnoti puruṣaḥ phalam  ViP tadāpnotyakhilaṃ samyagadhyāyaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti vai purāṇasyāsya viprarṣa keśavārpitamānasaḥ  ViP yamunāsalilasnātaḥ puruṣo munisattama jyeṣṭhāmūle site pakṣe dvādaśyāṃ samupoṣitaḥ  ViP samabhyarcyācyutaṃ samyaṅ mathurāyāṃ samāditaḥ aśvamedhasya yajñasya prāpnotyavikalaṃ phalam  ViP ālokyardhimathānyeṣāmunnītānāṃ svavaṃśajaiḥ etatkilocurapyeṣāṃ pitaraḥ sapitāmahāḥ  ViP kaccidasmatkule jātaḥ kālindīsalilāplutaḥ artayiṣyati govindaṃ mathurāyāmupoṣitaḥ  ViP jyoṣṭhāmūle site pakṣe kenaivaṃ vayamapyuta parāmṛddhimavāpsyāmastāritāḥsvakulodbhavaiḥ  ViP jyeṣṭhāmūle site pakṣe samabhyarcya janārdanam dhanyānāṃ kulajaḥ piṇḍānyamunāyāṃ pradāsyati  ViP tasminkāle samabhyarcya tatra kṛṣṇaṃ samāhitaḥ dattvā piṇḍaṃ pitṛbhyaś ca yamunāsalilāplutaḥ  ViP yadāpnoti naraḥ puṇyaṃ tārayansvapitāmahān śrutvādhyāyaṃ tadāpnoti purāṇasyāsya śaktitaḥ  ViP etatsaṃsārabhīrūṇāṃ paritrāṇamanuttamam śrāvyāṇāṃ paramaṃ śrāvyaṃ pavitrāṇāmanuttamam  ViP duḥsvapnanāśanaṃ nṝṇāṃ sarvaduṣṭanibarhaṇam maṅgalaṃ maṅgalānāṃ ca putrasaṃpatpradāyakam  ViP idamārṣaṃ purā prāha ṛbhave kamalodbhavaḥ ṛbhuḥ priyavratāyāha sa ca bhāguraye bavīt  ViP bhāguristaṃbhamitrāya dadhīcāya sa coktavān sārasvatāya tenoktaṃ bhṛguḥsārasvatena ca  ViP bhṛguṇā purukutsāya narmadāyai sa coktavān narmadā dhṛtarāṣṭrāyanāgāyāpūraṇāya ca  ViP tābhyāṃ ca nāgarājāya proktaṃ vāsukaye dvija vāsukiḥ prāha vatsāya vatsaścāśvatarāya vai  ViP kaṃbalāya ca tenoktamelāputrāya tena vai  ViP pātālaṃ samanuprāptaḥ tato vedaśirā muniḥ prāptavānetadakhilaṃ sa ca pramataye dadau  ViP dattaṃ pramatinā caitajjātukarṇāya dhīmate jātukarṇena caivoktamanyeṣāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām  ViP pulastyavaradānena mamāpyetatsmṛtiṃ gatam mayāpi tūbhyaṃ maitreya yathāvatkathitaṃ tbidam  ViP tvamapyetacchinīkāya kalerante vadiṣyasi  ViP ityetatparamaṃ guhyaṃ kalikalmaṣanāśanam yaḥ śṛṇoti naro bhaktyā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate  ViP samastatīrthasnānāni samastāmarasaṃstutiḥ kṛtā tena bhavedetadyaḥ śṛṇotidinedite  ViP kapilādānajanitaṃ pumyamatyantadurlabham śrutvaitasya daśādhyāyānavāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ  ViP yastvetatsakalaṃ śṛṇotipuruṣaḥ kṛtvā manasyacyutaṃ sarvaṃ sarvamayaṃ samastajagatāmādhāramātmāśrayam jñānajñeyamanādimantarahitaṃ sarvāmarāṇāṃ hitaṃ sa prāpnoti na saṃśayostyavikalaṃ yadvājimedhe phalam  ViP yatrādau bhagavāṃścarācaragururmadhye tathānte ca sa brahmajñānamayo cyuto khilajaganmadhyāntasargaprabhuḥ tatasarvaṃ puruṣaḥ pavitramamalaṃ śṛṇvanpaṭhanvācayanprāpnotyasti na tatphalaṃ tribhuvaneṣvekāntasiddhirhariḥ  ViP yasminnyastamanirna yāti narakaṃ svargo pi yaccintane vighno yatra niveśitātmamanaso brāhmo pi loko lpakaḥ muktiṃ cetasi yaḥsthito maladhiyāṃ puṃsāṃ dadātyavyayaḥ kiṃ citraṃ yadaghaṃ prayāti vilayaṃ tatrācyute kīrtite  ViP yajñair yajñavido yajanti satataṃ yajñeśvaraṃ karmiṇo yaṃ vai brahmamayaṃ parāvaramayaṃ dhyāyanti ca jñāninaḥ yaṃ saṃcitya na jāyate na mriyate no vardhate hīyate naivāsanna ca sadbhavatyati tataḥ kiṃ vā hareḥ śrūyatām  ViP kavyaṃ yaḥ putṛrūpadhṛgvidhihutaṃ havyaṃ ca bhuktaṃ vibhurdevatve bhagavānanādinidhanaḥsāvahāsvadhāsaṃjñite yasminbrahmaṇi sarvaśaktinilaye mānāni no mānināṃ viṣṭhāyai prabhavanti hanti kaluṣaṃ śrotraṃ sa yāto hariḥ  ViP nāntosti yasya na ca yasya samudbhavo sti vṛddhirna yasya pariṇāmavivarjitasya nāpakṣayaṃ ca samupaityavikāri vastu yastaṃ natosmi puruṣotmamīśamīḍyam  ViP tasyaiva yonu gumabhugbahudhaika eva suddhopyaśuddha iva bhāti hi mūrtibhedaiḥ jñānānvitaḥsakalasattvavibhūtikartā tasmai namostu puruṣāya sadāvyayāya  ViP jñānapravṛttiniyamaikyamayāya puṃso bhogapradānapaṭave triguṇātmakāya avyākṛtāya bhavabāvanakāraṇāya vande svarūpabhavanāya sadājarāya  ViP vyomānilāgnijalabhūracanāmayāya śabdādibhogyaviṣayopanayakṣamāya puṃsaḥsamastakaraṇair upakārakāya vyaktāya sūkṣmabṛhadātmavate natosmi  ViP iti vividhamajasya yasya rūpaṃ prakṛtiparātmamayaṃ sanātanasya pradiśatu bhagavānaśeṣapuṃsāṃ harirapajanmajarādikāṃ siddhim  ViP iti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇe ṣaṣṭhāṃśe ṣṭamo dhyāyaḥ samāpto yaṃ ṣaṣṭhāṃśaḥiti śrīviṣṇumahāpurāṇaṃ samāptam
